#!/usr/bin/perl

# terms of the GNU General Public License as published by the Free Software
# Foundation. It is distributed in the hope that it will be useful, but WITHOUT
# ANY WARRANTY WHATSOEVER.
#

# with the package; see the file 'COPYING'. If not, write to the Free Software
# Foundation, Inc., 51 Franklin Street, Fifth Floor, Boston, MA 02110-1301 USA.

# Output extended help corresponding to a given GP command. By default,
# extract relevant information from  from the PARI manual, run TeX, then open
# an xdvi display.
#
# The manual can be compressed.
#
# Usage: gphelp keyword
#
# Command line options:
#  -k: apropos (list of relevant GP functions)
#  -detex      (-d): don't use TeX + xdvi (implicit when DISPLAY is not set).
#  -color_help (-ch) <number>: use color "number" (same scheme as in GP)
#  -color_bold (-cb) <number>: display bold in color "number"
#  -color_underline (-cu) <number>: display underlined text in color "number"
#
#  -raw   use internal format for output with @x markers, -detex is implicit
#         (for the TeX-to-pod converter)
#
#  -to_pod file		convert file to POD (should be the only args)
#
#  -to_dumbpod file	same, but without nested formating
#  -utf8  in detex mode, use UFT-8 encoding for output
#
# Granted environment variables (override):
#  GPTMPDIR: where temporary files will go (/tmp by default).
#  GPDOCDIR: where is manual (by default, where make install will put it).
#  GPXDVI: which 'xdvi' program to call (xdvi by default)
#
$version= "2.9.1";
$datadir= "/ds/CENTOS/common/share/pari";
# no expanded material (@key@) below
$wwwsite= "http://pari.math.u-bordeaux.fr/";

$xdvi = $ENV{GPXDVI} || "xdvi";
$xdviref = $ENV{GPXDVIREF} || "$xdvi -paper 29.7x21cm";
$gzip = "gzip";
$zcat = "$gzip -dc";
$bzip = "bzip2";
$bzcat = "$bzip -dc";
$docdir = &get_docdir();
$tex = $ENV{GPTEX} || "tex";

$refcard = (@ARGV and $ARGV[-1] =~ /refcard/i);

$dumb_pod=1, $ARGV[0] = '-to_pod' if @ARGV && $ARGV[0] eq '-to_dumb_pod';
&to_pod() if @ARGV == 2 && $ARGV[0] eq '-to_pod';

&options(); &init();
if ($#ARGV < 0) { &treat(""); cleanexit(); }

&pretex() if (!$detex);
for (@ARGV) { &treat($_); }
if ($apropos) { &apropos_final_print(); cleanexit(); }
&posttex() if (!$detex);
print "ugly_kludge_done\n" if (!$detex && $fromgp);
cleanexit();

#
# Procedures
#
sub cleanexit {
  print "\e[0m" unless $to_pod or $raw;
  exit 0;
}

sub help {
  print "Usage: $0 [-k] [-detex] [-ch c1] [-cb c2] [-cu c3] keyword\n";
  print "where c1,c2,c3 denote background, bold and underline color\n";
  exit(1);
}

sub options {
  $utf8 = $raw = $detex = $fromgp = $apropos = $noskip = 0;
  $ch = $cb = $cu = '';
  while ($_ = $ARGV[0])
  {
    last if (! /^-[a-z]/);
    shift(@ARGV);
    if ($_ eq "-fromgp")
      { $fromgp = 1; }
    elsif ($_ eq "-k")
      { $apropos = $detex = 1; }
    elsif ($_ eq "-balloon")
      { $balloon = 1; }
    elsif ($_ eq "-detex" || $_ eq "-d")
      { $detex = 1; }
    elsif ($_ eq "-raw")
      { $raw = $detex = 1; }
    elsif ($_ eq "-utf8")
      { $utf8 = 1; }
    elsif ($_ eq "-noskip")
      { $noskip = 1; }
    elsif ($_ eq "-color_help" || $_ eq "-ch")
      { $ch = &color(shift(@ARGV)); }
    elsif ($_ eq "-color_bold" || $_ eq "-cb")
      { $cb = &color(shift(@ARGV)); }
    elsif ($_ eq "-color_underline" || $_ eq "-cu")
      { $cu = &color(shift(@ARGV)); }
    else
      { &help(); }
  }
  $ch = "\e[m$ch";
  $cu .= $cu ? "\e[1m": "\e[4m";
  $cb .= "\e[1m";
  $detex = 1 if (!$ENV{DISPLAY});
}

sub get_docdir {
  my $d = $ENV{GPDOCDIR} || $ENV{GPHELP_DOCDIR};
  if (!defined $d) {
    # work from TOPDIR/Oarch or TOPDIR too: may be uninstalled yet;
    $d = $0; $d =~ s,/gphelp,,;
    for ("$datadir", '.', '..', $d) {
      my $t = "$_/doc";
      if (-f "$t/translations") { $d = $t; last; }
    }
    $d ||= "$datadir/doc";	# Last resort
  }
  if ($d =~ /^\./) {
    eval { require Cwd;
      $d = Cwd::cwd() . "/$d";
      $d =~ s,doc/\.\./doc,doc,;
    }
  }
  return $d;
}

sub init {
  &inittr();

  $indent = "   ";
  # avoid Glob.pm! (for minimal Windows install)
  opendir(DIR, $docdir) || die "$docdir not found";
  @file_list = grep { /^usersch.*tex/ } readdir(DIR);
  closedir(DIR);

  chdir($docdir);
  $docfile = "usersch3.tex";
  open(IN,"translations") || die("Could not find translation file, docdir='$docdir'");
  while(<IN>)
  {
    chomp; @_ = split(/ *\@ */);
    $key = shift(@_);
    $transl{$key} = join('@',@_);
  }
  close(IN);
}

sub not_found {
  my($help) = shift;
  $help =~ s/\\\\/_B#K#S_/g;
  $help =~ s/\\(.)/$1/g;
  $help =~ s/_B#K#S_/\\/g;
  print "'$help' not found !\n";
}

sub choose_chap {
  while (s/\@([0-9])$//) { $docfile = "usersch$1.tex"; }
  if (-f $docfile) { $pipe = ""; }
  else
  {
    die "Cannot find $docfile"
      if (! -f "$docfile.z" &&
          ! -f "$docfile.gz" &&
          ! -f "$docfile.Z" &&
          ! -f "$docfile.bz2");
    if (-f "$docfile.bz2") {
        $pipe = $bzcat;
        $docfile = "$docfile.bz2";
    } else {
        $pipe = $zcat;
    }
  }
}

sub safe_setsid {
  eval {
    require POSIX;
    POSIX::setsid(); # detach from terminal (^C will not kill xdvi)
  };
}

# assume we're in $docdir
sub open_viewer_then_quit {
  my $F = shift;
  my ($f, $viewer, $redirect);
  my $cygwin = ($^O =~ /cygwin/);
  my $win32 = ($^O =~ /ms(win|ys)/);
  my $osx = ($^O =~ /darwin/);

  $f = "$F.dvi";
  $f = "$F.dvi.gz" if (! -f "$f");
  $f = "$F.pdf"    if (! -f "$f");
  die "could not find \'$F\'" if (! -f "$f");
  $F = $f;
  $redirect = ' 2>/dev/null >/dev/null &';
  if ($f =~ /\.dvi/)
  { # DVI
    $viewer = ($f =~ /refcard/)? $xdviref: $xdvi;
  }
  elsif ($cygwin)
  { # PDF Win32
    @_ = split(/"/, `acro.exe`);
    ($viewer = $_[1]) =~ s,\\,/,g;

    $redirect = "";
    $F =~ s,/cygdrive/(.),$1:, ; # Reader can't cope with Cygwin paths
    $F      = "\"$F\"";
    $viewer = "\"$viewer\"";
  }
  elsif ($win32)
  { # PDF Win32
    @_ = split(/"/, "$ENV{GP_PDF_VIEWER}");
    $viewer = $_[1];
    print "using \'$viewer\', ";
  }
  elsif ($osx)
  {
    $viewer = "open";
  }
  else
  { # PDF generic
    $viewer = "acroread";
  }

  print "displaying \'$F\'.";
  print "\n" if (!$fromgp);
  safe_setsid();
  if ($win32)
  {
    system($viewer,$F);
  }
  else
  {
    system("$viewer $F$redirect");
  }
  cleanexit();
}

sub treat {
  my($help);
  $_ = $_[0];
  s/_QUOTE/'/g;
  s/_BACKQUOTE/`/g;
  s/_DOUBQUOTE/"/g;
  s/^ *"(.*)"([^"]*) *$/$1$2/;
  if (s/\@$//)
  {
    $found = 0;
    $searchall = 1;
    $help = $_;
    for (@file_list)
    {
      next if (!/^usersch(.*)\.tex/);

      &treat("$help\@$1");
      if ($apropos && $#list > 0 || $#sentence_list > 0)
      {
        print "\nChapter $1:\n";
        print "==========\n";
        &apropos_final_print();
      }
    }
    return not_found($help) if (!$found && !$apropos);
    $searchall = 0;
    $apropos = 0; return;
  }
  &choose_chap;

  if (!$apropos)
  {
    $_ = "users" if (/^$/);
    open_viewer_then_quit($_) if (/^(users|tutorial|refcard|libpari)$/);
    if ($transl{$_}) { $_ = $transl{$_}; &choose_chap; }
  }

  s/(\W)/\\$1/g;
  s/_/\\\\_/g if (!/^se\\:/);
      ($pipe && open(DOC,"$pipe $docfile |"))
  || (!$pipe && open(DOC,"$docfile")) || die "Cannot open $docfile: $!";
  return &apropos($_) if ($apropos);

  if (/^\\[<>=!](\\=)?$/ || /^\\\|\\\||\\&\\&$/ || /\\\||&/ || /===/)
    { $_ = 'Comparison and Boolean operators'; }
  $help = $_;

  my ($first);
  my ($pat) = $help;
  if ($pat =~ /[a-zA-Z0-9]$/) { $pat .= '\b'; } else { $pat .= '}'; }
  while (<DOC>)
  {
    if (/\\(subsubsec[a-z]*|subsec[a-z]*|section|chapter|label)\{$pat/)
      { $first = $_; last; }
  }
  if (eof(DOC))
  {
    &not_found($help) if (!$searchall);
    return;
  }
  $found = 1;
  if (!$detex) { tex($first); }
  else
  {
    &detex(); print "\n" if (!$fromgp);
    # Avoid broken pipe from zcat
    do {local $/; <DOC>} if $^O eq 'os2' and $pipe;
  }
  close(DOC);
}

#
#  A propos
#

sub apropos_print_list {
  $current = "";
  @_ = sort(@_);
  for (@_)
  {
    next if ($_ eq $current);
    $current = $_; print "$indent$_\n";
  }
}

sub apropos_raw_print {
  $indent = "";
  &apropos_print_list(@sentence_list);
  &apropos_print_list(@list);
}

sub apropos_final_print {
  my($maxlen) = 0;
  my($i,$nbcol,$current);
  my($cols) = ($ENV{'COLUMNS'} || 80) - 1;

  if ($raw) { &apropos_raw_print(); return; }
  @list = sort(@list);
  for (@list)
  {
    $i= length($_);
    $maxlen = $i if ($i > $maxlen);
  }
  $maxlen++; $nbcol = $cols / $maxlen;
  $nbcol =~ s/\..*//;
  $nbcol-- if  ($nbcol * $maxlen == $cols);
  $nbcol = 1 if (!$nbcol);

  $current = ""; $i = 0;
  for (@list)
  {
    next if ($_ eq $current);
    $current = $_; print($_); $i++;
    if ($i >= $nbcol)
    {
      $i=0; print "\n"; next;
    }
    print " " x ($maxlen - length($_));
  }
  print "\n" if ($i);
  if ($#sentence_list > 0)
  {
    print "\nSee also:\n" if ($#list > 0);
    $indent = "  ";
    apropos_print_list(@sentence_list);
  }
}

sub apropos_check {
  my($line, $current) = @_;
  $line =~ s/\n/ /g;
  return if ($line !~ /$help/i);

  local($_) = $current;
  s/\\b\{(.)\}/\\$1/;
  s/\{\}//g;
  s/\\pow/^/;
  s/\\%/%/;
  s/\\bs/\\/;
  s/\\_/_/g;
  s/\\\#/\#/g;
  s,\+\$/\$-,+/-,;
  s/\$\(.*//; # remove argument lists
  if (/ /) { push(@sentence_list,$_); } else { push(@list,$_); }
}

sub apropos {
  my($line,$current,$new);
  $help = $_[0];
  $help='\\\\pow' if ($help eq '\^');
  $help='\\\\til' if ($help eq '\~');
  @sentence_list = @list = "";
  while (<DOC>)
  {
    if (/^\\(subsubsec[a-z]*|subsec[a-z]*|section|chapter)\{/)
    {
      $new = &get_match($_,'{','}');
      &apropos_check($line, $current);
      $current = $new; $line = "";
    }
    $line .= $_;
  }
  &apropos_check($line, $current);
}

##
##  Tex Part
##
# Actual text is in file TEX. Parimacro + Geometry info goes to WRAP
sub pretex {
  my ($basedir) = $ENV{GPHELP_TMPDIR} || $ENV{GPTMPDIR} || $ENV{TMPDIR} || "/tmp";
  $tmpdir = "$basedir/gp.help$$";
  mkdir $tmpdir, 0755 || die "Cannot create temporary directory";
  $texfile = "$tmpdir/gp.help";

  open(TEX,">$texfile.tex") || die "Couldn't open $texfile.tex";
}

sub endsection
{
  /^\\(section|sub[sub]*sec)/i && ($noskip || !/\%GPHELPskip/);
}

sub tex { my ($first) = @_;
  print TEX $first;
  while (<DOC>)
  {
    last if endsection();
    print TEX;
  }
}

sub posttex {
  my ($wrap) = "$tmpdir/gpwrapper.help";
  my (@goners) = ("$texfile.tex",
                  "$wrap.tex", "$wrap.dvi", "$wrap.log", "$wrap.aux");
  if (!$found) { unlink @goners; rmdir("$tmpdir"); cleanexit(); }

  open(WRAP, ">$wrap.tex") || die "Couldn't open $wrap.tex";
  if ($balloon) {
    print WRAP '\nopagenumbers\def\fromgphelp{}'
    . "\\input $docdir/parimacro.tex"
    . '\setbox0\vbox{'
    . "\\input $texfile.tex"
    . ' }
\dimen0=\the\ht0 \advance\dimen0 by \dp0
\advance\dimen0 by 60pt
\dimen1=\the\wd0
\advance\dimen1 by 60pt
\vsize \dimen0
\hsize \dimen1
\advance\voffset 30pt\advance\hoffset 30pt
\advance\hoffset-1in \advance\voffset-1in
\special{papersize=\the\dimen1,\the\dimen0}
\noindent\box0
\end';
  } else {
    print WRAP '\nopagenumbers\def\fromgphelp{}'
    . "\\input $docdir/parimacro.tex"
    . "\\input $texfile.tex"
    . '\end';
  }
  close(WRAP) || die "Error closing '$wrap.tex': $!";
  close(TEX) || die "Error closing '$texfile.tex': $!";

  chdir($tmpdir);
  $out = `$tex $wrap.tex 2>&1 < /dev/null`;
  -f "$wrap.dvi"
    || die "could not create '$wrap.dvi': status=$?, $out";
  safe_setsid();
  my ($goners) = join(" ", @goners);
  system("($xdvi $wrap.dvi 2>/dev/null >/dev/null; rm -f $goners; rmdir $tmpdir)&");
}

#
#  Detex Part
#
sub fit_loop {
  my($i);
  return if ($miss > 9 || $#_ <= 0);
  while ($miss > 0)
  {
#  print "1:$miss ";print @_;print "\n";
    for (@_) { $miss-- if (s/([?!\.;])$/$1 /);
       return if ($miss == 0);
    }
#  print "2:$miss ";print @_;print "\n";
    for (@_) { $miss-- if (s/([?!\.;]) $/$1  /);
       return if ($miss == 0);
    }
#  print "3:$miss ";print @_;print "\n";
    for (@_) { $miss-- if (s/([\),])$/$1 /);
       return if ($miss == 0);
    }
#  print "4:$miss ";print @_;print "\n";
    $i = 0;
    for (@_)
    {
      if (!$i) { $i = 1; next; }
      $miss-- if (s/^\(/ (/);
       return if ($miss == 0);
    }
#  print "5:$miss "; print @_;print "\n";
    for (@_)
    {
       next if (/^ *$/);
       $miss--; s/$/ /;
       return if ($miss == 0);
    }
  }
}

sub fit_line {
  my($wi, @a);
  my($l) = -1;
  my($rem) = $_[0];
  for (@l)
  {
     my ($l2) = $l; $l += ($_ + 1);
     if ($l > $rem) { $l = $l2; last; }
     $wi++;
  }
  $miss = $rem - $l;
  splice(@l, 0, $wi);
  @a = splice(@w, 0, $wi-1); &fit_loop(@a);
  push(@a, shift(@w)); return join(' ', @a);
}

# empty output line
sub is_void {
  my($in) = shift;
  $in =~ s/\@\[\w+\]//g;
  $in =~ s/\@[012]//g;
  ($in =~ /^\s*$/)? 1: 0;
}

sub nl { push(@f_text, shift); }

sub split_words { my ($txt) = @_;
  $txt =~ s/^ +//;
  for ( split(/\s+/, $txt) )
  {
    s/\Q$tr{nbrk}/ /g;
    my ($w) = $_;
    # these codes will be replaced by 1 character
    s/\@\[(obr|cbr|ldollar|lt|gt|\{|\})]/\@/g;
    if ($utf8)
    { s/\@\[(ouml|uuml|agrav|aacute|eacute|pm)]/\@/g; } # one char
    else
    {
      s/\@\[(ouml|uuml|agrav|aacute|eacute)]/\@\@/g;  # two chars
      s/\@\[pm]/+\/-/g; # three chars
    }
    # the rest will be replaced by zero-width characters
    s/\@\[\w+\]//g;
    my ($l) = length($_);
    # zero-width word
    if (!$l && $#w >= 0) { $w[$#w] .= $w; next; }
    push(@l, $l);
    push(@w, $w);
  }
  # first word might still be zero-width
  if ($#w >= 1 && !$l[0])
  {
    splice(@w, 0,2, "$w[0]$w[1]");
    splice(@l, 0,1);
  }
}

sub format_text {
  my($last_void) = 0;
  my($noindent) = 0;
  my($init) = 1;
  my($cols) = ($ENV{'COLUMNS'} || 80) - 1;
  my($first) = $cols - length($indent);

  for (@text)
  {
    if (s/^\@1//)       # start verbatim
    {
      nl(&fit_line($first)) if (@w);
      nl("") if (!$last_void && !is_void($_)); # add empty line
      nl("$indent$_"); next;
    }
    if (s/^\@0//)    # verbatim lines
    {
      nl("$indent$_"); next;
    }

    if (s/^\@2//)       # end verbatim, add indent
    {
      nl("") if (!$last_void);
      $last_void = 1;
      split_words($_); next;
    }

    if (s/^\@3//)       # end verbatim + no indent
    {
      nl("") if (!$last_void);
      $noindent = 1;
      $last_void = 1;
      split_words($_); next;
    }

    if (!is_void($_)) { split_words($_); next; }

    # line is empty, split out previous paragraph
    next if (!@l || !$l[0]); # nothing
    if ($init) {
      nl(&fit_line($first));
    } else {
      nl("") if (!$last_void);
      nl("\@[endbold]" . ($noindent? "": $indent) 
                       . &fit_line($noindent? $cols: $first));
    }
    while (@w) { nl(&fit_line($cols)); }
    $noindent = $init = $last_void = 0;
  }
}

# argument has the form s1${open}s2${close}s3
# Return 's2'. Set $remainder to 's3'.
sub get_match {
  local ($_, $open, $close) = @_;
  my (@tmp, $arg,$parity,$ok);
  my ($obr) = 1;
  $parity = ($open eq $close);
  /$open/; $_ = $'; # remove everything before (and including) first $open

  while ($_) {
    @tmp = split(/($open|$close)/);
    while ($#tmp >= 0) {
      $_ = shift(@tmp);
      $obr++ if (/^$open$/);
      if ($parity && $obr == 2) { $ok = 1; last }
      $obr-- if (/^$close$/);
      if (!$obr) { $ok = 1; last }
      $arg .= $_;
    }
    last if ($ok);
    $_ = <DOC>;
  }
  $remainder = join('',@tmp);
  return $arg;
}

sub detex {
  my($fun);
# 1: get the function "prototype"
  $fun = &get_match($_,'{','}');
  $fun = &basic_subst($fun);
  $_ = $remainder;
  $_ = <DOC> if (!&basic_subst($_));
  push(@text, "\@[startbold]$fun:\@[endbold]");
  push(@text, "");
# 2: parse the function description
  if ($_) { s/^ *://; &presubst(); }
  while (<DOC>)
  {
    last if endsection();
    &presubst();
  }
  if ($raw) { print join("\n", @text); return; }
#  for (@text) { print("AA{$_}BB\n"); } # DEBUG
  &format_text();
  for (@f_text) { &TeXprint($_); }
}

# We use the special char @ to transmit special sequences
sub inittr {
  @ou = qw( dollar nbrk startref endref startbold endbold startcode endcode
	    obr cbr uuml ouml agrave aacute eacute
	    startpodcode endpodcode startlink endlink
            startbc endbc
            startbg endbg
	    startbcode endbcode startbi endbi startit endit
	    startword endword startlword endlword pm empty gt lt podleader );

  @tr{@ou} = map "\@[$_]", @ou;
  $tr{dollar} = '$' if $to_pod;

  %pr = ( dollar => '',
	  ldollar => '$',	# literal dollar
	  nbrk => 'S< >',
	  startbold => 'B<',
	  endbold => '>',
	  startcode => 'C<',
	  startlink => 'L<',
	  endlink => '>',
	  endcode => '>',
	  obr => '{',
	  cbr => '}',
	  startpodcode => 'C<',
	  endpodcode => '>',
	  ( $dumb_pod
	    ? (startbcode => 'B<',
	       endbcode => '>',
	       startbi => 'B<',
	       endbi => '>',)
	    : (startbcode => 'B<C<',
	       endbcode => '>>',
	       startbi => 'B<I<',
	       endbi => '>>')),
          startbc => 'I<',
          endbc => '>',
          startbg => 'B<',
          endbg => '>',
	  startit => 'I<',
	  endit => '>',
	  startword => 'F<',
	  endword => '>',
	  startlword => ' F<',
	  endlword => '> ',
	  pm => 'F<+->',
	  "gt" => 'E<gt>',
	  "lt" => 'E<lt>',
	  ouml => 'E<ouml>',
	  uuml => 'E<uuml>',
	  eacute => 'E<eacute>',
	  agrave => 'E<agrave>',
	  aacute => 'E<aacute>',
	  empty => 'Z<>',
	  podleader => '=',
	);
}

sub indent_equally { my $in = shift; $in =~ s/^[ \t]*/    /mg; $in }
sub quote { my $in = shift; $in =~ s/~/\\~/g; $in }

sub basic_subst {
  local($_) = shift;

  s/\\teb\{([^\}]*)\}/"\\sidx{$1}$tr{startbold}" . quote($1) . "$tr{endbold}"/eg;
  s/\\tet\{([^\}]*)\}/"\\sidx{$1}$tr{startcode}" . quote($1) . "$tr{endcode}"/eg;
  s/\\url\{([^\}]*)\}/"\\sidx{$1}$tr{startcode}" . quote($1) . "$tr{endcode}"/eg;
  s/\\tev\{([^\}]*)\}/"\\sidx{$1}$tr{startit}" . quote($1) . "$tr{endit}"/eg;

  s/(\S)[ \t]*\n[ \t]+/$1\n/gm;
  s/([^\\])\\\{/$1$tr{obr}/g;
  s/([^\\])\\\}/$1$tr{cbr}/g;
  s/([^\\])\\-/$1/g;
  s/\A\\q?quad(?![a-zA-Z])\s*/$tr{nbrk}$tr{nbrk}/;
  s|\\wwwsite|$wwwsite|g;
  s/^\\def\\.*\{\n.*\n\}//gm;
  s/\\def\\.*//g;
  s(\\footnote\s*\{?\*+\}?\s*\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{(?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*\})*)\})
    {$tr{startbold}FOOTNOTE$tr{endbold}$tr{lt}$tr{lt}$tr{lt} $1 $tr{gt}$tr{gt}$tr{gt}}g;
  s/(\{[\w\s]+)\{\}([\s\w]+\})/$1$2/g;	# {nf{}init}
  s(\\op(?![a-zA-Z])\s*)({\\it op\\/})g;	# {nf{}init}
  s/\\emacs\b//;
  s/\\unix\b//;
  s/\\(leavevmode|strut)(?![a-zA-Z])\s*//g;
  s/ \\funno \s*
     { \s* ((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*) } \s*
     { \s* ((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*) } \s*
     { \s* ((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*) }
   /\\noindent{\\tt $1 \$\\key{$2}\$($3)}/gx;
  s/\\fun\s*\{([^{}]*)\}\s*\{((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\s*\{((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/\\kbd{$1 \\key{$2}($3)}\\sidx{$2}/g;

  s/\\\\(?=[a-zA-Z])/\\bs /g;
  s/\\b\{\}\\b\{\}/\\bs\\bs /g;
  s/\\\\/\\bs/g;
  s/(\'\'|\`\`)/"/g unless $to_pod;     # (english) double quotes
  # asymptotic or isomorphic (~) [beware of ties]
  s/(^|[^\\]) +~/$1~/;
  s/~ */~/;
  s/(^|[^\\])~/$1$tr{nbrk}/g;           # ties
  s/\\(simeq|sim|approx)(?![a-zA-Z])/ ~ /g;
  s/\\til(?![a-zA-Z])/~/g;		# ~ (transpose)
  s/\\(~|tilde|widetilde)/~/g;
  s/\\colon\b/:/g;

  s/\\(equiv)(?![a-zA-Z])/ = /g;
  s/\\'a/$tr{aacute}/g; s/\\'\{a\}/$tr{aacute}/g;
  s/\\`a/$tr{agrave}/g; s/\\`\{a\}/$tr{agrave}/g;
  s/\\"o/$tr{ouml}/g;   s/\\"\{o\}/$tr{ouml}/g;
  s/\\"u/$tr{uuml}/g;   s/\\"\{u\}/$tr{uuml}/g;
  s/\\'e/$tr{eacute}/g; s/\\'\{e\}/$tr{eacute}/g;
  s/{\\cal (.)}/$tr{startbc}$1$tr{endbc}/g;

  s/(^|[^\\])%.*/$1/g;		        # comments
  s/\\vadjust\s*\{\s*\\penalty\s*\d+\s*\}//g;

  # We do not strip %\n, thus:
  s/\\kbd\{\n\s*/\\kbd{/g;
  s/\$\\bf(\b|(?=[\d_]))\s*([^\$]+)\$/\$$tr{startbcode}$1$tr{endbcode}\$/g;
  s/\$/$tr{dollar}/g;		        # math mode
  s/\t/ /g; s/\\,//g; s/\\[ ;]/ /g;     # various spaces
  s/\\\///g;			# italic correction
  s/^&+//g;			# tab marks
  s/([^\\])&+/$1 /g;		# tab marks
  s/\\TeX\{\}/TeX/g;
  s/\\TeX(\W)/TeX$1/g;
  s/ *\\circ\b */ o /g;
  s/\\d?frac\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/($1)\/($2)/g;
  s(\\d?frac\s*(\d)\s*(\d))(($1/$2))g;
  s[{\s*(\w)\s*\\over(?![a-zA-Z])\s*(\w)\s*}]{($1/$2)}g;
  s[{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\\over(?![a-zA-Z])\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)}][($1)/($2)]g;

  # \def\synt#1#2{\syn{#1}{\tt #2}}
  # \def\syn#1#2{\synx{#1}{#2}{#1}}
  s/\\synt?\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/\\synx{$1}{$2}{$1}/g;
  # \def\synx#1#2#3{\sidx{#3}The library syntax is $\key{#1}({#2})$}
  # Often used with embedded {}.
  s/\\synx\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\{((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/\\sidx{$3}The library syntax is $tr{startcode}$tr{startbold}$1$tr{endbold}($2)$tr{endcode}/;

  # May be used with an empty arg
  s/\\typ\{([^\}]*)\}/$tr{startcode}t_$1$tr{endcode}/g;

  s/(\\string)?\\_/_/g;
  s/\\([#\$&%|])/$1/g;
  s/\\(hat(?![a-zA-Z])|\^)(\{\\?\s*\})?/^/g;
  s/\\hbox\{\\kbd\{\\pow}}/^/g; # from doc_make
  s/^(\@\[podleader\]head\d *)\\pow(?![a-zA-z])( *)/$1^$2/gm;
  s/ *\\pow(?![a-zA-z]) */^/g;

  s/\\neq?(?![a-zA-Z])/ != /g;
  s/\\enspace(?![a-zA-Z])/ /g;
  s/\\\*/ /g;
  s/\\times(?![a-zA-Z]) */ x /g;
  s/\\infty(?![a-zA-Z]) */ oo /g;
  s/ *\\(bmod|mod) */ mod /g;
  s/ *\\pmod(?![a-zA-Z]) *\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/ (mod $1)/g;
  s/ *\\cdot(?![a-zA-Z]) */./g;		# Maybe " . "?
  s/ *(\\|\@)[lc]?dots(?![a-zA-Z]) */.../g;
  # math operators
  s/\\(Norm | Frob | disc | Cl | Re | Im
    | exp | log | ln | arg | sin(h)? | cos(h)? | tan(h)? | sqrt
    | lim(proj)?
    | mod | gcd | lcm
    | Id | det | Hom | deg | expr | seq | args 
    | min | max )
    (?![a-zA-Z])/$tr{startlword}$1$tr{endlword}/xg;
#  s/\\pi(?![a-zA-Z])/$tr{startword}Pi$tr{endword}/g;

  # math symbols with HTML entities equivalents
  s/\\(Alpha | Beta | Chi | Delta | Epsilon | Phi | Gamma | Eta | Iota
    | vartheta | Kappa | Lambda | Mu | Nu | Omicron | Pi | Theta | Rho
    | Sigma | Tau | Ypsilon | varsigma | Omega | Xi | Psi | Zeta
    | alpha | beta | chi | delta | epsilon | varepsilon | phi | gamma | eta
    | iota | varphi | kappa | lambda | mu | nu | omicron | pi | theta | rho
    | sigma | tau | ypsilon | varpi | omega | xi | psi | zeta
    | ell | wp | cap | cup | sup | prod | sum | int | nmid)
    (?![a-zA-Z])/$tr{startword}$1$tr{endword}/xg;
#  s/ *\\in(?![a-zA-Z]) */ belongs to /g;
  s/\\pm(?![a-zA-Z])/$tr{pm}/g;
  s/ *\\mid(?![a-zA-Z]) */ | /g;

  s/\\idxtyp\{([^{}]*)\}/\\sidx{t_$1}/g;
  if (!$to_pod) {
    s/\\secref\{/Section \\ref{/g;
    s/\\ref\{([^\}]*)\}/$tr{startref}$1$tr{endref}/g;
    if ($raw)
    { s/\\label\{([^\}]*)\}/\@[label $1]/g; }
    else
    { s/\\label\{[^\}]*\}//g; }
  }

  s/ *\\noindent\b */\@3/;
  s/\\(medskip|bigskip|smallskip|left|right)(?![a-zA-Z])[ \t]*//g;
  s/\\vfill *(\\eject)?//g;
  s/\\(q|quad)(?![a-zA-Z])\s*/  /g;
  s/\\qquad(?![a-zA-Z])\s*/    /g;

  s/\\centerline\s*\{\s*(?:\\tt\b\s*)?(.*(\n[ \t].*)*)\}(?=\s*$)/indent_equally($1)/ge;
  s/\\centerline\s*\{\s*(?:\\tt\b\s*)?((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/ indent_equally($1)/ge;

  s/\\big\b//g;

  s/\\settabs.*//;
  s/^\\\+/\n$tr{nbrk}/gm;
  s/\\\+//g;
  s/\\cr(?![a-zA-Z])//g;
  s/\\B(?![a-zA-Z])/\\kbd{BIL}/g;

  s/ *([=><]) */ $1 /g;
  s/ *<  *([=<]) */ <$1 /g;
  s/ *>  *([=>]) */ >$1 /g;
  s/ *([*+-\/^&=|:]) += */ $1= /g;
  s/ *! *= */ != /g;
  # now fix spacing
  s/ == = / === /g;
  s/< *([-a-zA-Z]*) *>/<$1>/g;

  s/ *\\Rightarrow */ ==$tr{gt} /g;
  s/\\rangle(?![a-zA-Z])\s*/$tr{startcode}$tr{gt}$tr{endcode}/g;
  s/\\langle(?![a-zA-Z])\s*/$tr{startcode}$tr{lt}$tr{endcode}/g;
  s/\\rightarrow(?![a-zA-Z])\s*/$tr{startcode}--$tr{gt}$tr{endcode}/g;
  s/\\longleftrightarrow(?![a-zA-Z])\s*/$tr{startcode}$tr{lt}-----$tr{gt}$tr{endcode}/g;
  s/\\mapsto(?![a-zA-Z])\s*/$tr{startcode}:---$tr{gt}$tr{endcode}/g;
  s/ *\\geq?(?![a-zA-Z]) *([^ ])/ $tr{startcode}$tr{gt}=$tr{endcode} $1/g;
  s/ *\\leq?(?![a-zA-Z]) *([^ ])/ $tr{startcode}$tr{lt}=$tr{endcode} $1/g;
  s/ *\\gg?(?![a-zA-Z]) *([^ ])/ $tr{startcode}$tr{gt}$tr{gt}$tr{endcode} $1/g;
  s/ *\\ll?(?![a-zA-Z]) *([^ ])/ $tr{startcode}$tr{lt}$tr{ll}$tr{endcode} $1/g;

  s/\\(vers|PARIversion)(?![a-zA-Z])/$tr{startbold}$version$tr{endbold}/g;
  s/\\([QRCPFZN])(?![a-zA-Z])/$tr{startbi}$1$tr{endbi}$2/g;
  s/\\Bbb\b\s*(\w)/$tr{startbi}$1$tr{endbi}/g;

  s/\\([oc]br)/$tr{$1}/g;
  s/\\quo(?![a-zA-Z])/\"/g;
  s/(^|\s)\{(\w+)\}/$1$2/g;

  s/\\p(?![a-zA-Z])/$tr{startbold}p$tr{endbold}$1/g;
  s/^ *\\point\{([^\}]*)\}/\\item $1/g;
  s/\@\[dollar]\\bullet\@\[dollar]/\\item /g;
  s/\\bullet/\\item/g;
  s/^ *\\item/\@3$tr{startbold}*$tr{endbold}/g;
  s/\\item/$tr{startbold}*$tr{endbold}/g;
  s/^ *\\misctitle\{([^\}]*)\}/\@3$tr{startbold}$1.$tr{endbold}/g;
  s/\\subsubsec\{([^\}]*)\}/\@3$tr{startbold}$1.$tr{endbold}/g unless $to_pod;
  s/\\subsec\{([^\}]*)\}/\@3$tr{startbold}$1.$tr{endbold}/g unless $to_pod;
  s/\\\$/$tr{ldollar}/g;
  s/\\kbd\s*\{\s*</\\kbd{$tr{lt}/g if $to_pod;
  s/\\kbd\s*\{\s*>/\\kbd{$tr{gt}/g if $to_pod;
  s/\\kbd\s*\{((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/$tr{startcode}$1$tr{endcode}/g;

  s/\\key\{((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/$tr{startbold}$1$tr{endbold}/g unless $refcard;
  s/\\goth\{((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/$tr{startbg}$1$tr{endbg}/g;

  if ($refcard) {
    s/\\(?:key|li)\{((?:[^{}]+(?=[{}])|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\s*\{\}[ \t]*\n/\n\n=back\n\n$1\n\n=over\n\n/g;
    s/\\(?:key|li)\{((?:[^{}]+(?=[{}])|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\s*\{(([^{}]+(?=[{}])|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/\n=item $tr{startcode}$2$tr{endcode}\n\n$1\n/g;
  }

  s/\\(floor|ceil|round|binom)\{/$1\{/g;
  s/\\(var|emph)\{([^\}]*)\}/$tr{startit}$2$tr{endit}/g;
  s/\\fl(?![a-zA-Z])/$tr{startit}flag$tr{endit}/g;
  s/\\b\{([^}]*)\}/$tr{startcode}\\$1$tr{endcode}/g;
  s/\\kbdsidx/\\sidx/g;
  s/\\sidx\{[^\}]*\}//g unless $to_pod;
  s/\\[a-zA-Z]*idx\{([^\}]*)\}/$1/g unless $to_pod;
  s/\{\\text\{(st|nd|th)\}\}/\\text{$1}/g;
  s/\^\\text\{th\}/-th/g;
  s/1\^\\text\{st\}/1st/g;
  s/2\^\\text\{nd\}/2nd/g;
  s/\\text\{([a-zA-z0-9]*)\}/$1/g;
  s/\\(text|hbox|Big)//g;

  s/^([ \t]+)\{ *\\(it|sl|bf|tt)\b/S<$1>{\\$2/gm;
  s/\{ *\\(it|sl) *(([^{}]+(?=[{}])|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/$tr{startit}$2$tr{endit}/g;
  s/\{ *\\bf *(([^{}]+(?=[{}])|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/$tr{startbold}$1$tr{endbold}/g;
  s/\{ *\\tt *(([^{}]+(?=[{}])|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/$tr{startpodcode}$1$tr{endpodcode}/g;
  $seek=1 if (s/\\emph\{ */$tr{startit}/g);
  if ($seek) { $seek=0 if (s/\}/$tr{endit}/) }
  s/\\(backslash|bs)\{(\w)\}/\\$2/g;
  s/\\(backslash|bs)(?![a-zA-Z]) */\\/g;
  s/ *\\setminus */ \\ /g;

  s/\@com(.*)$/$tr{startcode}$1$tr{endcode}/g;

  # Last resort:
  s/\\kbd\s*\{(.*?)\}/$tr{startcode}$1$tr{endcode}/g;
  s/^([ \t]{3,})\Q$tr{startcode}\E(.*)\Q$tr{endcode}\E/$1$2/gmo if $to_pod;
  # Last resort:
  s/^([ \t]{3,})\Q$tr{startcode}\E(.*?)\Q$tr{endcode}\E/$1$2/gmso if $to_pod;
  # Remove leading spaces unless have embedded wrapped code:
  s/^[ \t]+//gm if $to_pod and /^\S/ and not /^[ \t]*\n[ \t]/m;
  s/\{ *\}//g;			# empty args

  s{\Q$tr{startcode}\E((ftp|http)://.*?)\Q$tr{endcode}\E}{$tr{startlink}$1$tr{endlink}}go if $to_pod;
  $_;
}

sub presubst {
  chomp;
  if ($in_prog && /\@eprog *(\\noindent)? */)
  {
    my ($eprog) = $1? '@3': '@2';
    $in_prog = 0;
    $_ = $eprog . &code_subst($`) . $tr{endcode};
    push(@text, $_);
    $_ = &basic_subst($');
  }
  elsif ($in_prog || s/\\bprog(tabs.*)?//g)
  {
    $in_prog++;  # = 1 on the \bprog line
                 # code should start on the next line
    $_ = &code_subst($_);
    s/^/\@1$tr{startcode}/ if ($in_prog == 2);
    s/^/\@0/ if ($in_prog > 2);
  }
  else { $_ = &basic_subst($_); }
  if (/^ *$/)
  {
    push(@text,"\n");
  }
  else
  {
    for (split(/\n/, $_)) { push(@text, $_); }
  }
}

sub code_subst {
  my $in = shift;
  $in =~ s/\@dots\b/.../g;
  if ($in =~ /\@com(.*)/)
  {
    my ($c) = &basic_subst($1);
    if (!$to_pod) { $c = $tr{endcode} . $c . $tr{startcode}; }
    $in = $` . $c . &code_subst($');
  }
  if ($in =~ /\@Ccom(.*)\*\//)
  {
    my ($c) = &basic_subst($1);
    if (!$to_pod) { $c = $tr{endcode} . $c . $tr{startcode}; }
    $in = $` .$c . "*/" . &code_subst($');
  }
  $in;
}

sub wrap_code {
  my $in = shift;
  $in =~ s/^[ \t]+$//mg;
  $in = &code_subst($in);
  $in =~ s/^(.)/  $1/mg;
  $in =~ s/\s*\Z//;
#  $in =~ s/\\kbd\{((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/$1/g if $to_pod;
  $in =~ s/\$([^\$\n]*)\$/$1/g if $to_pod;
  "\n\n$in\n\n";
}

sub indexify {
  my $in = shift;
  $in =~ s/(^|and\s+)(\w+)(\$?\()/$1\\idx{$2}$3/g;
  $in =~ s/^(\\b\{\w+\})(?!\S)/\\idx{$1}/g;
  $in;
}

sub for_index {
  my $in = shift;
  1 while $in =~ s/\Q$tr{startcode}\E(.*?)\Q$tr{endcode}\E/$1/go;
  $in;
}

sub strip_trail { my $in = shift; $in =~ s/\s+\Z//; $in }

# This subroutine works in paragraph mode
sub TeXprint_topod {
  s/\A\s+//;
  s/^\\def\\.*\{\n.*\n\}//gm;
  s/\\def\\.*//g;		# Repeated in basic_subst, as the next one
  s/(\{[\w\s]+)\{\}([\s\w]+\})/$1$2/g;	# {rnf{}llgram}

  s/\\vbox\s*\{\s*\\bprog/\\bprog/g;
  s/([\\\@])eprog\s*\}/$1eprog/g;

  #  \n is below to prevent splitting on ' '
  #  We also remove ':'
  s/\\sectype\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/\\subsec{Type \\typ{$1} (${2}s)}\n\\sidx{$2}/g;
  s/\\sectypeindex\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/\\subsec{Type \\typ{$1} (${2}s)}\n\\sidx{$3}/g;
  s/\\sectypes\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\{\s*((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/\\subsec{Type \\typ{$1} and \\typ{$1} (${3}s)}\n\\sidx{$3}/g;

  # Try to guard \label/\sidx (removing possible '.')
#  This somehow breaks index...
#  s/(\\(?:section|subsec(?:ref|idx|op)?(unix)?)\s*{(?:(?:[^{}]+(?=[{}])|{[^{}]+})+)})\.?\s*\\(label|sidx)/$1\n\\$2/;
  s/(\\(?:section|subsec(?:ref|idx|op)?)\s*\{(?:(?:[^{}]+(?=[{}])|{[^{}]+})+)\})\.?\s*\\(label|sidx)/$1\n\\$2/;

  # last if /\\subsec[\\{}ref]*[\\\${]$help[}\\\$]/o;
  s/\\chapter\s*\{((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\s*/\n\n$tr{podleader}head1 NAME\n\nlibPARI - $1\n\n/;
  s/\\appendix\s*\{((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\s*/\n\n$tr{podleader}head1 NAME\n\nAppendix - $1\n\n/;
  s/\\section\s*\{((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}\s*/"\n\n$tr{podleader}head1 " . indexify($1) . "\n\n"/e;

  # Try to delimit by :
  s/\\subsec(?:ref)?(?:unix)?\s*\{(([^{}]+(?=[{}])|{[^{}]+})+)\}([^\n]*):[\n ]/"\n\n$tr{podleader}head2 " . indexify("$1$3") . "\n\n"/e;
  s/\\subsubsec(?:ref)?(?:unix)?\s*\{(([^{}]+(?=[{}])|{[^{}]+})+)\}([^:]*):\s*/"\n\n$tr{podleader}head3 " . indexify("$1$3") . "\n\n"/e;
  s/\\subsubsec\s*{(([^{}]+(?=[{}])|{[^{}]+})+)}(.*)$/"\n\n$tr{podleader}head3 " . indexify("$1") . "$3\n\n"/me;
  s/\\subseckbd\s*{(([^{}]+(?=[{}])|{[^{}]+})+)}([^:]*):\s*/"\n\n$tr{podleader}head2 " . indexify("$1$3") . "\n\n"/e;
  # Try to delimit by ' '
  s/\\subsec(?:ref)?(?:unix)?\s*\{(([^{}]+(?=[{}])|{[^{}]+})+)\}(\S*)\s+/"\n\n$tr{podleader}head2 " . indexify("$1$3") . "\n\n"/e;
  s/\\subsec(?:title)?(?:unix)?\s*\{(([^{}]+(?=[{}])|{[^{}]*})+)\}:?\s*/"\n\n$tr{podleader}head2 " . indexify("$1") . "\n\n"/e;

  # This is to skip preface in refcard:
  /\Q$tr{podleader}\Ehead1|\\title(?![a-zA-Z])\s*\{/o and $seen_start = 1
    or $seen_start or return;	# Skip now!

  s/\\title\s*\{([^{}\s]*)(\s+([^{}]*))?\}(\s*\\centerline\s*\{([^{}]*)\})?\s*/$tr{podleader}head1 NAME\n\n$1 - $3.  $5\n\n/ and $seen_title++
    unless $seen_title;
  s/\\title\s*\{([^{}\s]*)(\s+([^{}]*))?\}(\s*\\centerline\s*\{([^{}]*)\})?\s*/\n\n/;
  s/\\parskip.*/\n/g;		# Up to end of the line
  #s/([A-Z])\</$1 < /g;		# Disambiguate with POD...

  # Duplicate removal of settabs, since they may contain \hskip
  s/\\settabs.*//;
  s/^[ \t]*\\hskip\s*\w+/$tr{nbrk}/g;
  s/[ \t]*\\hskip\s*\w+/\n$tr{nbrk}/g;
  1 while s/ \\
	     ( (small|big)skip | newcolumn | noindent
	     | (short)?copyrightnotice | hfill | break | par
	     | leavevmode | strut | endgroup | bye
             )
	     (?![a-zA-Z])[ \t]*(\n\s*)
	     /\n\n/gx;

  s/'(\W)'/{\\tt '$1'}/g;
  s/(\\\w+)(\\hbox)/$1 $2/g;
  s/\\hbox\s*\{(?:\\it\b\s*)?((?:\\[\{\}]|[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})*)\}/$1/g;

  # substitute non-verbatim code
  $acc = '';
  pos = 0;
  while ( s/\A(.*?)\\bprog//s ) {
    $acc .= basic_subst(strip_trail($1));
    $_ .= <DOC> until /(\\|@)eprog\b/ or eof(DOC);
    $acc .= wrap_code($1) if s/\A(?:tabs[^\n]*)?(?![a-zA-Z])[ \t]*\n?(.*?)(\\|@)eprog\s*//s;
  }
  $_ = $acc . basic_subst($_);

#  s/\\kbd\{/\{\\tt /g;		# startcode
#  s/\\typ\{/\{\\tt t_/g;	# startcode

  s/\$\s*(\@\[startbi\][A-Z]\@\[endbi\])\s*\$/$1/g;
#  s/\\p(\b|(?=[\d_]))/B<p>/g;
  #s/\$\\bf\b\s*([^\$]+)\$/C<B<$1>>/g;

  @lines = split /^$/m, $_;
  for (@lines) {
    s/>/\@[gt]/g unless /^\n*[ \t]/;
    s/</\@[lt]/g unless /^\n*[ \t]/;
  }
  $_ = join '', @lines;

  s/\$\$(.*?)\$\$\s*/\n\nS<  >$tr{startcode}$1$tr{endcode}\n\n/gs;
  s/\$([^\$]+)\$/$tr{startcode}$1$tr{endcode}/g;

  s/\\s(?:ref|idx)\{\s*([^{}]*)\}/"X<" . for_index($1) . ">"/ge; #
  s/\\(?:ref|idx)\{\s*([^{}]*)\}/"X<" . for_index($1) . ">$1"/ge;

# Conflict between different versions of PARI and refcard:
# s/\\(?:key|li)\s*\{(.*)\}\s*\{(.+)\}[ \t]*\n/\n\n=item C<$2>\n\n$1\n\n/msg;
# s/\\(?:key|li)\s*\{(.*)\}\s*\{\}[ \t]*\n/\n\n=back\n\n$1\n\n=over\n\n/mgs;
# s/\\(key|var)(?![a-zA-Z])\s*\{(\w+)\}/C<$2>/mg;
  s/\\var\s*\{X<(\w+)>(\w+)\}/X<$1>$tr{startcode}$2$tr{endcode}/mg;
  s/\\var\s*\{f\{\}lag\}/$tr{startcode}flag$tr{endcode}/mg;

  s/\\metax(?![a-zA-Z])\s*\{(.*)\}\s*\{\s*(\w+)(?=C\<)(.*)\}[ \t]*\n/\n\n=item C<L<$2>$3>\n\n$1\n\n/mg;
  s/\\metax(?![a-zA-Z])\s*\{(.*)\}\s*\{(.*)\}[ \t]*\n/\n\n=item C<$2>\n\n$1\n\n/mg;
  s/C\<\{\}=/C\<=/g;
  s/\\fl(?![a-zA-Z])/I<flag>/g;
  s/\\file(?![a-zA-Z])/F<file>/g;
  s/\\(unix|emacs)\b\s*(\{?)(\s*\\(no)?indent)?\s*/X<\U$1>$2/g;
  s/\A\\label\s*\{([\w:.-]*)\}([ \t]*\n\s*(?=[^\s=]))?/X<Label $1>/g;
  s/\\label\s*\{([\w:.-]*)\}/X<Label $1>/g;
  s/\\secref\s*\{([\w:.-]*)\}/L<Label $1>/g;
  s/\\begin(double)?indentedkeys\s*/\n\n=over\n\n/g;
  s/\\end(double)?indentedkeys\s*/\n\n=back\n\n/g;
  # begin/end group appear in very special context only
  s/\\begingroup\W.*//s;		# Eat to the end
  s/\n{3,}/\n\n/g;
  s/\\subsec\{((?:[^{}]|\{[^{}]*\})+)\}\s*/\n\n=back\n\nB<$1>\n\n=over\n\n/g; # In refcard
  # for refcard:
  s/{\\rm(?![a-zA-Z])\s*([^{}]*)}/$1/g;
  s/\\Z<>/\\/g;			# Optimize for readability

  # Now replace the POD stuff
  # Start with cosmetic stuff:
  $in_code = 0;
  s/(\@\[((start)|end)code\])/ ($3 ? $in_code++ : --$in_code) ? "" : $1 /ge;

  if ($dumb_pod) {
    my @stack;
    s /(\@\[((start)|end)(\w+)\])/
      if ($3) {			# Start
	push @stack, $4;
	(@stack > 1 ? "\@[end$stack[-2]]" : '') . $1
      } else {			# end
	pop @stack;
	$1 . (@stack ? "\@[start$stack[-1]]" : '')
      }
      /ge
  }
  1 while s/\@\[start(\w+)\](\s*)\@\[end\1\]/$2/g;

  s/\@\[(\w+)\]/\@!$pr{$1}/g;
  s/(\\\w+)\@!(\w)/$1 $2/g;
  s/\@!//g;
  s/\\([\{\}])/$1/g;

  # Normalize the spacing
  s/\n{3,}/\n\n/;
  s/\A([ \t]*\n)+//;
  # Single label is not healthy...
  print "\n" if $last_glued and /\A=/; # POD markup needs a new paragraph
  $last_glued = s/((\A|\n\n)(X<[^<>]+>)+)[ \t]*\n\n/$1\n/;

  print;
}

sub color {
  my($a);
  $_ = $_[0];
  if (/[^0-9]/ || $_ < 0 || $_ > 17)
    { print "bad color in gphelp: $_\n"; return ""; }
  if ($_ < 8) { $a = $_ + 30; } else { $a = $_ + 82; }
  return "\e[0;${a}m";
}

sub TeXprint {
  local($_) = $_[0];
  s/\@\[obr\]/{/g;
  s/\@\[cbr\]/}/g;
  if ($utf8)
  {
    s/\@\[ouml\]/Ã¶/g;
    s/\@\[uuml\]/Ã¼/g;
    s/\@\[aacute\]/Ã¡/g;
    s/\@\[agrave\]/Ã /g;
    s/\@\[eacute\]/Ã©/g;
    s/\@\[pm\]/Â±/g;
  }
  else
  {
    s/\@\[ouml\]/"o/g;
    s/\@\[uuml\]/"u/g;
    s/\@\[aacute\]/'a/g;
    s/\@\[agrave\]/`a/g;
    s/\@\[eacute\]/'e/g;
    s/\@\[pm\]/+\/-/g;
  }
  s/\@\[label\]//g;
  s/\@\[ldollar\]/\$/g;
  s/\@\[end(bold|code|bcode|ref|bi|bc|bg|it)\]/$ch/g;
  s/\@\[start(bold|code|bcode|ref|bi|bc|bg)\]/$cb/g;
  s/\@\[startit\]/$cu/g;
  s/\@\[(dollar|empty|endl?word|endpodcode|startl?word|startpodcode)\]//g;
  s/\@\[lt\]/</g;
  s/\@\[gt\]/>/g;
  s/\\([\{\}])/$1/g;
  s/\@\[nbrk\]/ /g; print "$_\n";
}

sub to_pod {
  $to_pod = $ARGV[1];
  inittr();
  $parifile = $to_pod;
  %compress = ('.gz', 'gzip -cd',
	       '.z', 'gzip -cd',
	       '.Z', 'zcat',
	      );
  foreach $suffix (keys %compress) {
    ($patt = $suffix) =~ s/(\W)/\\$1/;
    if ($to_pod =~ /$patt$/) { $pipe = $compress{$suffix}; last; }
  }
  if ($pipe) {
    open(DOC,"$pipe $parifile |") ||
      die "Cannot open pipe $pipe from $parifile: $!, stopped";
  } else {
    open(DOC,$parifile) || die "Cannot find file $parifile: $!, stopped";
  }
  $/='';			# Paragraph mode
  while (<DOC>) {
    &TeXprint_topod();
  }
  if ($pipe) {
    close(DOC) || die "Cannot close pipe `$pipe $parifile': $!, stopped";
  } else {
    close(DOC) || die "Cannot close file $parifile: $!, stopped";
  }
  cleanexit();
}

#handle_x12
#!/usr/bin/perl

# handle_837: manage reciept of daily 837 files
#
# Performs the following actions on received 837 files:
#
# 1) verifies integrity of file via zip test
# 2) compresses and encrypts file via gzip and ds_encrypt processes
# 3) renames converted file to appropriate name (e.g. adds ".gz.pgp" extention)
# 4) sets file access and modification times to match that of original incoming file
# 5) removes original incoming file after successful conversion
#
# Notes:
# - This program uses its own file lock mechanism that is designed to work
# across multiple servers in a clustered environment with a shared file system.
# It can be safely executed in parallel on a single and/or multiple servers.
#
# - Temporary files are created while processing files, but care has been taken
# to cleanup these temp files under both normal and abnormal termination conditions.
#
# - The program is designed for maximum reliability, not high performance (hence
#	temp files instead of pipe streams).
#
# Version history:
# 7/27/2006	Initial release
#

use File::Copy;
use File::Spec;
use File::stat;
use Sys::Hostname;
use String::CRC32;
use Cwd;
use Getopt::Long;

use Data::Dumper;
use strict;
use warnings;

use constant LOCKFILE_EXPIRY_SECONDS  => 60 * 60 * 1;	# lock file is stale after 1 hour

use constant FILES_OK                 => 0;
use constant FILES_UNPROCESSED        => 1;
use constant FILES_EXTRANEOUS         => 3;
use constant HAVE_ALL_COMPLETED_FILES => 1;
use constant MISSING_COMPLETED_FILES  => 0;

our $DESTINATION_AUDITLOG_TOP_DIR = '/ds/data_sources/incoming';
our $DESTINATION_TOP_DIR          = '/ds/data_sources/';

our $PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s|.*/||g;

our $FILES_TO_CLEANUP;	# temp files to remove in signal handler
our $FILES_TO_UNEXTRACT;  # files in zip to extract
sub usage() {
	print "Usage: $PGM [-success-exit #] [-dest-dir-top path] 837_filename [...]\n";
}


sub get_filelock($) {
	# get a cluster-friendly exclusive file lock	{no, flock() will not work across servers}

  my $lockfile_name = shift;
  my ($read_hostname, $read_pid);

	return undef if (! defined($lockfile_name));

	if (-f $lockfile_name) {
		my $stat = stat($lockfile_name);

		# check to see if existing lockfile is stale

		if ((time - $stat->mtime) > LOCKFILE_EXPIRY_SECONDS) {
			print STDERR "Warning: recreating stale lock file $lockfile_name : was more than " . LOCKFILE_EXPIRY_SECONDS . " seconds old\n";
		} else {
			return 0;	# fresh lock file already exists
		}
	}

	if (! open(LOCK, "> $lockfile_name")) {
		print STDERR "Warning: unable to create lock file $lockfile_name : $!\n";
		return undef;
	}

  my $hostname = hostname;

	if (! print LOCK "$hostname,$$\n") {
		close(LOCK);
		unlink($lockfile_name);
		print STDERR "Warning: unable to write identifying info to lock file $lockfile_name : $!\n";
		return undef;
	}

	if (! close(LOCK)) {
		unlink($lockfile_name);
		print STDERR "Warning: unable to close lock file created $lockfile_name : $!\n";
		return undef;
	}

	if (! open(LOCK, $lockfile_name)) {
		print STDERR "Warning: unable to open lock file $lockfile_name for reading : $!\n";
		return undef;
	}

	$_ = <LOCK>;
	chomp($_);

	($read_hostname, $read_pid) = split(',', $_);

	if (! close(LOCK)) {
		print STDERR "Warning: unable to close lock file $lockfile_name after reading : $!\n";
		return undef;
	}

	if (($read_pid != $$) || ($read_hostname ne $hostname)) {
		print STDERR "Warning: lock file $lockfile_name was overwritten by another process ($read_pid on $read_hostname). Current pid = $$, hostname = $hostname). Yielding to other process...\n";
		return undef;
	}


	return 1;	# all of that work just to guarantee that we got a cluster-aware exclusive lock created!
}


sub sig_handler() {
  my $signal = shift;

	print STDERR "$PGM: Received signal $signal ... cleaning up\n";

	print "Simulating removal of files: " . join("\n", keys %{$FILES_TO_CLEANUP}) . "\n";
	# unlink(keys %{$FILES_TO_CLEANUP});

	exit(1);
}

sub gzuncompress($$) {
  my ($compressed_file, $uncompressed_file) = (shift, shift);

	return undef if ((! defined($compressed_file)) || (! defined($uncompressed_file)));

	if ($compressed_file eq $uncompressed_file) {
		print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: compressed file name $compressed_file and desired uncompressed file name $uncompressed_file are the same!\n";
		return undef;
	}

	my $ret = system("gunzip -c $compressed_file > $uncompressed_file");
	$ret = $ret >> 8;

	if ($ret != 0) {
		return 0;
	} else {
		return 1;
	}
}

sub test_integrity($) {
  my $compressed_collection = shift;
  my $files_to_extract;  

  return undef if (! defined($compressed_collection) );
  my $list = `unzip -t $compressed_collection`;
  my $line = "";
  my $old_line = "";
  foreach $line (split /\n/, $list) {
    chomp $line;
    $old_line = $line;
    if ($line =~ m/^\s*testing:\s*(\S*)\s*(.*)$/) {
      my ($file, $result) = ($1, $2);
      if ($result ne "OK") {
        print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: file $file, compressed in $compressed_collection, failed integrity check.  From unzip: $line\n";
        return undef;
      }
      $file =~ m/^([^;]*);?(.*)$/;
      my ($file_base, $file_version) = ($1, $2);
      if (0 == length($file_version) ) {
        $file_version = "1";
      }
      $files_to_extract->{$file_base}->{$file_version} = $file;
    }
  }
  if ($old_line !~ m/^\s*No errors detected/) {
    print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: compressed file name $compressed_collection failed integrity check.  From unzip: $old_line\n";
    return undef;
  }
  return $files_to_extract;
}

sub uncompress($$$) {
  my ($compressed_collection, $compressed_file, $uncompressed_file) = (shift, shift, shift);
  return undef if ((! defined($compressed_collection)) || (! defined($compressed_file)) || (! defined($uncompressed_file)));

  #print "unzip -c $compressed_collection '$compressed_file' > '$uncompressed_file'\n";
  #return 1;
  my $ret = system("unzip -p $compressed_collection '$compressed_file' > '$uncompressed_file'");

  if ($ret != 0) {
    return 0;
  }
  else {
    return 1;
  }
}

sub gzcompress($$) {
  my ($uncompressed_file, $compressed_file) = (shift, shift);

	return undef if ((! defined($uncompressed_file)) || (! defined($compressed_file)));

	if ($uncompressed_file eq $compressed_file) {
		print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: uncompressed file name $uncompressed_file and desired compressed file name $compressed_file are the same!\n";
		return undef;
	}

	my $ret = system("gzip -c $uncompressed_file > $compressed_file");
	$ret = $ret >> 8;

	if ($ret != 0) {
		return 0;
	} else {
		return 1;
	}
}


sub ds_encrypt($$) {
  my ($unencrypted_file, $encrypted_file) = (shift, shift);

	return undef if ((! defined($unencrypted_file)) || (! defined($encrypted_file)));

	if ($unencrypted_file eq $encrypted_file) {
		print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: unencrypted file name $unencrypted_file and desired encrypted file name $encrypted_file are the same!\n";
		return undef;
	}

	my $ret = system("ds_encrypt $unencrypted_file");
	$ret = $ret >> 8;

	if ($ret != 0) {
		return 0;
	} else {

		if (-f $encrypted_file) {
			return 1;
		} else {
			print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: encrypted file $encrypted_file does not exist after encryption process!\n";
			return 0;
		}
	}
}


sub cleanup_files() {

  my $unlinkables = 0;

	foreach my $fname (keys %{$FILES_TO_CLEANUP}) {

		if (unlink($fname) != 1) {
			print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Could not remove file $fname : $!\n";
			$unlinkables++;
		}

		delete $FILES_TO_CLEANUP->{$fname};
	}

	foreach my $fname (keys %{$FILES_TO_UNEXTRACT}) {

		if (unlink($fname) != 1) {
			print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Could not remove file $fname : $!\n";
			$unlinkables++;
		}

		delete $FILES_TO_UNEXTRACT->{$fname};
	}

	if ($unlinkables) {
		return 0;
	} else {
		return 1;
	}
}

# Set modification and access times of files (@touch_files) to match that of reference file

sub ref_touch($@) {
  my ($ref_file) = shift;
  my @touch_files = @_;

  return undef if (! defined($ref_file));

  my $stat = stat($ref_file);
  my ($atime, $mtime) = ($stat->atime, $stat->mtime);

  return utime $atime, $mtime, @touch_files;
}

sub identify_data_source($) {
  my ($fname) = shift;

  return undef if (! defined($fname));

  my $ret = system("identify_data_source $fname");

	if ($ret != 0) {
		return 0;
	} else {
		return 1;
	}
}

# gather list of all processed (compressed/encrypted) 837 files 
# for specified day and determine whether any are missing
# are extraneous.

sub get_destination_dir($$) {
  my ($dest_top_dir, $date) = (shift, shift);
  my $yyyymm = substr($date, 0, 6);
	my $destination_dir = File::Spec->catdir($dest_top_dir, $yyyymm);

	if (! ((-d $destination_dir) || (-l $destination_dir))) {
		print STDERR "$PGM: Warning: destination directory $destination_dir does not exist!\n";
		return undef;
	}

	return $destination_dir;
}


sub move_all($$$@) {
  my ($source_dir, $destination_dir, $date) = (shift, shift, shift);
  my (@moved_files, $source_file);

	foreach my $fname (@_) {

		$source_file = File::Spec->catfile($source_dir, $fname);

		if (! move($source_file, $destination_dir)) {
			print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Unable to move file $source_file to $destination_dir : $!\n";
			print STDERR "$PGM: relocating $date files from $destination_dir back to $source_dir\n";

			foreach my $moved_fname (@moved_files) {

				if (! move($moved_fname, $source_dir)) {
					print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Cannot move file $moved_fname from $destination_dir back to $source_dir : $!\n";

					if (-f $moved_fname) {
						print STDERR "$PGM: Warning: (possibly partial) file $moved_fname may exist on both $source_dir and $destination_dir\n";
					}
				}

			}

			return 0;
		} else {
			push(@moved_files, $source_file);
		}
	}

	return $#moved_files + 1;
}



########################################################################################
# main
########################################################################################



if (! ($#ARGV >= 0)) {
	usage();
	exit(0);
}

my $exit_success = 0;

GetOptions(
            "success-exit=s" => \$exit_success,
            "dest-dir-top=s" => \$DESTINATION_TOP_DIR
) || exit(1);

# setup signal handler so we can cleanup before getting interrupted

foreach my $sig ('INT', 'QUIT', 'HUP', 'INT', 'TERM', 'ABRT', 'BUS', 'FPE', 'ILL', 'QUIT', 'SEGV', 'SYS', 'TRAP') {

  if ((! defined($SIG{$sig})) || ($SIG{$sig} ne 'IGNORE')) {
    $SIG{$sig} = \&sig_handler;
  }
}

#### Put file arguments into hash w/useful attributes about each file

my $curr_dir = getcwd;
my $exit_status = 0;
my @unsupported_files;
my $file_info;

foreach my $fname (@ARGV) {
	my ($volume, $dir, $file) = File::Spec->splitpath($fname);
	if ($dir eq '') {
		$dir = $curr_dir;
	}

	if ($file =~ /^(tulsa|indy|Cleveland)_?(835|ub|hcfa|hp|ph|Remits)?_?(\d\d\d\d)(\d\d)(\d\d)(\d\d)?(\d\d)?(\d\d)?([.][A-Za-z]+)?$/) {
		my ($sender, $format, $yyyy, $mm, $dd, $hour, $minute, $second, $suffix) = ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, $8, $9);
    my $yyyymmdd = "${yyyy}${mm}${dd}";
    my $yyyymm = "${yyyy}${mm}";
    if (!defined($format)) {
      $format = "837";
    }
		my $file_id = "${sender}${format}${yyyy}${mm}${dd}";
		my $lock_file = File::Spec->catfile($dir, "lock.$file_id");

		$file_info->{$yyyymmdd}->{$fname} = {
			source_dir => $dir,
			base_fname => $file,
      format     => $format,
      yyyy       => $yyyy,
      mm         => $mm,
      dd         => $dd,
      hour       => $hour,
      minute     => $minute,
      second     => $second,
      sender     => $sender,
			file_id    => $file_id,
			lock_file  => $lock_file,
			suffix     => $suffix,
      fname      => $fname,
		};

	} else {
		push(@unsupported_files, $fname);
	}

}

## report status info

if ($#unsupported_files >= 0) {
	print STDERR "The following files are not supported:\n";

	foreach my $unsup_fname (@unsupported_files) {
		print STDERR "UNSUPPORTED_FILE,$unsup_fname\n";
	}

	$exit_status += 2;
}

my $hostname = hostname;
my $pid = $$;
my $errors = 0;
my $files_extracted = 0;
my $files_converted = 0;

# handle any 837 files

foreach my $yyyymmdd (sort keys %{$file_info}) {
	foreach my $fname (keys %{$file_info->{$yyyymmdd}}) {

		my $info = $file_info->{$yyyymmdd}->{$fname};	# create convenient hash ref for this file

		if (! -f $fname) {
			print STDERR "$PGM: Warning: the following file does not exist: $fname . This will NOT be treated as an error condition\n";
			next;
		}

		next if (! get_filelock($info->{lock_file}));	# quietly skip if cannot obtain lock

		$FILES_TO_CLEANUP->{$info->{lock_file}} = 1;
    
    my $destination_dir = File::Spec->catfile($DESTINATION_TOP_DIR, lc($info->{sender}), $info->{yyyy}.$info->{mm});
    if (! -d $destination_dir) {
      if (! mkdir $destination_dir) {
        cleanup_files();

        print STDERR "$PGM: Error: Could not create directory $destination_dir: $!\n";
        $errors++;
        next;
      }
    }
    $destination_dir = File::Spec->catfile($destination_dir, $yyyymmdd);
    if (! -d $destination_dir) {
      if (! mkdir $destination_dir) {
        cleanup_files();

        print STDERR "$PGM: Error: Could not create directory $destination_dir: $!\n";
        $errors++;
        next;
      }
    }
    if ( defined($info->{suffix}) && (lc($info->{suffix}) eq '.zip') ) {
      #test integrity & get file list
      my $file_list = undef;
      $file_list = test_integrity($fname);
      if (! defined($file_list)) {
        cleanup_files();

        print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: at least one file failed integrity test $fname\n";
        $errors++;
        next;
      }
      #uncompress
      foreach my $key (keys %{$file_list}) {
        my @versions = keys %{$file_list->{$key}};
        foreach my $version (@versions) {
          my $uncompressed_fname = (File::Spec->splitpath($key))[2];
          $uncompressed_fname = File::Spec->catfile($destination_dir, $uncompressed_fname);
          $uncompressed_fname = $uncompressed_fname . '.' . $version;
          my $compressed_fname = $file_list->{$key}->{$version};
          if (-e $uncompressed_fname) {
            cleanup_files();
        
            print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: file $uncompressed_fname already exists!  Will NOT overwrite.\n";
            $errors++;
            next;
          }
          if (! uncompress($fname, $compressed_fname, $uncompressed_fname)) {
            cleanup_files();

    				print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Could not uncompress compressed file $compressed_fname in $fname to $uncompressed_fname\n";
		    		$errors++;
				    next;
          }
          $FILES_TO_CLEANUP->{$uncompressed_fname} = 1;        
          
          #compress file
          my $gzipped_fname = $uncompressed_fname . ".gz";
          if (-e $gzipped_fname) {
            cleanup_files();
        
            print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: file $gzipped_fname already exists!  Will NOT overwrite.\n";
            $errors++;
            next;
          }
          if (! gzcompress($uncompressed_fname, $gzipped_fname)) {
            cleanup_files();
        
            print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Could not gzip file $uncompressed_fname to $gzipped_fname\n";
            $errors++;
            next;
          }
          $FILES_TO_CLEANUP->{$gzipped_fname} = 1;
          
          #encrypt file
          my $encrypted_fname = $gzipped_fname . ".pgp";
          if (-e $encrypted_fname) {
            cleanup_files();

            print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: file $encrypted_fname already exists!  Will NOT overwrite.\n";
            $errors++;
            next;
          }
          if (! ds_encrypt($gzipped_fname, $encrypted_fname)) {
            cleanup_files();

            print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Could not encrypt file $gzipped_fname to $encrypted_fname\n";
            $errors++;
            next;
          }
          delete $FILES_TO_CLEANUP->{$gzipped_fname};
          $FILES_TO_UNEXTRACT->{$encrypted_fname} = 1;

      		ref_touch($fname, $encrypted_fname);	# make access/mod times of final file match that of original file
					$files_extracted++;

          identify_data_source($encrypted_fname); #Register file
        }
      }
      #All files extracted successfully.  Don't unextract.
      if (0 == $errors) {
        $FILES_TO_UNEXTRACT = undef;
      }
    }

		if (! cleanup_files()) {
			print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Could not remove some temp files for 837 file $fname . Keeping original file.\n";
			$errors++;
			next;
		}

		print "CONVERTED," . $info->{base_fname} . " to $destination_dir\n";
		$files_converted++;
	}
}

## report status info

if ($files_converted) {
	print "NUM_CONVERTED,$files_converted\n";
}

if ($files_extracted) {
	print "NUM_EXTRACTED,$files_extracted\n";
}

if ($errors) {
	print STDERR "ERRORS,$errors\n";
	$exit_status += 4;
}

## exit with proper exit code

if ($exit_status == 0) {
	exit($exit_success);
} else {
	exit($exit_status);
}


END {
	cleanup_files();
}


#index_report
#!/usr/bin/perl
use BLUELITE::Database;
use Data::Dumper;
use strict;
use Date::Calc qw(Delta_Days);
use Getopt::Long;

my $add_create;
my $add_failed;

GetOptions(  "add_create" => \$add_create,
             "add_failed" => \$add_failed
 );

my $detail_report_header;
my $enabled_indexes;
my $creating_indexes;
my $failed_indexes;
my $all_indexes;

my $temp_row;
my $key;

my $dbh = Get_Connection( env => 'ALPI_LOGIN');

my $sql_main = qq{ SELECT INDEX_ID, DESCRIPTION, PROCESS_DATE_BEGIN, to_char(sysdate - 1, 'yyyymmdd') PROCESS_DATE_END FROM ALPI_INDEX ORDER BY DESCRIPTION};
my $sth_main =  $dbh->prepare( $sql_main );
$sth_main->execute();

while ( $temp_row = $sth_main->fetchrow_hashref() )
{
   $all_indexes->{$temp_row->{'INDEX_ID'}}{'PROCESS_DATE_BEGIN'} = $temp_row->{'PROCESS_DATE_BEGIN'};
   $all_indexes->{$temp_row->{'INDEX_ID'}}{'PROCESS_DATE_END'} = $temp_row->{'PROCESS_DATE_END'};
   $all_indexes->{$temp_row->{'INDEX_ID'}}{'DESCRIPTION'} = $temp_row->{'DESCRIPTION'};
}

my $sql_dtl = qq{ SELECT INDEX_ID, PROCESS_DATE, STATUS FROM ALPI_INDEX_PROCESS_DATE };

my $sth_dtl = $dbh->prepare( $sql_dtl );
$sth_dtl->execute();

while ( $temp_row = $sth_dtl->fetchrow_hashref() )
{

     if ( $temp_row->{'STATUS'} eq 'ENABLED' ) {
    			push(@{$enabled_indexes->{$temp_row->{'INDEX_ID'}}}, $temp_row->{'PROCESS_DATE'});
     }
     elsif ( $temp_row->{'STATUS'} eq 'CREATING' ) {
    			push(@{$creating_indexes->{$temp_row->{'INDEX_ID'}}}, $temp_row->{'PROCESS_DATE'});
     }
     else {
    			push(@{$failed_indexes->{$temp_row->{'INDEX_ID'}}}, $temp_row->{'PROCESS_DATE'});
     }
}


foreach $key (keys %{$enabled_indexes}) {
   @{$enabled_indexes->{$key}} = sort @{$enabled_indexes->{$key}};
}

foreach $key (keys %{$creating_indexes}) {
   @{$creating_indexes->{$key}} = sort @{$creating_indexes->{$key}};
}

foreach $key (keys %{$failed_indexes}) {
   @{$failed_indexes->{$key}} = sort @{$failed_indexes->{$key}};
}


my $index_id;
my $index_desc;

write_enable_summary();
write_detail();

sub write_enable_summary {

    my $start_date;
    my $end_date;
    my $enable_start_date;
    my $enable_end_date;
    my $last_element;
    my $days_found;
    my $days_missing;
    my $days_between;
    my $date_range;
    
    my $start_date_year;
    my $start_date_month;
    my $start_date_day;
    
    my $end_date_year;
    my $end_date_month;
    my $end_date_day;
    
    my $enable_report_header = 'ENABLED INDEX SUMMARY';
    
    format INDEX_TOP =
    
    @|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||
    $enable_report_header
    
    ==============================================================================================================================
    @<<<<<<<  @<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<  @|||||||||||||||||   @<<<<<<<<<<<  @<<<<<<<<<<  @<<<<<<<<<<  @<<<<<<<<<<<  @<<<<<<<<<<<
    'INDEX ID', 'INDEX NAME','DATE RANGE','DAYS BETWEEN','START DATE','END DATE','DAYS ENABLED','DAYS MISSING'
    ==============================================================================================================================
.
    
    format INDEX =
    @<<<<<<<  @<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<  @<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<   @|||||||||||  @<<<<<<<<<<  @<<<<<<<<<<  @|||||||||||  @|||||||||||
    $index_id, $index_desc, $date_range, $days_between, $enable_start_date, $enable_end_date, $days_found, $days_missing
.
    
    $~ ='INDEX_TOP';
    write;
    
    $~ ='INDEX';
    foreach $key (sort keys %{$all_indexes}){
    
       $index_id = $key;
    
       $index_desc =  $all_indexes->{$key}{'DESCRIPTION'};
    
       $start_date = $all_indexes->{$key}{'PROCESS_DATE_BEGIN'};
       $end_date = $all_indexes->{$key}{'PROCESS_DATE_END'};
    
       $date_range = "$start_date-$end_date";
    
       $start_date_year = substr($start_date, 0, 4);
       $start_date_month = substr($start_date, 4, 2);
       $start_date_day = substr($start_date, 6, 2);
    
    
       $end_date_year = substr($end_date, 0, 4);
       $end_date_month = substr($end_date, 4, 2);
       $end_date_day = substr($end_date, 6, 2);
 
       $days_between = Delta_Days( $start_date_year, $start_date_month, $start_date_day,  $end_date_year,  $end_date_month, $end_date_day)+1;
    
       $last_element = $#{$enabled_indexes->{$key}};
       $enable_start_date = ${$enabled_indexes->{$key}}[0];
       $enable_end_date = ${$enabled_indexes->{$key}}[$last_element];
    
       $days_found = scalar(@{$enabled_indexes->{$key}});
    
       $days_missing = $days_between-$days_found;
    
        write;
    }
}

sub write_detail {
    
    my $index_date;
    
    format DETAIL_TOP =
    
    @||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||
    $detail_report_header
    
    =========================================================
    @<<<<<<<    @<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<     @<<<<<<<<<<<<
    'INDEX ID','INDEX NAME','DATE'
    =========================================================
.
    
    
    format DETAIL =
    @<<<<<<<    @<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<     @<<<<<<<<<<<<
    $index_id, $index_desc, $index_date
.
    

    if ($add_create) {

        $detail_report_header = 'CREATING INDEXES - DETAIL';
        $~ = 'DETAIL_TOP';
        write;
        $~ = 'DETAIL';
       

         foreach $key (sort keys %{$creating_indexes}){
            $index_id = $key;
            $index_desc =  $all_indexes->{$key}{'DESCRIPTION'};
            foreach $a (@{$creating_indexes->{$key}}) {
               $index_date = $a;
               write;
            }
        }
    }

    if ($add_failed) {

        $detail_report_header = 'FAILED INDEXES - DETAIL';
        $~ = 'DETAIL_TOP';
        write;
        $~ = 'DETAIL';

         foreach $key (sort keys %{$failed_indexes}){
            $index_id = $key;
            $index_desc =  $all_indexes->{$key}{'DESCRIPTION'};
            foreach $a (@{$failed_indexes->{$key}}) {
               $index_date = $a;
               write;
            }
         }

    }
}

$dbh->disconnect;

#install_module
#!/usr/bin/perl


if ($ARGV[0] eq "-install")
{
	shift (@ARGV);
	$install = uc(shift(@ARGV));
}
else
{
	print STDERR "make_makefile: Must specify option where the package is to be installed\n";
	print STDERR "\n";
	print STDERR "Usage: make_makefile -install common | std ... (other options)\n";
	print STDERR "\n";
	exit(1);
}

if ($install =~ /^COMMON|BLUELITE$/i)
{
	print "\n";
	print " *  Makefile will be generated to install into the *Common Bluelite* directories\n";
	print "\n";
	$install_base = "/ds/common";
}
elsif ($install =~ /^STD|STANDARD|PERL$/i)
{
	print "\n";
	print " * Makefile will be generated to install into the *Bluelite Perl* directories\n";
	print "\n";
	$install_base = "/ds/perl";

}
else
{
	print STDERR "make_makefile: Must specify where the package is to be installed\n";
	print STDERR "\n";
	print STDERR "Usage: make_makefile -install common | std ... (other options)\n";
	print STDERR "\n";
	
	exit(1);
}

$ARCH = $ENV{ARCH};
$install_lib = "$install_base/lib";
$install_man = "$install_base/man";
$install_bin = "$install_base/bin";
$install_arch = "$install_lib/$ARCH";

die "No install_base directory: $install_base\n" if (! -d $install_base);
die "No install_lib directory: $install_lib\n" if (! -d $install_lib);
die "No install_man directory: $install_man\n" if (! -d $install_man);
die "No install_bin directory: $install_bin\n" if (! -d $install_bin);
	

@parms = ();
push (@parms, "INSTALLDIRS=perl");

push (@parms, "LIB=$install_lib");
push (@parms, "INSTALLPRIVLIB=$install_lib");

push (@parms, "INSTALLMAN1DIR=$install_man");
push (@parms, "INSTALLMAN3DIR=$install_man");

push (@parms, "INSTALLBIN=$install_bin");
push (@parms, "INSTALLSCRIPT=$install_bin");

push (@parms, "INSTALLARCHLIB=$install_arch");

$cmd = "perl Makefile.PL " . join(" ", @parms) . " " . join(" ", @ARGV);

print "$cmd\n";

$ret = system ($cmd);
$ret = $ret >> 8;

if ($ret != 0) 
{
	print STDERR "\n";
	print	STDERR "ERROR: make_makefile: perl Makefile.PL failed!!!\n";
	print STDERR "\n";
}


#iqvia_check.sh
#!/bin/bash
# William Hampton / sdthgy6 / 24SEP2024
# Checks for delivery of the IQVIA FILE (weekly)


# This command name
export CMD=${0}

# Define the incoming, processed and failed dirs
export INCOMING_DIR=/ds/incomig/prescriber
export PROCESSED_DIR=/ds/incoming/prescriber/.processed
export FAILED_DIR=/ds/incoming/prescriber/.failed

# Check for file once a week
export OM404780_FILE=`find /ds/incoming/prescriber -type f -name 'OM404780*.zip' -mtime -7 -exec basename {} \;`
export OM404780_COUNT=`find /ds/incoming/prescriber -type f -name 'OM404780*.zip' -mtime -7 -exec basename {} \; | wc -l`

# Check if file has been processed
if [ $OM404780_COUNT -ge 1 ];
 then
  perl -we 'use DS::DSLOG; my $log_obj = DS::DSLOG->new(
              APP_ID      => q{PSCBR},
              PROCESS     => "IQVIA_FILE_CHECK",
              EVENT_CODE  => q{SUCCESS},
              LOG_LEVEL   => q{INFO},
              CMD_NAME    => $ENV{CMD},
              MESSAGE     => "Data Services received " . $ENV{OM404780_FILE} . " file for this week.");
    exit 0;'
  #echo "Data Services received an IQVIA file for this week." | mailx -s "IQVIA file check" william.hampton@McKesson.com
 exit 0


# Check to see if the IQVIA file in the incoming directory
elif [ -e  ${INCOMING_DIR}/${OM404780_FILE} ]
 then
  perl -we 'use DS::DSLOG; my $log_obj = DS::DSLOG->new(
              APP_ID      => q{PSCBR},
              PROCESS     => "IQVIA_FILE_CHECK",
              EVENT_CODE  => q{SUCCESS},
              LOG_LEVEL   => q{INFO},
              CMD_NAME    => $ENV{CMD},
              MESSAGE     => "The " . $ENV{OM404780_FILE} . " file is currently in the incoming folder.");
    exit 0;'
#  echo "IQVIA file is in incoming directory" | mailx -s "IQVIA file check" william.hampton@McKesson.com
 exit 0




# Check to see if the IQVIA file in the failed directory
elif [ -e  ${FAILED_DIR}/${OM404780_FILE} ]
 then
  perl -we 'use DS::DSLOG; my $log_obj = DS::DSLOG->new(
              APP_ID      => q{PSCBR},
              PROCESS     => "IQVIA_FILE_CHECK",
              EVENT_CODE  => q{ERROR},
              LOG_LEVEL   => q{ERROR},
              CMD_NAME    => $ENV{CMD},
              MESSAGE     => ""  . $ENV{OM404780_FILE} . " file is in the failed directory.");
    exit 0;'
  #echo "IQVIA file is in the failed directory." | mailx -s "IQVIA file check" william.hampton@McKesson.com
 exit 0
else
  perl -we 'use Env; use DS::DSLOG; my $log_obj = DS::DSLOG->new(
              APP_ID      => q{PSCBR},
              PROCESS     => "IQVIA_FILE_CHECK",
              EVENT_CODE  => q{ERROR},
              LOG_LEVEL   => q{ERROR},
              CMD_NAME    => $ENV{CMD},
              MESSAGE     => "Data Servies has not received an "  . $ENV{OM404780_FILE} . " this week.");
    exit 0;'
  echo "Data Services has not received an IQVIA file for last month." | mailx -s "IQVIA file check (ERROR)" DataServicesNotification@McKesson.com
  exit 1
fi


#job_clear_trigger
#!/usr/bin/perl

# job_trigger_post_date: Create a "end of day" trigger file BLUELITE::Job apps
#
# Author(s): John Hess		RelayHealth
#
# Version history:
# Version 1.0 - 3/27/2009
#

use IO::Compress::Gzip qw($GzipError);
use DateTime::Format::Strptime;
use Getopt::Long;
use Mail::SendEasy;
use File::Copy;
use File::PathConvert qw(rel2abs);
use File::Spec;

use BLUELITE::Job;
use BLUELITE::Logger;
use BLUELITE::Mail qw(email);

use strict;
use warnings;

my @dir_parts = File::Spec->splitdir(rel2abs($0));
our $PGM = pop(@dir_parts);


sub Usage() {
  print "$PGM: Clear trigger files for BLUELITE::Job apps\n\n";
  print "Usage: $PGM [-options] -app-id i\n";
  print " Required parameters\n";
  print "  -app-id i                     Application id as recorded in JOB_CONFIG table\n";
	print "  -post-date YYYYMMDD\n";
}


############# MAIN ###########

if (scalar(@ARGV) == 0) {
  Usage;
  exit(1);
}

# Get command-line options

my ($app_id, $post_date);

GetOptions(
            'app-id=s' => \$app_id,
            'post-date=s' => \$post_date,
) || exit(1);

die "ERROR: The mandatory -app-id parameter was not specified!\n" if (! defined($app_id));

my $job = BLUELITE::Job->new(app_id => $app_id) || die "Unable to obtain BLUELITE::Job object for app_id = '$app_id' : $@\n";
my @clear_opts;

if (defined($post_date)) {
	@clear_opts = (post_date => $post_date);
} else {
	die "Must provide -post-date parameter\n";
}

my @trigger_files = $job->clear_trigger(@clear_opts);

if (! @trigger_files) {
	die "Could not clear trigger file for post date $post_date\n";
}

print "Trigger files cleared from database:\n";
print join("\n", @trigger_files) . "\n";


#job_concat
#!/usr/bin/perl

#use lib '/ds/development/Job/dev/blib/lib';

# job_concat_post_date : Concatenate BLUELITE::Job worker output files into 1-file-per-post-date client deliverable files
# job_concat: Concatenate BLUELITE::Job worker output files into client deliverable files
#
# Author(s): John Hess		RelayHealth
#
# Version history:
#
# Version 1.0 - 10/4/2007
#
#
# Version 1.1 - 3/30/2009
#
# Fixed bug where output file was not being explicitly closed if encoding type is compressed and trailer is defined.
# Effect of bug was incorrect file size written to job_delivery table.
#
# Added -keep-worker-files option
#
# Added $! error output in addition to $GzipError error output
#
#
# Version 1.5 - 4/2/2009
# 
# Added support for running as "job_concat", in addition to existing "job_concat_post_date".
# As job_concat, output from any completed workers not already concatenated are concatenated.
# This required adding support for "post_date_seq" coming from $job->deliverable_fname_vars
# (in addition to existing support for "post_date").
#
# Version 1.6 - 4/13/2009
#
# Concatenation is now serialized for a given app, to prevent workers from being concatenated
# into multiple concatenation processes running simultaneously.
#
# Added calls to the following methods: concat_begin, concat_end, concatenation_minutes.
# Added DISCONNECT_ON_DESTROY option to constructor, so that concat_end will work in END block.
#
# Version 1.7 - 5/19/2009
#
# Temp dir for concatenation is now in /temp, or where ever a reasonable temp dir can be found
# (several possibilities are checked). Last resort is temp under deliverables dir, which will
# be created if necessary.
#
# Temp file name now has current PID ($$) as prefix of file name to avoid clobbering other temp
# files on same temp dir.
#
# Version 1.8 - 5/20/2009
#
# Added support for post-process command
#
# Version 1.9 - 2/20/2010
#
# Added -post-date, -max-concat-input-txns, -deliverable-dir, and -log-to-screen parameters
#
#
# Version 1.91 - 4/20/2010
#
# Changed signal handler setup to use std_abort_signals function from BLUELITE::Common instead of explicit list
#
#
# Version 1.4 6/22/2010 (version # adjusted down to match version of BLUELITE::Job package)
#
# Made -app-dir parameter optional (defaults to value returned by app_dir method of Job object)
#
# Change logging by providing desired logfile name to Job object constructor, and use logger method
# of Job object to obtain logger.
#
# Version 1.5 7/23/2010
#
# Using post-date command line option will now pass those post dates to the ready_to_deliver method.
# This will allow the method to override the usual search_days config parameter. Previously, this
# option only worked if the date requested was not beyond the search days.
#
# Version 1.6 8/6/2010
#
# Removed requirement to create valid XML document in STDERR of post-process to convey # of output records.
# Now only a XML tag must be present like:    <data_records>12345</data_records>
#
# Version 2.1 10/20/2010
#
# Fixed bug where logfile was not removed is no files were concatenated.
#
# Version 2.3 12/28/2010
#
# Added '-mark-delivered' command-line option. This should be used to avoid late file delivery warnings when
# a post process delivers the data via some non-standard means (i.e. database inserts) instead of
# transmitting a file via ftp.
#
# Added '-group-id' command-line option. This will sequentially attempt to perform concatenation for each app_id
# within the requested group_id.
#
# Fix "modification of a read-only value" bug when looking for a usable temp dir.
#
# Version 2.5 1/5/2011
#
# Added -exclude-app command-line option
#
# Version 2.63 - 2/23/2011
# - Fixed bug where sometimes neither of 2 concatenators attempting to run at the same time would properly detect the other
# one and the result would be a "Missing worker files" notification. This was resolved by: 
# 1) Adding a "AND concat_begin_time IS NULL" to the WHERE clause of the UPDATE inside the concat_begin_time method.
# 2) Having the concat_begin method return true only if the UPDATE of the concat_begin_time actually updated a row.
# 3) Changing the job_concat script to use the return value of the concat_begin method to determine whether it was
# actually able to update the concat_begin_time column in the job_config table. If not, then it logs warning or info
# and exits.
# 4) Checking concatenation_minutes method BEFORE calling ready_to_deliver method.
#
# - Changed "skipped concatenation" log message to be INFO level if reason is "already concatenating" for less than
# 10 minutes, or WARN if more than 10 minutes.
#
# Version 2.7 - 3/28/2011
#
# - Added -no-max-records-check to command line options
# - Fixed bug where no concatenation would occur if multiple post dates are provided on command line
# - Removed "no concatenation has ever occurred" message since it is often wrong when generating test
# files and it's not worth fixing.
#
# Version 2.8 - 4/26/2011
#
# - Added support for flexible date specifications in -post-date option (ranges, months, etc)
# - The "Added ## records from .." message is now logged only if ## is at least 1
# - Added -one-output-file command line option, which will put all output into a single file instead of seperating
#   by post date.
# - Refactored main concatenation loop by moving file start & finish steps into subroutines (due to new
#   -one-output-file option).
# - Removed "post_date_complete" behavior that was based on script name. Now handled as job_config setting internal
#   to ready_to_deliver method.
# - Added -ds-format command line option for concatenating workers that were launched with the same command-line option.
# - Fixed logging problem that caused logging to screen when -group-id specified
#
# Version 2.9 - 5/29/2011
#
# - Changed "skipped concatenation" log message to be ERROR if already concatenating more than 30 minutes, and DEBUG
# for less than 10 messages. The DEBUG will prevent this message from clearing a yellow alert in job_status script.
# - Changed log_type from 'INFO' to 'DEBUG' for 'Attempting concatenation' message of log() call. This will
# avoid a concat "attempt" from clearing a yellow alert in job_status script.
# - Changed log_type from 'INFO' to 'DEBUG' for 'A file concatenation attempt for $APP_ID was skipped ...'
# message of log() call. This will prevent this message from clearing a yellow alert in job_status script.
# - Added optional log_type to mydie subroutine, defaulting to ERROR
# - Added log_type of 'WARN' to mydie call when add_delivery method fails, so job_status will show details of problem
#
# Version 3.0 - 6/8/2011
#
# - Added support for gzip (.gz) input files to concat function
# - Added -all-or-none command line option
#
# Version 3.2 - 6/28/2011
#
# - Added new deliverable_fname_vars tokens supported in job_config table (YYYY, MM, DD).
# - Added -any command line option, which can be used with -span-post-dates to turn off -all-or-none option.
#
# Version 4.1 - 9/19/2011
#
# - Increased warning/error thresholds for "already concatenating" from 10/30 to 20/40.
#
# Version 4.2 - 9/26/2011
#
# - Shortened concat success log message in finish_output_file function.
# - Shortened "Created deliverable file.." message.
#
# Version 4.3 - 10/24/2011
#
# - Added -config-group-id command-line option, for getting default config settings from that group.
#
# Version 4.6 - 11/8/2012
#
# - Added "cd" to bin dir before running post process
#
# Version 4.7 - 4/16/2013
#
# - Added -no-mutex command line option, which will allow multiple job_concat processes for the same app-id to
# be executing simultaneously. The -post-date option becomes mandatory when using this option, as the caller
# must become the coordinator of parallel job_concat processing by segregating work via exclusive post dates/ranges.
#
# - Added error check in concat() function between end of read loop and file handle close to detect an error
# such as "unexpected end of file" when reading compressed files.
#
# - Added support for 'date_created' in deliverable_fname_vars config attribute
#
# Version 4.8 - 6/6/2013
#
# - The -app-id and -post-date parameters are now provided to the post-process command
# - Improved error display when errors caused by concat post-process. Not just "broken pipe" anymore.
#
# Version 4.9 - 6/20/2013
#
# - Warnings/errors generated for long concatenation times are now based on app config parameters instead of being
# hard-coded to 20 and 40 minutes for all apps. Can be disabled by setting config value <= 0.
#
# Version 5.0 - 3/5/2014
#
# - Added -keep-log option. Default is now to remove logfile is no errors.
# - Input workers with no filename are now skipped (i.e. filename no longer required)
# - Output file is no longer generated if deliverable_fname_sprintf is not defined and there is no input or output from post_concat_cmd
# - An attempt to remove an existing temp file of the same name is made prior to attempting to create it
# - Fixed bug that prevented STDERR of post_concat_cmd from appearing in log output
# - Logfile naming convention is now consistent with that of job_launcher script
#
# Version 5.1 - 6/9/2014
# - Add support for new auto_completion config parameter
#
# Version 6.0 - 10/31/2014
# - Added support for "autohoc" requests (i.e. automated on-demand ad-hoc processing).
#
# Version 6.2 - 12/15/2014 - Michael Carey <michael.carey@mckesson.com>
# - removing command line option -max-concat-input-txns, moving this parm
#   to the job config table  MAX_CONCAT_INPUT_TXNS.  This is being done to
#   support datafeed deliverable file size limitation for SENTRY datafeed.
#   04/16/2015 - Michael Carey <michael.carey@mckesson.com>
# - adding support for special record terminator of "NONE" which will disable
#   job_concat's line ending management (binary file deliverables).  The IO
#   loop is still not ideal for use where binary deliverables are large, but
#   job_concat shouldn't corrupt binary output from a post processor.
# - Add REQUEST_ID variable support for deliverable_fname_vars
#
# Version 6.3 - 7/2/2015 - J Hess
# - Add support for REFERENCE_ID file naming variable
#

use IO::Compress::Gzip qw($GzipError gzip);
use IO::Uncompress::Gunzip qw($GunzipError);
use IO::File;
use DateTime::Format::Strptime;
use Getopt::Long;
use Mail::SendEasy;
use File::Copy;
use File::PathConvert qw(rel2abs);
use File::Spec;
use Params::Validate qw(:all);
use Data::Dumper;
use File::Path;

use BLUELITE::Job;
use BLUELITE::Logger;
use BLUELITE::Mail qw(email);
use BLUELITE::Common qw(std_abort_signals);

use strict;
use warnings;

my @dir_parts = File::Spec->splitdir(rel2abs($0));
our $PGM = pop(@dir_parts);
my $pgm = rel2abs($0);

our $MAX_CONCAT_INPUT_TXNS;
our $POST_DATE;
our $JOB;
our $CONCATENATING = 0;
our $SCREEN_ONLY = 0;
our $MARK_DELIVERED;
our $DEFAULT_EXIT_SUCCESS = 0;
our ($SUCCESS_EMAIL, $FAILURE_EMAIL, $DEFAULT_FAILURE_EMAIL, $DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME, $REQUEST_ID);
our $DEFAULT_DATE_FORMAT = DateTime::Format::Strptime->new( pattern => '%Y%m%d%H%M%S') || die "ERROR: Unable to set default date format!\n";
our $FILES_CREATED = 0;
our ($DBH, $OUT_FH, $LOGGER, $APP_ID, $LOGFILE, $DELIVERABLE_DIR, $APP_DIR_TOP, $BIN_DIR);
our $custom_header = 0;
our $custom_trailer = 0;
our $KEEP_WORKER_FILES = 0;
our ($TEMP_OUTPUT_DIR, $HEADER, $TRAILER, $TODAY_DATE);
our $OUTPUT_FILE_OPEN = 0;


sub failure_email() {

	if (defined($FAILURE_EMAIL)) {
		return $FAILURE_EMAIL;
	} elsif (defined($DEFAULT_FAILURE_EMAIL)) {
		return $DEFAULT_FAILURE_EMAIL;
	}

	return undef;
}

sub mydie($;$) {
  my $message = shift;
	my $log_type = shift;
	$log_type = 'ERROR' if (! defined($log_type));

	# close output file

	if (defined($OUT_FH) && $OUT_FH->opened) {
		$OUT_FH->close;
	}

	# remove output file

	if (defined($DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME)) {
		if (-f $DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME) {

			eval '$LOGGER->info("Removing concatenated output file $DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME")' if (defined($LOGGER));

			if (! unlink($DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME)) {
				$message .= "\nCould not delete output file $DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME : $!\n";
			} else {
				$message .= "\nDeleted output file $DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME\n";
			}
		}
	}

	if (defined($LOGGER)) {
		eval '$LOGGER->info("Created $FILES_CREATED deliverable files")';
		$message .= "\nSee logfile $LOGFILE for more details\n" if (defined($LOGFILE));
	}

	if (defined($JOB)) {
		$JOB->rollback;
		$JOB->log(event_code => 'CCFAIL', log_type => $log_type, message => $message, email_subject => 'Concatenation failed');
	}

	if (defined($LOGGER)) {
		exit(1);
	} else {
		die $message . "\n";
	}
}


sub get_deliverable_fname($$$$$) {
	my ($post_date, $deliverable_dir, $temp_dir, $job, $post_date_spec) = @_;

  my $deliverable_fname_sprintf = $job->deliverable_fname_sprintf;
  my $deliverable_fname_vars = $job->deliverable_fname_vars;

	mydie "get_deliverable_fname: deliverable_fname_sprintf must be configured in the JOB_CONFIG table\n" if (! defined($deliverable_fname_sprintf));
	$deliverable_fname_sprintf =~ s/^\s+//;
	$deliverable_fname_sprintf =~ s/\s+$//;
	mydie "get_deliverable_fname: deliverable_fname_sprintf must be configured in the JOB_CONFIG table\n" if (length($deliverable_fname_sprintf) == 0);

	mydie "get_deliverable_fname: deliverable_fname_vars must be configured in the JOB_CONFIG table\n" if (! defined($deliverable_fname_vars));
	$deliverable_fname_vars =~ s/^\s+//;
	$deliverable_fname_vars =~ s/\s+$//;
