	mydie "get_deliverable_fname: deliverable_fname_vars must be configured in the JOB_CONFIG table\n" if (length($deliverable_fname_vars) == 0);

	my @var_list = split(/\s*,\s*/, uc($deliverable_fname_vars));
	mydie "get_deliverable_fname: could not parse any variables from deliverable_fname_vars value of '$deliverable_fname_vars'\n" if (scalar(@var_list) == 0);

	my @fname_vars = ();

	my $info = {};
	my $seq_num;
	my $pd_parm = $post_date;
	$pd_parm = $post_date_spec if (defined($post_date_spec));
	$pd_parm = 'POST_DATES' if (! defined($pd_parm));

	my $yyyy = '';
	my $mm = '';
	my $dd = '';

	if ($pd_parm =~ /^\s*(\d\d\d\d)/) {
		$yyyy = $1;
	}

	if ($pd_parm =~ /^\s*(\d\d\d\d)(\d\d)/) {
		$mm = $2;
	}

	if ($pd_parm =~ /^\s*(\d\d\d\d)(\d\d)(\d\d)/) {
		$dd = $3;
	}

	foreach my $var (@var_list) {
		if ($var eq 'POST_DATE') {
			push(@fname_vars, $pd_parm);
		} elsif ($var eq 'POST_DATE_SEQ') {
			$seq_num = $job->next_post_date_seq_num($pd_parm);

			push(@fname_vars, $seq_num);

			$info->{seq_num} = $seq_num;
		} elsif ($var eq 'YYYY') {
			push(@fname_vars, $yyyy);
		} elsif ($var eq 'MM') {
			push(@fname_vars, $mm);
		} elsif ($var eq 'DD') {
			push(@fname_vars, $dd);
		} elsif ($var eq 'DATE_CREATED') {
			push(@fname_vars, $TODAY_DATE);
		} elsif ($var eq 'REQUEST_ID') {
			push(@fname_vars, $job->rq_request_id);
		} elsif ($var eq 'REFERENCE_ID') {
			push(@fname_vars, $job->rq_reference_id);
		} else {
			mydie "get_deliverable_fname: deliverable_fname_vars = '$deliverable_fname_vars', which contains a unrecognized variable named '$var'\n";
		}
	}

	mydie "get_deliverable_fname: could not find any recognized variables from deliverable_fname_vars value of '$deliverable_fname_vars'\n" if (scalar(@fname_vars) == 0);

	my $fname = sprintf($deliverable_fname_sprintf, @fname_vars);
	my $fname_temp = "$temp_dir/$$.$fname";
	$fname = "$deliverable_dir/$fname";

	$info->{fname} = $fname;
	$info->{fname_temp} = $fname_temp;

	return $info;
}


sub Usage() {
  print "$PGM: Concatenate BLUELITE::Job worker output files into deliverable files\n\n";
  print "Usage 1: $PGM -group-id g [-options]\n";
  print "Usage 2: $PGM -app-id a   [-options]\n";
	print "\n";
  print " Options (defaults in parenthesis):\n";
  print "  -request-id #                 Concatenate request id in job_queue table\n";
  print "  -app-dir d                    Top-level application directory (from job_config table)\n";
  print "  -exit #                       Exit with status # on success. ($DEFAULT_EXIT_SUCCESS)\n";
  print "  -logging-level level          Set logging to level (INFO). Values: DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR, FATAL\n";
  print "  -success-email list           Send status to list addresses upon success (application default)\n";
  print "  -failure-email list           Send status to list addresses upon failure (application default)\n";
  print "  -default-failure-email list   Send status to list addresses upon failure (does not override app default)\n";
  print "  -check-only                   Only check to see if concatenation would be performed (off)\n";
  print "  -keep-worker-files            Preserve worker files after concatenation (off)\n";
#  print "  -max-concat-input-txns #      Max # of input txns\n";
  print "  -deliverable-dir dir          Output deliverable directory\n";
  print "  -mark-delivered               Mark output as 'delivered' (off)\n";
  print "  -exclude-app a                Exclude app_id a from group_id g (Usage 1 only, can repeat)\n";
  print "  -log-to-screen                Log to the screen\n";
  print "  -screen-only                  Log only to the screen\n";
  print "  -no-max-records-check         Do NOT check for violation of max # of output records (max records checked)\n";
  print "                                {in production, use only with management approval}\n";
  print "  -span-post-dates              Do NOT limit each output file to 1 post date (1 post date per file)\n";
  print "  -all-or-none                  Must concatenate all dates in pd_spec or none of them (default if -span-post-dates used)\n";
  print "  -any                          Turn off -all-or-none option (default except when -span-post-dates used)\n";
  print "  -ds-format fmt                Concatenate workers with data_source_format of fmt (e.g. POSTDATE)\n";
  print "  -config-group-id id           Get default group config params from group_id id\n";
  print "  -no-mutex                     Allow concatenation when other processes of same app_id are concatenating\n";
  print "  -keep-log                     Keep log file (removed if no errors encountered)\n";
  print "  -post-date PRIOR              Only concatenate workers from post dates prior to today\n";
  print "  -post-date pd_spec            Only concatenate workers from these post dates\n\n";
  print "Note: pd_spec may be a comma-separated list of any combination of the following syntaxes:\n";
  print "  YYYYMMDD\n";
  print "  YYYYMMDD-YYYYMMDD\n";
  print "  YYYYMM\n";
  print "  YYYYMM-YYYYMM\n";
  print "  YYYYMMDD-YYYYMM\n";
  print "  YYYYMM-YYYYMMDD\n";
}


sub sig_handler() {
  my $signal = shift;

  mydie "$PGM process was killed via $signal signal.\n";
}

sub concat($$$) {
	my ($fname, $record_terminator, $temp_stderr_fname) = (shift, shift, shift);
	my $records_added = 0;
	my $input_fh;

	return 0 if (! defined($fname));

	if ($fname =~ /[.]gz$/i) {
		$input_fh = new IO::Uncompress::Gunzip $fname || mydie "Cannot open gzipped input file $fname : $GunzipError\n";
	} else {
		$input_fh = new IO::File || mydie "Cannot get file handle to read input file $fname\n";
		$input_fh->open("< $fname") || mydie "Cannot open file handle to read input file $fname : " . $input_fh->error() . "\n";
	}

	my $line;
	while ($line = $input_fh->getline()) {
		
		if ($record_terminator ne 'NONE') {
			$line =~ s/[\015]?[\012]$//;	# remove CR/LF or LF at end of line
			$line .= $record_terminator;	# put appropriate record terminator at end of line
		}
		
		if (! $OUT_FH->print($line)) {
			my $general_error_txt = "$@ : $!";

			$OUT_FH->close;

			my @temp_pp_stderr = ();

			if (defined($temp_stderr_fname)) {
				if (open(TMP, $temp_stderr_fname)) {
					@temp_pp_stderr = <TMP>;
					close(TMP);
				}
			}

			mydie "Cannot append data from $fname to output file : " . join('', @temp_pp_stderr) . ": $general_error_txt\n";
		}

		$records_added++;
	}

	if ($input_fh->can('error') && $input_fh->error) {
		mydie "Cannot append data from $fname to output file : " . $input_fh->error;
	}

	if (! $input_fh->close()) {
		my $error;

		if ($input_fh->can('error')) {
			$error = $input_fh->error;
		} else {
			$error = $GunzipError;
			$error = $! if (! defined($error));
		}

		mydie "Cannot close input file $fname : $error\n";
	}

	if ($records_added) {
		$LOGGER->info("Added $records_added records from $fname") || mydie "Cannot write to log file $LOGFILE : $@\n";
	}

	return $records_added;
}



sub write_header() {
  my $header_string;

	return undef if (! defined($OUT_FH));

	my $start_time = DateTime->now(time_zone => 'local', formatter => $DEFAULT_DATE_FORMAT) || return undef;
	my $base_file_name = $DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME;
	$base_file_name =~ s/.*\///g;

	return undef if ((! defined($base_file_name)) || (length($base_file_name) == 0));
  
  if ( $custom_header) {
      $header_string = get_header($start_time, $base_file_name);
  }
  else {
      $header_string = get_std_header($start_time, $base_file_name);
  }

	if (defined($header_string)) {
		print $OUT_FH $header_string || mydie "ERROR: Cannot append header to $DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME : $! , $GzipError\n";
	}

	return 1;
}


sub get_std_header($$$) {
    my $start_time = shift;
    my $base_file_name = shift;

    my $header_string = sprintf("H%14.14s%100.100s" . "\n", $start_time, $base_file_name) || mydie "ERROR: Cannot create the header string\n";

    return $header_string;

}

sub get_std_trailer($$) {
    my $end_time = shift;
    my $num_records = shift;

    my $trailer_string = sprintf("T%10d%14.14s" . "\n", $num_records, $end_time) || mydie "ERROR: Cannot create the header string\n";

    return $trailer_string;

}

sub write_trailer($) {
  my ($num_records) = (shift);
  my $trailer_string;

	return undef if (! defined($OUT_FH));

	my $end_time = DateTime->now(time_zone => 'local', formatter => $DEFAULT_DATE_FORMAT) || return undef;

  if ( $custom_trailer ) {
      $trailer_string = get_trailer($end_time, $num_records);
  }
  else {
      $trailer_string = get_std_trailer($end_time, $num_records);
  }

  print $OUT_FH $trailer_string if (defined($trailer_string));

	return 1;
}



sub mymove($$) {
  my ($source_file, $dest_dir) = (shift, shift);

	return undef if (! move($source_file, $dest_dir));

	my $base_fname = $source_file;
	$base_fname =~ s/.*\///g;

	return "${dest_dir}/${base_fname}";
}



sub add_delivery($$$$$$$$) {
  my ($fname_temp, $job, $post_date, $data_records, $total_txns, $workers_in_output, $seq_num, $check_record_count) = @_;

	my $fsize = -s $fname_temp;

	my @is_delivered = ();
	push(@is_delivered, is_delivered => $MARK_DELIVERED) if (defined($MARK_DELIVERED));

	if (! $job->add_delivery(fname => $DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME, workers => $workers_in_output, commit => 0, data_records => $data_records, txn_processed => $total_txns, post_date => $post_date, seq_num => $seq_num, fsize => $fsize, @is_delivered, check_record_count => $check_record_count)) {
		mydie("Could not successfully call BLUELITE::Job->add_delivery() for output file $DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME . The temp filename is $fname_temp\n", 'WARN');	# use WARN because add_delivery method will log ERROR, which is what we want most recent status to show in job_status output
	}

	my $created_file = 0;

	if ($job->fname_spec_configured() || ($fsize > 0)) {
		move($fname_temp, $DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME) || mydie "Could not move temp file $fname_temp to deliverable directory $DELIVERABLE_DIR : $!\n";
		$created_file = 1;
	} else {
		unlink($fname_temp);
	}

	$job->commit || mydie "Could not commit addition of delivery for $DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME\n";

	# clean up temp worker files since we no longer need them

	if (! $KEEP_WORKER_FILES) {
		my @undeleted_files = ();
		my $output_file;

		foreach my $worker (@{$workers_in_output}) {
			$output_file = $worker->output_fname;

			next if (! defined($output_file));

			if (! unlink($output_file)) {
				push(@undeleted_files, "$output_file : $!");
			}
		}

		if (defined($FAILURE_EMAIL) && (scalar(@undeleted_files) >= 1)) {
			email(
				to => $FAILURE_EMAIL,
				subject => "$APP_ID concatenation process warning",
				msg => "The following worker output files could not be removed after successful concatenation into the deliverable file $DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME:\n" . join("\n", @undeleted_files) . "\n\nThis did not cause any problems, but it may warrant investigation."
			);
		}
	}

	return $created_file;
}


sub myexit($) {
	my $exit_code = shift;

	if ($FILES_CREATED && defined($LOGGER)) {
		eval '$LOGGER->info("$FILES_CREATED concatenations performed.")';
	} else {
		eval '$LOGGER->info("No worker files concatenated.")';
	}

	unlink($LOGFILE) if (defined($LOGFILE) && (! $FILES_CREATED));
	
	exit($exit_code);
}


sub start_output_file(%) {
  my %option = validate_with
    ( params  => \@_,
      spec    => {
                  post_date_spec => { type => SCALAR|UNDEF, optional => 0 },
                  post_date => { type => SCALAR|UNDEF, optional => 0 },
                  span_post_dates => { type => SCALAR, optional => 0 }
                },
      called  => 'start_output_file',
      normalize_keys => sub { my $k = shift; $k =~ s/^-//; return uc $k }
  );

	my $post_date_spec = $option{POST_DATE_SPEC};
	my $post_date = $option{POST_DATE};

	if ($option{SPAN_POST_DATES}) {
		$post_date = undef;
	} else {
		$post_date_spec = undef;
	}

	my $post_concat_cmd = $JOB->post_concat_cmd;
	my $via_text = '';
	$via_text = "via post-concat command '$post_concat_cmd'" if (defined($post_concat_cmd));

	my $file_info = get_deliverable_fname($post_date, $DELIVERABLE_DIR, $TEMP_OUTPUT_DIR, $JOB, $post_date_spec);
	$DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME = $file_info->{fname};
	my $fname_temp = $file_info->{fname_temp};

	my $eff_post_date = $post_date_spec;
	$eff_post_date = $post_date if (! defined($eff_post_date));

	$JOB->log(event_code => 'CCATT', post_date => $eff_post_date, log_type => 'DEBUG', email_subject => 'Attempting concatenation', message => "Attempting concatenation for post date $eff_post_date $via_text", email_to => undef);

	my $file_encoding = $JOB->deliverable_encoding;
	$file_encoding = '' if (! defined($file_encoding));

	my $temp_stderr_fname;

	unlink($fname_temp) if (-e $fname_temp);

	if (defined($post_concat_cmd)) {
		$OUT_FH = new IO::File "> $fname_temp" || mydie "Cannot create temp output file $fname_temp : $!\n";

		if (defined($HEADER)) {
			 write_header || mydie "Could not write header to $fname_temp : $! , $GzipError\n";
		}

		$OUT_FH->close || mydie "Could not close output file $fname_temp : $!\n";

		$temp_stderr_fname = "$fname_temp.err";
		chdir($BIN_DIR);
		unlink($temp_stderr_fname) if (-e $temp_stderr_fname);

		$OUT_FH = new IO::File "| $post_concat_cmd -app-id $APP_ID -post-date $eff_post_date >> $fname_temp 2> $temp_stderr_fname" || mydie "Cannot create temp output file $fname_temp via post-process command '$post_concat_cmd': $!\n";

	} elsif ($file_encoding =~ /^\s*(raw|uncompressed)\s*$/i) {
		$OUT_FH = new IO::File "> $fname_temp" || mydie "Cannot create temp output file $fname_temp : $!\n";

		if (defined($HEADER)) {
			 write_header || mydie "Could not write header to $fname_temp : $! , $GzipError\n";
		}
	} elsif ($file_encoding =~ /^\s*gzip\s*$/i) {
		$OUT_FH = new IO::Compress::Gzip $fname_temp || mydie "Gzip failed to create $fname_temp : $GzipError\n";

		if (defined($HEADER)) {
			 write_header || mydie "Could not write header to $fname_temp : $! , $GzipError\n";
		}
	} else {
		mydie "ERROR: file_encoding type of '$file_encoding' is not supported!\n";
	}

	$OUTPUT_FILE_OPEN = 1;

	return { fname_temp => $file_info->{fname_temp}, seq_num => $file_info->{seq_num}, temp_stderr_fname => $temp_stderr_fname };
}


sub finish_output_file(%) {

  my %option = validate_with
    ( params  => \@_,
      spec    => {
                  fname_temp => { type => SCALAR, optional => 0 },
                  temp_stderr_fname => { type => SCALAR|UNDEF, optional => 0 },
                  total_records => { type => SCALAR, optional => 0 },
                  post_date => { type => SCALAR|UNDEF, optional => 0 },
                  post_date_spec => { type => SCALAR|UNDEF, optional => 0 },
                  seq_num => { type => SCALAR|UNDEF, optional => 0 },
                  check_record_count => { type => SCALAR, optional => 0 },
                  total_txns => { type => SCALAR, optional => 0 },
                  workers_in_output => { type => ARRAYREF, optional => 0 },
                  span_post_dates => { type => SCALAR, optional => 0 },
                },
      called  => 'finish_output_file',
      normalize_keys => sub { my $k = shift; $k =~ s/^-//; return uc $k }
  );

	my $post_date = $option{POST_DATE};
	$post_date = $option{POST_DATE_SPEC} if ($option{SPAN_POST_DATES});

	my $post_concat_cmd = $JOB->post_concat_cmd;
	my $fname_temp = $option{FNAME_TEMP};
	my $temp_stderr_fname = $option{TEMP_STDERR_FNAME};
	my $total_records = $option{TOTAL_RECORDS};
	my $total_input_records = $option{TOTAL_RECORDS};
	my $file_encoding = $JOB->deliverable_encoding;
	$file_encoding = '' if (! defined($file_encoding));

		my $pp_input_records;

		if (defined($post_concat_cmd)) {

			my $post_concat_failed = 0;

			if (! $OUT_FH->close) {
				unlink($fname_temp) || $LOGGER->warn("Could not remove temp output file $fname_temp produced by post-process command : $!");
				$post_concat_failed = 1;
			}

			$LOGGER->info("Input records for post-process: $total_records");
			$total_records = undef;

			if ((-s $temp_stderr_fname) > 0) {

				if (open(SE, $temp_stderr_fname)) {
					my $stderr = '';

					while (<SE>) {
						if ($_ =~ /<data_records>\s*(\d+)\s*<\/data_records>/i) {
							if (! defined($total_records)) {
								$total_records = $1;
							} else {
								$LOGGER->error("Found <data_records> tag more than once in the post-process STDERR output");
								close(SE);
								mydie "Found <data_records> tag more than once in the post-process STDERR output\n";
							}
						} else {
							$stderr .= $_;
						}
					}

					$LOGGER->info("STDERR/log output from post-process:\n" . $stderr) if (length($stderr) > 0);
					close(SE);
				} else {
					$LOGGER->error("Could not open STDERR output file $temp_stderr_fname from post-process command : $!");
					mydie "Could not open STDERR output file $temp_stderr_fname from post-process command : $!";
				}
			}

			unlink($temp_stderr_fname) || $LOGGER->warn("Could not remove STDERR output file $temp_stderr_fname produced by post-process command : $!");
			mydie "The post-process command terminated abnormally: $! $@\n" if ($post_concat_failed);

			if (defined($TRAILER)) {
				$OUT_FH = new IO::File ">> $fname_temp";

				if (! defined($OUT_FH)) {
					unlink($fname_temp) || $LOGGER->warn("Could not remove temp output file $fname_temp produced by post-process command : $!");
					mydie "Cannot open temp output file $fname_temp for appending trailer: $!\n";
				}

				no warnings 'uninitialized';

				if (! write_trailer($total_records)) {
					unlink($fname_temp) || $LOGGER->warn("Could not remove temp output file $fname_temp produced by post-process command : $!");
					mydie "Could not append trailer to $fname_temp : $!\n";
				}

				$OUT_FH->close || mydie "Could not close output file $fname_temp after appending trailer: $!\n";
			}

			$LOGGER->warn("Number of output data_records could not be determined from STDERR of post-process command") if (! defined($total_records));

			# gzip post-process output, if appropriate

			if ($file_encoding =~ /^\s*gzip\s*$/i) {
				my $temp_fname_temp = "$fname_temp.temp";
				gzip $fname_temp => $temp_fname_temp or mydie "Could not compress temp output file $fname_temp to temp temp output file $temp_fname_temp: $GzipError\n";

				move($temp_fname_temp, $fname_temp) or mydie "Could not move temp temp output file $temp_fname_temp to $fname_temp : $!\n";
			}
		} else {

			if (defined($TRAILER)) {
				 write_trailer($total_records) || mydie "Could not write trailer to $fname_temp : $! , $GzipError\n";
			}

			$OUT_FH->close || mydie "Could not close output file $fname_temp : $! , $GzipError\n";
		}

	no warnings 'uninitialized';

	my $created_file = add_delivery($option{FNAME_TEMP}, $JOB, $post_date, $total_records, $option{TOTAL_TXNS}, $option{WORKERS_IN_OUTPUT}, $option{SEQ_NUM}, $option{CHECK_RECORD_COUNT});

 mydie "Could not add delivery $DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME\n" if (! defined($created_file));

	$FILES_CREATED++;

	my ($vol, $dir, $file) = File::Spec->splitpath($DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME);
	my $msg;

	if ($created_file) {
		$msg = "Created file $file .";
	} else {
		$msg = "Concatenated output for ${post_date} .";
	}

	$msg .= " Output records = $total_records." if (defined($total_records));
	$msg .= " Input records = $total_input_records." if ($total_input_records != $total_records);

	$JOB->log(event_code => 'CCSUCCESS', log_type => 'INFO', message => $msg, email_subject => 'file concatenation successful', post_date => $post_date) || mydie "Cannot write to log file $LOGFILE: $@";

	$OUTPUT_FILE_OPEN = 0;
	$DELIVERABLE_OUTFILE_NAME = undef;
}


sub my_size($) {
  my $worker = shift;

	my $fname = $worker->output_fname;

	return -s $fname if (defined($fname));
	return 0;
}

sub already_concatenating($) {
	my $no_mutex = shift;

	return 0 if ($no_mutex);

	my $concat_minutes = $JOB->concatenation_minutes;

	if (defined($concat_minutes)) {
		my $log_type;

		if (defined($JOB->max_concat_time_min) && ($concat_minutes > $JOB->max_concat_time_min)) {
			$log_type = 'ERROR';
		} elsif (defined($JOB->alert_concat_time_min) && ($concat_minutes > $JOB->alert_concat_time_min)) {
			$log_type = 'WARN';
		} else {
			$log_type = 'DEBUG';
		}

		$JOB->log(email_subject => 'skipped concatenation', log_type => $log_type, event_code => 'CCSKIP', message => sprintf("A file concatenation attempt for $APP_ID was skipped because another process for this application may still be concatenating (for %.2f minutes and counting). If concatenation is not actually being performed, then the CONCAT_BEGIN_TIME column of the JOB_CONFIG table will need to be reset to NULL for this application before any new concatenation can take place.", $concat_minutes));

		return 1;
	}

	return 0;
}

# # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # #
############# MAIN ###########

$APP_ID = 'UNKNOWN';
my $exit_success = $DEFAULT_EXIT_SUCCESS;
my $logging_level = 'INFO';
my $check_only = 0;
my $concat_interval_hours;	# number of hours required between actual concatenation activity
my $group_id;

# setup signal handler so we can cleanup before getting interrupted

foreach my $sig (&std_abort_signals) {
  if ((! defined($SIG{$sig})) || ($SIG{$sig} ne 'IGNORE')) {
    $SIG{$sig} = \&sig_handler;
  }
}


if (scalar(@ARGV) == 0) {
  Usage;
  exit(1);
}

# Get command-line options

my $log_to_screen = -t 1;

my @args = @ARGV;
my @exclude_app = ();
my $no_max_records_check;
my $span_post_dates;
my $no_mutex = 0;
my $keep_log = 0;
my ($data_source_format, $all_or_none, $any, $config_group_id);

GetOptions(
	'all-or-none'             => \$all_or_none,
	'any'                     => \$any,
	'app-dir=s'               => \$APP_DIR_TOP,
	'app-id=s'                => \$APP_ID,
	'check-only'              => \$check_only,
	'config-group-id=s'       => \$config_group_id,
	'default-failure-email=s' => \$DEFAULT_FAILURE_EMAIL,
	'deliverable-dir=s'       => \$DELIVERABLE_DIR,
	'ds-format=s'             => \$data_source_format,
	'exclude-app=s@'          => \@exclude_app,
	'exit=s'                  => \$exit_success,
	'failure-email=s'         => \$FAILURE_EMAIL,
	'group-id=s'              => \$group_id,
	'keep-log'                => \$keep_log,
	'keep-worker-files'       => \$KEEP_WORKER_FILES,
	'log-to-screen'           => \$log_to_screen,
	'logging-level=s'         => \$logging_level,
	'mark-delivered'          => \$MARK_DELIVERED,
	'no-max-records-check'    => \$no_max_records_check,
	'no-mutex'                => \$no_mutex,
	'post-date=s'             => \$POST_DATE,
	'request-id=i'            => \$REQUEST_ID,
	'screen-only'             => \$SCREEN_ONLY,
	'span-post-dates'         => \$span_post_dates,
	'success-email=s'         => \$SUCCESS_EMAIL,
	) || exit(1);

my $check_record_count = defined($no_max_records_check) ? 0 : 1;
$log_to_screen = 1 if ($SCREEN_ONLY);

if (defined($group_id)) {
	if ($APP_ID ne 'UNKNOWN') {
		mydie "ERROR: The parameters '-app-id' and '-group-id' cannot be used together!\n";
	}

	if (defined($config_group_id)) {
		mydie "ERROR: -config-group-id cannot be used with -group-id!\n";
	}

	if (defined($REQUEST_ID)) {
		mydie "ERROR: -group-id cannot be used with -request-id!\n";
	}

	my @job_list = BLUELITE::Job->new(GROUP_ID => $group_id, dbh_caching => 1, is_concatenator => 1, log_to_screen => $log_to_screen);

	if ( ! defined($job_list[0]) ) {
		mydie "ERROR: Unable to obtain a BLUELITE::Job object for GROUP_ID = '$group_id' : $@\n";
	}

	my (@common_args, @run_args);

	for(my $i = 0; $i <= $#args; $i++) {
		if ($args[$i] =~ /^[^a-z]*group-id\s*$/i) {
			$i++;
			next;
		}

		push(@common_args, $args[$i]);
	}

	my $exclude_apps = {};
	map { $exclude_apps->{$_} = undef } @exclude_app;

	my $exit_code = 0;

	foreach my $job (@job_list) {

		my $app_id = $job->app_id;

		next if (defined($exclude_apps) && exists($exclude_apps->{$app_id}));

		my $ret = system($pgm, '-app-id' => $job->app_id, @common_args);
		$ret = $ret >> 8;

		$exit_code = $exit_code | $ret;
	}

	exit($exit_code);
}

mydie "ERROR: -app-id or -group-id must be specified!\n" if ($APP_ID eq 'UNKNOWN');
mydie "ERROR: The -post-date option must be specified when using the -no-mutex option!\n" if ($no_mutex && ! defined($POST_DATE));
mydie "ERROR: The -post-date option must be specified when using the -request-id option!\n" if ($REQUEST_ID && ! defined($POST_DATE));

my $post_date_txt = $POST_DATE;

if (defined($post_date_txt)) {
	$post_date_txt =~ s/,/_/g;
	$post_date_txt .= '.';
} else {
	$post_date_txt = '';
}

$LOGFILE = "concat.${APP_ID}.${post_date_txt}$$.log";

my @job_constructor_opts = (app_id => $APP_ID, disconnect_on_destroy => 0);

push(@job_constructor_opts, logfile => $LOGFILE) if (! $SCREEN_ONLY);
push(@job_constructor_opts, log_to_screen => $log_to_screen);
push(@job_constructor_opts, logging_level => $logging_level) if (defined($logging_level));
push(@job_constructor_opts, config_group_id => $config_group_id) if (defined($config_group_id));
push(@job_constructor_opts, request_id => $REQUEST_ID) if (defined($REQUEST_ID));

$JOB = BLUELITE::Job->new(@job_constructor_opts) || mydie "Unable to obtain BLUELITE::Job object for app_id = '$APP_ID' : $@\n";

# maximum number of records per deliverable file, defined in job_config table
$MAX_CONCAT_INPUT_TXNS = $JOB->max_concat_input_txns;

my $output_scope = $JOB->output_scope;

# use "span post dates" mechanism to support output_scope=all config
if ((! defined($span_post_dates)) && ($output_scope eq 'ALL')) {
	$span_post_dates = 1;
}

if (! defined($span_post_dates)) {
	$span_post_dates = 0;
}

# default to all-or-none if span-post-dates requested
if ($span_post_dates && ! defined($all_or_none)) {
	$all_or_none = 1;
}

mydie "ERROR: The -post-date option must be specified when using the -span-post-dates option!\n" if ($span_post_dates && ! defined($POST_DATE));

$all_or_none = 0 if (defined($any));

$LOGFILE = $JOB->logfile;

$APP_DIR_TOP = $JOB->app_dir if (! defined($APP_DIR_TOP));
$BIN_DIR = "$APP_DIR_TOP/bin";

mydie "ERROR: The mandatory -app-dir parameter was not specified and is not set in the JOB_CONFIG table!\n" if (! defined($APP_DIR_TOP));
mydie "ERROR: Application directory $APP_DIR_TOP does not exist!\n" if (! -e $APP_DIR_TOP);

if (! defined($DELIVERABLE_DIR)) {
	$DELIVERABLE_DIR = $JOB->deliv_dir;
}

if ((! -e $DELIVERABLE_DIR) && ! mkpath $DELIVERABLE_DIR) {
	mydie "ERROR: Cannot create output directory $DELIVERABLE_DIR : $!\n";
}

mydie "ERROR: Deliverables directory $DELIVERABLE_DIR does not exist!\n" if (! -e $DELIVERABLE_DIR);
mydie "ERROR: Cannot write to deliverable directory $DELIVERABLE_DIR\n" if (! -w $DELIVERABLE_DIR);

foreach my $tmp_dir ($ENV{TMPDIR}, $ENV{TEMPDIR}, $ENV{TMP}, $ENV{TEMP}, '/temp', '/tmp') {
	next if (! defined($tmp_dir));

	my $t_dir = $tmp_dir;
	$t_dir =~ s/\/$//;

	if ((-d $t_dir) && (-w $t_dir)) {
		$TEMP_OUTPUT_DIR = $t_dir;
		last;
	}
}

if (! defined($TEMP_OUTPUT_DIR)) {
	$TEMP_OUTPUT_DIR = "$DELIVERABLE_DIR/temp";
}

if (! -d $TEMP_OUTPUT_DIR) {
	if (! mkdir $TEMP_OUTPUT_DIR) {
		mydie "ERROR: Cannot temp directory $TEMP_OUTPUT_DIR : $!\n";
	}
}

if (! -w $TEMP_OUTPUT_DIR) {
		mydie "ERROR: No write permission for temp directory $TEMP_OUTPUT_DIR\n";
}

eval '$LOGGER = $JOB->logger' || mydie "Cannot get logger: $@";

# setup default failure/success email addresses
$FAILURE_EMAIL = $JOB->failure_email if (! defined($FAILURE_EMAIL));
$SUCCESS_EMAIL = $JOB->success_email if (! defined($SUCCESS_EMAIL));

$HEADER = $JOB->header_name;
$TRAILER = $JOB->trailer_name;

if (defined($HEADER)) {
	if ($HEADER =~ /^$APP_ID/ ) {
		$custom_header = 1;
	} elsif ((length($HEADER) > 0) && ($HEADER !~ /^(std|standard)/i)) {
		mydie "ERROR: header name in job_config table is '$HEADER', which is not supported. It must begin with '$APP_ID' for a custom header, or can be NULL or 'STANDARD' for the standard header\n";
	}
}

if (defined($TRAILER)) {
	if ($TRAILER =~ /^$APP_ID/ ) {
		$custom_trailer = 1;
	} elsif ((length($TRAILER) > 0) && ($TRAILER !~ /^(std|standard)/i)) {
		mydie "ERROR: trailer name in job_config table is '$TRAILER', which is not supported. It must begin with '$APP_ID' for a custom trailer, or can be NULL or 'STANDARD' for the standard trailer\n";
	}
}

if ( ($custom_header) || ($custom_trailer) ) {
    my $HEADER_TRAILER_FILE = $APP_DIR_TOP . "/bin/" . lc($APP_ID) . "_header_trailer.pl";
    mydie "ERROR: Header Trailer script $HEADER_TRAILER_FILE does not exist!\n" if (! -e $HEADER_TRAILER_FILE);
    require $HEADER_TRAILER_FILE;
}

my ($seconds_since_last_creation, $hours_since_last_creation);
my $current_time = DateTime->now(time_zone => 'local');

if (already_concatenating($no_mutex)) {
	myexit($exit_success);
}

if (! $no_mutex) {
	if ($JOB->concat_begin) {
		$CONCATENATING = 1;
	} else {
		$JOB->log(message => "A file concatenation attempt for $APP_ID was skipped because another concatenation process for this application attempted to start at the same time as this one.", log_type => 'DEBUG', email_subject => 'skipped concatenation', event_code => 'CCSKIP');
		myexit($exit_success);
	}
}

my $last_creation_time = $JOB->last_creation_datetime;

if (defined($last_creation_time)) {
	$LOGGER->info("Last concatenation time for $APP_ID = $last_creation_time");
	$seconds_since_last_creation = ($current_time->subtract_datetime_absolute($last_creation_time))->seconds;
	$hours_since_last_creation = sprintf('%.2f', $seconds_since_last_creation / 3600);
	$LOGGER->info("It has been $hours_since_last_creation hours since the last concatenation.");
}

######

eval { $TODAY_DATE = DateTime->now(time_zone => 'local')->strftime('%Y%m%d'); };

if ($@) {
	mydie "Could not obtain today's date via DateTime module\n";
}

my @ready_opts = ();
my ($POST_DATES, $post_date_spec, %requested_post_dates);

if (defined($POST_DATE)) {
	$POST_DATE = uc($POST_DATE);

	if ($POST_DATE eq 'PRIOR') {

	} else {

		my $post_date_list = BLUELITE::Job->post_date_list($POST_DATE);
		mydie "ERROR: Could not decipher post date of '$POST_DATE'\n" if (! defined($post_date_list));

		$POST_DATES = { map { $_ => undef } @{$post_date_list}};
		push(@ready_opts, post_date => $post_date_list);

		$post_date_spec = $JOB->format_post_date_spec($POST_DATE);
		%requested_post_dates = map { $_ => undef } @{$post_date_list};
	}
}

if (defined($REQUEST_ID)) {
	push(@ready_opts, request_id => $REQUEST_ID);
}

$JOB->data_source_format($data_source_format) if (defined($data_source_format));

my @workers = $JOB->ready_to_deliver(@ready_opts);	# returns list of worker objects

if (scalar(@workers) == 0) {
	# no new files to concatenate
	my $msg = "No workers need to be concatenated";
	$msg .= " for $POST_DATE" if (defined($POST_DATE));
	$msg .= '.';

	$LOGGER->info($msg);
	myexit($exit_success)
}

# organize workers by post date in a data structure
my ($post_date_worker, $post_date);

foreach my $worker (@workers) {
	$post_date = $worker->post_date;
	$LOGGER->info("Post date $post_date is ready for concatenation.") if ($check_only && ! exists($post_date_worker->{$post_date}));
	push(@{$post_date_worker->{$post_date}}, $worker);
};

if ($all_or_none && scalar(%requested_post_dates)) {
	my @post_dates_not_ready = grep {! exists($post_date_worker->{$_})} keys %requested_post_dates;

	if (@post_dates_not_ready) {
		$LOGGER->warn("The -all-or-none option is in effect for post date $POST_DATE, but the following post dates were either previously concatenated or are not yet ready to be concatenated: " . join(' ', sort @post_dates_not_ready) . "\nNothing was concatenated.");
		myexit($exit_success);
	}
}

myexit($exit_success) if ($check_only);

#if (! $no_mutex) {
#print "debug: CONCAT begin time = " . `date` . "\n";
#	if ($JOB->concat_begin) {
#		$CONCATENATING = 1;
#	} else {
#		$JOB->log(message => "A file concatenation attempt for $APP_ID was skipped because another concatenation process for this application attempted to start at the same time as this one.", log_type => 'DEBUG', email_subject => 'skipped concatenation', event_code => 'CCSKIP');
#		myexit($exit_success);
#	}
#}

# for each post date, concatenate all worker output files into one deliverable file

my ($total_records, $total_txns, $records_added, @workers_in_output, @missing_files, $txns_processed, @skipped_workers, $file_info);
my $record_terminator = $JOB->concat_record_terminator;

if (! defined($record_terminator)) {
	mydie "Could not determine which record terminator to use. Check CONCAT_RECORD_TERMINATOR field in JOB_CONFIG table.\n";
}

foreach my $post_date (sort keys %{$post_date_worker}) {
	if (defined($POST_DATE)) {
		if ($POST_DATE eq 'PRIOR') {
			next if ($post_date ge $TODAY_DATE);
		} elsif (! exists($POST_DATES->{$post_date})) {
			next;
		}
	}

	if (@missing_files = grep {defined($_->output_fname) && ! -f $_->output_fname} @{$post_date_worker->{$post_date}}) {
		$JOB->log(log_type => 'ERROR', event_code => 'CCFAIL', email_subject => 'Missing worker files', message => "Could not concatenate post date $post_date because the following worker files are missing:\n" . join("\n", map { $_->output_fname } @missing_files) . "\n");
		mydie("Missing worker files!\n");
		exit(1);
	}

	# "main" concat loop
	do {
		
		if (scalar(@skipped_workers) >= 1) {
			@{$post_date_worker->{$post_date}} = @skipped_workers;
		}
		@skipped_workers = ();
		my $worker_num = 0;

		if (! $OUTPUT_FILE_OPEN) {
			$total_records = 0;
			$total_txns = undef;
			@workers_in_output = ();
			$file_info = start_output_file(
				post_date => $post_date,
				post_date_spec => $post_date_spec,
				span_post_dates => $span_post_dates
				);
		}

		# iterate over workers (sort by file size)
		foreach my $worker (sort { my_size($a) <=> my_size($b) } @{$post_date_worker->{$post_date}}) {

			$worker_num++;
			$txns_processed = $worker->txn_processed; # number of txns in worker

			# skip workers if we are past max number of records allowed
			if (defined($MAX_CONCAT_INPUT_TXNS)) {
				
				if (defined($txns_processed)) {
					no warnings 'uninitialized';

					# if number of txns concatted thus far, plus txns that WOULD
					# be concatted from this worker would exceeed the threshold,
					# skip this worker (and probably all subsequent)
					if (
							($total_txns + $txns_processed > $MAX_CONCAT_INPUT_TXNS) &&
							($worker_num != 1)
						) {

						$LOGGER->warn("Skipping worker " . $worker->worker_id . " containing $txns_processed txns due to max_concat_input_txns setting of $MAX_CONCAT_INPUT_TXNS");
						push(@skipped_workers, $worker);
						next;

					}
	
				} else {
					mydie "ERROR: max_concat_input_txns is set to $MAX_CONCAT_INPUT_TXNS , but txn_processed() returns NULL for worker ID " . $worker->worker_id . "\n";
				}

			}
			
			$records_added = concat(
				$worker->output_fname,
				$record_terminator,
				$file_info->{temp_stderr_fname}
				);
			
			if (! defined($records_added)) {
				mydie "ERROR: Could not append $worker to " . $file_info->{fname_temp} . " : $! , $GzipError\n";
			}

			$total_records += $records_added;
			$total_txns += $txns_processed if (defined($txns_processed));

			push(@workers_in_output, $worker);
		}

		if (@skipped_workers || ! $span_post_dates) {
			finish_output_file(
				fname_temp => $file_info->{fname_temp},
				temp_stderr_fname => $file_info->{temp_stderr_fname},
				total_records => $total_records,
				post_date => $post_date,
				post_date_spec => $post_date_spec,
				seq_num => $file_info->{seq_num},
				check_record_count => $check_record_count,
				total_txns => $total_txns,
				workers_in_output => \@workers_in_output,
				span_post_dates => $span_post_dates
			);
		}

	} until (scalar(@skipped_workers) == 0);
}


if ($OUTPUT_FILE_OPEN) {
	finish_output_file(
		fname_temp => $file_info->{fname_temp},
		temp_stderr_fname => $file_info->{temp_stderr_fname},
		total_records => $total_records,
		post_date => $post_date,
		post_date_spec => $post_date_spec,
		seq_num => $file_info->{seq_num},
		check_record_count => $check_record_count,
		total_txns => $total_txns,
		workers_in_output => \@workers_in_output,
		span_post_dates => $span_post_dates
	);
}

$LOGGER->info("Completed concatenation process.") || mydie "Cannot write to log file $LOGFILE: $@";

unlink($LOGFILE) if ((! $keep_log) && (! $SCREEN_ONLY) && -f $LOGFILE);
myexit($exit_success);

END {
	if (defined($JOB) && $CONCATENATING) {
		$CONCATENATING = 0;
		$JOB->concat_end;
	}
}


#job_concat_post_date

echo "ERROR: The job_concat_post_date script is no longer supported! Please use the 'job_concat' script instead." >&2

exit 1


#job_config
#!/usr/bin/perl

# job_config: Basic command-line interface to updating the config table associated with the BLUELITE::Job module
# Author: J Hess, RelayHealth
#
# Version 1.0 - 5/25/2011
# - Initial release
#
# Version 4.7 - 12/6/2012
# - config values displayed in sorted order
# - no longer display parameters with empty config values
#
# Version 5.0 - 3/5/2014
# - Added -no-email command-line option
#
# Version 6.0 - 10/31/2014
# - Added support for "autohoc" requests (i.e. automated on-demand ad-hoc processing).
#

use BLUELITE::Job;
use Data::Dumper;
use strict;
use warnings;
use List::Util qw(max);

our $PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s/.*\///g;

our $REQUEST_ID;

sub Usage {
	print "$PGM: Update or view config settings for various applications or application groups

Usage 1: $PGM [-options] -app-id app_id     column1=value1 [column2=value2] ...
Usage 2: $PGM [-options] -group-id group_id column1=value1 [column2=value2] ...
Usage 3: $PGM [-options] -app-id app_id     {view-only}

Options:
 -no-email
 -request-id #

Note: As a safeguard, certain columns are not supported\n";
}


sub show_config(@) {

	my @opts = ();
	push(@opts, request_id => $REQUEST_ID) if (defined($REQUEST_ID));

	foreach my $app_id (@_) {

		print "\nConfiguration for app_id '$app_id':\n\n";

		my $job = BLUELITE::Job->new(app_id => $app_id, @opts) || die;
		my $config = $job->get_config;

		my $max_length = max(map { length($_) } keys %{$config});

		foreach my $attribute_name (sort keys %{$config}) {
			my $value = $config->{$attribute_name};
			next if ((! defined($value)) || ($value =~ /^\s*$/));

			# translate end-of-line characters to something displayable
			$value =~ s/\r/\\r/g;
			$value =~ s/\n/\\n/g;

			printf("%-${max_length}s : %s\n", $attribute_name, $value);
		}
	}

}


if (! @ARGV) {
	Usage;
	exit(1);
}

use Getopt::Long;

my @app_id = ();
my @group_id = ();
my $post_date;
my $no_email = 0;

GetOptions(
            'app-id=s@' => \@app_id,
            'group-id=s@' => \@group_id,
            'no-email' => \$no_email,
            'request-id=i' => \$REQUEST_ID
) || exit(1);

if (! @app_id && ! @group_id) {
	print STDERR "ERROR: Neither -app-id or -group-id parameter not provided!\n\n";
	Usage;
	exit(1);
}

if (! @ARGV) {

	if (@group_id) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: Must provide assignments when using the -group-id parameter!\n\n";
		Usage;
		exit(1);
	}

	show_config(@app_id);
	exit(0);
}




my @update_opts = ();

push(@update_opts, app_id => [split(/\s*,\s*/, join(',', @app_id))]) if (@app_id);
push(@update_opts, group_id => [split(/\s*,\s*/, join(',', @group_id))]) if (@group_id);
push(@update_opts, request_id => $REQUEST_ID) if (defined($REQUEST_ID));


my %assigns = ();

foreach my $assignment (@ARGV) {
	if ($assignment =~ /^\s*([^=]+)=(.*)$/) {
		$assigns{"$1"} = $2;
	} else {
		print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: assignment '$assignment' does not conform to 'column=value' syntax\n\n";
		Usage;
		exit(1);
	}
}

my $update_result = BLUELITE::Job->update_job_config(@update_opts, assignments => \%assigns);

if (! exists($update_result->{rows})) {
	BLUELITE::Job->rollback;

	if (exists($update_result->{error})) {
		print STDERR "The following error occurred: " . $update_result->{error} . "\n";
	} else {
		print STDERR "Could not determine # of rows updated or retrieve an error message\n";
	}

	die "Nothing was updated!\n";
}

if (exists($update_result->{error}) && defined($update_result->{error}) && length($update_result->{error}) > 0) {
	BLUELITE::Job->rollback;

	print STDERR "The following error occurred: " . $update_result->{error} . "\n";
	die "Nothing was updated!\n";
}

my $rows = $update_result->{rows};

if ($rows <= 0) {
	die "ERROR: Could not find any rows to update!\n";
}

my $app_id = $update_result->{app_id};

print "This will update the following $rows APP_IDs in the config table:\n\n" . join("\n", @{$app_id}) . "\n\nProceed with update (y/N) ? : ";

my $response = <STDIN>;

if ($response !~ /^\s*(y|yes)\s*$/i) {
	BLUELITE::Job->rollback;
	print "Did not attempt to update anything\n";
	exit(1);
}

my $job;
my @emails = ();

my @opts;

if (defined($REQUEST_ID)) {
	push(@opts, request_id => $REQUEST_ID);
}

foreach my $app (@{$app_id}) {
	$job = BLUELITE::Job->new(app_id => $app, @opts);
	my $message = "Made the following update to the config table: " . join(', ', map { "$_ = $assigns{$_}" } keys %assigns);
	$job->log(event_code => 'JCU', log_type => 'DEBUG', to_table => 1, message => $message, commit => 0, dbh_caching => 1);
	push(@emails, $job->warning_email) if (defined($job->warning_email));
}

BLUELITE::Job->commit;
$job->log_dbh->commit; # committing 1 commits them ($job->log calls) all since dbh_caching was used

my $message = "Warning: The following $rows APP_IDs in the config table were updated:\n\n" . join("\n", @{$app_id});

if (defined($REQUEST_ID)) {
	$message .= " (request ID $REQUEST_ID)";
}

$message .= "\n\nThe updates were:\n\n" . join(', ', map { "$_ = $assigns{$_}" } keys %assigns);

BLUELITE::Job->email(
	to => BLUELITE::Job->email_addresses(@emails),
	subject => "WARN: Updated config table / " . $job->env,
	msg => $message
) if (scalar(@emails) && ! $no_email);

print $message . "\n";


#job_delivery_update
#!/usr/bin/perl

# job_delivery_update: Mark BLUELITE::Job deliverable as having been "delivered" (transmitted) to client
#
# Author(s): John Hess, RelayHealth
#
# Version history:
# Version 1.0 - 9/18/2007
#
# Version 6.0 - 10/31/2014
# - Added support for "autohoc" requests (i.e. automated on-demand ad-hoc processing).
#
# Version 6.2 - 5/22/2015
# - Added -suffix command line option (e.g. to find feed_20150325.txt when given feed_20150325.txt.pgp with -source-app-id)
#

use BLUELITE::Job;
use BLUELITE::Logger;
use Getopt::Long;
use DateTime;
use DateTime::Duration;

use warnings;
use strict;

our $PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s/.*\///g;

our $FAILURE_EMAIL;
our $SMTP_SERVER = $ENV{DEFAULT_SMTP_SERVER};


our $DS_BASE_DIR = $ENV{DS_BASE_DIR};
die "ERROR: environment variable DS_BASE_DIR not set!\n" if ((! defined($DS_BASE_DIR)) || (length($DS_BASE_DIR) == 0));
die "ERROR: environment variable DS_BASE_DIR points to $DS_BASE_DIR, which does not exist!\n" if (! -d $DS_BASE_DIR);

our $REMOVE_LOG_ON_SUCCESS = 1;
our ($LOGFILE, $APP_ID, $SOURCE_APP_ID);


sub email(%) {
  my %option = @_;

  my $mail = new Mail::SendEasy( smtp => $SMTP_SERVER);

  my $logger = get_logger;

  if (! defined($mail) ) {
    $logger->warn("Unable to establish a SMTP connection to $SMTP_SERVER. Cannot send email.");
    return undef;
  }

  if (exists($option{msg}) && ! exists($option{html})) {
    $option{html} = $option{msg};
    $option{html} =~ s/\n/<br>/g;
  }

  my $status = $mail->send(
    from => 'dataservicesnotification@relayhealth.com',
    from_title => 'RelayHealth Data Services',
    %option
  );

  if (! $status) {
    $logger->warn($mail->error);
    return undef;
  }

  return 1;
}



sub mydie(;$) {
  my $message = shift;
  my $exit_code;

  if (defined($message)) {
  	chomp($message);
		$message .= "\n\nSee logfile $LOGFILE for more details.\n" if (defined($LOGFILE));
	}

 	my $logger = get_logger;
	$logger->error($message);

  if (defined($FAILURE_EMAIL)) {
		$logger->info("Sending email to $FAILURE_EMAIL");

    email(
      to => $FAILURE_EMAIL,
      subject => "$APP_ID delivery update process FAILED",
      msg => $message
    );
  }

  exit(1);
}


sub Usage() {
	print STDOUT "Usage 1: $PGM -app-id a [options] filename\n";
	print STDOUT "Usage 2: $PGM -source-app-id a [options] filename\n";
	print STDOUT "Options:\n";
	print STDOUT "   -destination-host hostname\n";
	print STDOUT "   -log-dir dir\n";
	print STDOUT "   -keep-log\n";
	print STDOUT "   -logging-level level           (DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR, FATAL)\n";
	print STDOUT "   -smtp-server smtp\n";
}


################ MAIN ##############

if (scalar(@ARGV) == 0) {
        Usage;
        exit(1);
}

my ($destination_host, $keep_log, $log_dir, $suffix);
my $logging_level = 'INFO';

my $ret = GetOptions(
											'app-id=s' => \$APP_ID,
											'source-app-id=s' => \$SOURCE_APP_ID,
											'destination-host=s' => \$destination_host,
											'keep-log' => \$keep_log,
											'logging-level=s' => \$logging_level,
											'failure-email=s' => \$FAILURE_EMAIL,
											'smtp-server=s' => \$SMTP_SERVER,
											'log-dir=s' => \$log_dir,
											'suffix=s' => \$suffix

);

die "$PGM: ERROR: Invalid options\n" if (! $ret);

my $fname = $ARGV[0];

die "Mandatory -app-id or -source-app-id parameter not specified!" if (! (defined($APP_ID) || defined($SOURCE_APP_ID)));
die "Cannot use -app-id and -source-app-id parameters together!" if (defined($APP_ID) && defined($SOURCE_APP_ID));

if (defined($SOURCE_APP_ID)) {
	$APP_ID = $SOURCE_APP_ID;
}

die "app-id cannot be empty" if (length($APP_ID) == 0);

# Set the options for logger

$REMOVE_LOG_ON_SUCCESS = 0 if (defined($keep_log));
my @screen_options;
my $screen_logging = 0;

if (-t 1) {
  @screen_options = (screen_threshold => $logging_level);
	$screen_logging = 1;
} else {
  @screen_options = (screen_threshold => 'OFF');
}

my @file_options = ();

if (defined($log_dir)) {
	if (-d $log_dir) {
		my $outfile_suffix = $fname;

		$outfile_suffix =~ s/.*\///g;
		$outfile_suffix =~ s/[.].*$//g;

		$LOGFILE = $log_dir . "/${APP_ID}_delivery_update." . $outfile_suffix . '.log';
		@file_options = (file_threshold => $logging_level, logfile => $LOGFILE);
	} else {
		die "Log directory $log_dir does not exist!\n";
	}
} else {
	@file_options = (screen_only => 1) if ($screen_logging);
}

initialize_logging(@screen_options, @file_options);

my $logger = get_logger;

{
	no warnings;


	if (length($ARGV[0]) == 0) {
		print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Filename not provided\n";
		Usage;
		exit(1);
	}
}


mydie "Delivery file $fname does not exist!" if (! -f $fname);

my (@job_opts, $request_id);


if (defined($SOURCE_APP_ID)) {
	my $search_fname = $fname;

	if (defined($suffix)) {
		$suffix =~ s/^\.//;  # remove leading "." from suffix
		$suffix = quotemeta($suffix);  # escape non-"word" characters (e.g. ".")
		$search_fname =~ s/\.${suffix}$//;  # remove suffix from filename
	}

	my $select = "
			select q.rq_request_id
			from job_queue q, job_delivery d
			where q.rq_source_app_id = '$SOURCE_APP_ID'
				and q.app_id = d.app_id
				and d.delivery_output_file = '$search_fname'
			order by creation_date desc";

	my @request_id = BLUELITE::Job->dbh->selectrow_array($select);

	if (! @request_id) {
		mydie "Could not determine request ID for app_id = '$SOURCE_APP_ID', filename '$fname'";
	}

	$request_id = $request_id[0];
	push(@job_opts, app_id => $SOURCE_APP_ID, request_id => $request_id);
} else {
	push(@job_opts, app_id => $APP_ID);
}

my $job;
eval { $job = BLUELITE::Job->new(@job_opts) };

if (! defined($job)) {
	my $message = "Unable to obtain a BLUELITE::Job object for app_id = '$APP_ID', filename = '$fname'";
	$message .= ", request ID '$request_id'";
	mydie $message . "\n";
}

$FAILURE_EMAIL = $job->failure_email if (! defined($FAILURE_EMAIL));

my @opts = ();
my $destination_message = '';

if (defined($destination_host)) {
	push(@opts, destination_host => $destination_host);
	$destination_message = "Destination host = '$destination_host'";
}

if (defined($suffix)) {
	push(@opts, suffix => $suffix);
}

$APP_ID = $job->app_id;

if (! $job->update_delivery_date(fname => $fname, @opts)) {
	mydie "Unable to update delivery date in JOB_DELIVERY table for app_id = '$APP_ID' and filename = '$fname'";
}

$logger->info("Successfully updated $APP_ID delivery info for $fname . $destination_message");

unlink($LOGFILE) if ($REMOVE_LOG_ON_SUCCESS && defined($LOGFILE));

exit(0);


#job_enqueue_files
#!/usr/bin/perl

# Program: job_enqueue_files
# Purpose: move validated files from temporary location to dest dir to queue for transfer to destination
#

use strict;
use warnings;

use Data::Dumper;
use BLUELITE::Job;
use Getopt::Long;
use File::Spec;
use File::Basename;
use File::Copy;

use warnings;
use strict;

my @dir_parts = File::Spec->splitdir(File::Spec->rel2abs($0));
our $PGM = pop(@dir_parts);

sub Usage() {
  print "$PGM: Move validated files from temp dir to dest dir to queue for transfer to customer\n";
  print "\n";
  print "Usage: $PGM -app-id a -request-id # [filename ...]\n";
}


sub post_date_sql($$) {
  my ($post_date_spec, $alias) = @_;

	my $post_dates = BLUELITE::Job->post_date_list($post_date_spec);
	return "${alias}.post_date = '" . join("' or ${alias}.post_date = '", @{$post_dates}) . "'";
}


sub verify_files($@) {
  my ($job, @files_to_verify) = @_;

	my $app_id = $job->app_id;
	my $post_date_spec = $job->{RQ_POST_DATE};

	if (! defined($post_date_spec)) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: Could not determine rq_post_date for this request\n";
		return ();
	}

	my $post_date_sql = post_date_sql($post_date_spec, 'w');

	my $files_in_delivery_table = $job->dbh->selectall_hashref("
		select distinct delivery_output_file
		from job_delivery d, job_worker w
		where w.app_id = '$app_id' and d.app_id = w.app_id and ($post_date_sql)", 'DELIVERY_OUTPUT_FILE');

	my @does_not_exist = ();
	my @verified_files = ();
	my @not_in_delivery_table = ();

	foreach my $verify_filename (@files_to_verify) {
		my $verify_filename_full = File::Spec->rel2abs($verify_filename, $ENV{PWD});

		if (! -f $verify_filename_full) {
			push(@does_not_exist, $verify_filename_full);
			next;
		}

		if (exists($files_in_delivery_table->{$verify_filename_full})) {
			push(@verified_files, $verify_filename_full);
		} else {
			push(@not_in_delivery_table, $verify_filename_full);
		}
	}

	if (@does_not_exist) {
		die "$PGM: ERROR: The following files do not exist!\n" . join("\n", @does_not_exist) . "\n";
	}

	if (@not_in_delivery_table) {
		die "$PGM: ERROR: The following files could not be found in the job_delivery table!\n" . join("\n", @not_in_delivery_table) . "\n";
	}

	return @verified_files;
}


sub get_all_files($) {
	my $job = shift;

	my $app_id = $job->app_id;
	my $post_date_spec = $job->{RQ_POST_DATE};

	if (! defined($post_date_spec)) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: Could not determine rq_post_date for this request\n";
		return ();
	}

	my $post_dates = BLUELITE::Job->post_date_list($post_date_spec);

	if (! @{$post_dates}) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: Could not get a list of post dates for $post_date_spec\n";
		return ();
	}

	my $post_date_sql = post_date_sql($post_date_spec, 'w');
	
	my $files = $job->dbh->selectall_arrayref("
		select distinct
			d.delivery_output_file,
			d.delivery_date,
			w.post_date
		from job_delivery d, job_worker w
		where w.app_id = '$app_id' and w.app_id = d.app_id and w.delivery_file_id = d.delivery_file_id and ($post_date_sql)", { Slice => {} });

	my %file_list = ();
	my %post_dates_found = ();

	foreach my $row (@{$files}) {
		my $fname = $row->{DELIVERY_OUTPUT_FILE};
		$file_list{$fname} = $row->{DELIVERY_DATE};

		my $post_date = $row->{POST_DATE};
		$post_dates_found{$post_date}++;
	}

	my @post_dates_not_generated = ();
	my @dupe_post_dates = ();

	foreach my $post_date (@{$post_dates}) {
		if (! exists($post_dates_found{$post_date})) {
			push(@post_dates_not_generated, $post_date);
		} elsif ($post_dates_found{$post_date} > 1) {
			push(@dupe_post_dates, $post_date);
		}
	}

	if (@post_dates_not_generated) {
		die "$PGM: ERROR: The following post dates within $post_date_spec were not found in the job_worker/job_delivery table:\n" . join("\n", @post_dates_not_generated) . "\n";
	}

	if (@dupe_post_dates) {
		die "$PGM: ERROR: The following post dates within $post_date_spec are associated with more than one file in the job_delivery table:\n" . join("\n", @dupe_post_dates) . "\n";
	}

	my @to_enqueue = ();
	my @delivered_but_still_exists = ();
	my @does_not_exist = ();

	foreach my $fname (keys %file_list) {
		my $delivery_date = $file_list{$fname};

		if (defined($delivery_date)) {
			if ( -f $fname) {
				push(@delivered_but_still_exists, $fname);
			}

			next;
		}

		if (-f $fname) {
			push(@to_enqueue, $fname);
		} else {
			push(@does_not_exist, $fname);
		}
	}

	if (@delivered_but_still_exists) {
		die "$PGM: ERROR: The following files were delivered, but still exist:\n" . join("\n", @delivered_but_still_exists) . "\n";
	}

	if (@does_not_exist) {
		die "$PGM: ERROR: The following are missing:\n" . join("\n", @does_not_exist) . "\n";
	}

	return @to_enqueue;
}


sub update_job_delivery($$$) {
  my ($job, $curr_file, $new_file) = @_;
	my $app_id = $job->app_id;
	my $update_sql = "update job_delivery set delivery_output_file = '$new_file' where app_id = '$app_id' and delivery_output_file = '$curr_file'";

	my $rows = $job->dbh->do($update_sql);

	if ($rows != 1) {
		$job->dbh->rollback;
		die "$PGM: ERROR: The following update changed $rows rows instead of 1: $update_sql\n";
	}
}


### Main ###

my ($app_id, $request_id);

GetOptions(
            'app-id=s' => \$app_id,
            'request-id=i' => \$request_id,
) || exit(1);

if (! defined($app_id)) {
	print STDERR "$PGM: -app-id must be specified!\n";
  Usage;
  exit(1);
}

if (! defined($request_id)) {
	print STDERR "$PGM: -request-id must be specified!\n";
  Usage;
  exit(1);
}

if ($app_id =~ /^\s*$/) {
	print STDERR "$PGM: -app-id is '$app_id', which is not valid\n";
  Usage;
  exit(1);
}

if ($request_id !~ /^\s*\d+\s*$/) {
	print STDERR "$PGM: -request-id of '$request_id' is not valid. Must be a positive integer!\n";
  Usage;
  exit(1);
}

my $request_job;

eval { $request_job = BLUELITE::Job->new(app_id => $app_id, request_id => $request_id) } ;

if (! defined($request_job)) {
	die "$PGM: ERROR: Could not obtain a BLUELITE::Job object for app-id='$app_id', request-id='$request_id'\n";
}

my @file_list = ();

if (@ARGV) {
	@file_list = @ARGV;
	@file_list = verify_files($request_job, @file_list);
} else {
	@file_list = get_all_files($request_job);
}

if (! @file_list) {
	die "$PGM: No files found to enqueue!\n";
}

my $dest_job;

eval { $dest_job = BLUELITE::Job->new(app_id => $app_id) } ;

if (! defined($dest_job)) {
	die "$PGM: ERROR: Could not obtain a BLUELITE::Job object for app-id='$app_id'\n";
}

my $deliv_dir = $dest_job->rq_deliv_dir;

if (! defined($deliv_dir)) {
	die "$PGM: ERROR: Could not determine a destination directory to queue the files into!\n";
}

if (! -e $deliv_dir) {
	die "$PGM: ERROR: The destination directory '$deliv_dir' does not exist!\n";
}

if (! -w $deliv_dir) {
	die "$PGM: ERROR: No permission to write files to the destination directory '$deliv_dir' !\n";
}

my @already_exists = ();
my %filename_map = ();

foreach my $curr_file_full (@file_list) {
	my $curr_file_basename = basename($curr_file_full);
	my $new_file_full = "$deliv_dir/$curr_file_basename";

	if (-e $new_file_full) {
		push(@already_exists, $new_file_full);
	} else {
		$filename_map{$curr_file_full} = $new_file_full;
	}
}

if (@already_exists) {
	die "$PGM: ERROR: The following files already exist on the destination directory:\n\n" . join("\n", @already_exists) . "\n";
}

foreach my $curr_file_full (keys %filename_map) {
	update_job_delivery($request_job, $curr_file_full, $filename_map{$curr_file_full});
}

print "The following files will be moved:\n\n" . join("\n", @file_list) . "\n\n";

print "The above " . scalar(@file_list) . " files will be moved to the $deliv_dir directory, which will enqueue them for subsequent transfer to the final destination (i.e. customer site).\n\n";
print "ARE YOU SURE YOU WISH TO PROCEED (y/N) ? : ";

my $response = <STDIN>;

print "\n";

if ($response !~ /^\s*(y|yes)\s*$/i) {
	print "Did not attempt to move anything.\n";
	exit(1);
}

print "Moving files to $deliv_dir ..\n";

my %moved_files = ();

foreach my $curr_file_full (keys %filename_map) {
	my $new_file = $filename_map{$curr_file_full};

	if (move($curr_file_full, $new_file)) {
		$moved_files{$new_file} = $curr_file_full;
	} else {
		print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Could not move the file $curr_file_full to $new_file : $!\n";

		if (%moved_files) {
			print STDERR "Attempting to undo successful file moves.\n";
		}

		foreach my $moved_file (keys %moved_files) {
			if (! move($moved_file, $moved_files{$moved_file})) {
				print STDERR "WARNING: COULD NOT UNDO MOVE FROM " . $moved_files{$moved_file} . " TO $moved_file : $!\n";
			}
		}

		$request_job->rollback;
		exit(1);
	}
}

$request_job->commit;

print "Done\n";


#job_enqueue_request
#!/usr/bin/perl

# # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # #
#
# job_enqueue_request
#
# Read in a request file passed on the command line, validate and write the
# details of this request to the job_queue.  Largely uses BLUELITE::Job to
# interact with Oracle.
#
# 20141031 - Michael Carey <michael.carey@mckesson.com>
# Initial requirements gathering and development.
#
# 20150114 - Michael Carey <michael.carey@mckesson.com>
# Adding logic to generate an error if unrecognized name value pair are
# provided in the request file.  Also making minor fixes from first code review.
#
# 20140203 - Michael Carey <michael.carey@mckesson.com>
# Continuing minor fixes from first code review.
#
# 20150526 - Michael Carey <michael.carey@mckesson.com>, John Hess (john.hess2@relayhealth.com)
# Add support for new RQ_VALIDATE_CMD, for custom request validation hook.
# Make -app-id required command-line parameter.
#
# 20150701 - J Hess
# Allow the following parameters to be customized via config or custom validation:
#    deliverable_fname_sprintf
#    trigger_fname_sprintf
#    deliverable_fname_vars
#    trigger_fname_vars
# Allow only RECOGNIZED "a=b" setting (above) from custom validator.
#
# 20160421 - J Hess
# Add name of field when duplicate encountered
#
# # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # #

# TODO: remove this for production
#use lib '/ds/development/Job/dev/blib/lib';

use strict;
use warnings;
use IO::File;
use File::Spec;
use File::Copy;
use File::Path qw(mkpath);
use DateTime;
use Getopt::Long;
use BLUELITE::Common;
use BLUELITE::Logger;
use BLUELITE::Job;
use Data::Dumper;

STDOUT->autoflush(1);
STDERR->autoflush(1);

# if no command line parms are given, print usage and exit
if (scalar @ARGV == 0) {
	show_help();
	exit 0;
}

# a list of valid field names that can occur in a standard request.  an error is
# generated if anything other than the names listed below occur in a request.
my $VALNAMES = [
	'description',
	'app id',
	'post date',
	'reference id',
	'reset id',
	'resume id',
	'file scope',
	'requester email',
];

# command line arguments
my $group_id   = '';
our $APP_ID    = '';
my $nomove     = 0;
my $debug      = 0;
my $help       = 0;
my $opt_result = GetOptions(
	'group-id|group_id=s' => \$group_id,
	'app-id|app_id=s'     => \$APP_ID,
	'nomove'              => \$nomove,
	'debug'               => \$debug,
	'help|?'              => \$help,
	);

if ($help) {
	show_help();
	exit 0;
}

if (!$group_id) {
	show_help();
	print "ERROR: you must provide a group id on the command line.\n";
	exit 0;
}

if (!$APP_ID) {
	show_help();
	print "ERROR: you must provide a app id on the command line.\n";
	exit 0;
}

$APP_ID = uc($APP_ID);

# get request file passed in by filed from command line
my $REQ_PATHFILE = join( ' ', @ARGV );

# make sure a request file value was passed
if ( !defined $REQ_PATHFILE || !$REQ_PATHFILE ) {
	show_help();
	print "ERROR: you must provide a request file to process.\n";
	exit 0;
}

# initialize some important globals
my $APP_ENV     = init_pgm();                     # local function
my $logger      = $APP_ENV->{logger};             # lowercase pls
my $PGM         = $APP_ENV->{pgm_name};           # file name of pgm
my $REQ_SUCCDIR = $APP_ENV->{req_succdir};        # dir for parsed requests
my $REQ_FAILDIR = $APP_ENV->{req_faildir};        # dir for invalid requests
my $REQ_FILE    = $APP_ENV->{req_file};           # basename
my $ARC_TS      = $APP_ENV->{arc_ts};             # timestamp for archived files
my $EMAIL_DEFTO = 'dataservicesnotification@relayhealth.com';
my $GROUP_ID    = uc( trim($group_id) );          # from the command line,
                                                  # required, not validated.

if ( !-e $REQ_PATHFILE ) {
	abend_pgm("request file, $REQ_PATHFILE, does not exist");
}

if ( !-r $REQ_PATHFILE ) {
	abend_pgm("request file is not readable, $REQ_PATHFILE");
}

$logger->info("starting $PGM");
$logger->info("processing request file, $REQ_PATHFILE");

my $req = read_request($REQ_PATHFILE); # local function

# print Dumper( $req ); # todo: remove this
my $REQUEST_ID = ''; # file level global

# check to see if there was some fundamental problem parsing the request
if ( $req->{error} ) {
	# there was a problem parsing the request, write error job_queue record
	insert_failed( $req );
	move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
	exit 0;
}

# is this a reset
if ($req->{'reset id'}) {
	process_reset( $req ); # never returns, local function
}

# is this a resume
if ($req->{'resume id'}) {
	process_resume( $req ); # never returns, local function
}

# we are processing a normal new request

# get new job object
my $template_app;
eval {
	$template_app = BLUELITE::Job->new(app_id => $req->{'app id'})
		|| die("cannot create template application object, $!");
};

if ($@) {
	# an error condition with the supplied app id occurred, we cannot create
	# a failure record with an invalid app id
	abend_pgm($@);
}

my $dbh = $template_app->dbh();

# make sure the provided app id is a valid one
# need object database connection to perform this test
# if app id is not valid, we cannot insert a failure record.  abend_pgm
if ( !appid_valid( $template_app, $req ) ) {
	$req->{error} .= 'App id provided in request is not valid. ';
	insert_failed( $req, $dbh );
	move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
	exit 0;
}


my $new_app;
eval {
	$new_app = $template_app->create_new_request() || die $!;
};

if (!defined $new_app) {
	$req->{error} .= 'could not create new request from template. ';
	insert_failed( $req, $dbh );
	move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
	exit 0;
}

$dbh = $new_app->dbh();  # new request, new connection
$req->{RQ_SOURCE_APP_ID} = $new_app->source_app_id();

# check post date spec, set data_source_format
my $post_date_list;
my $num_post_dates = 0;
eval {
	$post_date_list = $new_app->post_date_list($req->{'post date'});
	$num_post_dates = scalar( @{$post_date_list} );
};

if ($@ || !defined $post_date_list || $num_post_dates < 1) {
	# an invalid post date spec was provided
	$req->{error} = 'invalid post date spec provided. ' . $req->{'post date'};
	insert_failed( $req, $dbh );
	move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
	exit 0;
}

if ($num_post_dates > 20) {
	$req->{data_source_format} = 'POSTDATE';
} else {
	$req->{data_source_format} = '';
}

# first set of updates
my $updates = {
	description               => $req->{description},
	rq_requester_email        => $req->{email_string},
	output_scope              => $req->{'file scope'},
	rq_post_date              => $req->{'post date'},
	rq_reference_id           => $req->{'reference id'},
	group_id                  => $GROUP_ID,
	data_source_format        => $req->{data_source_format},
};

# set deliverable/trigger fname/vars according to this precedence:
# 1) value returned by custom validator
# 2) value configured via corresponding rq_*() method (i.e. from rq_* column in job_config table)
# 3) default convention: ${reference_id}_*fname_sprintf (from job_config table)

if (defined($template_app->rq_deliverable_fname_sprintf)) {
	#2
	$updates->{deliverable_fname_sprintf} = $template_app->rq_deliverable_fname_sprintf;
} else {
	#3
	$updates->{deliverable_fname_sprintf} = $req->{'reference id'} . '_' . $template_app->deliverable_fname_sprintf;
}

if (defined($template_app->rq_trigger_fname_sprintf)) {
	#2
	$updates->{trigger_fname_sprintf} = $template_app->rq_trigger_fname_sprintf;
} elsif (defined($template_app->trigger_fname_sprintf)) {
	#3
	$updates->{trigger_fname_sprintf} = $req->{'reference id'} . '_' . $template_app->trigger_fname_sprintf;
}

if (defined($template_app->rq_deliverable_fname_vars)) {
	#2
	$updates->{deliverable_fname_vars} = $template_app->rq_deliverable_fname_vars;
} else {
	#3
	$updates->{deliverable_fname_vars} = $template_app->deliverable_fname_vars;
}

if (defined($template_app->rq_trigger_fname_vars)) {
	#2
	$updates->{trigger_fname_vars} = $template_app->rq_trigger_fname_vars;
} elsif (defined($template_app->trigger_fname_vars)) {
	#3
	$updates->{trigger_fname_vars} = $template_app->trigger_fname_vars;
}

my %allowed_custom_rq_settings = map { $_ => undef } (qw/
	worker_opts
	deliverable_fname_sprintf
	trigger_fname_sprintf
	deliverable_fname_vars
	trigger_fname_vars
/);

# check for unrecognized parameters from custom validator
foreach my $custom_rq_setting (keys %{$req->{rq_settings}}) {
	if (! exists($allowed_custom_rq_settings{$custom_rq_setting})) {
		$req->{error} = "Custom validator set an unrecognized parameter '$custom_rq_setting'";
		insert_failed( $req, $dbh );
		move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
		exit 0;
	}
}

# override above settings w/values from custom validator
foreach my $setting_key (keys %allowed_custom_rq_settings) {
	if (exists($req->{rq_settings}->{$setting_key})) {
		$updates->{$setting_key} = $req->{rq_settings}->{$setting_key};
	}
}

# at this point, the request has been validated, time to commit it

my $result;
eval{ $result = $new_app->update_job_config(assignments => $updates) };
# print Dumper $updates; # todo: remove this

if (!defined $result || $result->{error}) {
	$req->{error} .= 'cannot update job config ' . $result->{error};
	insert_failed( $req, $dbh );
	move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
	exit 0;
}

$new_app->commit;

$REQUEST_ID = $new_app->{RQ_REQUEST_ID};

# get a fresh object to query/update
my $fresh_app;
eval {
	$fresh_app = BLUELITE::Job->new(
		app_id => $req->{'app id'},
		request_id => $REQUEST_ID,
		) || die("cannot get fresh job object, $!");
};

if ($@) {
	# an error condition occurred while attempting to get a fresh job object
	# for newly created request.  This is a system problem, not caused by user
	$req->{error} .= 'system error, cannot get job obj for new request.';
	insert_failed($req, $dbh);
	move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
	exit 0;
}


# create file system resources for this request
$logger->debug("creating output dir " . $fresh_app->output_dir);
mkpath( $fresh_app->output_dir, 0, 0770 );

# do we need to write a drug list file?

if ( scalar(@{$req->{drugs}}) > 0 ) {
	
	my $fname = File::Spec->catfile( $fresh_app->worker_dir, "${REQUEST_ID}_drugs.txt" );
	$logger->debug("opening file: $fname");
	my $fh;
	
	eval {
		$fh = IO::File->new( $fname, O_WRONLY | O_CREAT | O_TRUNC )
			or die("$fname, $!");
		
		foreach my $drug ( @{$req->{drugs}} ) {
			print $fh "$drug\n" || die $!;
		}
		
		$logger->debug("closing file: $fname");
		$fh->close() || die $!;
	};
	
	if ($@) {
		$req->{error} .= "problem writing drug file, $@, $!";
		insert_failed($req, $dbh);
		move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
		exit 0;
	}
	
	$req->{drug_filename} = $fname;
}

# do we need to write a pharmacy list file?
if ( scalar(@{$req->{pharms}}) > 0 ) {
	
	my $fname = File::Spec->catfile( $fresh_app->worker_dir, "${REQUEST_ID}_pharms.txt" );
	$logger->debug("opening file: $fname");
	my $fh;
	
	eval {
		$fh = IO::File->new( $fname, O_WRONLY | O_CREAT | O_TRUNC )
			or die("$fname, $!");
		
		foreach my $pharm ( @{$req->{pharms}} ) {
			print $fh "$pharm\n" || die $!;
		}
		
		$fh->close() || die $!;
	};
	
	if ($@) {
		$req->{error} .= "problem writing pharmacy file, $@, $!";
		insert_failed($req, $dbh);
		move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
		exit 0;
	}
	
	$req->{pharmacy_filename} = $fname;
}

# last set of updates
my $last_updates = {
	RQ_DRUG_FILENAME     => $req->{drug_filename},
	RQ_PHARMACY_FILENAME => $req->{pharmacy_filename},
	RQ_STEP              => 'VALIDATE',
	RQ_SUBMITTED_DATE    => 'sysdate',
	RQ_STATUS            => 'COMPLETE'
};

eval { $result = $fresh_app->update_job_config(assignments => $last_updates); };

if (!defined $result || $result->{error}) {
	$req->{error} .= 'system error, cannot perform last set of updates.';
	insert_failed( $req, $dbh );
	move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
	exit 0;
}

$fresh_app->commit;

$logger->info("New request, " . $fresh_app->{APP_ID} . ", enqueued.");
$logger->info("ending $PGM normally");

move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_SUCCDIR);
exit 0;

# # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # # #

sub read_request {
	# read request file passed on command line, return hash of parms
	my $file = shift;

	# hash in which the request details reside
	my $req     = {
		drugs => [],
		pharms => []
	};

	$logger->debug("opening file: $file");
	my $fh = IO::File->new( $file, O_RDONLY ) or abend_pgm("$file, $!");
	my $app_id;

	while (my $line = <$fh>) {
		if ($line =~ /^\s*app id:\s*(\S+)\s*$/i) {
			if (defined $app_id) {
				$req->{error} = "App id specified more than once in $file";
#				return $req;
			}

			$app_id = uc($1);
		}
	}

	close($fh);

	if (! defined($app_id)) {
		$req->{error} = "App ID not specified in $file";
#		return $req;
	}

	if (($APP_ID ne 'ANY') && ($app_id ne $APP_ID)) {
		$req->{error} = "App ID of '$app_id' specified in $file does not match App ID of '$APP_ID' on command line";
#		return $req;
	}

	my $job = BLUELITE::Job->new(app_id => $app_id);
	my ($validate_cmd, $temp_err_fname);

	if (defined $job->rq_validate_cmd) {
		$temp_err_fname = "${file}.stderr";
		$validate_cmd = $job->rq_validate_cmd() . " -app-id $app_id $file 2> $temp_err_fname |";
		if (! open($fh, "$validate_cmd")) {
			$req->{error} = "Could not start rq_validate_cmd $validate_cmd : $!";
			return $req;
		}
	} else {
		$fh = IO::File->new( $file, O_RDONLY ) or abend_pgm("$file, $!");
	}

	my $l       = 0;            # current request file line number
	my $parsing = 'nameval';    # initialize state to parsing of namevals
	while ( my $line = <$fh> ) {
		$l++;
		$line =~ s/\r|\n//g;
		$line = trim( $line );
		
		$logger->debug("line: >$line<");
		
		if (!$line) {
			$logger->debug("skipping blank Line $l");
			next;
		}
		
		if ($line =~ m/^\s*#+/) {
			$logger->debug("skipping comment on Line $l");
			next;
		}
		
		# set "parsing mode"
		if ( lc($line) =~ m/^drug:?$/) {
			# make sure drugs have not been previously specified
			if (exists $req->{drugs} && scalar @{ $req->{drugs} } > 0) {
				# since this could be read from a pipe now, the line number is
				# no longer a reflection of the actual line from the request
				# $req->{error} .= "Line $l, duplicate drug specification. ";
				$req->{error} .= "Duplicate drug specification. ";
			} else {
				$req->{drugs} = [];
			}
			$parsing = 'drugs';
			next;
		} elsif ( lc($line) =~ m/^pharmacy:?$/ ) {
			# make sure pharmacies have not been previously specified
			if (exists $req->{pharms} && scalar @{ $req->{pharms} } > 0) {
				# $req->{error} .= "Line $l, duplicate pharmacy specification. ";
				$req->{error} .= "Duplicate pharmacy specification. ";
			} else {
				$req->{pharms} = [];
			}
			$parsing = 'pharms';
			next;
		} elsif ($line =~ /^\s*([a-z0-9_]+)\s*=\s*(.*)$/i) {
			my ($rq_setting_key, $rq_setting_value) = (lc($1), $2);

			if (exists($req->{rq_settings}->{$rq_setting_key})) {
				# $req->{error} .= "Line $l, duplicate $rq_setting_key specified. ";
				$req->{error} .= "Duplicate $rq_setting_key specified. ";
				next;
			}

			$req->{rq_settings}->{$rq_setting_key} = $rq_setting_value;
			next;
		} elsif ($line =~ m/\:/) {
			$parsing = 'nameval';
		}
		
		$logger->debug("currently parsing $parsing");
		
		if ($parsing eq 'nameval') {
			
			# we are parsing a name value pair
			my ($name, $value) = split(':', $line, -1);
			$name  = lc( trim($name) );
			$value = trim( $value );
			
			# make sure we are parsing an accepted parm name
			if ( !grep(/^$name$/, @{$VALNAMES}) ) {
				# error condition
				# $req->{error} .= "Line $l, $name is not a valid field name. ";
				$req->{error} .= "$name is not a valid field name. ";
				next;
			}
			
			# check to make sure we haven't seen this name value already
			# to prevent duplicate specification in the file
			if (exists $req->{$name}) {
				# $req->{error} .= "Line $l, duplicate field in request. ";
				$req->{error} .= "Duplicate field ($name) in request. ";
				next;
			}
			
			$req->{$name} = $value;
			$logger->debug("Name: $name, Value: $value");
		
		} elsif ($parsing eq 'drugs') {
			
			# we are parsing drugs
			if ( length($line) != 11 ) {
				# error condition
				# $req->{error} .= "Line $l, drug $line must be 11 chars. ";
				$req->{error} .= "Drug $line must be 11 chars. ";
				next;
			}
			
			push( @{$req->{drugs}}, $line );
			$logger->debug("Drug: $line");
			
		} elsif ($parsing eq 'pharms') {
			
			# we are parsing a pharmacy
			if ( length($line) != 7 && length($line) != 10 ) {
				# error condition
				$req->{error} .= "Line $l, pharmacy $line must be 7 or 10 chars. ";
				$req->{error} .= "Pharmacy $line must be 7 or 10 chars. ";
				next;
			}
			
			push( @{$req->{pharms}}, $line );
			$logger->debug("Pharmacy: $line");
			
		}
	}
	
	$logger->debug("closing file: $file");

	if (! $fh->close()) {

		if (defined $validate_cmd) {

			$logger->debug("returned non-zero: $validate_cmd");
			$req->{error} .= "Custom validation command failed for file: $file ";

			if (-f $temp_err_fname) {
				open(ERR, $temp_err_fname);
				$req->{error} .= join('', <ERR>);
				close(ERR);
#				unlink($temp_err_fname); unlinked below
			}
		} else {
			$req->{error} .= "Could not close $file : $!";
		}

		# return $req;
	}

	if (defined $temp_err_fname) {
		unlink($temp_err_fname);
	}
	
	# BEGIN LOGICAL VALIDATION OF HASH
	
	# app id of application on which this is based must be provided
	if (!$req->{'app id'}) {
		$req->{error} .= "Request did not contain an app id. ";
	}
	
	$req->{'app id'} = uc( $req->{'app id'} );  # uppercase it
	
	# reset id and resume id may not both be specified (they can be null)
	if ($req->{'reset id'} && $req->{'resume id'}) {
		$req->{error} .= "Reset and resume id may not both be specified. ";
	}
	
	if ($req->{'reset id'}) {
		return $req;
	}
	
	if ($req->{'resume id'}) {
		return $req;
	}
	
	# email address(es) must be provided.
	if (!$req->{'requester email'}) {
		$req->{error} .= "Request did not contain a requester email. ";
	}
	
	# parse/validate email addresses
	my @emails = split('\,', $req->{'requester email'});
	
	foreach my $email (@emails) {
		$logger->debug("testing: $email");
		$email = trim( $email );  # trim it
		$email = lc( $email );    # lowercase it
		if ($email =~ m/\@mckesson\.com$|\@relayhealth\.com$/) {
			$req->{email_string} .= "$email,";
		} else {
			$logger->debug("rejecting invalid email, $email");
		}
	}
	
	# remove trailing comma
	$req->{email_string} =~ s/\,$//;
	
	$logger->debug( "email string: " . $req->{email_string} );
	
	if (!$req->{email_string}) {
		$req->{error} .= "Request did not contain a valid requester email. ";
	}
	
	# memorable description must be provided
	if (!$req->{description}) {
		$req->{error} .= "Request did not contain a description. ";
	}
	
	# post date must be provided
	if (!$req->{'post date'}) {
		$req->{error} .= "Request did not contain a post date spec. ";
	}
	
	# reference id must be provided (jtrac number)
	if (!$req->{'reference id'}) {
		$req->{error} .= "Request did not contain a reference id. ";
	}
	
	$req->{'reference id'} = uc( $req->{'reference id'} );
	
	# make sure reference id begins with AH followed by some word chars
	if ($req->{'reference id'} !~ m/^AH[a-zA-Z0-9]+$/) {
		$req->{error} .= "Reference id must begin with AH and contain only letters or numbers. ";
	}
	
	# if specified, file scope must be daily|monthly|yearly|all,
	# (daily|all for now)
	if (exists $req->{'file scope'} && $req->{'file scope'}) {
		$req->{'file scope'} = uc( $req->{'file scope'} ); # uppercase it
		if ($req->{'file scope'} !~ m/^(DAILY|ALL)$/) {
			$req->{error} .= "Specified file scope, " . $req->{'file scope'} . ", not valid. ";
		}
	}

#	print Dumper $req; # todo: remove this

	return $req;
}

sub appid_valid {
	my $ta = shift;
	my $r  = shift;
	
	# return true  = app id ok
	# return false = app id not ok
	
	# if the autohoc_support value from job_config record is 'Y', return true
	if ($ta->autohoc_support() eq 'Y') {
		return 1;
	}
	
	# if autohoc support value from job_config is set to 'N', return false
	if ($ta->autohoc_support() eq 'N') {
		$r->{error} .= "Autohoc for this app_id is not allowed. ";
		return 0;
	}

	# if environment is dev, skip further checks
	if ($ENV{JOBPKG_ENV} eq 'DEV') {
		$logger->debug("dev environment, not checking validity of app id");
		return 1;
	}

	# otherwise make sure there have been recent deliveries
	my $dbh = $ta->dbh();
	
	my $sql = q{
		SELECT
			'ok'
		FROM
			job_delivery
		WHERE
			creation_date BETWEEN trunc(sysdate) - 7 AND trunc(sysdate)
			AND DELIVERY_TYPE = 'DATA'
			AND destination_host IS NOT NULL
			AND app_id = ?
		GROUP BY
			app_id
		HAVING
			count(1) = 7
	};
	
	my $sth = $dbh->prepare($sql) or abend_pgm('prep: ' . $dbh->errstr);

	$sth->execute( $ta->app_id ) or abend_pgm('exec: ' . $sth->errstr);
	
	# fetch
	my ($ok) = $sth->fetchrow_array;
	
	if ( $sth->err ) { abend_pgm('fetch: ' . $sth->errstr) }
	
	$sth->finish;
	
	if (defined $ok) {
		# the app is a 'go', return true
		return 1;
	}
	
	$r->{error} .= "This app_id has no recent data delivery. ";
	return 0;
}

sub insert_failed {
	my $req                = shift;
	my $dbh2               = shift;
	my $group_id           = $GROUP_ID;
	my $rq_requester_email = $EMAIL_DEFTO; # initialize to default

	# if there is no provided app id, we cannot insert anything into job_queue
	# oracle constraint
	if (!exists $req->{'app id'} || !$req->{'app id'}) {
		my $m = "no valid app id provided";
		if (defined $req->{error}) {
			$m .= ", " . $req->{error};
		}
		abend_pgm($m);
	}

	my $app_id  = $req->{'app id'};

	# if I haven't been able to bootstrap a connection, create one
	if (!defined $dbh2 || !$dbh2->ping ) {
		$logger->debug("creating database connection for generic update");
		$dbh2 = BLUELITE::Job->dbh();
		if (!defined $dbh2 || !$dbh2->ping) {
			abend_pgm("could not get db connection to insert request failure");
		}
	}
	
	# from here, insert a record in job queue representing a failed validation
	# Job records inserted because of failed request parsing
	# will never be executed.  Job records inserted because of failed request
	# parsing will always need to be resubmitted by uploading a new file.
	# The exact detail of the request need not be written, only a description
	# of the ways in which the request failed validation.
	
	# if I have an email address in the request, use that
	if ($req->{email_string}) {
		$rq_requester_email = $req->{email_string};
	} else {
		$req->{error} .= "request did not contain a valid email, using default $EMAIL_DEFTO. ";
	}
	
	my $rq_status = "$REQ_FILE, UNKNOWN ERROR"; # initialize to something generic
	
	# if I have an error messsage, use that
	if ($req->{error}) {
		$rq_status = "$REQ_FILE, " . $req->{error};
		$rq_status = substr($rq_status, 0, 1023); # limit of the column
	}
	
	$logger->error( $rq_status );

	$logger->info("inserting parsing error record");
	
	# get request id sequence number
