	my $seqsth = $dbh2->prepare('select JOB_REQUEST_ID_SEQ.NEXTVAL from dual')
		|| abend_pgm( 'prep: ' . $dbh2->errstr );
	
	$seqsth->execute() or abend_pgm('exec: ' . $dbh2->errstr);
	
	($REQUEST_ID) = $seqsth->fetchrow_array;
	
	$seqsth->finish;
	
	# insert error record
	my $if_sth = $dbh2->prepare( qq{
		insert into job_queue (
			APP_ID,
			GROUP_ID,
			RQ_SOURCE_APP_ID,
			RQ_REQUESTER_EMAIL,
			RQ_STATUS,
			RQ_STATUS_DETAIL,
			RQ_SUBMITTED_DATE,
			RQ_REQUEST_ID,
			RQ_REFERENCE_ID,
			RQ_STEP )
		values (
			?,
			?,
			?,
			?,
			'ERROR',
			?,
			sysdate,
			?,
			?,
			'VALIDATE' )
		} ) || abend_pgm( 'prep: ' . $dbh2->errstr );
	
	$if_sth->execute(
			"$app_id.$REQUEST_ID",
			$group_id,
			$app_id,
			$rq_requester_email,
			$rq_status,
			$REQUEST_ID,
			$req->{'reference id'}
			) || abend_pgm( 'exec: ' . $if_sth->errstr );
	
	$dbh2->commit() || abend_pgm( 'commit: ' . $dbh2->errstr );
	
	return 1;
}

sub process_reset {
	my $req      = shift;
	my $app_id   = $req->{'app id'};
	my $reset_id = $req->{'reset id'};
	
	my $reset_app;
	eval{
		$reset_app = BLUELITE::Job->new(
			app_id     => $app_id,
			request_id => $reset_id,
			) || die("app id: $app_id, reset id: $reset_id, combination invalid.");
	};
	
	if (!defined $reset_app) {
		$req->{error} .= $@;
		insert_failed( $req );
		move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
		exit 0;
	}
	
	$logger->info("source app id is " . $reset_app->source_app_id() );
	$req->{RQ_SOURCE_APP_ID} = $reset_app->source_app_id();
	$req->{email_string}     = $reset_app->{RQ_REQUESTER_EMAIL};
	
	if ($reset_app->{GROUP_ID} ne $GROUP_ID) {
		$req->{error} .= "reset request is not in proper group, origional request group is " . $reset_app->{GROUP_ID} . ". ";
		$GROUP_ID = $reset_app->{GROUP_ID}; # error notification should be in the original group
		insert_failed($req);
		move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
		exit 0;
	}
	
	# RQ_STEP must be EXTRACT and RQ_STATUS must be ERROR
	if ($reset_app->{RQ_STEP} ne 'EXTRACT') {
		$req->{error} .= "cannot reset $app_id $reset_id, it is not currently extracting, step is currently " . $reset_app->{RQ_STEP} . ". ";
		insert_failed($req);
		move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
		exit 0;
	}
	
	if ($reset_app->{RQ_STATUS} ne 'ERROR') {
		$req->{error} .= "cannot reset $app_id $reset_id, it is not currently in an error status, status is currently " . $reset_app->{RQ_STATUS} . ". ";
		insert_failed($req);
		move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
		exit 0;
	}
	
	my $updates = {
		RQ_RESET  => 'Y',
		RQ_RESUME => 'N',
		RQ_STEP   => 'VALIDATE',
		RQ_STATUS => 'COMPLETE',
	};

	my $result;
	eval { $result = $reset_app->update_job_config(assignments => $updates); };
	
	if (!defined $result || $result->{error}) {
		$req->{error} .= 'system error, cannot update reset job config';
		insert_failed( $req, $dbh );
		move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
		exit 0;
		}

	if ($result->{error}) {
		abend_pgm( $result->{error} );
	}
	
	$reset_app->commit;
	
	$logger->info("flagged " . $reset_app->{APP_ID} . " for reset.");
	
	move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_SUCCDIR);
	exit 0;
}

sub process_resume {
	my $req       = shift;
	my $app_id    = $req->{'app id'};
	my $resume_id = $req->{'resume id'};
	
	my $resume_app;
	eval{
		$resume_app = BLUELITE::Job->new(
			app_id     => $app_id,
			request_id => $resume_id,
			) || die("app id: $app_id, resume id: $resume_id, combination invalid.");
	};
	
	if (!defined $resume_app) {
		$req->{error} .= $@;
		insert_failed( $req );
		move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
		exit 0;
	}
	
	$logger->debug("source app id is " . $resume_app->source_app_id() );
	$req->{RQ_SOURCE_APP_ID} = $resume_app->source_app_id();
	$req->{email_string}     = $resume_app->{RQ_REQUESTER_EMAIL};
	
	if ($resume_app->{GROUP_ID} ne $GROUP_ID) {
		$req->{error} .= "resume request is not in proper group, original request group is " . $resume_app->{GROUP_ID} . ". ";
		$GROUP_ID = $resume_app->{GROUP_ID}; # error notification should be in the original group
		insert_failed($req);
		move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
		exit 0;
	}
	
	# RQ_STEP must be EXTRACT and RQ_STATUS must be ERROR
	if ($resume_app->{RQ_STEP} ne 'EXTRACT') {
		$req->{error} .= "cannot resume $app_id $resume_id, it is not currently extracting, step is currently " . $resume_app->{RQ_STEP};
		insert_failed($req);
		move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
		exit 0;
	}
	
	if ($resume_app->{RQ_STATUS} ne 'ERROR') {
		$req->{error} .= "cannot resume $app_id $resume_id, it is not currently ERROR, status is currently " . $resume_app->{RQ_STATUS};
		insert_failed($req);
		move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
		exit 0;
	}
	
	my $updates = {
		RQ_RESUME => 'Y',
		RQ_RESET  => 'N',
		RQ_STEP   => 'VALIDATE',
		RQ_STATUS => 'COMPLETE',
	};

	my $result;
	eval { $result = $resume_app->update_job_config(assignments => $updates); };
	
	if (!defined $result || $result->{error}) {
		$req->{error} .= 'cannot update resume job config';
		insert_failed( $req, $dbh );
		move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);
		exit 0;
	}
	
	$resume_app->commit;
	
	$logger->info("flagged " . $resume_app->{APP_ID} . " for resume.");
	
	move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_SUCCDIR);
	exit 0;
}

sub abend_pgm {
	my $msg = shift;
	my ( $pkg, $filnm, $lin ) = caller;
	$msg = "(abend\@$PGM:" . $lin . ") $msg";

	move_req($REQ_PATHFILE, $REQ_FAILDIR);

	if ( defined $logger ) {
		$logger->debug("ending $PGM abnormally");
		$logger->error($msg);
	} else {
		print "$msg\n";
	}
	
	exit 1;
} ## end sub abend_pgm

sub init_pgm {

	# get a logger
	my $logger = get_logger();

	if ($debug) {
		initialize_logging( screen_only => 1, screen_level => "DEBUG" );
		$logger->debug("debug logging enabled");
	} else {
		initialize_logging( screen_only => 1, screen_level => "INFO" );
	}

	# get application filename and standard directories
	my $pgm = File::Spec->rel2abs($0);    # $0 = builtin var, name/path of pgm
	my ( $vol, $path, $file ) = File::Spec->splitpath($pgm);
	my $pgmname = $file;
	my $pgmdir  = $path;

	# formulate request file directories
	$REQ_PATHFILE = File::Spec->rel2abs($REQ_PATHFILE);
	my ( $rvol, $rpath, $rfile ) = File::Spec->splitpath($REQ_PATHFILE);
	my $req_path    = $rpath;
	my $req_file    = $rfile;
	my $req_succdir = File::Spec->catfile( $req_path, '.processed' );
	my $req_faildir = File::Spec->catfile( $req_path, '.failed' );
	
	# make the dirs if they don't exist
	if (!-d $req_succdir) {
		$logger->debug("success directory doesn't exist, creating it");
		mkpath( $req_succdir );
	}

	if (!-d $req_faildir) {
		$logger->debug("failed directory doesn't exist, creating it");
		mkpath( $req_faildir );
	}

	# get start time
	my $start_time = DateTime->now();
	$start_time->set_time_zone( 'America/New_York' );
	my $start_yyyy = $start_time->year;
	my $start_mo   = sprintf( "%02d", $start_time->month );
	my $start_dd   = sprintf( "%02d", $start_time->day );
	my $start_hh   = sprintf( "%02d", $start_time->hour );
	my $start_mi   = sprintf( "%02d", $start_time->minute );
	my $start_ss   = sprintf( "%02d", $start_time->second );
	# used as prefix for processed filenames
	my $arc_ts     = $start_yyyy . $start_mo . $start_dd . $start_hh
	                 . $start_mi . $start_ss;

	# populate hashref for return
	my $app_env = {
		logger      => $logger,
		pgm_name    => $pgmname,
		req_path    => $req_path,
		req_file    => $req_file,
		req_succdir => $req_succdir,
		req_faildir => $req_faildir,
		arc_ts      => $arc_ts,
		};

	return ($app_env);
} ## end sub init_pgm

sub move_req {
	my $source_file   = shift;
	my $dest_dir      = shift;
	my $rid           = shift;
	
	if (!-d $dest_dir) {
		$logger->error("cannot move $source_file, $dest_dir is not a directory");
		return 0;
	}
	
	# should already be absolute path
	my ($s_vol, $s_path, $s_file) = File::Spec->splitpath( $source_file );
	
	$dest_dir = File::Spec->rel2abs( $dest_dir );

	# if a reference id has been assigned, use it in the destination
	# filename
	if (defined $REQUEST_ID && $REQUEST_ID) {
		$s_file = $REQUEST_ID . "-" . $s_file;
	} else {
		$s_file = "NONE-" . $s_file;
	}
	
	my $dest_file = File::Spec->catfile( $dest_dir, $ARC_TS . '-' . $s_file );
	
	if ($nomove) {
		$logger->debug("not moving request, -nomove specified on command line");
	} else {
		
		$logger->debug("moving $source_file to $dest_file");
		if ( move( $source_file, $dest_file ) ) {
			return 1;
		} else {
			# the move did not happen.  must die here with error
			$logger->error("Could not move $source_file to $dest_file, $!");
			exit 1;
		}
		
	}
	
	return 1;
}

sub trim {
	my $str = shift;
	
	if (defined $str) {
		$str =~ s/^\s+//;    # strip leading whitespace
		$str =~ s/\s+$//;    # strip trailng whitespace
	} else {
		return ''; # if it's undefined, return null string
	}
	
	return $str;
}

sub show_help {
	print q{job_enqueue_request [options] -group_id AUTOHOC request_file.txt

Read in an Autohoc request file and add a record to the job queue.

Options:
-group-id|group_id          The group id of the request we are processing.
                            (AUTOHOC|AUTOHOC2)

-app-id|app_id              REQUIRED The application id for which a request
                            is being submitted.

-nomove                     Do NOT move request files to .processed or .failed

-debug                      Show debug statements

-help

Examples:
job_enqueue_request -group_id AUTOHOC -app_id EVPAR_HIST sample_req.txt
job_enqueue_request -group_id AUTOHOC -app_id EVPAR_HIST sample_reset.txt
job_enqueue_request -group_id AUTOHOC -app_id EVPAR_HIST sample_resume.txt
job_enqueue_request -nomove -group_id AUTOHOC2 -app_id EVPAR_HIST sample_req.txt
job_enqueue_request -nomove -group_id AUTOHOC2 -app_id EVPAR_HIST sample_reset.txt
job_enqueue_request -nomove -group_id AUTOHOC2 -app_id EVPAR_HIST sample_resume.txt
job_enqueue_request -nomove -group_id AUTOHOC2 -app_id EVPAR_HIST sample_req.txt -debug
	};
	print "\n";
} ## end sub show_help


#job_launcher
#!/usr/bin/perl

#use lib '/ds/development/Job/dev/blib/lib';

# job_launcher: Launch job workers via BLUELITE::Job
#
# Author(s): Meenu Narang, John Hess		RelayHealth
#
# Version history:
# Version 1.0 - 9/18/2007
#
# Version 1.4 - 4/16/2010
# - Add -post-dates command-line option
#
# Version 1.4 - 6/22/2010 (aligned version to match that of BLUELITE::Job package)
# - Updated Usage display to reflect the fact that -app-dir and -worker-script are optional
#
# Version 1.5 - 7/26/2010
# - Removed 'uninitialized value' warning if we can't get the current date via date command in setup_logging function
#
# Version 2.3 - 12/8/2010
# - If still_running_status returned by launcher is true, launches will not be attempted for any remaining apps.
# This was done to avoid an app_id launcher ordering issue when using -group-id and minimum_processes is set in job_config.
#
# - Aligned version with Job pkg.
#
# Version 2.61 - 2/2/2011
# - Fixed bug in launcher where apps in a group_id could be indefinitely prevented from launching new workers
# under the following scenario:
# 1) Launcher 1 launches via -group-id
# 2) app_id 1 completes its workers
# 3) app_id 2 workers begin, with some dying without signal handler kicking in (e.g. "out of memory", "kill -9", etc).
#    These workers are left in 'PROCESSING' state.
# 4) Launcher 1 exits
# 5) Launcher 2 launches same -group-id
# 6) No workers are launched due to "# workers already in PROCESSING state", where # is at least the configured minimum.
#
# The above bug was introduced another bug fix (group_id_order issue) in version 2.3, because the launcher no longer
# continued to try subsequent app_ids in the group after passing the "min_processes running" check. This fix moved the
# detect_long_work_units call to be moved from the launch method to the job_launcher script.
#
# Version 2.7 - 3/28/2011
#
# - Added -worker-opts command line option
# - Removed -worker-script command line option
#
# Version 2.8 - 4/26/2011
#
# - Added support for flexible date specifications in -post-date option (ranges, months, etc)
# - Added -ds-format command line option (e.g. so we can run work units as post dates)
# - Fixed problem that caused logging to screen when -group-id used.
# - Added -log-dir command line option, plus removal of main log file on normal exit if empty.
#
# Version 3.0 5/x/2011
# - Added -log-level command line option
# - Changed default logging level from INFO to DEBUG
#
# Version 3.3 7/20/2011
# - Added call to notify_late_delivery method so that notifications will go out even if "still running" result
#   has been encountered.
#
# Version 4.3 10/24/2011
# - Fixed bug that failed to remove main logfile at end of successful execution. This resulted in lots of junk log
#   files in bin dir of apps that used preprocessor.
# - For main logfile, look for log subdir to write to in current or parent dir before resorting to current dir.
# - Randomize job launch order if files are processed as they stream in and min_processes setting is used.
#   This effectively ignores the group_id_order setting to avoid app starvation.
# - Added -config-group-id command line parameter, which allows config settings to be temporarily obtained from the
# specified group instead of from the job_config table.
#
# Version 5.0 3/5/2014
# - Changed default logging level from DEBUG to INFO
# - Added -skip-pre-launch-cmd command line option
#
# Version 5.1 5/23/2014
# - Enhanced the way worker_script is checked for existence since that parameter will sometimes be used as
# a command line instead of just the name of the worker script (e.g. due to use of /ds/bin/run_env.sh)
#
# Version 6.0 - 10/31/2014
# - Added support for "autohoc" requests (i.e. automated on-demand ad-hoc processing).
#
# Version 6.4 - 12/01/2015
# - Skip app from $GROUP_ID if the app is no longer in the $GROUP_ID. Minimizes delay when attempting to
# stop processing by removing it from a group.
#

use Getopt::Long;
use BLUELITE::Job;
use BLUELITE::Logger;
use BLUELITE::Mail qw(email);
use File::Spec;
use File::PathConvert qw(rel2abs);
use Data::Dumper;
use List::Util qw(min shuffle);

use strict;
use warnings;

our ($APP_ID, $GROUP_ID);
our $SCREEN_ONLY_LOGGING = 0;

my @dir_parts = File::Spec->splitdir(rel2abs($0));
our $PGM = pop(@dir_parts);

our ($FAILURE_EMAIL, $LOGGER, $STATS_EMAIL, $REQUEST_ID);
our $SMTP_SERVER = $ENV{DEFAULT_SMTP_SERVER};

our ($APP_DIR, $logfile);
our $LOGGING_LEVEL = 'INFO';

sub mydie($) {
	my $message = shift;

	if (defined($message) && (length($message) >= 1)) {
		$message .= "\n";

		if (defined($LOGGER)) {
			$LOGGER->error($message);
		} else {
			print STDERR $message;
		}
	}

	if (defined($FAILURE_EMAIL)) {

		if ((! defined($message)) || (length($message) == 0)) {
			$message = "No error message available\n";
		}

    email(
      to => $FAILURE_EMAIL,
      subject => "$APP_ID launcher process FAILED",
      msg => $message
    );
	}

	exit(1);
}


sub Usage() {
	print "$PGM: Launch BLUELITE::Job worker processes\n\n";
	print "Usage: $PGM [-options] -app-id i\n";
  print "OR\n";
	print "Usage: $PGM [-options] -group-id i\n";
  print " Parameters\n";
  print "  -group-id i                  Group id as recorded in JOB_CONFIG table\n";
  print "  -app-id i                    Application id as recorded in JOB_CONFIG table\n";
	print " Options:\n";
  print "  -request-id #                Request ID to process from job_queue table\n";
  print "  -app-dir d                   Top-level application directory (Can be passed with app-id only)\n";
  print "  -worker-opts 's'             Extra command line options to pass to worker command\n";
	print "  -keep-log                    Keep log file (removed if no warnings or errors encountered)\n";
	print "  -default-failure-email list  Send status to list addresses upon failure (does not override app default)\n";
	print "  -stats-email list            Send launch stats to list addresses (unless nothing was launched)\n";
	print "  -log-dir dir                 Log to dir (mostly for non-app-specific logging)\n";
	print "  -log-level L                 Logging level (DEBUG,INFO,WARN,ERROR,FATAL)\n";
	print "  -ds-format fmt               Change data_source_format for workers to fmt (e.g. POSTDATE)\n";
	print "  -config-group-id id          Get default group config params from group_id id\n";
	print "  -post-date pd_spec           Only launch workers for these post dates\n\n";
  print "Note: pd_spec may be a comma-separated list of any combination of the following syntaxes:\n";
  print "  YYYYMMDD\n";
  print "  YYYYMMDD-YYYYMMDD\n";
  print "  YYYYMM\n";
  print "  YYYYMM-YYYYMM\n";
  print "  YYYYMMDD-YYYYMM\n";
  print "  YYYYMM-YYYYMMDD\n";

}


sub setup_logging() {
    my ( $log_dir, $orig_log_dir);

    $log_dir = "$APP_DIR/log";
    $orig_log_dir = $log_dir;
    
    if (! -d $log_dir) {
        $log_dir = '.';
    }
    
    my $dt = `date +%Y%m%d`;

		if (defined($dt)) {
			chop($dt);
		} else {
			$dt = '';
		}

    $logfile = "$log_dir/launcher.$APP_ID.$dt.$$.log";
    
    # Set the options for logger
    my @screen_options;
    
    if ((-t 1) || $SCREEN_ONLY_LOGGING) {
			initialize_logging(screen_threshold => $LOGGING_LEVEL, screen_only => 1, force => 1);
    } else {
			initialize_logging(screen_threshold => 'OFF', file_threshold => $LOGGING_LEVEL, logfile => $logfile, force => 1);
    }
    
    # Intialize the logger
    
    $LOGGER = get_logger;
    $LOGGER->warn("log directory $orig_log_dir does not exist. Logging to current directory instead") if ((! $SCREEN_ONLY_LOGGING) && ($log_dir eq '.'));
}


sub worker_script($) {
  my @command_line = split(/\s+/, shift);

	if (@command_line) {
		return $command_line[0];
	} else {
		return undef;
	}
}


my $keep_log = 0;

if (scalar(@ARGV) == 0) {
  Usage;
  exit(1);
}

my ($worker_command, $worker_script, $post_dates, @worker_opts, $data_source_format, $log_dir, $config_group_id);
my $skip_pre_launch_cmd = 0;

my $ret = GetOptions(
	'keep-log' => \$keep_log,
	'screen-only' => \$SCREEN_ONLY_LOGGING,
	'default-failure-email=s' => \$FAILURE_EMAIL,
	'stats-email=s' => \$STATS_EMAIL,
	'group-id=s' => \$GROUP_ID,
	'app-id=s' => \$APP_ID,
	'request-id=i' => \$REQUEST_ID,
	'app-dir=s' => \$APP_DIR,
	'post-date=s' => \$post_dates,
	'ds-format=s' => \$data_source_format,
	'worker-opts=s@' => \@worker_opts,
	'config-group-id=s' => \$config_group_id,
	'log-dir=s' => \$log_dir,
	'log-level=s' => \$LOGGING_LEVEL,
	'skip-pre-launch-cmd' => \$skip_pre_launch_cmd
);

mydie "ERROR: $PGM: Invalid options\n" if ((! $ret) || (scalar(@ARGV) >= 1));

mydie "ERROR: app-id or group-id must be specified!\n" if ( ! defined($APP_ID) && ! defined($GROUP_ID));
mydie "ERROR: Both app-id and group-id can not be specified!\n" if ( defined($APP_ID) && defined($GROUP_ID));
mydie "ERROR: app-dir can only be specified with app-id!\n" if ( defined($APP_DIR) && defined($GROUP_ID));
mydie "ERROR: config-group-id cannot be used with group-id!\n" if (defined($config_group_id) && defined($GROUP_ID));
mydie "ERROR: Both request-id and group-id can not be specified!\n" if ( defined($GROUP_ID) && defined($REQUEST_ID));
mydie "ERROR: The post-date must be specified when using request-id!\n" if (defined($REQUEST_ID) && ! defined($post_dates));

my (@job_list, $group_id, $job_list, @launch_opts);

# Set the options for logger
my $id;

if (defined($GROUP_ID)) {
	$id = $GROUP_ID;
} else {
	$id = $APP_ID;
}

my $screen_threshold;

if (-t 1) {
	$screen_threshold = $LOGGING_LEVEL;
} else {
	$screen_threshold = 'OFF';
}

if (! defined($log_dir)) {
	foreach my $ld ('log', '../log', '.') {
		if (-d $ld) {
			$log_dir = $ld;
			last;
		}
	}
}

my $main_logfile = "$log_dir/launcher.$id.$$.log";

if ($SCREEN_ONLY_LOGGING) {
	initialize_logging(screen_threshold => $LOGGING_LEVEL, force => 1, screen_only => 1);
} else {
	initialize_logging(screen_threshold => $screen_threshold, file_threshold => $LOGGING_LEVEL, logfile => $main_logfile, force => 1);
}

my @launcher_opts = (is_launcher => 1);
push(@launcher_opts, config_group_id => $config_group_id) if (defined($config_group_id));
push(@launcher_opts, request_id => $REQUEST_ID) if (defined($REQUEST_ID));

if (defined $APP_ID) {
   my $job = BLUELITE::Job->new(APP_ID => $APP_ID, @launcher_opts);
   mydie "ERROR: Unable to obtain a BLUELITE::Job object for APP_ID = '$APP_ID' : $@\n" if (! defined($job));

   @job_list = $job;

	if (defined($APP_DIR)) {
		$job->app_dir($APP_DIR);
	}

} else {
   @job_list = BLUELITE::Job->new(GROUP_ID => $GROUP_ID, @launcher_opts);

   if (scalar(@job_list) == 0) {
       mydie "ERROR: HERE Unable to obtain any BLUELITE::Job objects for GROUP_ID = '$GROUP_ID' : $@\n";
   }

	# Randomize job launch order if files are processed as they stream in and min_processes setting is used.
	# This effectively ignores the group_id_order setting to avoid app starvation.

	my $post_date_complete = 0;
	my $min_processes_used = 0;

	foreach my $job (@job_list) {
		$post_date_complete = 1 if ($job->get_post_date_complete =~ /^\s*Y\s*/i);
		$min_processes_used = 1 if ($job->min_processes >= 2);
	}

	@job_list = shuffle(@job_list) if ((! $post_date_complete) && $min_processes_used);
}

my $begin_post_date;
my @long_work_units_opts = ();

if (defined($post_dates)) {
	my $post_date_list = BLUELITE::Job->post_date_list($post_dates);

	mydie "ERROR: Could not decipher post date of '$post_dates'\n" if (! defined($post_date_list));

  $begin_post_date = min(@{$post_date_list});

	push(@launch_opts, post_date => $post_date_list);
	push(@long_work_units_opts, begin_post_date => $begin_post_date);
}

my @job_stats = ();
my $stats_email_list;
my $num_workers_launched = 0;
my $total_stats;
my $encountered_still_running = 0;

for my $job (@job_list) {

		# skip app from $GROUP_ID if the app is no longer in the $GROUP_ID
		if (defined($GROUP_ID)) {
			my $app_current_group = $job->current_group;

			if (! defined($app_current_group) || ($GROUP_ID ne $app_current_group)) {
				next;
			}
		}

    $FAILURE_EMAIL = $job->failure_email if (defined($job) && defined($job->failure_email));
    $APP_ID = $job->app_id;

    $APP_DIR = $job->app_dir;
    mydie "ERROR: The mandatory -app-dir parameter was not passed or defined in JOB_CONFIG table for application $APP_ID!\n" if (! defined($APP_DIR));
    mydie "ERROR: Application directory $APP_DIR does not exist!\n" if (! -e $APP_DIR);
    mydie "ERROR: Application directory $APP_DIR is not a directory!\n" if (! -d $APP_DIR);

    $worker_command = $job->worker_script;

    mydie "ERROR: The mandatory -worker-script parameter was not defined in JOB_CONFIG table for application $APP_ID!\n" if (! defined($worker_command));

		$worker_script = worker_script($worker_command);

    mydie "ERROR: worker script $worker_script does not exist!\n" if (! -e $worker_script);
    mydie "ERROR: worker script $worker_script is a directory!\n" if (-d $worker_script);
    mydie "ERROR: worker script $worker_script is not executable!\n" if (! -x $worker_script);

    setup_logging;

		# Detect work units which have been processing too long.
		# This also kills workers running too long, which must be attempted for all app_ids in
		# the group, even if we stop attempting to launch (due to "still running" status).

		my $num_workers_running_long = $job->detect_long_work_units(@long_work_units_opts);

		# Detect late deliveries.
		# This is performed for all app_ids in the group, even if we stop attempting to launch
		# (due to "still running" status).

		my $late_delivery = $job->notify_late_delivery(@long_work_units_opts);

		# don't launch another app_id if previous one encountered "still running" result

		if ($encountered_still_running) {
			unlink($logfile) if (defined($logfile) && (! $keep_log));
			next;
		}
 
		push(@launch_opts, log_file => $logfile) if (! $SCREEN_ONLY_LOGGING);
#		push(@launch_opts, log_file => 'screen.log') if ($SCREEN_ONLY_LOGGING);
		push(@launch_opts, worker_opts => \@worker_opts) if (scalar(@worker_opts));
		push(@launch_opts, skip_pre_launch_cmd => $skip_pre_launch_cmd) if ($skip_pre_launch_cmd);

		$job->data_source_format($data_source_format) if (defined($data_source_format));

    my $launch_result = $job->launch(@launch_opts);

    if ( defined($launch_result)) {

			if ($launch_result->{still_running_status}) {
				# This prevents the launcher from continuing while another launcher still has control, which avoids
				# a launch order issue when using minimum processes and group_id_order settings.

				$LOGGER->warn("Minimum workers are still running or queued. This launcher will not attempt any additional apps.");
				unlink($logfile) if (defined($logfile) && (! $keep_log) && ($num_workers_running_long == 0));
				$encountered_still_running = 1;
				next;
			}

			$num_workers_launched += $launch_result->{num_workers_launched};
			push(@job_stats, { app_id => $job->app_id, %{$launch_result} });

			map { $total_stats->{$_} += $launch_result->{$_} if ($launch_result->{$_} =~ /^\d+$/) } (keys %{$launch_result});

       if ( ($launch_result->{num_workers_failed} == 0)
             && ($num_workers_running_long == 0) && ($launch_result->{num_workers_dequeued} == 0)
    				 && ($launch_result->{prun2_return_status} == 0)
    			) {
           unlink($logfile) if (defined($logfile) && ! $keep_log);
        }
    } else {
        $LOGGER->fatal("Error in launching the workers. Please see the logfile $logfile for details");
    }
}

if (defined($STATS_EMAIL) && ($num_workers_launched > 0)) {
	my $msg = '';
	$msg = "$GROUP_ID " if (defined($GROUP_ID));

	$msg .= "worker launch stats";
	my $subject = $msg;

	$msg .= ":\n";

	foreach my $job_stat (@job_stats) {
		$msg .= "\n" . $job_stat->{app_id} . ': ';
		delete $job_stat->{app_id};

		$msg .= join(', ', map { "$_ = " . $job_stat->{$_} } (sort keys %{$job_stat}));
	}

	if (scalar(@job_stats) >= 1) {
		$msg .= "\n\nTotals: ";
		$msg .= join(', ', map { "$_ = " . $total_stats->{$_} } (sort keys %{$total_stats}));
	}

	email(
		to => $STATS_EMAIL,
		subject => $subject,
		msg => $msg
	);
}

unlink($main_logfile);

if ($encountered_still_running) {
	exit(99);
} else {
	exit(0);
}


#job_log_add
#!/usr/bin/perl

use BLUELITE::Job;
use Data::Dumper;
use strict;
use warnings;

our $PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s/.*\///g;

if (scalar(@ARGV) == 0) {
	print "$PGM: Manually add an entry into the BLUELITE::Job log table for an app_id.

This can be used by support personnel to temporarily force a specific external alert
status.  For example, to set BigBrother alert status to green for at least 2 hours:

$PGM -app-id DUMMY -message 'Temporarily set to green by John Hess' -event-code SPSTATUS -log-date +2h

To limit max BigBrother alert status to yellow for at least 45 minutes:

$PGM -app-id DUMMY -message 'Limiting max alert status to yellow for 45 mins (M Narang)' -event-code SPSTATUS -log-date +45m -log-type WARN

Usage: $PGM -app-id app_id -message 'your quoted message' [-options]
Options:

-post-date YYYYMMDD
-event-code code         {use 'SPSTATUS' to force BB status}
-log-type INFO|WARN|LATE
-log-date 'YYYYMMDD HH:MI' | +#m | +#h

-log-date defaults to current date/time. Examples:
1) -log-date '20101022 13:59'    {future dates allowed}
2) -log-date +90m   {90 minutes from now}
3) -log-date +1h    { 1 hour    from now}
\n";
	exit(1);
}

use Getopt::Long;

my ($app_id, $post_date, $event_code, $message, $log_type, $log_date);

GetOptions(
            'app-id=s' => \$app_id,
            'post-date=s' => \$post_date,
            'event-code=s' => \$event_code,
            'message=s' => \$message,
            'log-type=s' => \$log_type,
            'log-date=s' => \$log_date
) || exit(1);


die "$PGM: -app-id parameter not provided!\n" if (! defined($app_id));
die "$PGM: -message parameter not provided!\n" if (! defined($message));

my $job = BLUELITE::Job->new(app_id => $app_id) || die "Could not obtain BLUELITE::Job object\n";

my @log_parameters = (message => $message);

push(@log_parameters, post_date => $post_date) if (defined($post_date));
push(@log_parameters, event_code => $event_code) if (defined($event_code));
push(@log_parameters, log_type => $log_type) if (defined($log_type));
push(@log_parameters, log_date => $log_date) if (defined($log_date));

$job->log(@log_parameters);

#job_manage_queue
#!/usr/bin/perl

# Program: job_manage_queue
# Purpose: Scan and "manage" the job_queue table (send email notifications, fix status of dead jobs, etc)
#
# This process will be scheduled to run via cron automatically every 10 minutes.
#
# Initial version (6.0): Nov 3, 2014
#
# Version 6.2: Jan 2, 1015
# - Auto-delete requests from job_queue with bad app_id (to avoid repeated error emails)
#

use Params::Validate qw(:all);
use Data::Dumper;
use BLUELITE::Job;
use Getopt::Long;
use File::Spec;
use File::PathConvert qw(rel2abs);

use warnings;
use strict;

#our $JOB_PROCESS_QUEUE_CMD = "perl -I /ds/development/Job/dev/blib/lib /ds/development/Job/dev/job_process_queue";
#our $JOB_QUEUE_NOTIFY_CMD = "perl -I /ds/development/Job/dev/blib/lib /ds/development/Job/dev/job_queue_notify";

our $JOB_PROCESS_QUEUE_CMD = "job_process_queue";
our $JOB_QUEUE_NOTIFY_CMD = "job_queue_notify";

my @dir_parts = File::Spec->splitdir(rel2abs($0));
our $PGM = pop(@dir_parts);
our @GROUP_ID = ();
our $LOOKBACK_DAYS = 21;

sub update_queue($$) {
  my ($app_obj, $updates) = @_;

	my $app_id = $app_obj->app_id;
	my $update_result = $app_obj->update_job_config( assignments => $updates);

	if ($update_result->{error}) {
		die "Could not update job_queue for $app_id : " . $update_result->{error} . "\n\nThe updates were: " . Dumper $updates;
	}

	$app_obj->commit;
}


sub mylog($) {
	my $msg = shift;
	$msg =~ s/\n$//;
	$msg .= "\n";

	if (-t 0) {
		print  $msg;
	}
}

sub manage_validate($$) {
  my ($rq, $app_obj) = @_;

	my $rq_status = $rq->{RQ_STATUS};
	my $detail = $rq->{RQ_STATUS_DETAIL};
	my @updates = ();

	if ($rq_status eq 'COMPLETE') {
		$detail = "Request validated and queued for processing.";

		push(@updates,
			rq_status => 'QUEUE',
			rq_step => 'EXTRACT',
			rq_status_detail => $detail,
			rq_step_begin_date => 'sysdate',
			rq_step_end_date => 'sysdate'
		);
	} elsif ($rq_status eq 'ERROR') {
		if (! defined($detail)) {
			$detail = "Error validating request";
		}

		push(@updates,
			rq_process_begin_date => 'sysdate',
			rq_process_end_date => 'sysdate',
		);

		if (! defined($rq->{RQ_STEP_NOTIFY_DATE})) {
			push(@updates,
				rq_step_begin_date => 'sysdate',
				rq_step_end_date => 'sysdate'
			);
		}
	} else {
		return 0;
	}

	update_queue($app_obj, { @updates });

	mylog($detail);

	my $job_queue_notify_cmd = "$JOB_QUEUE_NOTIFY_CMD " . join(' ', map { "-group-id $_" } @GROUP_ID) . " -lookback-days $LOOKBACK_DAYS";
	system($job_queue_notify_cmd);

	return 1;
}

sub manage_reset($$) {
  my ($rq, $app_obj) = @_;

	my $rq_status = $rq->{RQ_STATUS};

	if (($rq_status ne 'COMPLETE') && ($rq_status ne 'ERROR')) {
		return 0;  # probably still PROCESSING or QUEUE
	}

	my $detail = 'Reset queued';

	update_queue($app_obj, {
		rq_status => 'QUEUE',
		rq_step => 'EXTRACT',
		rq_status_detail => $detail,
		rq_process_begin_date => '',
		rq_process_end_date => '',
		rq_step_notify_date => '',
		rq_step_begin_date => 'sysdate',
		rq_step_end_date => 'sysdate',
		rq_job_attempts => 0
	});

	my $job_queue_notify_cmd = "$JOB_QUEUE_NOTIFY_CMD " . join(' ', map { "-group-id $_" } @GROUP_ID) . " -lookback-days $LOOKBACK_DAYS";
	system($job_queue_notify_cmd);

	mylog($detail);
	return 1;
}


sub manage_extract($$) {
  my ($rq, $app_obj) = @_;

	my $rq_status = $rq->{RQ_STATUS};
	my @updates = ();

	if (($rq_status ne 'COMPLETE') && ($rq_status ne 'ERROR')) {
		return 0;  # probably still PROCESSING or QUEUE
	}

	my $detail;

	if ($rq_status eq 'COMPLETE') {
		my $dfa_dir = $app_obj->dfa_dir;

		if (($app_obj->qaqc() eq 'Y') && glob("$dfa_dir/*.dmp.gz")) {

			$detail = 'All data extracted. DataFeed Analyzer queued.';

			push(@updates,
				rq_step => 'DFA',
				rq_status => 'QUEUE',
				rq_step_begin_date => 'sysdate',
				rq_step_end_date => 'sysdate',
				rq_status_detail => $detail
			);
		} else {
			$detail = 'All data extracted. No DataFeed Analyzer needed.';
			push(@updates, rq_process_end_date => 'sysdate', rq_status_detail => $detail);
		}

		update_queue($app_obj, { @updates });
		mylog($detail);

		return 1;
	}

	if ($rq_status ne 'ERROR') {
		return 0;
	}

  my ($max_job_attempts, $job_attempts);

	if (defined($rq->{RQ_MAX_JOB_ATTEMPTS}) && $rq->{RQ_MAX_JOB_ATTEMPTS} >= 1) {
		$max_job_attempts = $rq->{RQ_MAX_JOB_ATTEMPTS};
	} else {
		$max_job_attempts = 1;
	}

	if (defined($rq->{RQ_JOB_ATTEMPTS}) && $rq->{RQ_JOB_ATTEMPTS} >= 1) {
		$job_attempts = $rq->{RQ_JOB_ATTEMPTS};
	} else {
		$job_attempts = 0;
	}

	if (($job_attempts >= $max_job_attempts) && ((! defined($rq->{RQ_RESUME})) || ($rq->{RQ_RESUME} !~ /^\s*Y\s*/i))) {
		# max attempts reached, and no resume requested
		return 0;
	}

	$detail = 'Retry queued';

	update_queue($app_obj, {
		rq_status => 'QUEUE',
		rq_status_detail => $detail,
		rq_process_begin_date => '',
		rq_process_end_date => '',
		rq_step_begin_date => 'sysdate',
		rq_step_end_date => 'sysdate'
	});

	mylog($detail);
	return 1;
}


sub manage_dfa($$) {
  my ($rq, $app_obj) = @_;

	my $rq_status = $rq->{RQ_STATUS};

	if (! (defined($rq_status) && ($rq_status eq 'ERROR'))) {
		return 0;
	}

	my $rq_resume = $rq->{RQ_RESUME};

	if (! (defined($rq_resume) && ($rq_resume =~ /^\s*Y\s*$/i))) {
		return 0;
	}

	my $detail = 'Failed DataFeed Analyzer queued for retry';

	update_queue($app_obj, {
		rq_status => 'QUEUE',
		rq_status_detail => $detail,
		rq_step_begin_date => 'sysdate',
		rq_step_end_date => 'sysdate',
		rq_resume => 'N'
	});

	mylog($detail);
	return 1;
}


sub Usage() {
	print "$PGM: manage job requests in job_queue table\n";
	print "\n";
	print "Usage: $PGM -group-id g [-group-id g ...] [-lookback-days #]\n";
}

#### Main ####

GetOptions(
            'group-id=s@' => \@GROUP_ID,
            'lookback-days=i' => \$LOOKBACK_DAYS,
) || exit(1);

if (@ARGV) {
	print STDERR "$PGM: Extraneous command-line arguments!\n";
	Usage;
	exit(1);
}

if (! @GROUP_ID) {
	Usage;
	exit(0);
}

my $requests = BLUELITE::Job->get_requests(
		add_where              => "rq_process_end_date is null",
		submission_search_days => $LOOKBACK_DAYS,
		group_id               => \@GROUP_ID,
		order_by               => 'rq_submitted_date'
);

foreach my $rq (@{$requests}) {
  my $app_id = $rq->{RQ_SOURCE_APP_ID};
  my $request_id = $rq->{RQ_REQUEST_ID};
  my $rq_step = $rq->{RQ_STEP};
  my $rq_status = $rq->{RQ_STATUS};
  my $rq_status_detail = $rq->{RQ_STATUS_DETAIL};

	my $app_obj;

	eval { $app_obj = BLUELITE::Job->new(app_id => $app_id, request_id => $request_id, force_log_init => 1) };

	if (! defined($app_obj)) {
		if (($rq_step eq 'VALIDATE') && ($rq_status eq 'ERROR') && ($rq_status_detail =~ /app.*id\s+.*n.*valid/i)) {
			my $rows = BLUELITE::Job->dbh->do("DELETE from job_queue WHERE rq_request_id = $request_id");
			print STDERR "Removed request ID $request_id due to: $rq_status_detail\n";
			BLUELITE::Job->dbh->commit;
		}

		next;
	}


  if (defined($rq->{RQ_RESET}) && ($rq->{RQ_RESET} =~ /^\s*Y\s*/i)) {
		print "calling reset for $app_id/$request_id\n" if (-t 1);
		manage_reset($rq, $app_obj);
	} elsif ($rq_step eq 'VALIDATE') {
		print "calling validate for $app_id/$request_id\n" if (-t 1);
		manage_validate($rq, $app_obj);
	} elsif ($rq_step eq 'EXTRACT') {
		print "calling extract for $app_id/$request_id\n" if (-t 1);
		manage_extract($rq, $app_obj);
	} elsif ($rq_step eq 'DFA') {
		print "calling dfa for $app_id/$request_id\n" if (-t 1);
		manage_dfa($rq, $app_obj);
	} else {
		print "didn't call anything for $app_id/$request_id\n" if (-t 1);
	}
}

my $process_queue_cmd = "$JOB_PROCESS_QUEUE_CMD " . join(' ', map { "-group-id $_" } @GROUP_ID) . " -lookback-days $LOOKBACK_DAYS";
print "cmd = $process_queue_cmd\n" if (-t 0);
exec($process_queue_cmd);


#job_process_queue
#!/usr/bin/perl

# Program: job_process_queue
# Purpose: Scan for and process incomplete Job pkg requests in job_queue table
#
# Note: As of October, 2014, this is initially intended to handle ad-hoc history extract
# requests based on existing established daily automated data feeds in the job_config table.
# The request entries in job_queue are placed there by a separate process which watches for,
# validates, and sets up on-demand requests initiated via incoming request files.
#
# This process will be scheduled to run via cron automatically every 5 minutes. Parallelism will be handled
# and limited via job_run/job_launcher by way of all requests being in the same group_id and the
# min_processes configuration for that group in the job_param_default_set table.

# 1) Search job_queue table for the highest priority requests that have not yet finished or started processing,
#    and have not yet hit the max # of job_run attempts.
# 2) If none found, do nothing and quietly exit.
# 3) Set request status to PROCESSING and attempt to process via job_run
# 4) If successful (exit 0), change status to WAITING_QA, send notification email, then exit.
# 5) If exited w/99, skip request and try next request (i.e. go back to step 3).
# 6) Set request status to PROCESSING_ERROR, increment job_attempts, send notification email, then exit.

# Note: "Highest priority" will initially mean just first come, first serve. However, future versions
# will likely have a more sophisticated definition (e.g. specific priority # could be provided in each
# request).
#
# 7/10/2015 - Remove '-keep-worker-files' from job_run call
#
# 5/12/2020 - Disable checking of Max Records during concatenation by adding -no-max-records-check option to job_run command line.

use Params::Validate qw(:all);
use Data::Dumper;
use BLUELITE::Job;
use Getopt::Long;
use File::Spec;
use File::PathConvert qw(rel2abs);

use warnings;
use strict;

our ($LOG_FH, $LOGFILE);
my @dir_parts = File::Spec->splitdir(rel2abs($0));
our $PGM = pop(@dir_parts);

#my $job_run_cmd = 'perl -I /ds/development/Job/dev/blib/lib /ds/development/Job/dev/job_run';
#my $df_report_cmd = 'perl -I /ds/development/DataFeed/Analyzer_v2.2/blib/lib -S df_report';

my $job_run_cmd = 'job_run';
my $df_report_cmd = 'df_report';

sub update_queue($$) {
  my ($app_obj, $updates) = @_;

	my $app_id = $app_obj->app_id;
	my $update_result = $app_obj->update_job_config( assignments => $updates);

	if ($update_result->{error}) {
		mylog("Could not update job_queue for $app_id : " . $update_result->{error} . "\n\nThe updates were: " . Dumper $updates);
	} else {
		$app_obj->commit;
	}
}


sub mylog($) {
  my $msg = shift;

	$msg =~ s/\n$//;
	$msg .= "\n";

	if (-t 0) {
		print $msg;
	}

	if (defined($LOG_FH)) {
		print $LOG_FH $msg;
	}
}


sub extract_step($$) {
	my ($rq, $app_obj) = @_;

	my $job_reset = 0;

	if (defined($rq->{RQ_RESET}) && ($rq->{RQ_RESET} =~ /^\s*Y\s*/i)) {
		$job_reset = 1;
	}

	# do not attempt if it has no post date range

	my $post_date = $rq->{RQ_POST_DATE};

	if ((! defined($post_date)) || ($post_date =~ /^\s*$/)) {
		return 0; # do not attempt
	}

	# attempt to process the request

	my $app_id = $rq->{RQ_SOURCE_APP_ID};
	my $request_id = $rq->{RQ_REQUEST_ID};
	my $job_attempts = $rq->{RQ_JOB_ATTEMPTS};
	my $max_attempts = $rq->{RQ_MAX_JOB_ATTEMPTS};

	if (! defined($job_attempts)) {
		$job_attempts = 0;
	}

	if (! defined($max_attempts)) {
		$max_attempts = 1;
	}

	# do not attempt if request id or app id is missing
	return 0 if ((! defined($request_id)) || ! defined($app_id));

	my $current_attempt_num = $job_attempts + 1;

	update_queue($app_obj, {
			rq_step => 'EXTRACT',
			rq_status => 'PROCESSING',
			rq_process_begin_date => 'sysdate',
			rq_step_begin_date => 'sysdate',
			rq_process_end_date => '',
			rq_step_end_date => '',
			rq_status_detail => "Extracting data (attempt $current_attempt_num)",
			rq_job_attempts => $current_attempt_num
	});

	my $job_run = "$job_run_cmd -app-id $app_id -request-id $request_id -post-date $post_date -screen-only -no-max-records-check";
	my $dfa_dir = $app_obj->dfa_dir;

	if ($job_reset || ($job_attempts == 0)) {
		$job_run .= ' -rerun';
		empty_dfa_dir($app_obj);
		remove_deliverable_files($app_obj);
	}

	if ($LOGFILE) {
		$job_run .= " >> $LOGFILE 2>&1";
	}

	mylog "Processing attempt # $current_attempt_num for $app_id\n";
	mylog "$job_run\n";

	my $ret = system($job_run);
	$ret = $ret >> 8;

	if ($ret == 99) {
		update_queue($app_obj, { rq_status => 'QUEUE', rq_process_begin_date => '', rq_step_begin_date => '', rq_status_detail => 'Wating to extract data', rq_job_attempts => $job_attempts});
		return 0; # did not attempt
	}

# make conditional reset/resume based on 99 return status

	my $updates = {
		RQ_STEP_END_DATE => 'sysdate',
		RQ_RESET => 'N',
		RQ_RESUME => 'N'
	};

	if ($ret == 0) {
		$updates->{RQ_STATUS} = 'COMPLETE';
		$updates->{RQ_STATUS_DETAIL} = 'All data extracted.';
	} else {
		$updates->{RQ_STATUS} = 'ERROR';
		my $attempts_remaining = $max_attempts - $current_attempt_num;

		if ($attempts_remaining < 0) {
			$attempts_remaining = 0;
		}

		my $detail = "job_run command failed. $attempts_remaining attempts remaining.";

		if ($LOGFILE) {
			$detail .= " See logfile for details: $LOGFILE";
		}

		$updates->{RQ_STATUS_DETAIL} = $detail;
	}

	update_queue($app_obj, $updates);

	return 1;
}


sub dfa_log_fname($) {
  my $app_obj = shift;
	my $dfa_log_fname;

	my $dfa_output_fname = dfa_output_fname($app_obj);

	if (defined($dfa_output_fname)) {
		$dfa_log_fname = $dfa_output_fname;
		$dfa_log_fname =~ s/\.[^.]+$//;
		$dfa_log_fname .= '.log';
	}

	return $dfa_log_fname;
}

sub dfa_output_fname($) {
  my $app_obj = shift;
	my $dfa_dir = $app_obj->dfa_dir;
	my $app_id = $app_obj->app_id;

	if (defined($dfa_dir)) {
		return "$dfa_dir/${app_id}.dfa.txt";
	}

	return undef;
}

sub empty_dfa_dir($) {
  my $app_obj = shift;

	my $dfa_dir = $app_obj->dfa_dir;

	if (defined($dfa_dir) && ($app_obj->qaqc() eq 'Y')) {
		unlink(glob("$dfa_dir/*.dmp.gz"), dfa_output_fname($app_obj));
	}
}

sub remove_deliverable_files($) {
  my $app_obj = shift;
	my $app_id = $app_obj->app_id;

	my $files = $app_obj->dbh->selectcol_arrayref("select delivery_output_file from job_delivery where app_id = '$app_id'");

	my @files_removed = grep { unlink($_) } @{$files};

	if (@files_removed) {
		mylog("Removed the following existing files: " . join(', ', @files_removed));
	}
}


sub dfa_step($$) {
	my ($rq, $app_obj) = @_;

	my $current_status = $rq->{RQ_STATUS};
	my $resume = $rq->{RQ_RESUME};

	if ($current_status ne 'QUEUE') {
		return 0;
	}

	my $detail = 'Running DataFeed Analyzer';
	mylog $detail;

	update_queue($app_obj, { rq_step => 'DFA', rq_step_begin_date => 'sysdate', rq_step_end_date => '', rq_status => 'PROCESSING', rq_status_detail => $detail});

	my $app_id = $app_obj->app_id;
	my $dfa_dir = $app_obj->dfa_dir;
	my $dfa_output_fname = dfa_output_fname($app_obj);
	my $report_opts = "";

	if (! opendir(DIR, $dfa_dir)) {
		my $message = "ERROR: Cannot open DFA dir $dfa_dir : $!";
		update_queue($app_obj, { rq_step_end_date => 'sysdate', rq_status => 'ERROR', rq_status_detail => $message});
		mylog($message);
		return 0;
	}

	my ($job_id, $current_job_id);

# change all DIEs to STDERR/return

	while (my $fname = readdir(DIR)) {
		if ($fname =~ /^([A-Z0-9_\-]+)_[0-9]{8,8}.*\.dmp\.gz$/) {
			$job_id = $1;

			if (defined($current_job_id) && ($job_id ne $current_job_id)) {
				my $message = "ERROR: Found more than one DFA job id in the $dfa_dir directory: $job_id, $current_job_id !";
				update_queue($app_obj, { rq_step_end_date => 'sysdate', rq_status => 'ERROR', rq_status_detail => $message});
				mylog($message);
				return 0;
			}

			$current_job_id = $job_id;
		}
	}

	if (! closedir(DIR)) { 
		my $message = "ERROR: Cannot close DFA dir $dfa_dir : $!";
		update_queue($app_obj, { rq_step_end_date => 'sysdate', rq_status => 'ERROR', rq_status_detail => $message});
		mylog($message);
		return 0;
	}

	if (! defined($job_id)) {
		my $message = "ERROR: Could not find any DFA files in the $dfa_dir directory!";
		update_queue($app_obj, { rq_step_end_date => 'sysdate', rq_status => 'ERROR', rq_status_detail => $message});
		mylog($message);
		return 0;
	}

	unlink($dfa_output_fname);
	unlink($LOGFILE) if ($LOGFILE);

	my $dfa_cmd = "$df_report_cmd -job_id $job_id -report_id CON -input_dir $dfa_dir > $dfa_output_fname";
	$dfa_cmd .= " 2>> $LOGFILE" if ($LOGFILE);

	my $ret = system($dfa_cmd);
	$ret = $ret >> 8;

	if (($ret != 0) || ! -s $dfa_output_fname) {
		my $message = "ERROR: DataFeed Analyzer failed: $dfa_cmd\n";
		$message .= " . See log file for details: $LOGFILE" if ($LOGFILE);
		update_queue($app_obj, { rq_step_end_date => 'sysdate', rq_status => 'ERROR', rq_status_detail => $message});
		mylog($message);
		return 1;
	}

	unlink(glob("$dfa_dir/*.dmp.gz"));

	update_queue($app_obj, {
		rq_step_end_date => 'sysdate',
		rq_process_end_date => 'sysdate',
		rq_status => 'COMPLETE',
		rq_status_detail => 'Extract and DataFeed Analyzer complete'
	});

	return 1;
}

sub Usage() {
	print "$PGM: find a queued job in job_queue table and process it\n";
	print "\n";
  print "Usage: $PGM -group-id g [-group-id g ...] [-lookback-days #]\n";
}


####### Main ######

my @group_id = ();
my $lookback_days = 21;

GetOptions('lookback-days=i' => \$lookback_days, 'group-id=s@' => \@group_id) || exit(1);

if (@ARGV) {
  print STDERR "$PGM: Extraneous command-line arguments!\n";
  Usage;
  exit(1);
}

if (! @group_id) {
  Usage;
  exit(0);
}


my $logging_to_file = ! -t 0;

# look for all recent requests that may need to be processed/resumed
my $requests = BLUELITE::Job->get_requests(
		add_where              => "rq_status = 'QUEUE' and rq_process_end_date IS NULL",
		submission_search_days => $lookback_days,
    group_id               => \@group_id,
		order_by               => 'rq_submitted_date'
);

my $step_attempted = 0;

foreach my $rq (@{$requests}) {

	my $app_id = $rq->{RQ_SOURCE_APP_ID};
	my $request_id = $rq->{RQ_REQUEST_ID};
	my $step = $rq->{RQ_STEP};
	my $post_date = $rq->{RQ_POST_DATE};
	my @job_opts = ();

	if ($logging_to_file) {
		$LOGFILE = "${step}.${app_id}.${post_date}.$$.log";
		push(@job_opts, logfile => $LOGFILE);
	}

	my $app_obj;
	eval { $app_obj = BLUELITE::Job->new(app_id => $app_id, request_id => $request_id, force_log_init => 1, @job_opts) };

	if (! defined($app_obj)) {
		mylog("Could not obtain a BLUELITE::Job object for app_id '$app_id' $@ !\n");
		next;
	}

	if ($logging_to_file) {
		my $base_logfile = $LOGFILE;
		$LOGFILE = $app_obj->logfile;

		if ( ! open($LOG_FH, ">> $LOGFILE")) {
			mylog("Could not open logfile $LOGFILE for append mode, app_id = $app_id, request_id = $request_id, base logfile = $base_logfile, step = $step : $!\n");
			next;
		}
	}

	if ($step eq 'EXTRACT') {
		$step_attempted = extract_step($rq, $app_obj);
	} elsif ($step eq 'DFA') {
		$step_attempted = dfa_step($rq, $app_obj);
	}

	if ($LOG_FH) {
		if (! close($LOG_FH)) {
			print STDERR "Could not close logfile $LOGFILE : $!\n";
		}
	}

	if ($step_attempted) {
		# Attempt no more than 1 step, then exit (do not change)
		last;
	}

	if ($LOG_FH) {
		unlink($LOGFILE);
	}
}


#job_queue_notify
#!/usr/bin/perl

# Program: job_queue_notify
# Purpose: Scan job_queue for new (email) notifications that need to be sent, and send them
# Version 6.2: Add request ids to email subject and only output attempt # in email if set

use Data::Dumper;
use BLUELITE::Job;
use Getopt::Long;
use File::Spec;
use File::PathConvert qw(rel2abs);

use warnings;
use strict;

my @dir_parts = File::Spec->splitdir(rel2abs($0));
our $PGM = pop(@dir_parts);

sub mylog($) {
  my $msg = shift;
  $msg =~ s/\n$//;
  $msg .= "\n";

  if (-t 0) {
    print  $msg;
  }
}

sub update_queue($$) {
  my ($app_obj, $updates) = @_;

	my $app_id = $app_obj->app_id;
  my $update_result = $app_obj->update_job_config( assignments => $updates);

  if ($update_result->{error}) {
    die "Could not update job_queue for $app_id : " . $update_result->{error} . "\n\nThe updates were: " . Dumper $updates;
  }
}

sub Usage() {
  print "$PGM: Send notifications for job_queue status changes\n";
  print "\n";
  print "Usage: $PGM -group-id g [-group-id g ...] [-lookback-days #]\n";
}

#### Main ####

my @group_id = ();
my $lookback_days = 21;

GetOptions(
            'group-id=s@' => \@group_id,
            'lookback-days=i' => \$lookback_days,
) || exit(1);

if (@ARGV) {
  print STDERR "$PGM: Extraneous command-line arguments!\n";
  Usage;
  exit(1);
}

if (! @group_id) {
  Usage;
  exit(0);
}


my $email_step_map = {
	VALIDATE => 'RQ_REQUESTER_EMAIL',
	EXTRACT => 'RQ_EXTRACT_EMAIL',
	DFA => 'RQ_DFA_EMAIL',
	DELIVERY => 'RQ_DELIVERY_EMAIL'
};

my $requests = BLUELITE::Job->get_requests(
		add_where              => "rq_step_notify_date < nvl(rq_step_end_date, rq_step_begin_date) or rq_step_notify_date is null",
		submission_search_days => $lookback_days,
    group_id               => \@group_id,
		order_by               => 'rq_submitted_date'
);

my %email_list;

foreach my $rq (@{$requests}) {
	my $app_id = $rq->{RQ_SOURCE_APP_ID};
	my $request_id = $rq->{RQ_REQUEST_ID};
	my $rq_step = $rq->{RQ_STEP};
	my $app_obj;

	eval { $app_obj = BLUELITE::Job->new(app_id => $app_id, request_id => $request_id, force_log_init => 1) };

	if (! defined($app_obj)) {
		next;
	}

	my @email_list;

	push(@email_list, $app_obj->{RQ_REQUESTER_EMAIL}, $app_obj->{$email_step_map->{$rq_step}});

	if ($rq->{RQ_STATUS} eq 'ERROR') {
		push(@email_list, $app_obj->failure_email);
	}

	my @rq_text;

	{
		no warnings 'uninitialized';

		@rq_text = (
				"           App ID: $rq->{RQ_SOURCE_APP_ID}",
				"     Reference ID: $rq->{RQ_REFERENCE_ID}",
				"       Request ID: $rq->{RQ_REQUEST_ID}",
				"        Post Date: $rq->{RQ_POST_DATE}",
				"     Current Step: $rq->{RQ_STEP}",
				"   Current Status: $rq->{RQ_STATUS}",
				"    Status detail: $rq->{RQ_STATUS_DETAIL}",
				"       Output dir: " . $app_obj->output_dir
		);
	}

	if (defined($rq->{RQ_JOB_ATTEMPTS})) {
		push(@rq_text, "Extract attempt #: $rq->{RQ_JOB_ATTEMPTS}");
	}

	if (defined($rq->{RQ_SUBMITTED_DATE})) {
		push(@rq_text, "        Submitted: $rq->{RQ_SUBMITTED_DATE}");
	}

	if (defined($rq->{RQ_STEP_BEGIN_DATE})) {
		push(@rq_text, "  Step begin date: $rq->{RQ_STEP_BEGIN_DATE}");
	}

	if (defined($rq->{RQ_STEP_END_DATE})) {
		push(@rq_text, "    Step end date: $rq->{RQ_STEP_END_DATE}");
	}

	if (defined($rq->{RQ_PROCESS_BEGIN_DATE})) {
		push(@rq_text, "    Process begin: $rq->{RQ_PROCESS_BEGIN_DATE}");
	}

	if (defined($rq->{RQ_PROCESS_END_DATE})) {
		push(@rq_text, "      Process end: $rq->{RQ_PROCESS_END_DATE}");
	}

	my $rq_text .= join("\n", @rq_text);

	foreach my $email (BLUELITE::Job->email_addresses(@email_list)) {
		if (defined($email)) {
			push(@{$email_list{lc($email)}}, { rq_text => "$rq_text", app_obj => $app_obj, rq_reference_id => $rq->{RQ_REFERENCE_ID}});
		}
	}
}

my @apps;

foreach my $email_to (keys %email_list) {
	my $email_info = $email_list{$email_to};
	my $body;

	my %rq_reference_ids;

	foreach my $rq_info (@{$email_list{$email_to}}) {
		$body .= $rq_info->{rq_text} . "\n\n";
		push(@apps, $rq_info->{app_obj});

		if (exists($rq_info->{rq_reference_id}) && defined($rq_info->{rq_reference_id})) {
			$rq_reference_ids{$rq_info->{rq_reference_id}} = undef;
		}
	}

	my $ref_ids_txt = join(',', keys %rq_reference_ids);
	
	mylog($body);
	BLUELITE::Job->email(to => $email_to, subject => "JobPkg Request Status ($ref_ids_txt)", msg => $body);
}

foreach my $app (@apps) {
	update_queue($app, { rq_step_notify_date => 'sysdate' });
	$app->commit;
}


#job_remove_post_date
#!/usr/bin/perl

use BLUELITE::Job;
use List::Util qw(min max);
use Data::Dumper;
use strict;
use warnings;

# Version 2.75 - 4/6/2011
#
# - Added support for flexible date specifications in -post-date option (ranges, months, etc).
# - Added interactive confirmation when more than 1 post date is requested for removal.
# - Added -no-confirm command line option in case this script ever needs to be used non-interactively.
#
# Version 4.7 - 4/17/2013
#
# - Added '-no-confirm' to usage display
#
# Version 6.0 - 10/31/2014
# - Added support for "autohoc" requests (i.e. automated on-demand ad-hoc processing).
#
# Version 6.2 - 5/27/2015
# - Exit with error status when remove_post_date method says something failed
#
# Version 6.4e - 12/8/2017
# - Added -log-level command-line option. Can use to disable outgoing email via "-log-level INFO".
#

our $PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s/.*\///g;

if (scalar(@ARGV) == 0) {
	print "$PGM: Completely remove entire post dates from the database for a specific BLUELITE::Job-based application.

This will remove all rows associated to the given application and post dates from the following tables:
JOB_WORKER, JOB_DELIVERY, JOB_DELIVERY_SEQ

Usage: $PGM [-no-confirm] [-log-level INFO|WARN|ERROR|FATAL] -app-id app_id -post-date pd_spec

Note: pd_spec may be a comma-separated list of any combination of the following syntaxes:

 YYYYMMDD
 YYYYMMDD-YYYYMMDD
 YYYYMM
 YYYYMM-YYYYMM
 YYYYMMDD-YYYYMM
 YYYYMM-YYYYMMDD
";
	exit(1);
}

use Getopt::Long;

my ($app_id, $post_date, $no_confirm, $request_id, $log_level);
my $confirm= 1;

GetOptions(
            'app-id=s' => \$app_id,
            'request-id=i' => \$request_id,
            'post-date=s' => \$post_date,
            'no-confirm' => \$no_confirm,
            'log-level=s' => \$log_level
) || exit(1);

$confirm = 0 if (defined($no_confirm));

die "$PGM: -app-id parameter not provided!\n" if (! defined($app_id));
die "$PGM: -post-date parameter not provided!\n" if (! defined($post_date));

my $post_date_list = BLUELITE::Job->post_date_list($post_date);
die "ERROR: Could not decipher post date of '$post_date'\n" if (! defined($post_date_list));

if ($confirm && (scalar(@{$post_date_list}) > 1)) {
	print "WARNING! This will remove up to " . scalar(@{$post_date_list}) . " post dates between " . min(@{$post_date_list}) . " and " . max(@{$post_date_list}) . "\n";
	print "ARE YOU SURE YOU WISH TO PROCEED? (y/N) : ";

	my $response = <STDIN>;

	if ($response !~ /^\s*(y|yes)\s*$/i) {
		print "Did not attempt to remove anything\n";
		exit(1);
	}
}

my @job_opts = (app_id => $app_id);

if (defined($request_id)) {
	push(@job_opts, request_id => $request_id);
}

my $job = BLUELITE::Job->new(@job_opts) || die "Could not obtain BLUELITE::Job object\n";

my @params = (post_date => $post_date_list, post_date_spec => $post_date);

if (defined($log_level)) {
	push(@params, log_type => $log_level);
}

my ($num_not_removed, $num_removed) = $job->remove_post_date(@params);

if ($num_not_removed) {
	print "$num_not_removed post dates could not be removed!\n";
	exit(1);
}

if (! $num_removed) {
	print "Nothing to remove\n";
}

exit(0);

#job_remove_workers
#!/usr/bin/perl

use BLUELITE::Job;
use Data::Dumper;
use strict;
use warnings;

#	job_remove_workers: Remove workers with the requested status from the JOB_WORKER table, as long as they have not been concatenated via the job_concat command. If no status is specified, only FAILED workers are removed. Use job_remove_post_date to remove already concatenated workers.
#
# 3/5/2014
#
# - Initial release
#
# Version 6.0 - 10/31/2014
# - Added support for "autohoc" requests (i.e. automated on-demand ad-hoc processing).
#

our $PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s/.*\///g;

if (scalar(@ARGV) == 0) {
	print "$PGM: Remove workers with the requested status from the JOB_WORKER table, as long as they have not been concatenated via the job_concat command. If no status is specified, only FAILED workers are removed. Use job_remove_post_date to remove already concatenated workers.

Usage: $PGM -app-id app_id -post-date pd_spec [-options]

Options:
   -request-id i
   -failed      {default if no other status specified}
   -completed
   -queued
   -processing
   -incomplete  {shorthand for every status except -completed}

Note: pd_spec may be a comma-separated list of any combination of the following syntaxes:

 YYYYMMDD
 YYYYMMDD-YYYYMMDD
 YYYYMM
 YYYYMM-YYYYMM
 YYYYMMDD-YYYYMM
 YYYYMM-YYYYMMDD
";
	exit(1);
}

use Getopt::Long;

my ($app_id, $request_id, $post_date);
my @status = ();
my $force = 0;
my $failed = 0;
my $completed = 0;
my $queued = 0;
my $processing = 0;
my $all = 0;
my $quick = 0;
my $incomplete = 0;

GetOptions(
            'app-id=s' => \$app_id,
            'request-id=i' => \$request_id,
            'post-date=s' => \$post_date,
						'failed' => \$failed,
						'completed' => \$completed,
						'queued' => \$queued,
						'processing' => \$processing,
						'all' => \$all,
						'incomplete' => \$incomplete,
            'force' => \$force,
            'quick' => \$quick
) || exit(1);

die "$PGM: -app-id parameter not provided!\n" if (! defined($app_id));
die "$PGM: -post-date parameter not provided!\n" if (! defined($post_date));
die "$PGM: Cannot combine -all option with -failed, -completed, -queued, -processing, or -incomplete options\n" if ($all && ($failed || $completed || $queued || $processing || $incomplete));
die "$PGM: Cannot combine -incomplete option with -failed, -completed, -queued, or -processing options\n" if ($incomplete && ($failed || $completed || $queued || $processing || $all));

my @opts = ();
if (defined($request_id)) {
	push(@opts, request_id => $request_id);
}

my $job = BLUELITE::Job->new(app_id => $app_id, @opts) || die "Could not obtain BLUELITE::Job object\n";

my @remove_opts = (post_date => $post_date);

push(@status, 'FAILED') if ($failed || $all || $incomplete);
push(@status, 'COMPLETED') if ($completed || $all);
push(@status, 'QUEUED') if ($queued || $all || $incomplete);
push(@status, 'PROCESSING') if ($processing || $all || $incomplete);

@status = ('FAILED') if (! @status);
push(@remove_opts, status => \@status);

push(@remove_opts, quick => $quick) if ($quick);

if ($force) {
	push(@remove_opts, force => $force);
  print "WARNING! This will remove all unconcatenated $app_id workers for $post_date with status " . join(', ', @status) . ", even if they recently changed to QUEUED or PROCESSING status (i.e. they MIGHT still be running or in the queue of an already-running job_launcher)!\nYou should manually verify that this is safe before proceeding (i.e. make sure the job_launcher and all of it's workers are no longer running).\n";
  print "ARE YOU SURE YOU WISH TO PROCEED? (y/N) : ";

  my $response = <STDIN>;

  if ($response !~ /^\s*(y|yes)\s*$/i) {
    print "Did not attempt to remove anything\n";
    exit(1);
  }
}

print "Please wait...\n" unless $quick;

my ($workers_removed, $files_removed) = $job->remove_workers(@remove_opts);

if ($workers_removed) {
	print "Removed $workers_removed workers and $files_removed worker files.\n";
} else {
	print "No unconcatenated workers with " . join(', ', @status) . " status within post date $post_date\n";
}


#job_reset_concat
#!/usr/bin/perl

use BLUELITE::Job;
use List::Util qw(min max);
use Data::Dumper;
use strict;
use warnings;

# Version 2.75 - 4/6/2011
#
# - Added support for flexible date specifications in -post-date option (ranges, months, etc).
# - Added interactive confirmation when more than 1 post date is requested for reset.
# - Added -no-confirm command line option in case this script ever needs to be used non-interactively.
#
# Version 6.0 - 10/31/2014
# - Added support for "autohoc" requests (i.e. automated on-demand ad-hoc processing).
#

our $PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s/.*\///g;

if (scalar(@ARGV) == 0) {
	print "$PGM: Reset concatenation/deliverable info in the database for specific post dates and app_id (+ optional request_id).

This will remove all rows associated to the given application and post date from the
JOB_DELIVERY and JOB_DELIVERY_SEQ tables, and will disassociate all related workers
in the JOB_WORKER table from any concatenated deliverables.

Usage: $PGM -app-id a [-request-id #] -post-date pd_spec

Note: pd_spec may be a comma-separated list of any combination of the following syntaxes:

 YYYYMMDD
 YYYYMMDD-YYYYMMDD
 YYYYMM
 YYYYMM-YYYYMM
 YYYYMMDD-YYYYMM
 YYYYMM-YYYYMMDD
";
	exit(1);
}

use Getopt::Long;

my ($app_id, $post_date, $no_confirm, $request_id);
my $confirm = 1;

GetOptions(
            'app-id=s' => \$app_id,
            'request-id=i' => \$request_id,
            'post-date=s' => \$post_date,
            'no-confirm' => \$no_confirm
) || exit(1);

$confirm = 0 if (defined($no_confirm));

die "$PGM: -app-id parameter not provided!\n" if (! defined($app_id));

my @job_params = (app_id => $app_id);
push(@job_params, request_id => $request_id) if (defined($request_id));

my $job = BLUELITE::Job->new(@job_params) || die "Could not obtain BLUELITE::Job object\n";

if (defined($request_id)) {
	die "$PGM: Cannot provide -post-date parameter when using -request-id!\n" if (defined($post_date));

	$post_date = $job->{RQ_POST_DATE};
}

die "$PGM: -post-date parameter not provided!\n" if (! defined($post_date));

my $post_date_list = BLUELITE::Job->post_date_list($post_date);
die "ERROR: Could not decipher post date of '$post_date'\n" if (! defined($post_date_list));

if ($confirm && (scalar(@{$post_date_list}) > 1)) {
  print "WARNING! This will reset concatenation for up to " . scalar(@{$post_date_list}) . " post dates between " . min(@{$post_date_list}) . " and " . max(@{$post_date_list}) . "\n";
  print "ARE YOU SURE YOU WISH TO PROCEED? (y/N) : ";

  my $response = <STDIN>;

  if ($response !~ /^\s*(y|yes)\s*$/i) {
    print "Did not attempt to reset anything\n";
    exit(1);
  }
}

if ($job->reset_concat(post_date => $post_date_list, post_date_spec => $post_date)) {
	if (defined($request_id)) {
		$job->update_job_config(assignments => { rq_resume => 'Y', rq_process_end_date => '', rq_step => 'EXTRACT', rq_status => 'QUEUE', rq_status_detail => 'Queued by job_concat_reset for re-concatenation'});
	}

  $job->commit;
} else {
  print "No concatenations to reset\n";
}


#job_run
#!/usr/bin/perl

use BLUELITE::Job;
use Data::Dumper;
#use autodie qw(:all); # so that CTRL-C also kills this script during system() calls
use strict;
use warnings;

#	job_run: Invoke job_launcher and job_concat for all requested post dates
#
# 2/27/2014
#
# - Initial release
#
# 8/7/2014 - Version 5.2
# - Added call to detect_long_work_units() method just before calling ready() method. This causes
# the status of non-running work units in the PROCESSING status to change to FAILED status so they
# can be retried.
#
# - Added -no-max-records-check command line option, to be passed down to job_concat when used
#
# - When -daily option is used, post dates are now removed one at a time prior to each launch call
# instead of all dates being removed prior to the first launch.
#
# Version 6.0 - 10/31/2014
# - Added support for "autohoc" requests (i.e. automated on-demand ad-hoc processing).
#
# Version 6.2 - 5/26/2015
# - Accomodate additional return value from remove_post_date method

our $PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s/.*\///g;

if (scalar(@ARGV) == 0) {
	print "$PGM: Invoke job_launcher and job_concat for all requested post dates

Usage: $PGM -app-id app_id -post-date pd_spec [-options]

Options:
  -rerun                 Process post dates even if ALREADY processed (unconditionally runs job_remove_post_date)
  -request-id #          Process existing request in job_queue table
  -daily                 Run job_launcher/job_concat cycles 1 post date at a time
  -keep-log              Keep both job_launcher and job_concat logfiles, even if no errors are encountered
  -keep-concat-log       Keep job_concat logfiles, even if no errors are encountered
  -span-post-dates       Do NOT limit each output file to 1 post date (1 post date per file)
  -keep-launcher-log     Keep job_launcher logfiles, even if no errors are encountered
  -keep-worker-files     Preserve worker files after concatenation
  -mark-delivered        Mark concatenated output as 'delivered'
  -no-max-records-check  Do NOT check for violation of max # of output records (max records checked)
                         {in production, use only with management approval}

Note: pd_spec may be a comma-separated list of any combination of the following syntaxes:

 YYYYMMDD
 YYYYMMDD-YYYYMMDD
 YYYYMM
 YYYYMM-YYYYMM
 YYYYMMDD-YYYYMM
 YYYYMM-YYYYMMDD
";
	exit(1);
}

use Getopt::Long;

my ($APP_ID, $post_date_spec);
our $RERUN = 0;
our $KEEP_LOG = 0;
our $KEEP_CONCAT_LOG = 0;
our $KEEP_LAUNCH_LOG = 0;
our $SCREEN_ONLY = 0;
our $KEEP_WORKER_FILES = 0;
our $MARK_DELIVERED = 0;
my $daily = 0;
our $SPAN_POST_DATES = 0;
our $NO_MAX_RECORDS_CHECK = 0;
our ($REQUEST_ID, $WORKER_OPTS);

GetOptions(
            'app-id=s' => \$APP_ID,
            'request-id=i' => \$REQUEST_ID,
            'post-date=s' => \$post_date_spec,
            'rerun' => \$RERUN,
            'daily' => \$daily,
            'keep-log' => \$KEEP_LOG,
            'screen-only' => \$SCREEN_ONLY,
            'keep-concat-log' => \$KEEP_CONCAT_LOG,
            'span-post-dates' => \$SPAN_POST_DATES,
            'keep-launch-log' => \$KEEP_LAUNCH_LOG,
            'keep-worker-files' => \$KEEP_WORKER_FILES,
            'mark-delivered' => \$MARK_DELIVERED,
            'no-max-records-check' => \$NO_MAX_RECORDS_CHECK,
            'worker-opts=s' => \$WORKER_OPTS,
) || exit(1);

die "$PGM: -app-id parameter not provided!\n" if (! defined($APP_ID));
die "$PGM: -post-date parameter not provided!\n" if (! defined($post_date_spec));
die "$PGM: -span-post-dates cannot be used with -daily option!\n" if ($SPAN_POST_DATES && $daily);

$KEEP_LAUNCH_LOG = 1 if ($KEEP_LOG);
$KEEP_CONCAT_LOG = 1 if ($KEEP_LOG);

my @obj_options = ();

if (defined($REQUEST_ID)) {
	push(@obj_options, request_id => $REQUEST_ID);
}

our $JOB = BLUELITE::Job->new(app_id => $APP_ID, @obj_options) || die "Could not obtain BLUELITE::Job object\n";

# use span-post-dates mechanism to support output scope=ALL if not requested on command line
my $output_scope = $JOB->output_scope;

if ((! $SPAN_POST_DATES) && ($output_scope eq 'ALL')) {
	$SPAN_POST_DATES = 1;
}

my $post_dates = $JOB->post_date_list($post_date_spec);

# todo: swap these back for production
#my $launcher = 'perl -I /ds/development/Job/dev/blib/lib /ds/development/Job/dev/job_launcher';
#my $concat = 'perl -I /ds/development/Job/dev/blib/lib /ds/development/Job/dev/job_concat';
my $launcher = 'job_launcher';
my $concat = 'job_concat';

sub elapsed_min($) {
  my $curr_time = time;
	my $prev_time = shift;

	return sprintf('%.1f', ($curr_time - $prev_time) / 60);
}

sub mylog($) {
  my $msg = shift;
	chomp($msg);
	my $ltime = localtime;

	print "$ltime - $msg\n";
}

sub unconcatenated_dates($@) {
 my ($post_date_spec, @post_dates) = @_;

 my @unconcatenated_dates = ();

 if ($SPAN_POST_DATES) {
		my $post_date_spec_alt = $post_date_spec;
		$post_date_spec_alt =~ s/,/_/g;

		my $concat_history = $JOB->get_delivery_history(recent_post_dates => 1, post_date_spec => $post_date_spec_alt, delivery_type => 'DATA');

		if (! @{$concat_history}) {
			return ($post_date_spec);
		}
	} else {
	 foreach my $post_date (sort @post_dates) {
		my $concat_history = $JOB->get_delivery_history(recent_post_dates => 1, max_post_date => $post_date, delivery_type => 'DATA');

		if (! @{$concat_history}) {
			push(@unconcatenated_dates, $post_date);
		}
	 }
	}

 return @unconcatenated_dates;
}

sub concat($@) {
 my ($post_date_spec, @post_dates) = @_;

 if (! unconcatenated_dates($post_date_spec, @post_dates)) {
	mylog("All " . scalar(@post_dates) . " post dates in $post_date_spec have already been concatenated. job_concat was not needed.");
	return 0;  # already concatenated (success)
 }

 my ($msg, $time0);

	my $cmd = "$concat -app-id $APP_ID -post-date $post_date_spec";
	$cmd .= " -request-id $REQUEST_ID" if (defined($REQUEST_ID));
	$cmd .= ' -keep-log' if ($KEEP_CONCAT_LOG);
	$cmd .= ' -keep-worker-files' if ($KEEP_WORKER_FILES);
	$cmd .= ' -mark-delivered' if ($MARK_DELIVERED);
	$cmd .= ' -span-post-dates' if ($SPAN_POST_DATES);
	$cmd .= ' -no-max-records-check' if ($NO_MAX_RECORDS_CHECK);
	$cmd .= " -screen-only" if ($SCREEN_ONLY);

	mylog("Concatenation attempt: $cmd");
	$time0 = time;

	system($cmd);

 my @missing_post_dates = unconcatenated_dates($post_date_spec, @post_dates);

 if (@missing_post_dates) {
	mylog("The following " . scalar(@missing_post_dates) . " post dates have not yet been concatenated!:\n" . join(',', @missing_post_dates));
	return 2;  # concat problem
 } else {
	mylog("All " . scalar(@post_dates) . " post dates in $post_date_spec are now concatenated");
	return 0;  # success
 }

}


sub launch($@) {
 my ($post_date_spec, @post_dates) = @_;
 my ($msg, $time0);
 my @dates_to_launch = ();

 POST_DATE:
 foreach my $post_date (sort @post_dates) {
	my $concat_history = $JOB->get_delivery_history(recent_post_dates => 1, max_post_date => $post_date, delivery_type => 'DATA');

	if (@{$concat_history}) {
		if (! $RERUN) {
			# Skipping $post_date since it is already concatenated
			next POST_DATE;
		} else {
			$msg = "Concatenation record for $post_date exists, even though it was previously removed due to the -rerun option!";
			print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: $msg\n";
			return 1;  # launch problem
		}
	}

	my $num_workers_running_long = $JOB->detect_long_work_units(begin_post_date => $post_date);

	if ($num_workers_running_long) {
		return 99;
	}

	my $ready_to_launch = $JOB->ready(enqueue => 0, post_date => $post_date);

#print "\ngot back $ready_to_launch\n" if (defined($ready_to_launch));

	if (! defined($ready_to_launch)) {
		my $num_incomplete = scalar($JOB->incomplete_workers(post_date => $post_date));

		if ($num_incomplete) {
			$msg = "No workers are ready to launch for $post_date because $num_incomplete remain in an incomplete state. Use 'job_remove_workers -app-id $APP_ID -post-date $post_date -incomplete' to fix and then retry.";
			print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: $msg\n";
			return 1;  # launch problem
		}

		next POST_DATE;
	}

	if ($ready_to_launch eq 'STILL_RUNNING') {
		return 99;
	}

	push(@dates_to_launch, $post_date);
 }

 if (@dates_to_launch) {
	my $time_start = time;

	for(my $attempt_num = 0; $attempt_num <= ($JOB->worker_retry_attempts() + 1); $attempt_num++) {
		if ($attempt_num == ($JOB->worker_retry_attempts() + 1)) {
			print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: unprocessed work units remain after $attempt_num launch attempts\n";
			return 1;  # launch problem
		}

		my $cmd = "$launcher -app-id $APP_ID -post-date $post_date_spec";
		$cmd .= " -request-id $REQUEST_ID" if (defined($REQUEST_ID));
		$cmd .= ' -keep-log' if ($KEEP_LAUNCH_LOG);
		$cmd .= " -worker-opts '$WORKER_OPTS'" if ($WORKER_OPTS);
		$cmd .= " -screen-only" if ($SCREEN_ONLY);

		mylog("Launch attempt #" . ($attempt_num + 1) . " : $cmd");

		$time0 = time;
		my $ret = system($cmd);
		$ret = $ret >> 8;

		if ($ret == 99) {
			return $ret;  # too many workers already running for this app or group
		}

		mylog("Launch attempt #" . ($attempt_num + 1) . " for $post_date_spec completed in " . elapsed_min($time0) . " minutes");

		my $ready_to_launch = $JOB->ready(enqueue => 0, post_date => \@dates_to_launch);

		if (defined($ready_to_launch) && ($ready_to_launch eq 'STILL_RUNNING')) {
			return 99;
		}

		if ((! defined($ready_to_launch)) || ($ready_to_launch ne 'READY')) {
			foreach my $post_date (@dates_to_launch) {
				my $num_incomplete = scalar($JOB->incomplete_workers(post_date => $post_date));

				if ($num_incomplete) {
					$msg = "No workers are ready to launch for $post_date because $num_incomplete remain in an incomplete state. Use 'job_remove_workers -app-id $APP_ID -post-date $post_date -incomplete' to fix and then retry.";
					print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: $msg\n";
					return 1;  # launch problem
				}
			}

			last;
		}
	}

	mylog("Completed launchers for " . scalar(@dates_to_launch) . " post dates in $post_date_spec in " . elapsed_min($time_start) . " minutes");

 } else {
	mylog("All workers for all " . scalar(@post_dates) . " post dates in $post_date_spec have already completed successfully. job_launcher was not needed.");
 }

	return 0;  # success
}


sub cycle_daily($@) {
 my ($post_date_spec, @post_dates) = @_;
 my ($msg, $time0);

 POST_DATE:
 foreach my $post_date (sort @post_dates) {

	if ($RERUN) {
		remove_post_dates($post_date, $post_date);
	}

	my $concat_history = $JOB->get_delivery_history(recent_post_dates => 1, max_post_date => $post_date, delivery_type => 'DATA');

	if (@{$concat_history}) {
		if (! $RERUN) {
			mylog("Skipping $post_date since it is already concatenated");
			next POST_DATE;
		} else {
			$msg = "Concatenation record for $post_date exists, even though it was previously removed due to the -rerun option!";
			print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: $msg\n";
			return 1;  # launch problem
		}
	}

	LAUNCH:
	for(my $attempt_num = 0; $attempt_num <= ($JOB->worker_retry_attempts() + 1); $attempt_num++) {
		my $ready_to_launch = $JOB->ready(enqueue => 0, post_date => $post_date);

		if (! defined($ready_to_launch)) {
			my $num_incomplete = scalar($JOB->incomplete_workers(post_date => $post_date));

			if ($num_incomplete) {
				$msg = "No workers are ready to launch for $post_date because $num_incomplete remain in an incomplete state. Use 'job_remove_workers -app-id $APP_ID -post-date $post_date -incomplete' to fix and then retry.";
				print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: $msg\n";
				return 1;  # launch problem
			}

			if ($attempt_num == 0) {
				if (! $RERUN) {
					mylog("No workers to launch for $post_date");
				} else {
					$msg = "Even though the -rerun option was used, there are no workers ready for the 1st attempt to launch $post_date";
					print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: $msg\n";
					return 1;  # launch problem
				}
			}

			last LAUNCH;
		}

		if ($attempt_num == ($JOB->worker_retry_attempts() + 1)) {
			print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: unprocessed work units remain for $post_date after $attempt_num launch attempts\n";
			return 1;  # launch problem
		}

		my $cmd = "$launcher -app-id $APP_ID -post-date $post_date";
		$cmd .= " -request-id $REQUEST_ID" if (defined($REQUEST_ID));
		$cmd .= ' -keep-log' if ($KEEP_LAUNCH_LOG);
		$cmd .= " -worker-opts '$WORKER_OPTS'" if ($WORKER_OPTS);
		$cmd .= " -screen-only" if ($SCREEN_ONLY);

		mylog("Launch attempt #" . ($attempt_num + 1) . " : $cmd");

		$time0 = time;
		my $ret = system($cmd);
		$ret = $ret >> 8;

		if ($ret == 99) {
			return $ret;  # too many workers already running for this app or group
		}

		mylog("Launch attempt #" . ($attempt_num + 1) . " for $post_date completed in " . elapsed_min($time0) . " minutes");
	}

	my $cmd = "$concat -app-id $APP_ID -post-date $post_date";
	$cmd .= " -request-id $REQUEST_ID" if (defined($REQUEST_ID));
	$cmd .= ' -keep-log' if ($KEEP_CONCAT_LOG);
	$cmd .= ' -keep-worker-files' if ($KEEP_WORKER_FILES);
	$cmd .= ' -mark-delivered' if ($MARK_DELIVERED);
	$cmd .= ' -span-post-dates' if ($SPAN_POST_DATES);
	$cmd .= " -screen-only" if ($SCREEN_ONLY);

	mylog("Concatenation attempt: $cmd");
	$time0 = time;

	system($cmd);

	$concat_history = $JOB->get_delivery_history(recent_post_dates => 1, max_post_date => $post_date, delivery_type => 'DATA');

	if (! @{$concat_history}) {
		print STDERR "$PGM: ERROR: Could not concatenate $post_date !\n";
		return 2;  # concat problem
	}

	mylog("Completed $post_date concatenation in " . elapsed_min($time0) . " minutes");
 }

	return 0;  # success
}

sub remove_post_dates($@) {
  my ($post_date_spec, @post_dates) = @_;

	my ($time0, $msg);
	$time0 = time;

	my $post_date_list = \@post_dates;
	my ($post_dates_not_removed, $post_dates_removed) = $JOB->remove_post_date(post_date => $post_date_list, post_date_spec => $post_date_spec);

	foreach my $post_date (sort @{$post_date_list}) {
		my $concat_history = $JOB->get_delivery_history(recent_post_dates => 1, max_post_date => $post_date, delivery_type => 'DATA');

		if (@{$concat_history}) {
			my $msg = "The -rerun option was used, but the concatenation record for $post_date was not removed for some reason!";
			die "$PGM: ERROR: $msg\n";
		}
	}

	mylog("Completed removing $post_dates_removed post dates in " . elapsed_min($time0) . " minutes\n");
}


### main ###

if ($daily) {
	exit(cycle_daily($post_date_spec, @{$post_dates}));
} else {

	if ($RERUN) {
		remove_post_dates($post_date_spec, @{$post_dates});
	}
	my $ret = launch($post_date_spec, @{$post_dates});

	if ($ret != 0) {
		exit($ret);
	}

	exit(concat($post_date_spec, @{$post_dates}));
}


#job_setup
#!/usr/bin/perl

# Program: job_setup - Create directories, template scripts, and add job_config row for new BLUELITE::Job application
# Author: John Hess, RelayHealth

# Version 1.0 - 5/10/2011
# Initial release
#
# Version 4.0 - 8/17/2011
# Reduced # of parameters with defaults, to bring into alignment with new job_param_default view.
# Changed app_dir setting in job_config table to relative path.
#

use Getopt::Long;
use File::Path qw(mkpath);
use File::Copy;
use Fcntl qw( :mode );
use DateTime;
use BLUELITE::Job;
use Data::Dumper;

use strict;
use warnings;

our $PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s/^[.\/]+//;

our $APP_DIR;
our $WARN_EMAIL;

sub Usage() {
	print "$PGM: Setup new BLUELITE::Job application\n\n";
	print "Usage: $PGM -app-id app_id [-options]\n";
	print "Options (with defaults):\n";
	print "  -subdir subdir   Create in $APP_DIR/app_id/subdir ($APP_DIR/app_id)\n";
	print "  -dir dir         Create in dir ($APP_DIR/app_id)\n";
	print "  -warn-email e    Set warning_email address to e\n";
	print "  -? | -help       Display this help\n";
}


sub copy_scripts($$$) {
  my $meta = shift;
  my $worker_script = shift;
  my $wrapper_script = shift;

	if (exists($meta->{SCRIPT})) {
		my $source_dir = $meta->{SCRIPT}->{source_dir};

		if (-d $source_dir) {
			my $bin_dir = "$APP_DIR/bin";
			my $wrapper_script_source = "$source_dir/" . $meta->{SCRIPT}->{wrapper};
			my $extract_script_source = "$source_dir/" . $meta->{SCRIPT}->{extract};

			if (-f $wrapper_script_source) {
				if (-f $extract_script_source) {
					my $output_worker = "$bin_dir/$worker_script";
					my $perms = S_IRWXU | S_IRGRP | S_IXGRP;
					if (copy($extract_script_source, $output_worker)) {
						chmod $perms, $output_worker;
					} else {
						print STDERR "Warning: unable to copy extract script '$extract_script_source' to $bin_dir : $!\n";
					}

					my $output_wrapper = "$bin_dir/$wrapper_script";

					if (system("sed 's/app_extract[.]pl/$worker_script/g' $wrapper_script_source > $output_wrapper") != 0) {
						print STDERR "Warning: unable to copy extract wrapper script '$wrapper_script_source' to $bin_dir : $!\n";
					} else {
						chmod $perms, $output_wrapper;
					}
				} else {
					print STDERR "Warning: the extract script '$extract_script_source' does not exist\n";
				}
			} else {
				print STDERR "Warning: the extract wrapper script '$wrapper_script_source' does not exist\n";
			}
		} else {
			print STDERR "Warning: the source template script directory '$source_dir' does not exist\n";
		}
	}
}


my ($help, $app_id, $subdir, $dir);
my $env = BLUELITE::Job->env;

my $first_post_date = DateTime->today(time_zone => 'local')->subtract(days => 1)->ymd('');
my $max_run_date = DateTime->today(time_zone => 'local')->add(months => 3)->ymd('');
my $base_dir = $ENV{DS_BASE_DIR};

my %meta = (
	ENV => {
		DEV => {
			root_app_dir => "$base_dir/development/data_feeds",
			root_outgoing_dir => "$base_dir/outgoing/development"
		},

		ADHOC => {
			root_app_dir => "$base_dir/adhocs",
			root_outgoing_dir => "$base_dir/outgoing/adhocs"
		}
	},
	SCRIPT => {
		source_dir => "$base_dir/common/etc/job",
		extract => "app_extract.pl",
		wrapper => "app_extract.sh"
	}
);

my %config_app = ();
my $outgoing_dir;

if (exists($meta{ENV}->{$env})) {
	$APP_DIR = $meta{ENV}->{$env}->{root_app_dir} if (exists($meta{ENV}->{$env}->{root_app_dir}));
	$outgoing_dir = $meta{ENV}->{$env}->{root_outgoing_dir} if (exists($meta{ENV}->{$env}->{root_outgoing_dir}));
} else {
