	die "ERROR: The '$env' environment is not recognized\n";
}

my $ret = GetOptions(
	'help|?' => \$help,
	'app-id=s' => \$app_id,
	'subdir=s' => \$subdir,
	'dir=s' => \$dir,
	'warn-email=s' => \$WARN_EMAIL
);

if (! $ret) {
	print STDERR "Could not parse command-line options\n";
	Usage;
	exit(2);
}

if (defined($help)) {
	Usage;
	exit(0);
}

eval "use BLUELITE::Job";

if ($@) {
	print STDERR "The Data Services environment was not properly sourced!\n";
	print STDERR $@ . "\n\n";
	Usage;
	exit(2);
}

if (! defined($app_id)) {
	Usage;
	exit(1);
}

$app_id =~ s/^\s+//g;
$app_id =~ s/\s+$//g;
$app_id = uc($app_id);
my $app_id_lc = lc($app_id);

if (defined($dir) && defined($subdir)) {
	die "ERROR: The -dir and -subdir options are mutually exclusive!\n";
}

my ($app_symlink_to, $app_symlink_from);

$APP_DIR .= "/$app_id_lc";
my $config_app_dir = $APP_DIR;
my $config_app_dir_setting = $app_id_lc;

$outgoing_dir .= "/$app_id_lc" if (defined($outgoing_dir));

if (defined($subdir)) {
	$subdir =~ s|^\s+||;
	$subdir =~ s|\s+$||;
	$subdir =~ s|^\.?/||;
	$subdir =~ s|/+$||;

	$config_app_dir = "$APP_DIR/dev";
	$config_app_dir_setting = "$app_id_lc/dev";
	$APP_DIR .= "/$subdir";
	$app_symlink_to = $config_app_dir;
	$app_symlink_from = $subdir;
} elsif (defined($dir)) {
	$APP_DIR = $dir;
	$config_app_dir_setting = $APP_DIR;
	$outgoing_dir = undef;
}

my %config_opts = ();

if (-d $APP_DIR) {
	die "ERROR: The application directory '$APP_DIR' already exists!\n";
}

$config_app{app_dir} = $config_app_dir_setting;
my $worker_script = "${app_id_lc}_extract.pl";
my $wrapper_script = "${app_id_lc}_extract.sh";

my %config_defaults = (
	deliverable_encoding => 'gzip',
	group_id_order => 999,
	first_post_date => $first_post_date,
	max_run_date => $max_run_date,
	worker_script => $wrapper_script,
	trigger_fname_sprintf => "${app_id}_%s.dat.done.gz", trigger_fname_vars => 'post_date', trigger_encoding => 'gzip',
	deliverable_fname_sprintf => "${app_id}_%s.dat.gz", deliverable_fname_vars => 'post_date',
	warn_notify_email => $WARN_EMAIL
);

if (! BLUELITE::Job->new_app_config(app_id => $app_id, defaults => \%config_defaults, %config_app)) {
	die "ERROR: Could not add new app_id '$app_id'\n";
}

# create directories

my @created_dirs = ();
my @links_created = ();

my @subdirs = qw(bin wu log worker);
push(@subdirs, 'deliverables') if (! defined($outgoing_dir));

foreach my $dir (@subdirs) {
	my $dir_to_create = "$APP_DIR/$dir";

	if (! mkpath($dir_to_create)) {
		map { rmdir($_) } (@created_dirs, $APP_DIR);
		die "Could not create application directory '$dir_to_create' : $!\n";
	}

	push(@created_dirs, $dir_to_create);
}

# create deliverables dir with symlink, if appropriate

if (defined($outgoing_dir)) {
	if (! -d $outgoing_dir) {
		if (! eval { mkpath($outgoing_dir) }) {
			map { rmdir($_) } (@created_dirs, $APP_DIR);
			die "ERROR: Could not create outgoing directory '$outgoing_dir' : $@\n";
		}

		push(@created_dirs, $outgoing_dir);
	}

	my $deliverables_link_to = "$APP_DIR/deliverables";

	if (! symlink($outgoing_dir, $deliverables_link_to)) {
		map { rmdir($_) } (@created_dirs, $APP_DIR);
		die "ERROR: Could not create symbolic link to $outgoing_dir : $!\n";
	} else {
		push(@links_created, $deliverables_link_to);
	}
}

if (defined($app_symlink_to)) {
	if (! symlink($app_symlink_from, $app_symlink_to)) {
		unlink(@links_created);
		map { rmdir($_) } (@created_dirs, $APP_DIR);
		die "ERROR: Could not create symbolic link to $app_symlink_to : $!\n";
	}
}

# copy template scripts to bin dir

copy_scripts(\%meta, $worker_script, $wrapper_script);

# commit database insert

eval { BLUELITE::Job->dbh->commit };

# remove created dirs if commit failed

if ($@) {
	print STDERR "$@\n";
	map { rmdir($_) } (@created_dirs, $APP_DIR);
}

# display info about what was setup

print "Added -app-id '$app_id' to the $env environment:\n";
print "	app_dir=$APP_DIR\n";
print "	first_post_date=$first_post_date\n";
print "	max_run_date=$max_run_date\n";
print "	warn_notify_email=$WARN_EMAIL\n" if (defined($WARN_EMAIL));



#job_status
#!/usr/bin/env python3

# Program: job_status - Report current status of Data Services Job package data feeds
# Author: John Hess, RelayHealth

# Version 1.0 - 11/4/2010
# Initial release (perl implementation)
#
# Version 1.1 - 5/10/2011
# - An app will now automatically be forced to red if it has been yellow (due to ERROR) for at least 3 hours (by default)
# - Added -max-yellow-minutes command-line option
# - Overall status will be forced to red if too many apps are currently in yellow status
# - Added -max-yellow-apps and -max-pct-yellow-apps command-line options (default of 4 apps and 20% of apps)
# - When running in bigbrother mode, each message in MESSAGE column is limited to 800 characters (by default)
# - Added -max-message-length command-line option (for bigbrother mode) (default of 800)
# - Removed reference to Data::Dumper module, since it is only used for debugging in dev
# - For each app, green status will display latest event date and message logged at INFO or DEBUG level. However,
# green status can only be obtained via INFO or FD* log message (e.g. WARN or ERROR followed by DEBUG is still yellow, but
# INFO followed by DEBUG is green with event date and message of the DEBUG). In other words, in a green or purple status the
# event date and message reflect the most recent event, but in a yellow or red status they reflect the most recent event
# keeping the app in it's current status.
#
# Version 4.0 - 8/18/2011
# - Fixed bug where perl error was encountered if any requested app_id had no activity within the requested time period.
#
# Version 4.9 - 6/20/2013
# - Truncated event_date to eliminate seconds from displaying.
# - Removed trailing spaces from end of message display.
#
# Version 5.0 - 20160406 Larry Spiwak <lawrence.spiwak@relayhealth.com>
# - add in DSMONITOR Bridge functionality to push statistics into DSMONITOR for Orion monitoring
#
# Version 6.4d - 4/28/2017 J Hess
# - Make status immediately go red when encountering MAX ATTEMPTS REACHED (LAMA). Leave red until launcher
#   completes with all successful workers (LAEND).
#
# Version 6.5 - 2/21/2022 J Hess
# - Rewrite/port from perl to python

import cx_Oracle, re, sys, os, argparse
from operator import itemgetter



def get_dbh(schema_prefix):
	env = os.environ.get('JOBPKG_ENV')

	if not env:
		print('environment variable JOBPKG_ENV is not set')
		sys.exit(1)

	login_env_var = schema_prefix + '_' + env + '_LOGIN'
	login_str = os.environ.get(login_env_var)

	if not login_str:
		print(f'environment variable {login_env_var} is not set')
		sys.exit(2)

	login_re = re.compile('^([^/]+)/([^@]+)@[^:]+:[^:]+:(.+)$')
	login_re_match = login_re.match(login_str)

	if not login_re_match:
		print ('Could not parse username, password, and service from environment variable ' + login_env_var)
		sys.exit(1)

	(username, pwd, service) = (login_re_match.group(1,2,3))

	dbh = None

	try:
		dbh = cx_Oracle.connect(username, pwd, service)

	except cx_Oracle.DatabaseError as e:
		print('db connection error: ' + e.args[0].message)

	return dbh



def log_history(app_list, dbh, as_of_datetime, event_days_subtract):
	# Run query to retrieve recent logged events for all desired App IDs.
	# Note: replace query with recent_events() method call after converting
	#       perl Job.pm package to python

	# build query

	log_history_sql = """
	SELECT
		app_id,
		to_char(event_date, 'YYYYMMDD HH24:MI:SS') as event_date_str,
		log_type,
		event_code,
		(sysdate - cast(event_date AS date)) * 24 * 60 as minutes_since_logged,
		message
	FROM job_log
	WHERE	"""

	if as_of_datetime is None:
		# get most recent events
		log_history_sql = log_history_sql + """event_date >= trunc(systimestamp) - """ + str(event_days_subtract)
	else:
		# get events up through point in time if specified on command-line
		as_of_re = re.compile('^\d\d\d\d\d\d\d\d \d\d:\d\d:\d\d$')

		if as_of_re.match(as_of_datetime):
			log_history_sql = log_history_sql + """event_date < to_date('""" + as_of_datetime + """', 'YYYYMMDD HH24:MI:SS') and event_date > to_date('""" + as_of_datetime + """', 'YYYYMMDD HH24:MI:SS') - """ + str(event_days_subtract)
		else:
			raise Exception("As_of date/time value of '" + as_of_datetime + "' is not formatted properly")

	# limit to desired list of apps
	log_history_sql = log_history_sql + "\nAND app_id in ('" + '\', \''.join(app_list) + '\')'

	log_history_sql = log_history_sql + """
	ORDER BY app_id, event_date ASC
	"""

	log_info = {}


	# fetch events into log_info structure
	try:
		with dbh.cursor() as sth:
			sth.execute(log_history_sql)

			while True:
				row = sth.fetchone()

				if row is None:
					break

				app_id = row[0]

				if app_id in log_info:
					log_info[app_id].append(row)
				else:
					log_info[app_id] = [row]

	except Exception as e:
		print('query error: ' + e.args[0].message)
		sys.exit(1)

	return log_info


def app_id_list(dbh, app_id, group_id):
	# Get list of App IDs, based on command line option or via query (default)
	app_list = []

	if app_id:
		app_list.append(app_id)
	else:
		# Run query to obtain list of desired app_IDs

		app_list_sql = """
		SELECT c.app_id
		FROM job_config c
		LEFT OUTER JOIN job_param_default jpg
			ON c.group_id = jpg.group_id and
			jpg.param = \'STATUS_MONITOR\'
		LEFT OUTER JOIN job_param_default jp_global
			ON jp_global.group_id = \'GLOBAL\' and
			jp_global.param = \'STATUS_MONITOR\'
		WHERE nvl(c.status_monitor, nvl(jpg.value, jp_global.value)) = \'Y\'
			AND (max_run_date > sysdate or max_run_date is null)
		"""

		if group_id:
			app_list_sql = app_list_sql + "	AND c.group_id = '" + group_id + "'\n"

		app_list_sql = app_list_sql + '	ORDER BY c.app_id'

		try:
			with dbh.cursor() as sth:
				sth.execute(app_list_sql)

				while True:
					row = sth.fetchone()

					if row is None:
						break

					app_id = row[0]
					app_list.append(app_id)

		except Exception as e:
			print('query error: ' + e.args[0].message)
			sys.exit(1)

	return app_list


def color_to_agg_status(color):
	if color == 'green':
		return 'INFO'
	elif color == 'yellow':
		return 'WARN'
	elif color == 'red':
		return 'ERROR'
	else:
		return 'UNK'


def color_to_agg_status_text(color):
	if color == 'green':
		return 'All data feeds OK'
	elif color == 'yellow':
		return 'Warning'
	elif color == 'red':
		return 'ALERT'
	else:
		return 'Unknown/No activity'

################ Main ################

# setup and parse command-line options
parser = argparse.ArgumentParser()
parser.add_argument("-app_id", help = "Only show status of APP_ID")
parser.add_argument("-group_id", help = "Only show status of apps in GROUP_ID")
parser.add_argument("-days", type = int, default = 21, help = "Look back DAYS to find status info (default=21)")
parser.add_argument("-max_yellow_minutes", type = int, default = 180, help = "Force app to red alert if yellow for # minutes (default=180)")
parser.add_argument("-max_yellow_apps", type = int, default = 4, help = "Number of yellow apps required to force red alert (default=4, disable=0)")
parser.add_argument("-max_pct_yellow_apps", type = int, default = 20, help = "%% of apps in yellow status that will force red alert (default=20, disable=0)")
parser.add_argument("-as_of", help = "Report status as of the specified time. Format: YYYYMMDD HH:MI:SS")
parser.add_argument("-bridge", action = 'store_true', default = False, help = "Send status to DSMONITOR")

args = parser.parse_args()


# Get database connection handles

job_dbh = get_dbh('JOBPKG')

dsmon_dbh = None

if args.bridge:
	dsmon_dbh = get_dbh('DSMONITOR')
	with dsmon_dbh.cursor() as cursor:
		cursor.execute("DELETE FROM ds_aggregate_status WHERE source = 'DATAFEED_BRIDGE'")


# Get list of desired App IDs
app_list = app_id_list(job_dbh, args.app_id, args.group_id)


# Get recently logged events for each App ID
log_info = log_history(app_list, job_dbh, args.as_of, args.days - 1)


# If no apps found, force 1 dummy app into app list to avoid
# handling special handling logic and allow for consistent
# display of results.

if not app_list:
	app_list.append('')

# Force empty log info for desired app_IDs with no recent job_log history.
# This is so we can display "purple" status with "No activity"

for app_id in app_list:
	if app_id not in log_info:
		log_info[app_id] = []


# Loop through each recent job_log record for each app_id to determine latest status
# of each app_id.

fd_re = re.compile('^FD')
spstatus_re = re.compile('^SPSTATUS')
status_info = []


for key_app_id in log_info:

	# initialize status variables for this app
	red = False
	yellow = False
	yellow_minutes = 0
	green = False
	purple = False
	max_attempts = False

	red_info = ""
	yellow_info = ""
	green_info = ""
	purple_info = ""
	max_attempts_info = ""
	yellow_datetime = ""

	# Loop through each recent job_log event (oldest to newest order)
	# for this app and set various status variables (green, yellow, red
	# max attempts, etc)

	for t_log_rec in log_info[key_app_id]:
		# convert tuple to list so we can modify items later
		log_rec = list(t_log_rec)

		event_date = log_rec[1]
		log_type = log_rec[2]
		event_code = str(log_rec[3])
		minutes_since_logged = log_rec[4]

		if fd_re.match(event_code):
			green = True
			green_info = log_rec
			yellow = False
			yellow_minutes = 0
			red = False	
		elif log_type == "LATE":
			red = True
			red_info = log_rec
			yellow_minutes = 0
		elif event_code == 'LAMA':
			max_attempts = True
			max_attempts_info = log_rec
		elif event_code == 'LAEND':
			max_attempts = False
			max_attempts_info = ""
			green = True
			green_info = log_rec
			yellow_minutes = 0
			yellow = False
		elif log_type == "WARN" or log_type == "ERROR":
			yellow = True

			if log_type == "ERROR":
				if yellow_minutes == 0:
					yellow_minutes = minutes_since_logged
					yellow_datetime = event_date

				yellow_info = log_rec
			elif yellow_minutes == 0:
				yellow_info = log_rec

			if (spstatus_re.match(event_code)):
				red = False
		elif log_type == "INFO":
			green = True
			green_info = log_rec
			yellow = False
			yellow_minutes = 0

			if spstatus_re.match(event_code):
				red = False
				max_attempts = False
		elif log_type == 'DEBUG':
			green_info = log_rec
			purple_info = log_rec

	if max_attempts and not red:
		red = True
		red_info = max_attempts_info

	status = ""
	status_row = [];

	if red:
		status = 'red'
		status_row = red_info
	elif yellow:
		if yellow_minutes < args.max_yellow_minutes:
			status = 'yellow'
		else:
			status = 'red'
			yellow_info[5] += f". Status turned yellow at {yellow_datetime}, but was automatically set to red after being yellow (due to ERROR) for at least {args.max_yellow_minutes} minutes. It has been {int(yellow_minutes)} minutes since the first problem."

		status_row = yellow_info
	elif green:
		status = 'green'
		status_row = green_info
	else:
		status = 'purple'
		status_row = purple_info

	status_info.append({'STATUS': status, 'APP_ID': key_app_id})

	if len(status_row) > 0:
		status_info[-1]['EVENT_DATE'] = status_row[1]
		status_info[-1]['LOG_TYPE'] = status_row[2]
		status_info[-1]['EVENT_CODE'] = status_row[3]
		status_info[-1]['MINUTES_SINCE_LOGGED'] = status_row[4]
		status_info[-1]['MESSAGE'] = status_row[5]
	else:
		status_info[-1]['MESSAGE'] = "No activity"
		status_info[-1]['EVENT_DATE'] = ""


# Determine max length needed for each display field, for subsequent display formatting
max_lengths = {}

for status_rec in status_info:
	for status_field in ["STATUS", "APP_ID", "EVENT_DATE", "MESSAGE"]:
		length = len(status_rec[status_field])

		if len(status_field) > length:
			length = len(status_field)

		if status_field in max_lengths.keys():
			if length > max_lengths[status_field]:
				max_lengths[status_field] = length
		else:
			max_lengths[status_field] = length

# Force max length of EVENT_DATE to 14 to strip off trailing seconds from display
max_lengths['EVENT_DATE'] = 14


# Use max length of each display field to construct display format string
print_format = ''

for field in ["STATUS", "APP_ID", "EVENT_DATE"]:
	print_format = print_format + '%-' + str(max_lengths[field]) + '.' + str(max_lengths[field]) + 's' + '  '

print_format = print_format + '%-1.' + str(max_lengths['MESSAGE']) + 's'


# display header
if sys.stdin.isatty():
	print(print_format % ('STATUS', 'APP ID', 'EVENT DATE', 'MESSAGE'))
	print(print_format % ('-' * max_lengths['STATUS'], '-' * max_lengths['APP_ID'], '-' * max_lengths['EVENT_DATE'], '-' * max_lengths['MESSAGE']))

# Display latest status for each app_id and determine overall status

overall_red = False
overall_yellow = False
overall_green = False
exit_status = False
num_yellow_apps = False
num_apps = 0
dsmon_rows = []

for status_rec in sorted(status_info, key=itemgetter('EVENT_DATE', 'APP_ID'), reverse=True):
	status = status_rec['STATUS']

	if status == 'red':
		overall_red = True
	elif status == 'yellow':
		overall_yellow = True
		num_yellow_apps += 1
	elif status == 'green':
		overall_green = True

	num_apps += 1

	if sys.stdin.isatty():
		print(print_format % (status_rec['STATUS'], status_rec['APP_ID'], status_rec['EVENT_DATE'], status_rec['MESSAGE']))

	dsmon_rows.append((color_to_agg_status(status_rec['STATUS']), status_rec['APP_ID'], status_rec['EVENT_DATE'], status_rec['MESSAGE'], num_apps))


# Determine overall status color/text

overall_status_text = ''

if overall_red:
	overall_color = 'red'
	exit_status = 2
elif overall_yellow:
	pct_yellow_apps = 100 * num_yellow_apps / num_apps

	if (args.max_yellow_apps >= 1) and (num_yellow_apps >= args.max_yellow_apps) and (args.max_pct_yellow_apps > 0) and (pct_yellow_apps >= args.max_pct_yellow_apps):
		overall_color = 'red'
		exit_status = 2
		overall_status_text = "Too many feeds in {yellow_ind} status ({num_yellow_apps})"
	else:
		overall_color = 'yellow'
		exit_status = 1
elif overall_green:
	overall_color = 'green'
	exit_status = 0
else:
	overall_color = 'purple'
	exit_status = 0

if len(overall_status_text) == 0:
	if overall_color == 'green':
		overall_status_text = 'All data feeds OK'
	elif overall_color == 'yellow':
		overall_status_text = 'Warning'
	elif overall_color == 'red':
		overall_status_text = 'ALERT'
	elif overall_color == 'purple':
		overall_status_text = 'Unknown/No activity'


# Display overall status color/text if this is an interactive session

overall_message_text = f"Overall status - {overall_status_text} ({overall_color})"

if sys.stdin.isatty():
	print(f"\n{overall_message_text}")
else:
	print('job_status: Refusing to generate output: STDIN is NOT a terminal!', file=sys.stderr)

# Add status rows to ds_aggregate_status table if -bridge command-line option used
if dsmon_dbh:
	# add overall status row to dsmon_rows w/sequence # 0
	dsmon_rows.append((color_to_agg_status(overall_color), 'OVERALL_STATUS', '', overall_message_text, 0))

	# insert rows to ds_aggregate_status table for each app id (+ overall status row)
	with dsmon_dbh.cursor() as cursor:
		cursor.executemany("""
			INSERT INTO ds_aggregate_status (
				entry_date,
				status,
				application,
				process_appid,
				event_date,
				message,
				seq_num, source
			) VALUES (
				sysdate,
				:status,
				'DS_DATAFEED',
				:process_appid,
				to_date(:event_date, 'YYYYMMDD HH24:MI:SS'),
				:message,
				:seq_num,
				'DATAFEED_BRIDGE')""", dsmon_rows)

	dsmon_dbh.commit()

#job_trigger_post_date
#!/usr/bin/perl

# job_trigger_post_date: Create a "end of day" trigger file BLUELITE::Job apps
#
# Author(s): John Hess		RelayHealth
#
# Version history:
# Version 1.0 - 4/2/2009
#
# Version 1.1 - 9/09/2010
# Adding template option to allow trigger file create base on provided template.
#
# Version 3.1 - 6/14/2011
# Fixed bug in mydie where call to log method would fail if $JOB object was not yet created
#
# Version 6.0 - 10/31/2014
# - Added support for "autohoc" requests (i.e. automated on-demand ad-hoc processing).
#

use IO::Compress::Gzip qw($GzipError);
use DateTime;
use DateTime::Format::Strptime;
use Getopt::Long;
use Mail::SendEasy;
use File::Copy;
use File::PathConvert qw(rel2abs);
use File::Spec;
use Data::Dumper;

use BLUELITE::Job;
use BLUELITE::Logger;

use strict;
use warnings;

my @dir_parts = File::Spec->splitdir(rel2abs($0));
our $PGM = pop(@dir_parts);


our $DEFAULT_EXIT_SUCCESS = 0;
our ($SUCCESS_EMAIL, $FAILURE_EMAIL, $DEFAULT_FAILURE_EMAIL, $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME);
our $DEFAULT_DATE_FORMAT = DateTime::Format::Strptime->new( pattern => '%Y%m%d%H%M%S') || die "ERROR: Unable to set default date format!\n";
our $FILES_CREATED = 0;
our ($DBH, $OUT_FH, $LOGGER, $APP_ID, $SOURCE_APP_ID, $LOGFILE, $TRIGGER_DIR, $APP_DIR_TOP, $TEMPLATE);
our $custom_header = 0;
our $custom_trailer = 0;
our ($JOB, $TODAY_DATE);



sub mydie($) {
  my $message = shift;

	# close output file

	if (defined($OUT_FH) && $OUT_FH->opened) {
		$OUT_FH->close;
	}

	# remove output file

	if (defined($TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME)) {
		if (-f $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME) {

			eval '$LOGGER->info("Removing trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME")' if (defined($LOGGER));

			if (! unlink($TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME)) {
				$message .= "\nCould not delete output file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME : $!\n";
			} else {
				$message .= "\nDeleted output file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME : $!\n";
			}
		}
	}

	if (defined($LOGGER)) {
		eval '$LOGGER->info("Created $FILES_CREATED trigger files")';

		$message .= "\nSee logfile $LOGFILE for more details\n";
	}

	$JOB->log(event_code => 'TRFAIL', log_type => 'ERROR', message => $message, email_subject => 'trigger file creation failed') if (defined($JOB));

	if (defined($LOGGER)) {
		$LOGGER->error($message);
		exit(1);
	} else {
		die $message . "\n";
	}
}


sub get_trigger_fname($$$) {
	my ($post_date, $trigger_dir, $job) = @_;

  my $trigger_fname_sprintf = $job->trigger_fname_sprintf;
  my $trigger_fname_vars = $job->trigger_fname_vars;

	mydie "get_trigger_fname: trigger_fname_sprintf must be configured in the JOB_CONFIG table\n" if (! defined($trigger_fname_sprintf));
	$trigger_fname_sprintf =~ s/^\s+//;
	$trigger_fname_sprintf =~ s/\s+$//;
	mydie "get_trigger_fname: trigger_fname_sprintf must be configured in the JOB_CONFIG table\n" if (length($trigger_fname_sprintf) == 0);

	mydie "get_trigger_fname: trigger_fname_vars must be configured in the JOB_CONFIG table\n" if (! defined($trigger_fname_vars));
	$trigger_fname_vars =~ s/^\s+//;
	$trigger_fname_vars =~ s/\s+$//;
	mydie "get_trigger_fname: trigger_fname_vars must be configured in the JOB_CONFIG table\n" if (length($trigger_fname_vars) == 0);

	my @var_list = split(/\s*,\s*/, uc($trigger_fname_vars));
	mydie "get_trigger_fname: could not parse any variables from trigger_fname_vars value of '$trigger_fname_vars'\n" if (scalar(@var_list) == 0);

	my @fname_vars = ();

	foreach my $var (@var_list) {
		if ($var eq 'POST_DATE') {
			push(@fname_vars, $post_date);
		} elsif ($var eq 'DATE_CREATED') {
			push(@fname_vars, $TODAY_DATE);
		} else {
			mydie "get_trigger_fname: trigger_fname_vars = '$trigger_fname_vars', which contains a unrecognized variable named '$var'\n";
		}
	}

	mydie "get_trigger_fname: could not find any recognized variables from trigger_fname_vars value of '$trigger_fname_vars'\n" if (scalar(@fname_vars) == 0);

	my $fname = sprintf($trigger_fname_sprintf, @fname_vars);

	$fname = "$trigger_dir/$fname";
	return $fname;
}


sub Usage() {
  print "$PGM: Create end-of-day trigger files for BLUELITE::Job apps\n\n";
  print "Usage 1: $PGM [-options] -app-id a -app-dir d\n";
  print "Usage 2: $PGM [-options] -source-app-id a -app-dir d data_fname\n";
  print " Required parameters\n";
  print "  -app-id or -source-app-id     Application id as recorded in JOB_CONFIG table\n";
  print "  -app-dir d                    Top-level application directory\n";
  print " Options (defaults in parenthesis):\n";
  print "  -exit #                       Exit with status # on success. ($DEFAULT_EXIT_SUCCESS)\n";
  print "  -logging-level level          Set logging to level (INFO). Values: DEBUG, INFO, WARN, ERROR, FATAL\n";
  print "  -success-email list           Send status to list addresses upon success (application default)\n";
  print "  -failure-email list           Send status to list addresses upon failure (application default)\n";
  print "  -default-failure-email list   Send status to list addresses upon failure (does not override app default)\n";
  print "  -check-only                   Only check to see if trigger creation would be performed (off)\n";
  print "  -template                     Create .done file based on template provided\n";

}


sub sig_handler() {
  my $signal = shift;

  mydie "$PGM process was killed via $signal signal.\n";
}



sub mymove($$) {
  my ($source_file, $dest_dir) = (shift, shift);

	return undef if (! move($source_file, $dest_dir));

	my $base_fname = $source_file;
	$base_fname =~ s/.*\///g;

	return "${dest_dir}/${base_fname}";
}



sub add_trigger($$$$$) {
  my ($output_fname, $job, $post_date, $data_records, $workers_in_output) = @_;

	my $trigger_id = $job->add_trigger(fname => $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME, workers => $workers_in_output, commit => 0, post_date => $post_date);

	if (! $trigger_id) {
		mydie "Could not successfully call BLUELITE::Job->add_trigger() for output file $output_fname\n";
	}

	# clean up temp worker files since we no longer need them

	return $trigger_id;
}


sub myexit($) {
	my $exit_code = shift;

	if ($FILES_CREATED && defined($LOGGER)) {
		eval '$LOGGER->info("Created $FILES_CREATED trigger files.")';
	} else {
		eval '$LOGGER->info("No worker trigger files created.")';
	}

	unlink($LOGFILE) if (defined($LOGFILE) && (! $FILES_CREATED));
	
	exit($exit_code);
}


sub basename($) {
  my $fname_full = shift;
  my $bname;

	if (defined($fname_full)) {
		$bname = $fname_full;
		$bname =~ s/.*\///g;
	}

	return $bname;
}


sub my_print($$;$) {
	my ($fh, $mesg, $err_mesg) = @_;

	if (! print $fh $mesg) {
		no warnings 'uninitialized';
		mydie "ERROR: $err_mesg : $!";
	}
}

############# MAIN ###########

eval { $TODAY_DATE = DateTime->now(time_zone => 'local')->strftime('%Y%m%d'); };

if ($@) {
  mydie "Could not obtain today's date via DateTime module\n";
}

my $exit_success = $DEFAULT_EXIT_SUCCESS;
my $logging_level = 'INFO';
my $check_only = 0;

# setup signal handler so we can cleanup before getting interrupted

foreach my $sig ('INT', 'QUIT', 'HUP', 'INT', 'TERM', 'ABRT', 'BUS', 'FPE', 'ILL', 'QUIT', 'SEGV', 'SYS', 'TRAP') {
  if ((! defined($SIG{$sig})) || ($SIG{$sig} ne 'IGNORE')) {
    $SIG{$sig} = \&sig_handler;
  }
}


if (scalar(@ARGV) == 0) {
  Usage;
  exit(1);
}

# Get command-line options

GetOptions(
            'exit=s' => \$exit_success,
            'logging-level=s' => \$logging_level,
            'success-email=s' => \$SUCCESS_EMAIL,
            'failure-email=s' => \$FAILURE_EMAIL,
            'default-failure-email=s' => \$DEFAULT_FAILURE_EMAIL,
            'check-only' => \$check_only,
            'app-id=s' => \$APP_ID,
            'source-app-id=s' => \$SOURCE_APP_ID,
            'app-dir=s' => \$APP_DIR_TOP,
            'template=s' => \$TEMPLATE,
) || exit(1);

mydie "ERROR: Mandatory -app-id or -source-app-id parameter not specified!\n" if (! (defined($APP_ID) || defined($SOURCE_APP_ID)));
mydie "ERROR: Cannot use -app-id and -source-app-id parameters together!" if (defined($APP_ID) && defined($SOURCE_APP_ID));
mydie "ERROR: The mandatory -app-dir parameter was not specified!\n" if (! defined($APP_DIR_TOP));
mydie "ERROR: Application directory $APP_DIR_TOP does not exist!\n" if (! -e $APP_DIR_TOP);

my $fname;

if (defined($SOURCE_APP_ID)) {
	if (! @ARGV) {
		mydie "ERROR: When using -source-app-id, must provide delivered filename\n";
	}

	if (scalar(@ARGV) > 1) {
		mydie "ERROR: No more than 1 filename may be specified\n";
	}

	$fname = $ARGV[0];
  $APP_ID = $SOURCE_APP_ID;
}

my $LOG_DIR = "$APP_DIR_TOP/log";
my $ORIG_LOG_DIR = $LOG_DIR;

if (! -d $LOG_DIR) {
    $LOG_DIR = '.';
}

# Check if template exist
our @temp_content;
if (defined $TEMPLATE && $TEMPLATE  !~ /^\s*$/) {

	if (! open(TEMP_FILE, $TEMPLATE)) {
  	$TEMPLATE = "$APP_DIR_TOP/bin/$TEMPLATE";
    open(TEMP_FILE, $TEMPLATE) or mydie "Could not open Template $TEMPLATE: $!\n";
	}

  while (my $line = <TEMP_FILE>) {
     push (@temp_content, $line);
  }

  close (TEMP_FILE) or mydie "Could not close template file $TEMPLATE: $!\n";
}



# Set up logger options and get a logger

$LOGFILE = "$LOG_DIR/${APP_ID}_trigger.$$.log";

# Set screen options for logger
my @screen_options;

if (-t 1) {
  @screen_options = (screen_threshold => $logging_level);
} else {
  @screen_options = (screen_threshold => 'OFF');
}

eval 'initialize_logging(@screen_options, file_threshold => $logging_level, logfile => $LOGFILE)';
die "Cannot initialize logging : $@" if (! logging_initialized);

eval '$LOGGER = get_logger' || die "Cannot get logger: $@";

if ($LOG_DIR eq '.') {
	eval '$LOGGER->warn("log directory \$ORIG_LOG_DIR does not exist. Logging to current directory instead.")' || die "Cannot write to log file $LOGFILE: $@";
}

my (@job_opts, $request_id);

if (defined($SOURCE_APP_ID)) {
  my $select = "
      select q.rq_request_id
      from job_queue q, job_delivery d
      where q.rq_source_app_id = '$SOURCE_APP_ID'
        and q.app_id = d.app_id
        and d.delivery_output_file = '$fname'
				and d.delivery_type = 'DATA'
      order by creation_date desc";

  my @request_id = BLUELITE::Job->dbh->selectrow_array($select);

  if (! @request_id) {
    mydie "Could not determine request ID for app_id = '$SOURCE_APP_ID', filename '$fname'";
  }

  $request_id = $request_id[0];
  push(@job_opts, app_id => $SOURCE_APP_ID, request_id => $request_id);
} else {
  push(@job_opts, app_id => $APP_ID);
}

eval { $JOB = BLUELITE::Job->new(@job_opts) };

if (! defined($JOB)) {
	mydie "Unable to obtain BLUELITE::Job object for app_id = '$APP_ID' : $@\n";
}

if (defined($request_id)) {
	my $temp_job;

	eval { $temp_job = BLUELITE::Job->new(app_id => $APP_ID) };

	if (! defined($temp_job)) {
		mydie "Unable to obtain BLUELITE::Job object for app_id = '$APP_ID' : $@\n";
	}

	$TRIGGER_DIR = $temp_job->rq_deliv_dir;
} else {
	$TRIGGER_DIR = $JOB->deliv_dir;
}

mydie "ERROR: Deliverables directory $TRIGGER_DIR does not exist!\n" if (! -e $TRIGGER_DIR);
mydie "ERROR: Cannot write to deliverable directory $TRIGGER_DIR\n" if (! -w $TRIGGER_DIR);

my ($seconds_since_last_creation, $hours_since_last_creation);
my $current_time = DateTime->now(time_zone => 'local');
my $last_creation_time = $JOB->last_creation_datetime(delivery_type => 'TRIGGER');
my $tz = $current_time->time_zone->name;

if (defined($last_creation_time)) {
	$LOGGER->info("Last trigger creation time = $last_creation_time");
	$seconds_since_last_creation = ($current_time->subtract_datetime_absolute($last_creation_time))->seconds;
	$hours_since_last_creation = sprintf('%0.2f', $seconds_since_last_creation / 3600);
	$LOGGER->info("It has been $hours_since_last_creation hours since creating the last trigger file.");
} else {
	$LOGGER->info("No trigger files have ever been created.");
}


######


$DBH = $JOB->dbh || mydie "Could not get database handle from BLUELITE::Job package : $@\n";

my $limit_pd = 1;

if (defined($SOURCE_APP_ID)) {
	$limit_pd = 0;
}

my @workers = $JOB->ready_to_trigger(post_date_complete => 1, post_date_limit => $limit_pd);	# returns list of worker objects

if (scalar(@workers) == 0) {
	# no new trigger files to create
	$LOGGER->info("No post dates are ready to trigger.");
	myexit($exit_success)
}

# organize workers by post date in a data structure
my ($post_date_worker, $post_date);

foreach my $worker (@workers) {
	$post_date = $worker->post_date;
	$LOGGER->info("Post date $post_date is ready to trigger.") if ($check_only && ! exists($post_date_worker->{$post_date}));
	push(@{$post_date_worker->{$post_date}->{workers}}, $worker);

	if (! exists($post_date_worker->{$post_date}->{deliveries}->{$worker->delivery_file_id})) {
		$post_date_worker->{$post_date}->{deliveries}->{$worker->delivery_file_id} = $worker->delivery_info;
		$post_date_worker->{$post_date}->{num_deliveries}++;
		$post_date_worker->{$post_date}->{data_records} += $worker->delivery_info->{DATA_RECORDS};
	}


};

myexit($exit_success) if ($check_only);

# For each post date for which all data has been processed and delivered, create a trigger file.

my ($total_records, $records_added, @workers_in_output, @missing_files);
my $file_encoding = $JOB->trigger_encoding;
$file_encoding = '' if (! defined($file_encoding));
my $record_terminator = $JOB->concat_record_terminator;

if (! defined($record_terminator)) {
	mydie "Could not determine which record terminator to use. Check CONCAT_RECORD_TERMINATOR field in JOB_CONFIG table.\n";
}

my ($append_error_mesg, $num_data_files, $xml_file_info, $trigger_id, $total_data_records, $total_files, @file_names);

foreach my $post_date (sort keys %{$post_date_worker}) {

	$TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME = get_trigger_fname($post_date, $TRIGGER_DIR, $JOB);
	$total_data_records = $post_date_worker->{$post_date}->{data_records};

	$trigger_id = add_trigger($TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME, $JOB, $post_date, $total_data_records, $post_date_worker->{$post_date}->{workers});

	if (! $trigger_id) {
		$JOB->rollback;
		mydie "Could not add trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME\n";
	}

	if ($file_encoding =~ /^\s*(raw|uncompressed)\s*$/i) {
		$OUT_FH = new IO::File "> $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME" || mydie "Cannot create trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME : $!\n";
	} elsif ($file_encoding =~ /^\s*gzip\s*$/i) {
		$OUT_FH = new IO::Compress::Gzip $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME || mydie "Gzip failed to create trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME : $GzipError\n";
	} else {
		mydie "ERROR: file_encoding type of '$file_encoding' is not supported!\n";
	}

	$current_time = DateTime->now(time_zone => 'local');
	$total_files = scalar(keys %{$post_date_worker->{$post_date}->{deliveries}});

  if (! defined $TEMPLATE) {

	  my_print($OUT_FH, '<trigger id="' . $trigger_id . '" name="' . basename($TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME) . '">' . "\n", "Could not create <trigger> tag for trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME");
	  my_print($OUT_FH, '   <creation date="' . $current_time->strftime('%Y%m%d') . '" time="' . $current_time->strftime('%H:%M:%S') . '" zone="' . $tz . '"></creation>' . "\n", "Could not create <creation> tag for trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME");

	  my_print($OUT_FH, '   <data_files count="' . $total_files . '">' . "\n", "Could not create <data_files> tag for trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME");


  }

	$num_data_files = 0;

	foreach my $delivery_id (sort { $post_date_worker->{$post_date}->{deliveries}->{$a}->{SEQ_NUM} <=> $post_date_worker->{$post_date}->{deliveries}->{$b}->{SEQ_NUM} } keys %{$post_date_worker->{$post_date}->{deliveries}}) {

		my $delivery_info = $post_date_worker->{$post_date}->{deliveries}->{$delivery_id};
		push (@file_names, basename($delivery_info->{DELIVERY_OUTPUT_FILE}));

		no warnings 'uninitialized';

    if (! defined $TEMPLATE) {
		  my_print($OUT_FH, '      <file id="' . $delivery_id . '" name="' . basename($delivery_info->{DELIVERY_OUTPUT_FILE}) . '">' . "\n", "Cannot create <file> tag in trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME");

		  my_print($OUT_FH, '         <size bytes="' . $delivery_info->{FILE_SIZE} . '" data_records="' . $delivery_info->{DATA_RECORDS} . '" txns_processed="' . $delivery_info->{TXN_PROCESSED} . '"></size>' . "\n" , "Cannot create <size> tag in trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME");

		  my_print($OUT_FH, '         <creation date="' . $delivery_info->{CREATION_DATE} . '" time="' . $delivery_info->{CREATION_TIME} . '" zone="' . $tz . '">' . "</creation>\n", "Cannot create file <creation> tag in trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME");

		  my_print($OUT_FH, '         <transmission date="' . $delivery_info->{DELIVERY_DATE} . '" time="' . $delivery_info->{DELIVERY_TIME} . '" zone="' . $tz . '">' . "</transmission>\n", "Cannot create file <transmission> tag in trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME");

		  if (defined($delivery_info->{DESTINATION_HOST})) {
			  my_print($OUT_FH, '         <destination host="' . $delivery_info->{DESTINATION_HOST} . '"></destination>' . "\n", "Cannot create file <creation> tag in trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME");
		  }

		  $xml_file_info = {
			  seq_num => $delivery_info->{SEQ_NUM},
			  post_date => $post_date,
		  };

		  foreach my $tag (keys %{$xml_file_info}) {
			  $append_error_mesg = "Cannot append <$tag> tag to trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME";

			  if (defined($xml_file_info->{$tag})) {
				  my_print($OUT_FH, "         <$tag>" . $xml_file_info->{$tag} . "</$tag>\n", $append_error_mesg);
			  }
		  }

		  my_print($OUT_FH, "      </file>\n", $append_error_mesg);

		  $num_data_files++;

	  } #end  (! defined $TEMPLATE) 
	} #foreach loop 

	if (! defined $TEMPLATE) {

	  my_print($OUT_FH, "   </data_files>\n", "Could not create </data_files> tag in trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME");
	  my_print($OUT_FH, "</trigger>\n", "Could not create </trigger> tag in trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME");
	}


  if (defined $TEMPLATE) {

    my @new_temp_content;

    my $files;
    foreach my $file (@file_names) {
      $files = $file . "\n";
    }

    #remove the last end of line character if has multiple files in string
    chomp ($files);

    my ($y, $m, $d)=  unpack('a4a2a2', $post_date);

    foreach my $line (@temp_content) {

      $line =~ s/\%yyyy/$y/;
      $line =~ s/\%mm/$m/;
      $line =~ s/\%dd/$d/;
      $line =~ s/\%total_files/$total_files/;
      $line =~ s/\%num_records/$total_data_records/;
      $line =~ s/\%file_names/$files/;
      push (@new_temp_content, $line);
   }

   foreach my $line (@new_temp_content) {
     my_print($OUT_FH, $line) ; 
   }
 }

	$OUT_FH->close || mydie "Could not close output trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME : $!\n";

	my $new_output_fname = mymove($TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME, $TRIGGER_DIR) || mydie "Could not move trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME to deliverable directory $TRIGGER_DIR : $!\n";

	$TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME = $new_output_fname;

	$JOB->commit || mydie "Could not commit addition of trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME\n";

	$JOB->log(event_code => 'TRSUCCESS', log_type => 'INFO', post_date => $post_date, email_subject => 'trigger file created successfully', message => "Created trigger file $TRIGGER_OUTFILE_NAME . Data Records = ${total_data_records}. Number of data files = ${num_data_files}.");

	$FILES_CREATED++;
}


$LOGGER->info("Completed trigger file creation process.") || mydie "Cannot write to log file $LOGFILE: $@";

myexit($exit_success);


#killzombie

user=$USER
match=$1

if [ "$match" != '' ]
  then
		match_expr="$match"
  else
		match_expr=.
fi

delay=4

while :
 do
	pids=`ps -fwu $user |
	egrep "$match_expr" |
	egrep -v "gvim|java|qas" |
	sed 's/  */ /g' |
	cut -d' ' -f2,3 |
	grep ' 1$' |
	cut -d' ' -f1`

	if [ "$pids" = '' ]
  then
			echo all done
			exit 0
	fi

	echo About to kill these processes...

	ps -o cmd $pids

	echo hit CTRL-C within $delay secs to avoid killing processes and terminate script

	sleep $delay
	sleep 1

	echo killing $pids

	kill $pids

	sleep 1
 done



#libusb-config
#!/bin/sh

prefix=/ds/common
exec_prefix=${prefix}
exec_prefix_set=no

usage()
{
	cat <<EOF
Usage: libusb-config [OPTIONS] [LIBRARIES]
Options:
	[--prefix[=DIR]]
	[--exec-prefix[=DIR]]
	[--version]
	[--libs]
	[--cflags]
EOF
	exit $1
}

if test $# -eq 0; then
	usage 1 1>&2
fi

while test $# -gt 0; do
  case "$1" in
  -*=*) optarg=`echo "$1" | sed 's/[-_a-zA-Z0-9]*=//'` ;;
  *) optarg= ;;
  esac

  case $1 in
    --prefix=*)
      prefix=$optarg
      if test $exec_prefix_set = no ; then
        exec_prefix=$optarg
      fi
      ;;
    --prefix)
      echo_prefix=yes
      ;;
    --exec-prefix=*)
      exec_prefix=$optarg
      exec_prefix_set=yes
      ;;
    --exec-prefix)
      echo_exec_prefix=yes
      ;;
    --version)
      echo 0.1.12
      exit 0
      ;;
    --cflags)
      if test "${prefix}/include" != /usr/include ; then
        includes="-I${prefix}/include"
      fi
      echo_cflags=yes
      ;;
    --libs)
      echo_libs=yes
      ;;
    *)
      usage 1 1>&2
      ;;
  esac
  shift
done

if test "$echo_prefix" = "yes"; then
	echo $prefix
fi
if test "$echo_exec_prefix" = "yes"; then
	echo $exec_prefix
fi
if test "$echo_cflags" = "yes"; then
	echo $includes
fi
if test "$echo_libs" = "yes"; then
	echo -L${exec_prefix}/lib -lusb 
fi

#load_dim_awp_ndc_price
#!/usr/bin/perl

use strict;
use warnings;

use File::Basename;

use BLUELITE::Mail qw(email);
use BLUELITE::Dimension::AWP_NDC_Price;

my $PROGNAME = basename($0);
my $FAILURE_EMAIL = q{DataServicesNotification@relayhealth.com};

eval { BLUELITE::Dimension::AWP_NDC_Price->load };

email(
	to => $FAILURE_EMAIL,
	subject => qq{$PROGNAME Failed},
	msg => qq{Failed to load DIM_AWP_NDC_PRICE: $@},
) if $@;

exit 0;

#mailfile
#!/usr/bin/perl

use BLUELITE::Mail;

$prog_name = "mailfile";

use IO::File;
use Getopt::Std;

use FileHandle;
use File::Spec;

autoflush STDOUT 1;
autoflush STDERR 1;

sub usage()
{
	print "Usage: mailfile -r recepient[,recepient...] [ -s subject ] file [ file ... ]\n";
	exit(1);
}



if (scalar(@ARGV) == 0 || ! getopts('r:s:', \%opt))
{
        &usage();
}

if ($opt{r})
{
	$to = $opt{r};
}
else
{
	print STDERR "$prog_name: No receipents listed.  See usage.\n";
	exit (1);
}


@files = @ARGV;

if ($opt{s})
{
	$subject = $opt{s};
}
else
{
	$subject = "Files " . join(", ", @files);
}


if (scalar(@files) == 0)
{
	print STDERR "$prog_name: No files to send listed. See usage\n";
	exit(1);
}

for $file (@files)
{
	if (! -f $file)
	{
		print STDERR "$prog_name: Unable to locate file \"$file\"\n";
		exit (1);
	}

	$size = (stat($file))[7];
	$file_info{$file} = $size;

	$total_size = $total_size + $size;
	
}

if ($total_size > 30000000)
{
	print STDERR "$prog_name:  Total size of files is greater than 30M - aborting\n";
	exit(1);
}

$msg = "\n\nFiles from the Bluelite User (attached):\n";
foreach $_ (keys %file_info)
{
	$msg .= "\tFile: $_ ($file_info{$_})\n";
}

$msg .= "\n";

$ret = 
&sendmail ( TO => $to,
						MSG => $msg,
						SUBJECT => $subject,
						attachment => join(",", @files)
);


if (! $ret)
{
	print STDERR "$prog_name: Mail appears to have failed - $! ($ret)\n";
	exit (1);
}

print scalar(@files) . " files have been sent succesfully.\n";
exit (200);



#medrecon
#!/usr/bin/perl -w

use SOAP::Lite;
use Data::Dumper;
use strict;
use Time::HiRes;
use BLUELITE::GPG;
use Data::UUID qw(NameSpace_URL);

sub encrypt {
  my $string = shift;

  my $pgp = new BLUELITE::GPG(homedir => '/ds/gnupg',
                              armor   => 0,
                 );
  my $encrypted_string = $pgp->sign_encrypt("Jessica.Landisman\@per-se.com", 'Niwthh', $string, "data.services\@per-se.com");

  if ($pgp->error()) {
    print $pgp->error();
    return undef;
  }
  else {
    return$encrypted_string; 
  }
}

my $verbose_flag = 0;
if ($ARGV[0] eq "-v") {
  $verbose_flag = 1;
  shift @ARGV;
}
my $host = shift @ARGV;
my $start_date = shift @ARGV;
my $end_date = shift @ARGV;
my $last_name = shift @ARGV;
my $first_name = shift @ARGV;
my $dob = shift @ARGV;
my $gender = shift @ARGV;
my $zip_code = shift @ARGV;
my $cardholder = shift @ARGV;

if (! defined $cardholder) {
 $cardholder = q{};
}
 
my $ug = new Data::UUID;
my $uuid = $ug->create_str();
my $time = time();
#generate xml string
my $unencrypted_criteria = qq{<start_date>$start_date</start_date>
<end_date>$end_date</end_date>
<last_name>$last_name</last_name>
<first_name>$first_name</first_name>
<dob>$dob</dob>
<gender>$gender</gender>
<zip_code>$zip_code</zip_code>
};
if (defined $cardholder) {
  $unencrypted_criteria .= "<member_id>$cardholder</member_id>\n";
} 
my $criteria = encrypt($unencrypted_criteria);

my $message = qq{<data_services_request id="$uuid" timestamp="$time">
  <Header>
    <authentication>
      <auth_mode>ppk</auth_mode>
      <user_name>Jessica.Landisman\@per-se.com</user_name>
    </authentication>
  </Header>
  <request_format>
    <request_data>med_history</request_data>
    <request_version>1</request_version>
  </request_format>
  <response_format>
    <predefined_response>NCPDPScript</predefined_response>
    <response_version>1</response_version>
  </response_format>
  <request_criteria>$criteria</request_criteria>
</data_services_request>};

#CONNECTION:
my $uri   = 'MedHistory';
my $proxy = "http://$host/soap";
my $soap = SOAP::Lite
           ->uri($uri)
           ->proxy($proxy, timeout => 180);

my $start_time = Time::HiRes::gettimeofday();
my $result = $soap->GetMedHistory($message);
my $end_time = Time::HiRes::gettimeofday();

my $return = 1;
my $fault_code = '-';
if ($result->fault) {
  $return = 0;
  $fault_code = $result->fault->{'detail'}->{'ErrorCode'}->{'code'};
}

my $elapsed_time = $end_time - $start_time;
if ($verbose_flag) {
  print Dumper $result;
  if ($result->fault) {
    print Dumper $result->fault;
  }
  else {
    my $result_string = $result->result;
    print $result_string, "\n";
    my @lines = split /\n/, $result_string;
    my $encrypted_text;
    my $cdata_flag = 0;
    foreach my $line (@lines) {
      if ($cdata_flag == 1) {
        if ($line =~ m/]]/) {
          $cdata_flag = 0;
        } else {
          $encrypted_text .= "$line\n";
        }
      } else {
        if ($line =~ m/CDATA/) {
          $cdata_flag = 1;
          $line =~ s/^\s+\<!\[CDATA\[//;
          $encrypted_text = "$line\n";
        }
      }
    }

    if (0 < length($encrypted_text)) {
      my $pgp = new BLUELITE::GPG(homedir => '/ds/gnupg',
      );

      my $result = $pgp->decrypt_verify('Niwthh', $encrypted_text);
      if ($pgp->error()) {
        print "Failed decryption: " . $pgp->error() . "\n";
      }
      else {
        print "Signature verified for " . $result->{'key_user'} . "\n";
        my $decrypted_text = $result->{'text'};
        print Dumper $result;
        print $decrypted_text;
      }
    }
  }
} 

print "\n$host|$start_date|$end_date|$last_name|$first_name|$dob|$gender|$zip_code|$cardholder|$return|$fault_code|$start_time|$end_time|$elapsed_time\n";

#medrecon2
#!/usr/bin/perl -w

use SOAP::Lite;
use Data::Dumper;
use strict;
use Time::HiRes;
use BLUELITE::GPG;
use Data::UUID qw(NameSpace_URL);

sub encrypt {
  my $string = shift;

  my $pgp = new BLUELITE::GPG(homedir => '/ds/gnupg',
                              armor   => 0,
                 );
  my $encrypted_string = $pgp->sign_encrypt("Jessica.Landisman\@per-se.com", 'Niwthh', $string, "data.services\@per-se.com");

  if ($pgp->error()) {
    print $pgp->error();
    return undef;
  }
  else {
    return$encrypted_string; 
  }
}

my $verbose_flag = 0;
if ($ARGV[0] eq "-v") {
  $verbose_flag = 1;
  shift @ARGV;
}

my $start_date = shift @ARGV;

my $zip;

#CONNECTION:

           ->uri($uri)

}

my $elapsed_time = $end_time - $start_time;
if ($verbose_flag) {
  if ($result->fault) {
    print Dumper $result->fault;
  }
  else {
    my $result_string = $result->result;
    print STDERR $result_string, "\n";
    my @lines = split /\n/, $result_string;
    my $encrypted_text;
    my $cdata_flag = 0;
    foreach my $line (@lines) {
      if ($cdata_flag == 1) {
        if ($line =~ m/]]/) {
          $cdata_flag = 0;
        } else {
          $encrypted_text .= "$line\n";
        }
      } else {
        if ($line =~ m/CDATA/) {
          $cdata_flag = 1;
          $line =~ s/^\s+\<!\[CDATA\[//;
          $encrypted_text = "$line\n";
        }
      }
    }

    if (0 < length($encrypted_text)) {
      my $pgp = new BLUELITE::GPG(homedir => '/ds/gnupg',
      );

      my $result = $pgp->decrypt_verify('Niwthh', $encrypted_text);
      if ($pgp->error()) {
        print "Failed decryption: " . $pgp->error() . "\n";
      }
      else {
        print "Signature verified for " . $result->{'key_user'} . "\n";
        my $decrypted_text = $result->{'text'};
        #print Dumper $result;
        print $decrypted_text;
      }
    }
  }
} 

print "\n$host|$start_date|$end_date|$cardholder|$person_code|$relationship_code|$group_id|$pcn||$return|$fault_code|$start_time|$end_time|$elapsed_time|$uuid\n";

#medrecon_ssl
#!/usr/bin/perl -w

use SOAP::Lite;
use Data::Dumper;
use strict;
use Time::HiRes;
use Data::UUID qw(NameSpace_URL);

my $verbose_flag = 0;
if ($ARGV[0] eq "-v") {
  $verbose_flag = 1;
  shift @ARGV;
}
my $host = shift @ARGV;
my $start_date = shift @ARGV;
my $end_date = shift @ARGV;
my $last_name = shift @ARGV;
my $first_name = shift @ARGV;
my $dob = shift @ARGV;
my $gender = shift @ARGV;
my $zip_code = shift @ARGV;
my $cardholder = shift @ARGV;

if (! defined $cardholder) {
 $cardholder = q{};
}
 
my $ug = new Data::UUID;
my $uuid = $ug->create_str();
my $time = time();
#generate xml string
my $unencrypted_criteria = qq{<start_date>$start_date</start_date>
<end_date>$end_date</end_date>
<last_name>$last_name</last_name>
<first_name>$first_name</first_name>
<dob>$dob</dob>
<gender>$gender</gender>
<zip_code>$zip_code</zip_code>
};
if (defined $cardholder) {
  $unencrypted_criteria .= "<member_id>$cardholder</member_id>\n";
} 
my $criteria = $unencrypted_criteria;
 
my $command = q{curl -s -k -X POST https://} . $host . q{/soap -d '<soap:Envelope xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance" 
               xmlns:soapenc="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/encoding/" 
   xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" 
   soap:encodingStyle="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/encoding/" 
   xmlns:soap="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/">
<soap:Body>
<GetMedHistory xmlns="MedHistory">
<c-gensym3 xsi:type="xsd:string">&lt;data_services_request id="} . $uuid . q{" timestamp="} . $time . q{"&gt;
  &lt;Header&gt;
    &lt;authentication&gt;
      &lt;auth_mode&gt;ppk&lt;/auth_mode&gt;
      &lt;user_name&gt;Jessica.Landisman@per-se.com&lt;/user_name&gt;
    &lt;/authentication&gt;
  &lt;/Header&gt;
  &lt;request_format&gt;
    &lt;request_data&gt;med_history&lt;/request_data&gt;
    &lt;request_version&gt;1&lt;/request_version&gt;
  &lt;/request_format&gt;
  &lt;response_format&gt;
    &lt;predefined_response&gt;NCPDPScript&lt;/predefined_response&gt;
    &lt;response_version&gt;1&lt;/response_version&gt;
  &lt;/response_format&gt;
  &lt;request_criteria&gt;&lt;start_date&gt;} . $start_date . q{&lt;/start_date&gt;
&lt;end_date&gt;} . $end_date . q{&lt;/end_date&gt;
&lt;last_name&gt;} . $last_name . q{&lt;/last_name&gt;
&lt;first_name&gt;} . $first_name . q{&lt;/first_name&gt;
&lt;dob&gt;} . $dob . q{&lt;/dob&gt;
&lt;gender&gt;} . $gender . q{&lt;/gender&gt;
&lt;zip_code&gt;} . $zip_code . q{&lt;/zip_code&gt;
&lt;member_id&gt;} . $cardholder . q{&lt;/member_id&gt;
&lt;/request_criteria&gt;
&lt;/data_services_request&gt;</c-gensym3></GetMedHistory></soap:Body></soap:Envelope>'};

my $start_time = Time::HiRes::gettimeofday();
my $result = qx/$command/;
my $end_time = Time::HiRes::gettimeofday();

my $return = 1;
my $exception = q{-};
if ($result !~ m/GetMedHistoryResponse/) {
  $return = 0;
  $exception = $result;
}
elsif ($result =~ m/errorMsg(.*)errorMsg/) {
  print "FOUND IT\n";
  $return = 0;
  $exception = $1;
  $exception = substr($exception,4);
  $exception = substr($exception,0,-5); 
}
my $elapsed_time = $end_time - $start_time;

if ($verbose_flag) {
  print Dumper $result;
  if (1 == 0) {
  }
  else {
    my $result_string = $result;
    #print $result_string, "\n";
    my @lines = split /\n/, $result_string;
    my $encrypted_text;
    my $cdata_flag = 0;
    foreach my $line (@lines) {
      if ($cdata_flag == 1) {
        if ($line =~ m/]]/) {
          $cdata_flag = 0;
        } else {
          $encrypted_text .= "$line\n";
        }
      } else {
        if ($line =~ m/CDATA/) {
          $cdata_flag = 1;
          $line =~ s/^\s+\<!\[CDATA\[//;
          $encrypted_text = "$line\n";
        }
      }
    }

    if (defined($encrypted_text) && (0 < length($encrypted_text))) {
      my $pgp = new BLUELITE::GPG(homedir => '/ds/gnupg',
      );

      my $result = $pgp->decrypt_verify('Niwthh', $encrypted_text);
      if ($pgp->error()) {
        print "Failed decryption: " . $pgp->error() . "\n";
      }
      else {
        print "Signature verified for " . $result->{'key_user'} . "\n";
        my $decrypted_text = $result->{'text'};
        print Dumper $result;
        print $decrypted_text;
      }
    }
  }
} 

print "\n$host|$start_date|$end_date|$last_name|$first_name|$dob|$gender|$zip_code|$cardholder|$return|$exception|$start_time|$end_time|$elapsed_time\n";

#move_sources
#!/usr/bin/perl

use BLUELITE::Common;
use Getopt::Std;        # for parsing command line arguments

# version info:
# April 25, 2005 - Changed "mv" invokation to "cp -> touch -r -> rm" method

our $DS_BASE_DIR = $ENV{DS_BASE_DIR};
die "ERROR: DS_BASE_DIR environment variable is '$DS_BASE_DIR', which is not an existing directory\n" if (! ((defined($DS_BASE_DIR)) && (-d $DS_BASE_DIR)));

$SOURCE_INFO{T}{IN_DIR} = '/ds/data_sources/incoming/tulsa';
$SOURCE_INFO{T}{FMASK} = '*.dat.gz';

$SOURCE_INFO{P}{IN_DIR} = '/ds/data_sources/incoming/vftp';
$SOURCE_INFO{P}{FMASK} = '*.zip *.dat.gz';

$SOURCE_INFO{INC}{IN_DIR} = '/ds/data_sources/incoming/cps';
$SOURCE_INFO{INC}{FMASK} = '*.DOWNLOAD.IL* *.HCPSDNLD.IL* *.DOWNLOAD.PX* *.HCPSDNLD.PX*';
$SOURCE_INFO{INC}{OUT_DIR} = "$DS_BASE_DIR/pal/lookup_data/contract_exclusions";

$PCLAIMS_TOP = '/ds/data_sources/pclaims';
$HCLAIMS_TOP = '/ds/data_sources/hospital_claims';

$EXIT_CODE = 0;

$WU_FILE = "$DS_BASE_DIR/common/etc/wu.move_sources";

$minimum_file_age = 60 * 20;	# files wont be moved if modified within the last $minimum_file_age seconds

$PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s!^.*/!!;

sub usage() {

	print "Usage: $PGM [-t] -s T|P|INC [-o] [-q] -a|YYYYMM
Note:	-o means overwrite existing OLDER files
	-a means move all files regardless of year and month
	-s means source to move (T for Tulsa, P for Proxymed)
	-t means test only (only displays move commands, does not actually move or rename anything
	-q means quiet mode\n";
}

if (! defined($ARGV[0])) {
	&usage;
	exit(0);
}

getopts('-as:otdq');

if (defined($opt_d)) {
	$DEBUG = 1;
}

if (defined($opt_q)) {
	$quiet_mode = 1;
}

if (defined($opt_o)) {
	$overwrite_older_files = 1;
} else {
	$overwrite_older_files = 0;
}

if (defined($opt_a)) {
	$do_all_yyyymm = 1;
	$date_request_text = 'ALL';
} else {
	$do_all_yyyymm = 0;
}

if ($ARGV[0] =~ /^[0-9][0-9][0-9][0-9][0-9][0-9]$/) {
	$requested_yyyymm = $ARGV[0];
	$date_request_text = $requested_yyyymm;
	$do_all_yyyymm = 0;
} elsif (! $do_all_yyyymm) {
	die "ERROR: Must specify -a or valid YYYYMM\n";
}


if (defined($opt_s)) {
	$SOURCE = $opt_s;
	$source_dir = $SOURCE_INFO{$SOURCE}{IN_DIR};

	if (! defined($source_dir)) {
		die "ERROR: Source value of $SOURCE is not valid.\n";
	}
} else {
	die "ERROR: Must specify source via -s option\n";
}

if (defined($opt_t)) {
	$test_only = 1;
} else {
	$test_only = 0;
}

chdir($source_dir) || die "ERROR: Unable to cd to $source_dir: $!\n";

if (! -w $source_dir) {
	die "ERROR: File movement did not begin because no write permission exists for source directory $source_dir\n";
}

foreach $curr_name (glob($SOURCE_INFO{$SOURCE}{FMASK})) {

	$new_full_name = '';

	if ($SOURCE eq 'INC') {
		if ($curr_name =~ /^\$?([^.]+)[.](DOWNLOAD|HCPSDNLD)[.]([^0-9]+)([0-9][0-9])([0-9][0-9])([0-9][0-9])[^0-9]*$/i) {
			($prefix, $root, $suffix, $yy, $mm, $dd) = ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6);
			$REQUESTED_YEAR_MONTH = substr($requested_yyyymm, 2, 4);	# YYMM
			$FILE_YEAR_MONTH = "${yy}${mm}";
			$new_full_name = $SOURCE_INFO{$SOURCE}{OUT_DIR} . "/${prefix}.${root}.${suffix}${yy}${mm}${dd}.gz";
		}
	} else {
		$REQUESTED_YEAR_MONTH = $requested_yyyymm;	# YYYYMM
		$fname_date = &get_filename_date($curr_name);
		($yyyy, $mm) = (substr($fname_date, 0, 4), substr($fname_date, 2, 2));
		$FILE_YEAR_MONTH = "${yyyy}${mm}";

		$new_full_name = &get_std_full_filename($curr_name);
	}

	$curr_full_name = "${source_dir}/${curr_name}";

	if (length($new_full_name) > 0) {
		$YYYYMM = "${yyyy}${mm}";

		if (($FILE_YEAR_MONTH eq $REQUESTED_YEAR_MONTH) or ($do_all_yyyymm)) {

			$output_dir = $new_full_name;
			$output_dir =~ s/\/[^\/]+$//;

			if ((! -d $output_dir) && (! -l $output_dir)) {
				die "ERROR: File movement did not begin because output directory $output_dir does not exist!\n";

				# add sym link creation logic later

				#print STDERR "Note: Creating output directory $output_dir\n";
				#system('mkdir', $output_dir);

				#if (! -d $output_dir) {
				#	die "ERROR: File movement did not begin because output directory $output_dir could not be created\n";
				#}
			}

			if (! -w $output_dir) {
				die "ERROR: File movement did not begin due to no write permission on output directory $output_dir\n";
			}

			$move_list{$curr_full_name} = $new_full_name;
		}
	}
}

if ($DEBUG) {
	print STDERR "Source directory: $source_dir\n";
	print STDERR "Source data: $opt_s\n";
	print STDERR "Month requested: $date_request_text\n\n";
}

$curr_time = time;	# get current time

foreach $old_file (keys %move_list) {

	if (! -r $old_file) {
		print STDERR "Warning: No read permission for file $old_file\n";
		delete $move_list{$old_file};
		$EXIT_CODE = 1;
		next;
	}

	$new_file = $move_list{$old_file};

	if (! (length($new_file) > 0)) {
		print STDERR "Warning: Could not determine new location or name for file $old_file\n";
		delete $move_list{$old_file};
		$EXIT_CODE = 1;
		next;
	}

	($dev,$ino,$mode,$nlink,$uid,$gid,$rdev,$fsize,$atime,$old_mtime,$ctime,$blksize,$blocks) = stat($old_file);
	($dev,$ino,$mode,$nlink,$uid,$gid,$rdev,$fsize,$atime,$new_mtime,$ctime,$blksize,$blocks) = stat($new_file);

	if (-f $new_file) {
		if ($new_mtime < $old_mtime) {
			if ($overwrite_older_files) {
				print STDERR "Note: older existing file will be overwritten: $new_file\n";
			} else {
				print STDERR "Warning: older existing file will NOT be overwritten: $new_file . Use -o to override\n";
				delete $move_list{$old_file};
				$EXIT_CODE = 1;
				next;
			}
		} else {
			print STDERR "ERROR: newer existing file will NOT be overwritten: $new_file . Incoming file = $old_file\n";
			delete $move_list{$old_file};
			$EXIT_CODE = 1;
			next;
		}
	}

	if (exists($unique_output_files{$new_file})) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: A new location the output file $new_file was derived from two different input files:
$old_file
$unique_output_files{$new_file}
Those files will NOT be moved\n";
		delete $move_list{$old_file};
		delete $move_list{$unique_output_files{$new_file}};
		next;
	} else {
		$unique_output_files{$new_file} = $old_file;
	}

	if ($old_mtime > ($curr_time - $minimum_file_age)) {
		print STDERR "Warning: The following file has been modified within the last $minimum_file_age seconds seconds, and will not be moved: $old_file\n";
		delete $move_list{$old_file};
		next;
	}

	$preliminary_num_files++;
}

if (! ($preliminary_num_files > 0)) {
	if (! $quiet_mode) {
		print STDERR "No $opt_s files to move\n";
	}

	exit(0);
}

if ($SOURCE ne 'INC') {
	$WU_FILE_DONE = $WU_FILE . '.done';

	open(WU, "> $WU_FILE") || die "Cannot create $WU_FILE : $!\n";

	foreach $old_file (keys %move_list) {
		print WU $old_file . "\n" || die "Cannot write to $WU_FILE : $!\n";
	}

	close(WU);

	if (-f $WU_FILE_DONE) {
		if (unlink($WU_FILE_DONE) != 1) {
			die "Cannot remove $WU_FILE_DONE : $!\n";
		}
	}

	print STDERR "Checking compression integrity of $preliminary_num_files files\n";

	$ret = system("prun2 -q -r rx -f $WU_FILE gunzip -t %p > /dev/null 2>&1");
	$ret = $ret >> 8;

	if (! -f $WU_FILE_DONE) {
		die "Unable to determine how many files passed zip integrity. File $WU_FILE_DONE missing\n";
	}

	open(WU_DONE, $WU_FILE_DONE) || die "Unable to open $WU_FILE_DONE : $!\n";

	while (<WU_DONE>) {
		chop;
		($done_filename) = split(',', $_);

		$goodzip_files{$done_filename} = 1;
	}

	close(WU_DONE);

	print STDERR "\n";

	foreach $old_file (keys %move_list) {

		if (! exists($goodzip_files{$old_file})) {
			delete $move_list{$old_file};

			print STDERR "ERROR: The following file did not pass zip integrity check: $old_file\n";

			$EXIT_CODE = 1;
		}
	}
}

$total_file_size = 0;
$files_moved = 0;

foreach $old_file (keys %move_list) {

	$file_ok = 0;
	$new_file = $move_list{$old_file};

	$bname_old_file = $old_file;
	$bname_old_file =~ s!^.*/!!;

	print STDERR "move $bname_old_file to ${new_file} ... ";

	($dev,$ino,$mode,$nlink,$uid,$gid,$rdev,$fsize,$atime,$mtime,$ctime,$blksize,$blocks) = stat($old_file);

	if (! $test_only) {
		if ($SOURCE ne 'INC') {
			move_file($old_file, $new_file);
		} else {
			$type = `file '$old_file'`;

			if ($type =~ /text/i) {
				$ret = system("gzip -c '$old_file' > $new_file");
				$ret = $ret >> 8;

				if ($ret == 0) {
					if (-f $new_file) {
						unlink($old_file);
					}
				} else {
					print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to gzip $old_file to $new_file\n";
					unlink($new_file);
					$EXIT_CODE = 1;
				}
			} else {
				move_file($old_file, $new_file);
			}
		}

		if (-f $old_file) {
			print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to move $old_file to $new_file\n";
			$EXIT_CODE = 1;
		} elsif (! -f $new_file) {
			print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to move $old_file to $new_file\n";
			$EXIT_CODE = 1;
		} else {
			$file_ok = 1;
			$files_moved++;
			print STDERR "done\n";
		}
	} else {
		$file_ok = 1;
		print STDERR "test ok\n";
	}

	if ($file_ok) {
		$total_file_size += $fsize;
	}
}

print STDERR "\nTotal size of moveable files: $total_file_size\n";
print STDERR "Files moved: $files_moved\n";

exit($EXIT_CODE);


#move_tulsa_files.pl
#!/usr/bin/perl
use File::Copy;
use strict;

#Make sure DS_BASE_DIR is set
our $DS_BASE_DIR = $ENV{DS_BASE_DIR};
die "ERROR: DS_BASE_DIR environment variable is '$DS_BASE_DIR', which is not an existing directory\n" if (! ((defined($DS_BASE_DIR)) && (-d $DS_BASE_DIR)));

#source directory
my $tulsa_root_directory = $DS_BASE_DIR . "/data_sources/incoming/tulsa";
#target directory
my $data_source_root_directory = $DS_BASE_DIR . "/data_sources/pclaims/T";
#input file
my $full_source_filename = shift @ARGV;

if ($full_source_filename =~ m/tulsa/) {

	if ( $full_source_filename =~ m/(CMST)_(\d{4})(\d{2})(\d{2}).dat.gz/ 
		|| $full_source_filename =~ m/(NSFe)_(\d{4})(\d{2})(\d{2})t.dat.gz/) {
		my $file_type = $1;
    my $year      = $2;
    my $month     = $3;
    my $day       = $4;

    #Check the file integrity
    my $gunzip_code = system("gunzip -t $full_source_filename");
    print "Checking file integrity...";
		$gunzip_code = $gunzip_code >> 8;
    if (0 != $gunzip_code) {
      print "File failed integrity check!: $full_source_filename returned code $gunzip_code\n";
      exit(100);
    }
    print "OK\n";

		my $abbr_name;
		my $subdir;

		if ( $file_type =~ 'CMST') {

			$abbr_name = 'NSFc_T';
			$subdir    = 'NSF_clean';

		} elsif ( $file_type =~ 'NSFe' ) {

			$abbr_name = 'NSFe_T';
			$subdir    = 'NSF_c1';

		#This should *NEVER* occur
		} else {

			print "Unknown file type: $file_type\n";
			exit(110);

		}

    #Create file name
		my $filename = $abbr_name . "_" . $year . $month . $day . ".dat.gz";
   	my $full_data_source_filename = $data_source_root_directory . "/" . $subdir . "/" . $year. $month . "/" . $filename;
  
    #Move file to destination
    print "Moving $full_source_filename to $full_data_source_filename...";
    if (! move($full_source_filename, $full_data_source_filename) ) {
      print "Error moving $full_source_filename to $full_data_source_filename: $!\n";
      exit(120);
    }
    print "OK\n";

  }
  else {
    print "File did not match expected naming convention (CMST)_(\d{4})(\d{2})(\d{2}).dat.gz or (NSFe)_(\d{4})(\d{2})(\d{2})t.dat.gz: $full_source_filename\n";
    exit(140);
  }
} else {
  print "Do not understand file source: $full_source_filename\n";
  exit(150);
}

#move_ubs.pl
#!/usr/bin/perl

use File::Copy;
use strict;

my $verispan_root_directory = "/ds/production/verispan/incoming";
my $data_source_root_directory = "/ds/data_sources/hospital_claims";
my $full_source_filename = shift @ARGV;

if ($full_source_filename =~ m/tulsa/) {
  my $file_source  = "tulsa";
  my $short_source = "T";
  if ($full_source_filename =~ m/ub_(raw|phi)_(\d{4})(\d{2})(\d{2}).dat.gz/) {
    my $file_type = $1;
    my $year      = $2;
    my $month     = $3;
    my $day       = $4;
    
    #Test file
    my $gunzip_code = system("gunzip -t $full_source_filename");
    print "Checking file integrity...";
    if (0 != $gunzip_code) {
      print "File failed integrity check!: $full_source_filename returned code $gunzip_code\n";
      exit(100);
    }
    print "OK\n";
    
    #Set up file naming conventions
    my $short_type = undef;
    if ($file_type eq "raw") {
      $file_type  = "raw";
      $short_type = "r";
    }
    elsif ($file_type eq "phi") {
      $file_type  = "c1";
      $short_type = "e";
    }
    else {
      print "Error - Do not understand file type: $full_source_filename has type $file_type\n";
      exit(110);
    }
    
    #Create file name
    my $filename = "UB" . $short_type . "_" . $short_source . "_" . $year . $month . $day . ".dat.gz";
    my $full_data_source_filename = $data_source_root_directory . "/" . $file_source . "/UB_" .$file_type . "/" . $year . $month . "/" . $filename;

    #Move file to destination
    print "Moving $full_source_filename to $full_data_source_filename...";
    if (! move($full_source_filename, $full_data_source_filename) ) {
      print "Error moving $full_source_filename to $full_data_source_filename: $!\n";
      exit(120);
    }
    print "OK\n";
    
		# COMMENTED OUT (dliu) on 3/29/2010. Verispan has been disabled.

    #Copy raw files to verispan incoming directory
    #if ($file_type eq "raw") {
      #Create verspan file name
    #  my $full_verispan_filename = $verispan_root_directory . "/" . $filename;
    #  print "Copying $full_data_source_filename to $full_verispan_filename...";
    #  if (! copy($full_data_source_filename, $full_verispan_filename) ) {
    #    print "Error moving $full_data_source_filename to $full_verispan_filename: $!\n";
    #    exit(130);
    #  }
    #  print "OK\n";
    #}
  }
  else {
    print "File did not match expected naming convention ub_(raw|phi)_YYYYMMDD.dat.gz: $full_source_filename\n";
    exit(140);
  }
} else {
  print "Do not understand file source: $full_source_filename\n";
  exit(150);
}

    if 0; # not running under some shell

#mrdd_delta_data_checker.sh
#!/usr/bin/bash

#Author: William Hampton

#Checks that the rxbc_mrdd_delta_extract.pl is extracting current days worth of data.

if [ $(find /ds/env/prod/RXBC/common/log -name "mrdd_delta*" -mtime 0.1 -exec grep -iP 'starting to process post-date' {} \; | wc -l) -gt 0 ]; then
    echo "Yesterday's post-date data has been processed for the MRDD Delta Load"  | mailx -s "MRDD Delta Load Data Check" william.hampton@McKesson.com
else 
    echo "Yesterdays's post-date data has not been processed for the MRDD Delta Load" | mailx -s "MRDD Delta Load Data Check" DataServicesNotification@McKesson.com
fi   

#mrun


if [ ! -d "$DS_BASE_DIR" ]
  then
    echo "ERROR: DS_BASE_DIR environment variable is '$DS_BASE_DIR', which is not an existing directory"
    exit 1
fi


server_file="$DS_BASE_DIR/common/etc/server.info"

if [ ! -f $server_file ]
  then
	echo "Cannot find server file $server_file"
	exit 1
fi

server_list=`cut -d: -f1 < $server_file | tr "\012" ' '`

usage() {
	echo "usage: $0 [-p] command [options] -- server1 [server2] ..."
	echo "server list = $server_list"
	exit 0
}

if [ "$1" = "" ]
  then
	usage
	exit 0
fi

if [ "$1" = '-p' ]
  then
		background='&'
		shift
fi

case $1 in
	-*)	echo "$1 is not a supported option"
			usage
			break;;
esac

command=$1
shift 1

found_sep=0

for parm in $*
  do
	shift

	if [ "$parm" != '--' ]
	  then
		if [ "$parm_list" = "" ]
		  then
			parm_list="$parm"
		  else
			parm_list="$parm_list $parm"
		fi
	  else
		found_sep=1
		break
	fi
  done

if [ "$found_sep" -eq 0 ]
  then
	echo "Did not find --"
	usage
	exit 1
fi

if [ $# -eq 0 ]
  then
	echo "No server list found after --"
	usage
	exit 1
fi

for server_info in `cat $server_file | cut -d: -f1,4,5`
  do
	s_name=`echo $server_info | cut -d: -f1`
	s_rsh=`echo $server_info | cut -d: -f2`
	s_grp=`echo $server_info | cut -d: -f3`

	for server in $*
	  do
		s_prefix_name=`echo $server | cut -d. -f1`

		if [ "$s_name" = "$server" -o "$s_grp" = "$server" -o "$s_name" = "$s_prefix_name" ]
		  then
			echo RUNNING $s_rsh $s_name $command $parm_list "#######################"
			cmd="$s_rsh -q -X $s_name \"[ -f /etc/profile ] && . /etc/profile; [ -f \$HOME/.bash_profile ] && . \$HOME/.bash_profile; [ -d $PWD ] && cd $PWD ; eval $command $parm_list\""
			eval "$cmd | sed 's/^/$server:/' $background"
			break
		fi
	  done
  done

wait

#nsf_clean_wrap
#!/usr/bin/perl

# nsf_clean: Applies NDCHealth standardization of non-encrypted NSF (HCFA 1500) files from H, L, C, P, N or M sources
# Author: jmh, NDCHealth
#
# - Removes non-standard records
# - Removes unterminated, orphaned, and operationally duplicate claims
# - Fixes YA0 and ZA0 records in H,L,C,N,P sources
# - Blanks out appropriate AA0 (submitter) fields
# - Sets submitter id field in AA0 records to value passed in as -s option
# - Fixes bad record ID character for DA records (caused by MU bug)
# - Converts Windows/DOS record delimiters to UNIX record delimiters (replaces ending CR/LF with LF)
# - Converts binary characters to spaces
#

# Version history:
# 2004 - Version 1.0
# - Initial release
#
# 2004 - Version 1.1 - 1.41
# - Added other options :-)
#
# 20050610 - Version 1.42
# - Added -k option to enable skipping generation if existing output file is newer than input file
#	- Added -g option to enable debugging output
#
# 20050615 - Version 1.43
# - Empty file error now generated when output goes to STDOUT
# - Output files now removed when input file is empty or other output error happens
#
# 20051109 - Version 1.44
# - Added TC as valid source
# - Limited fix of YA0 and ZA0 records to H,L,C,N,P sources
# - Added -L option to add structured logging of stats
# - Added -v valid_set option to support named "valid NSF record ID sets"
#		(supported sets are 'external' (default) and 'ihr')
#

use Getopt::Std;
use String::CRC;
use BLUELITE::Common;
use DateTime;

$VERSION = '1.44';
$prog_name = "nsf_clean";


if (! defined($ARGV[0])) {
	print STDERR "$prog_name : Version $VERSION\n\n";

	print STDERR "Usage 1: $0 [-kgL] [-f file_id] [-s submitter_id] [-d|D output_dir [-r dest_host]] [-e success_exit_status] [-v valid_set] -i input_list_file
Usage 2: $0 [-kgL] [-f input_file] [-s submitter_id] [-d|D output_dir [-r dest_host]] [-e success_exit_status] [-v valid_set] [raw_input_file] [raw_input_file ...]

-d	Top-level output directory. Output dir is derived to YYYYMM based on input file name
-D	Output directory
-r	Use write_file (ftp) to send file to dest_host
-k	Skip clean process if output file already exists and is newer than input file
-v	Use valid record set named valid_set as record inclusion list (supported sets are 'external' (default) and 'ihr')
-L	Use structured format for stats log output
-g	Turn on debugging output\n";
	exit(1);
}

getopts('d:D:i:r:f:s:e:kgLv:');

@valid_nsf_rec_types = (
'AA0',
'BA0',
'BA1',
'CA0',
'CA1',
'CB0',
'DA0',
'DA1',
'DA2',
'DA3',
'EA0',
'EA1',
'EA2',
'FA0',
'FB0',
'FB1',
'FB2',
'FB3',
'FD0',
'FE0',
'GA0',
'GC0',
'GD0',
'GD1',
'GE0',
'GP0',
'GU0',
'GX0',
'GX1',
'GX2',
'HA0',
'XA0',
'YA0',
'ZA0'
);

if (defined($opt_v)) {
	if ($opt_v =~ /^\s*ihr\s*$/i) {
		push(@valid_nsf_rec_types, 'DA9', 'EA9', 'FA9', 'GD9');
	} elsif ($opt_v !~ /^\s*external\s*$/i) {
		die "ERROR: Only 'ihr' or 'external' may be used for -v option. '$opt_v' is not a recognized valid_set\n";
	}
}

foreach $rec_type (@valid_nsf_rec_types) {
	$valid_nsf_rec_types{$rec_type} = 1;
}


if (defined($opt_L)) {
	$STRUCTURED_LOG = 1;
} else {
	$STRUCTURED_LOG = 0;
}

if (defined($opt_g)) {
	$DEBUG = 1;
} else {
	$DEBUG = 0;
}

if (defined($opt_k)) {
	$skip_if_newer = 1;
} else {
	$skip_if_newer = 0;
}

if (defined($opt_e)) {
	$success_exit = $opt_e;
} else {
	$success_exit = 200;
}

if (defined($opt_f)) {
	$file_id = $opt_f;
	$file_id_base = $file_id;
}

if (defined($opt_D)) {
	$output_dir = $opt_D;

	if (! -d $output_dir) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: Output directory $output_dir does not exist\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	$USE_STDOUT = 0;

	if (defined($opt_r)) {
		$remote_host = $opt_r;
	}
} elsif (defined($opt_d)) {
	$output_dir_top = $opt_d;
	if (! -d $output_dir_top) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: Output top directory $output_dir_top does not exist\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	$USE_STDOUT = 0;

	if (defined($opt_r)) {
		$remote_host = $opt_r;
	}
} else {
	$USE_STDOUT = 1;

	if (defined($opt_r)) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: -r option can only be used with -d or -D option\n";
		exit(1)
	}

	if ($file_id eq '') {
		$file_id = 'STDOUT';
		$file_id_base = $file_id;
	}
}

if (defined($opt_i)) {

	if (defined($ARGV[0])) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: Cannot specify input file name when using -i option\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	$input_list_file = $opt_i;

	if (($input_list_file ne '-') and (! &file_exists($input_list_file))) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: Input list file $input_list_file does not exist\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	open(FILE_LIST, $input_list_file) || die "Cannot open input list file $input_list_file : $!\n";
	while (<FILE_LIST>) {
		chop;
		s/^[	 ]+//;

		if (length($_) > 0) {
			push(@input_files, $_);
		}
	}

	close(FILE_LIST);

} else {
	if (! defined($ARGV[0])) {
		if (-t 0) {
			print STDERR "ERROR: Input data from terminal not supported. Must get input via -i option, command line file names, or via non-terminal standard input (STDIN)\n";
			exit(1);
		} else {
			if (! $USE_STDOUT) {
				print STDERR "ERROR: Cannot use -d option when input is from STDIN\n";
				exit(1);
			}

			$USE_STDIN = 1;
			$input_files[0] = '-';
		}
	} else {
		@input_files = @ARGV;
	}
}


if (! ($#input_files >= 0)) {
	print STDERR "ERROR: No input files to clean!\n";
	exit(1);
}

if (! $USE_STDIN) {
	foreach $input_file (@input_files) {

		if (! &file_exists($input_file)) {
			print STDERR "ERROR: Input file $input_file does not exist!\n";
			exit(1);
		}

		$data_type = &get_filename_data_type($input_file);

		if (! defined($data_type)) {
			print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to determine whether data is NSF\n";
			exit(1);
		}

		if ($data_type ne 'NSF') {
			print STDERR "ERROR: Data type for input file $input_file is not NSF\n";
			exit(1);
		}

		$data_source = &get_filename_data_source($input_file);

		if (! defined($data_source)) {
			print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to determine where data source is from (T, L, H, C, N, P, TC) for $input_file\n";
			exit(1);
		}

		# $submitter = "CMS${data_source}";

		if (! $USE_STDOUT) {
			$fname_date = &get_filename_date($input_file);

			if (! defined($fname_date)) {
				print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to determine filename date of input file $input_file\n";
				exit(1);
			}

			$YYYYMM = substr($fname_date, 0, 6);

			if (defined($opt_d)) {
				$output_dir = "$output_dir_top/$YYYYMM";

				if (! -d $output_dir) {
					print STDERR "Note: Creating output month directory $output_dir\n";

					system('mkdir', $output_dir);

					if (! -d $output_dir) {
						print STDERR "ERROR: Unable to create output month directory $output_dir\n";
						exit(1);
					}
				}
			}

			$seq = &get_filename_unique_seq($input_file);

			if ($seq == 1) {
				$seq = '';
			}

			if (length($seq) > 0) {
				$seq = "_$seq";
			}

			$output_file_new_base = "${data_type}c_${data_source}_${fname_date}${seq}.dat.gz";
			$output_file_new = "$output_dir/$output_file_new_base";

			if ($output_file_new eq $input_file) {
				print STDERR "ERROR: Output file name is the same as input file name: $output_file_new\n";
				exit(1);
			}

			if (exists($outfiles{$output_file_new})) {
				print STDERR "ERROR: Output file name $output_file_new is the same for at least the following two different input files: $outfiles{$output_file_new} and $input_file\n";
				exit(1);
			}

			if (-f $output_file_new) {
				if ($skip_if_newer) {
					($dev,$ino,$mode,$nlink,$uid,$gid,$rdev,$file_size,$atime,$outfile_mtime,$ctime,$blksize,$blocks) = stat($output_file_new);
					($dev,$ino,$mode,$nlink,$uid,$gid,$rdev,$file_size,$atime,$inputfile_mtime,$ctime,$blksize,$blocks) = stat($input_file);

					if ($outfile_mtime >= $inputfile_mtime) {

						if ($DEBUG) {
 	      	   print STDERR "debug: existing output file $output_file_new is newer or same age as input file $input_file . Skipping.\n";
 	      	 	}

						next;

					} else {
						print STDERR "Regenerating older existing file $output_file_new\n";
					}
				} else {
					if ($DEBUG) {
						print STDERR "debug: existing file $output_file will be overwritten\n";
					}
				}
			} else {
 		    print STDERR "New file will be generated: $output_file_new\n";
			}

			if (! exists($outfiles{$output_file_new})) {
				$num_output_files++;
			}

			$outfiles{$output_file_new} = $input_file;
			$infiles{$input_file} = $output_file_new;
		} else {
			$infiles{$input_file} = '-';
		}
	}
} else {
	$infiles{'-'} = '-';
}

if (($file_id eq '') and ($num_output_files == 1)) {
	$file_id = $output_file_new;
	$file_id_base = $output_file_new_base;
}

if (defined($opt_s)) {
	$submitter = uc($opt_s);

	if ($submitter !~ /^CMS([HLCPNT]|TC)$/) {
		print STDERR "$prog_name: submitter must be CMS[H|L|C|P|N|T|TC]\n";
		exit(10);
	}
} elsif ($USE_STDIN) {
	print STDERR "ERROR: Must specify submitter id via -s option when input is from STDIN\n";
	exit(1);
}

#if (! open(COMPRESS_OUT, "| gzip -c | write_file -f -h $remote_host $output_file")) {
#	die "Cannot start gzip process to create $output_file : $!\n";
#}

if ($USE_STDOUT) {

	if (! open(OUTPUT, '>-')) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: Cannot output STDOUT : $!\n";
		exit(1);
	}
}

sub replace_substr() {
  my($string, $start, $end, $sub) = (@_);
  my($begin, $begin_length, $sub_length, $end_length);

$begin = substr($string, 0, ($start - 1));
$begin_length = $start; 
$sub_length = $end - $start + 1;
$end_length = length($string) - $sub_length;

return sprintf("%-0.${begin_length}s%-${sub_length}.${sub_length}s%-0.${end_length}s", substr($string, 0, $begin_length), $sub, substr($string, $begin_length + $sub_length));

}

sub remove_output() {

	if ((! $USE_STDOUT) and ($num_output_files > 0)) {
			unlink(values %infiles);	# this removes the output files, despite how it looks
	}

}

$num_input_records = 0;

foreach $input_file (keys %infiles) {

	$outfile = $infiles{$input_file};

	if ($input_file =~ /[.](pgp|gz|zip)$/) {
		$infile_cmd = "read_file $input_file |";

		if ($submitter eq '') {
			$data_source = &get_filename_data_source($input_file);
			$submitter = "CMS${data_source}";
		}
	} elsif ($input_file eq '-') {
		$infile_cmd = '-';
	} else {
		$infile_cmd = $input_file;

		if ($submitter eq '') {
			$data_source = &get_filename_data_source($input_file);
			$submitter = "CMS${data_source}";
		}
	}

	if ($submitter eq '') {
		print STDERR "ERROR: Cannot determine correct submitter for input file $input_file\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	if (! open(INPUT, $infile_cmd)) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: Cannot open input '$infile_cmd' : $!\n";
		exit(1);
	}

	if (! $USE_STDOUT) {

		if (defined($remote_host)) {
			if (! open(OUTPUT, "| gzip -c | write_file -f -h $remote_host $outfile")) {
				print STDERR "ERROR: Cannot start output compression process for input file $input_file : $!\n";
				exit(1);
			}
		} else {
			if (! open(OUTPUT, "| gzip -c > $outfile")) {
				print STDERR "ERROR: Cannot start output compression process for input file $input_file : $!\n";
				exit(1);
			}
		}
	}


	### NSF CLEAN LOGIC BEGINS HERE ###

	$in_claim = 0;
	@claim_record = ();
	$num_claims_input = 0;
	$unique_claims_output = 0;
	$num_unterminated_claims = 0;
	$valid_claims_input = 0;
	$duplicate_claims_skipped = 0;

	while (<INPUT>) {

		s/^D\301/DA/;	# fix bad DA recs
