			$curr_host = $server;
		}
	}

	&print_mesg("Had to use alternate method to select $curr_host as best server\n") if (defined($curr_host));

	return $curr_host;
}


sub get_available_server($) {
  my $threads_running = shift;

	my $curr_time = time;
	my $hinfo = {};

	$SCHEDULER = Schedule::Load::Schedule->fetch;

	my ($hname, $ho, $curr_load_factor);
	my $avail_server = {};

	foreach my $server (keys %server_info) {
		next if ($server_info{$server}{'threads_max'} == 0);

		$Debug && print "debug: considering server $server, tr = " . $server_info{$server}{'threads_running'} . ", prc = " . $server_info{$server}{'processors'} . "\n";

		if (defined($server_info{$server}{'threads_running'}) && ($server_info{$server}{'threads_running'} >= $server_info{$server}{'processors'})) {
			$Debug && print "debug: already running " . $server_info{$server}{'threads_running'} . " work units on $server (max " . $server_info{$server}{'processors'} . ")\n";
			next;
		}

		if (exists($server_info{$server}->{last_launch_time}) &&
			(($curr_time - $server_info{$server}->{last_launch_time}) < $MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS)) {
			$Debug && print "debug: has not yet been $MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS seconds since last work unit launched on $server\n";
			next;
		}

		$ho = $SCHEDULER->get_host($server);

		if (! defined($ho)) {
			$Debug && &print_mesg("debug: WARNING: could not get host object for $server\n");
			next;
		}

		$prev_stat_time = $server_info{$server}->{last_stat_time};

		$curr_rss = $ho->total_rss;
		$prev_rss = $server_info{$server}->{last_rss};

		$curr_vir = $ho->total_size;
		$prev_vir = $server_info{$server}->{last_vir};

		if (
			($curr_rss != $prev_rss) ||
			($curr_vir != $prev_vir) ||
			(($threads_running == 0) && (($curr_time - $prev_stat_time) >= $MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS)) ||
			(($curr_time - $prev_stat_time) >= (3 * $MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS))
		) {

			$server_info{$server}->{last_stat_time} = $curr_time;
			$server_info{$server}->{last_rss} = $curr_rss;
			$server_info{$server}->{last_vir} = $curr_vir;

			$Debug && print "debug: On $server . curr_rss = $curr_rss, prev_rss = $prev_rss, curr_time = $curr_time, prev time = $prev_stat_time\n";

			if (accelerating_mem($curr_rss, $prev_rss, $server_info{$server}->{phys_mem}, $curr_time, $prev_stat_time, $MIN_SECONDS_TIL_RSS_FULL)) {
				$Debug &&	print "debug: RSS accelerating too fast on $server\n";
				$server_info{$server}->{rss_accel} = 1;
			} else {
				$server_info{$server}->{rss_accel} = 0;
			}

			$Debug && print "debug: On $server . curr_vir = $curr_vir, prev_vir = $prev_vir, curr_time = $curr_time, prev time = $prev_stat_time\n";

			if (accelerating_mem($curr_vir, $prev_vir, $server_info{$server}->{phys_mem}, $curr_time, $prev_stat_time, $MIN_SECONDS_TIL_VIRT_FULL)) {
				$Debug &&	print "debug: VIRTUAL accelerating too fast on $server\n";
				$server_info{$server}->{vir_accel} = 1;
			} else {
				$server_info{$server}->{vir_accel} = 0;
			}

			next if ($server_info{$server}->{rss_accel} || $server_info{$server}->{vir_accel});
		} elsif ($server_info{$server}->{rss_accel}) {
			$Debug &&	print "debug: RSS was accelerating too fast on $server the last time it's memory stats were gathered\n";
			next;
		} elsif ($server_info{$server}->{vir_accel}) {
			$Debug &&	print "debug: VIR was accelerating too fast on $server the last time it's memory stats were gathered\n";
			next;
		}

		$curr_load_factor = curr_load($ho);

		$Debug &&	print "debug: $server : total_size = " . $ho->total_size . ", " . $server_info{$server}->{phys_mem} . ", total_rss = " . $ho->total_rss . ", lf = $curr_load_factor, total pctcpu = " . $ho->total_pctcpu . "\n";

		if (high_memory($ho->total_size, $ho->total_rss, $server_info{$server}->{phys_mem})) {
			$Debug &&	print "debug: MEMORY TOO HIGH ON $server (total = " . $ho->total_size . ' , rss = ' . $ho->total_rss . ' , phys = ' . $server_info{$server}->{phys_mem} . ") \n";
			next;
		}

		$server_info{$server}->{ho} = $ho;

		$Debug && &print_mesg("debug: $server : curr_load_factor = $curr_load_factor, total_load = " . $ho->total_load . "\n");

		if (! can_launch($threads_running, $curr_load_factor)) {
			$Debug && print "debug: cannot launch on $server due to: total work units running = $threads_running. min work units = " . grid_min_processes() . ". nominal server load = $SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR . max server load = $SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR . $server curr_load_factor = $curr_load_factor\n";
			next;
		}

		$Debug && print "debug: can_launch($threads_running, $curr_load_factor) for $server is true\n";
		$avail_server->{$server} = { curr_load_factor => $curr_load_factor };
	}

	my @available_servers = (keys %{$avail_server});

	if (scalar(@available_servers) == 0) {
		$Debug && print "debug: No potential servers to choose from\n";
		return undef;
	}

	my $avail_txt = join(', ', map { "\'$_\' => 1" } @available_servers);
  my @best_opts = ();

	if ($threads_running >= grid_min_processes()) {
		push(@best_opts, allow_none => 1);
	} else {
		push(@best_opts, allow_none => 0);
	}

	$Debug && &print_mesg("debug: choosing among these servers (@best_opts): @available_servers \n");

	my $hname = $SCHEDULER->best(@best_opts, favor_host => undef, match_cb => 'sub { my %available_servers = (' . $avail_txt . '); my $hname = $_[0]->hostname; return exists($available_servers{$hname});}');

	# if "best" method won't come up with a server, try picking the one with the lowest load
	$hname = get_avail_server_alt($avail_server, $threads_running) if (! defined($hname));

	if (! defined($hname)) {
		$Debug && &print_mesg("debug: could not use alternate method to pick a server!\n");
		return;
	}

	$ho = $SCHEDULER->get_host($hname);

	if (! defined($ho)) {
		$Debug && &print_mesg("debug: could not get host info for $hname !\n");
		return;
	}

	# this block helps minimize chances of multiple prun2's picking the same heavily loaded server at the same time.
	# The more loaded the chosen server, the more likely we'll skip choosing it (this time).

	my $curr_load_factor = curr_load($ho);

	#my $rand_threshold = (1 - $curr_load_factor / 2) / (($curr_load_factor + 0.4) ** 2);
	my $rand_threshold = ($SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR - $curr_load_factor / 2) / (($curr_load_factor + 1.1) ** 2);

	#my $rand_threshold = (1 - $curr_load_factor / 2) / (($curr_load_factor + 1) ** 3);
	$rand_threshold = 0 if ($rand_threshold < 0);	# don't let threshold go negative
	$rand_threshold += .01;	# always guarantee some minimum chance (1%) of hitting threshold

#			my $elapsed_secs = $curr_time - $server_info->{$hname_short}->{last_launch_time};
#			if ($elapsed_secs > ($MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS * 3)) {
#				$elapsed_secs = $MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS * 3;
#			}
#
#			$rand_threshold += $elapsed_secs * $MAX_RND_THRESH_ADJ / ($MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS * 3);

	my $rnd = rand();

	if ($rnd >= $rand_threshold) {
		$Debug && &print_mesg("debug: not choosing $hname this time (lf = $curr_load_factor, rnd = $rnd, thresh = $rand_threshold)\n");
		return undef;
	}

	$Debug && &print_mesg("debug: choosing $hname (lf = $curr_load_factor, rnd = $rnd, thresh = $rand_threshold)\n");

	return $hname;
}


sub init_server_info() {
	my($server_name, $processors, $rsh_cmd, $mem, $group, $line_num, $original_line, %server_info_temp);
	my($SERVER_INFO_FILE) = shift;

	if (! open(SI, "$SERVER_INFO_FILE")) {
		&print_mesg("Warning: Unable to open server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE : $!\n");
		return 1;
	}

	%SERVER_GROUPS = ();

	$line_num = 0;

	while (<SI>) {
		chomp;
		$line_num++;
		$original_line = $_;

		$_ =~ s/^ +//;
		$_ =~ s/ +$//;

		if ($_ =~ /^#/) {
			next;
		}

		if ($_ =~ /^\s*([a-z0-9_]+)\s*=\s*['"]?([a-z0-9_.]+)['"]?\s*/i) {
			($parm, $val) = (uc($1), $2);

			if ($parm =~ /DEFAULT_HOST_SUFFIX/i) {
				if ($val ne '') {
					$DEFAULT_HOST_SUFFIX = $val;

					if ($DEFAULT_HOST_SUFFIX !~ /^[.]/) {
						$DEFAULT_HOST_SUFFIX = ".${DEFAULT_HOST_SUFFIX}";
					}
				} else {
					&print_mesg("Warning: DEFAULT_HOST_SUFFIX in $SERVER_INFO_FILE is empty!\n");
				}
			} elsif ($parm =~ /SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR/i) {
				if ($val ne '') {
					if ($val =~ /^\s*\d+([.]\d+)?\s*$/) {
						if (($val <= 2) && ($val > 0)) {
							my $old_server_max_load_factor = $SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR;
							$SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR = $val;

							if (defined($old_server_max_load_factor)) {
								if ($old_server_max_load_factor != $SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR) {
									&print_mesg("Note: SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR changed from $old_server_max_load_factor to $SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR in server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE\n");
								}
							} else {
								&print_mesg("SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR = $SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR from server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE\n");
							}

						} else {
							&print_mesg("Warning: SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR setting of '$val' is outside accepted range. Must be > 0 and <= 2. Setting of $SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR will remain unchanged.\n");
						}
					} else {
						&print_mesg("Warning: SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR setting of '$val' is invalid. Must be > 0 and <= 2. Setting of $SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR will remain unchanged.\n");
					}
				}
			} elsif ($parm =~ /SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR/i) {
				if ($val ne '') {
					if ($val =~ /^\s*\d+([.]\d+)?\s*$/) {
						if (($val <= 2) && ($val > 0)) {
							if ($val <= $SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR) {
								my $old_server_nominal_load_factor = $SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR;
								$SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR = $val;

								if (defined($old_server_nominal_load_factor)) {
									if ($old_server_nominal_load_factor != $SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR) {
										&print_mesg("Note: SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR changed from $old_server_nominal_load_factor to $SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR in server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE\n");
									}
								} else {
									&print_mesg("SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR = $SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR from server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE\n");
								}
							} else {
								&print_mesg("Warning: In server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE, SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR of $val exceeds current SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR of $SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR, which is not allowed. Ignoring setting.\n");
							}
						} else {
							&print_mesg("Warning: SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR setting of '$val' is outside accepted range. Must be > 0 and <= 2. Setting of $SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR will remain unchanged.\n");
						}
					} else {
						&print_mesg("Warning: SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR setting of '$val' is invalid. Must be > 0 and <= 2. Setting of $SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR will remain unchanged.\n");
					}
				}
			} elsif ($parm =~ /MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS/i) {
				if ($val ne '') {
					if ($val =~ /^\s*\d+(.\d+)?\s*$/) {
						if ($val > 0) {
							my $old_server_launch_delay_secs = $MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS;
							$MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS = $val;

							if (defined($old_server_launch_delay_secs)) {
								if ($old_server_launch_delay_secs != $MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS) {
									&print_mesg("Note: MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS changed from $old_server_launch_delay_secs seconds to $MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS seconds in server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE\n");
								}
							} else {
								&print_mesg("MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS = $MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS from server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE\n");
							}
						} else {
							&print_mesg("Warning: MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS setting of '$val' in server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE is invalid! Setting must be > 0 seconds. Existing setting of $MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS will remain unchanged.\n");
						}
					} else {
						&print_mesg("Warning: MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS setting of '$val' in server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE is invalid!  Existing setting of $MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS seconds will remain unchanged.\n");
					}
				}
			} elsif ($parm =~ /MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS/i) {
				if ($val ne '') {
					if ($val =~ /^\s*\d+(.\d+)?\s*$/) {
						if ($val > 0) {
							my $old_server_launch_delay_secs = $MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS;
							$MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS = $val;

							if (defined($old_server_launch_delay_secs)) {
								if ($old_server_launch_delay_secs != $MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS) {
									&print_mesg("Note: MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS changed from $old_server_launch_delay_secs seconds to $MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS seconds in server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE\n");
								}
							} else {
								&print_mesg("MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS = $MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS from server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE\n");
							}
						} else {
							&print_mesg("Warning: MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS setting of '$val' in server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE is invalid! Setting must be > 0 seconds. Existing setting of $MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS will remain unchanged.\n");
						}
					} else {
						&print_mesg("Warning: MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS setting of '$val' in server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE is invalid!  Existing setting of $MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS seconds will remain unchanged.\n");
					}
				}
			} else {
				&print_mesg("Warning: the following line in $SERVER_INFO_FILE is not a recognized setting!: '$_'\n");
			}

			next;
		}

		next if (! ($_ =~ /[:,]/));

		($server_name, $processors, $mem, $rsh_cmd, $group) = split('[:,]', $_);

		if ($server_name eq '') {
			&print_mesg("Warning: Server name missing from line $line_num of server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE : line = '$original_line'\n");
			next;
		}

		$server_name .= $DEFAULT_HOST_SUFFIX if (defined($DEFAULT_HOST_SUFFIX) && ($server_name !~ /[.]/));

		if (! ($processors =~ /^[0-9]+$/)) {
			&print_mesg("Warning: Number of physical processors for server $server_name is not valid ($processors). Forcing to 1.\n");
			$processors = 1;
		}

		if (($rsh_cmd ne 'rsh') and ($rsh_cmd ne 'ssh')) {
			&print_mesg("Warning: rsh_cmd for $server_name is not rsh or ssh ($rsh_cmd). Assuming rsh\n");
			$rsh_cmd = 'rsh';
		}

		$server_info_temp{$server_name}{'processors'} = $processors;
		$server_info_temp{$server_name}{'rsh_method'} = $rsh_cmd;

		if (length($group) > 0) {
			$server_info_temp{$server_name}{'server_group'} = $group;
			$SERVER_GROUPS{$group}{'servers'}{$server_name} = 1;
		} else {
			$server_info_temp{$server_name}{'server_group'} = '';
		}

		if ($mem =~ /^\s*(\d+[.]?\d*)\s*g\s*$/i) {
			if (($1 >= 0.1) && ($1 <= 1000)) {
				$server_info_temp{$server_name}{'phys_mem'} = sprintf('%.1f', $1 * 1073741824);	# convert memory GB to bytes
#print "debug: physical mem for $server_name set to " . $server_info_temp{$server_name}{'phys_mem'} . "\n";
			} else {
				&print_mesg("Warning: physical memory setting for $server_name is '$1', which is outside the accepted range of 0.1 to 1000 GB. Ignoring\n");
			}
		} elsif ($mem !~ /^\s*$/) {
			&print_mesg("Warning: physical memory setting for $server_name is '$mem', which is invalid. Ignoring\n");
		}
	}

	close(SI);

	if (! defined($DEFAULT_HOST_SUFFIX)) {
		$DEFAULT_HOST_SUFFIX = $LOCAL_HOSTNAME;
		$DEFAULT_HOST_SUFFIX =~ s/^[^.]+[.]/./;
	}

	foreach my $sname (keys %server_info_temp) {
		if ($sname !~ /[.]/) {
			$full_sname = "${sname}${DEFAULT_HOST_SUFFIX}";
		} else {
			$full_sname = $sname;
		}

		foreach my $key (keys %{$server_info_temp{$sname}}) {
			$server_info{$full_sname}{$key} = $server_info_temp{$sname}{$key};
		}
	}


	if (! defined($SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR)) {
		$SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR = $DEFAULT_SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR;
		&print_mesg("Defaulting SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR to $SERVER_NOMINAL_LOAD_FACTOR\n");
	}

	if (! defined($MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS)) {
		$MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS = $DEFAULT_MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS;
		&print_mesg("Defaulting SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS to $MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS\n");
	}

	if (! defined($SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR)) {
		$SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR = $DEFAULT_SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR;
		&print_mesg("Defaulting SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR to $SERVER_MAX_LOAD_FACTOR\n");
	}
}


$return_code = 0;
$num_success = 0;
$num_fail = 0;
$threads = 0;


sub usage {

	no warnings;

	&print_mesg("Usage:\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("$PGM [-f workunit_file] [-e normal_exit_status] [-r host[:threads[%][:rsh|ssh]][,...]] [-p priority] [--] command [-options] [%p]\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("Note: If any options are specified for command, -- must be specified just prior to command.\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("Note: If no arguments or options for command are specified, %p is assumed.\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("Options and defaults:\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-f: Source of %p argument values for command (default standard input)\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-r: comma-seperated list of hosts to run on. Each host may be followed by :threads, :threads:#, or :threads:#% . Default " . (exists($ENV{PRUN_PARALLEL_HOST_SPEC}) ? $ENV{PRUN_PARALLEL_HOST_SPEC} : '{localhost}') . "\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-p: Set scheduling priority (nice value) to priority. Valid values are integers between 0 and 19. (Default 0)\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-l: Set scheduling priority to $DEFAULT_CPU_PRIORITY\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-e: Normal return/exit status from work unit (Default 0)\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-a: Max # of work unit failures allowed (Default unlimited)\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-x: Max # of successive work unit failures allowed per host (Default $MAX_SERVER_FAILURES). Use 0 to disable.\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-s: Min # of seconds between control file inspections (Default 10)\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-m: Max # of times a specific work unit can be attempted (Default 1)\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-t: Do NOT remove control file, temp work units and done files when at least one work unit fails (no effect when work units obtained via -f option)\n", 'HELP');
	print STDERR "	-h:\n"; 
	&print_mesg("	-j: job name. Displayed in execution report\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-d: temp directory used to create work unit and done files when -f option not used\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-w: comma-seperated list of email addresses to send execution report to.\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-k: comma-seperated list of email addresses to send successful execution report to.\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-u: comma-seperated list of email addresses to send UNsuccessful execution report to.\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-b: If work units are files, DO NOT attempt to launch them in descending file size order.\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("	-v: Explicit location of server info file (overrides PRUN2_SERVER_INFO environment variable)\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("general syntax: prun2 [options] [--] cmd [options] [%p] [--] [arg1] [%p] [arg2] [...] \n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("example syntax: prun2 [options] cmd [%p] [arg1] [%p] [arg2] [...] \n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("example syntax: prun2 [options] -- cmd <cmd_options> [-cmd_opt %p] [%p] -- [arg1] [arg2] [...] \n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("example syntax: prun2 [options] -- cmd <cmd_options> [%p] [arg1] [arg2] [...] \n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("Example 1: run gzip 5 at a time on local host, getting work units from command line arguments (*.dat)\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("prun2 -p 5 gzip *.dat\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("Example 2: same as #1, but get work units from workunit file\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("prun2 -f workunit -p 5 gzip\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("Example 3: same as #1, but get work units from standard input\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("find . -name '*.dat' -print |  prun2 -p 5 gzip\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("Example 4: same as #1, but passing -c option to gunzip, and running max processors on host1 and host2\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("prun2 -r host1,host2 -- gunzip -c *.dat.gz\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("(must use -- before gunzip to avoid confusion between prun2 options and gunzip options)\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("Example 5: run gzip 6 at a time, with '-S .GZ option' passed to gzip, getting work units from command line arguments (*.dat)\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("(must use -- before *.dat so prun2 won't mistakenly think that '.GZ' is one of the work units)\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("prun2 -p 6 -- gzip -S .GZ -- *.dat\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("Example 6: same as #4, with alternate syntax\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("prun2 -p 6 -- gzip -S .GZ %p *.dat\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("(any occurrance of %p is replaced by a work unit with each execution of gzip)\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("Example 7: run cmd 6 at a time on host1 and 4 at a time on host2, passing '-s %p' work unit arguments as first argument to cmd, work units\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("obtained from command line arguments (*.dat)\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("prun2 -p 6 -r host2:4,host1 -- cmd -s %p -k -c *.dat\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("Note: Perform 'echo rx:0 > workunit.control' to prevent new work units from being executed on rx.\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("Note: Perform 'echo rx:2 > workunit.control' to change parallel_degree on rx to 2 while prun2 is still running.\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("Note: Parallel degree precedence: '-r host:threads', '-p threads', '-v server info default file'\n", 'HELP');
	&print_mesg("Note: Perform 'echo priority = 15 >> workunit.control' to change/set CPU priority for unlaunched (remaining) work units\n", 'HELP');

}

getopts('f:e:a:s:lh-i:r:m:qtj:k:u:w:bp:v:d:x:g:z');

if ($#ARGV < 0) {
	&usage;
	my_exit(0);
}

if (defined($opt_z)) {
	$Debug = 1;
}

if (defined($opt_g)) {
	if ($opt_g =~ /^\s*\d+\s*$/) {
		if ($opt_g >= 1) {
			$GRID_MIN_PROCESSES = $opt_g;
			&print_mesg("Warning: The -g option (grid_minimum_processes) was specified on the command line as $GRID_MIN_PROCESSES\n");
		} else {
			&print_mesg("ERROR: When specified, the -g option (grid_minimum_processes) must be at least 1. Value requested = $opt_g\n");
			my_exit(1);
		}
	} else {
		&print_mesg("ERROR: When specified, the -g option (grid_minimum_processes) must be a positive integer of at least 1. Value requested = $opt_g\n");
		my_exit(1);
	}
}


if (defined($opt_x)) {
	if ($opt_x =~ /^\s*\d+\s*$/) {
		$MAX_SERVER_FAILURES = $opt_x;

		if ($MAX_SERVER_FAILURES < 0) {
			&print_mesg("ERROR: Negative value of '$opt_x' not supported for -x option\n");
			my_exit(1);
		}

		if ($MAX_SERVER_FAILURES == 0) {
			$MAX_SERVER_FAILURES = undef;
		}

	} else {
		&print_mesg("ERROR: Must specify integer value for -x option. Value passed was '$opt_x'\n");
		my_exit(1);
	}
}


$TEMP_DIR = '.';

if (defined($opt_d)) {
	$TEMP_DIR = $opt_d;
}

if (! -w $TEMP_DIR) {
	$TEMP_DIR = '/tmp';
}

# Determine which server info file to use.
# Precedence is: command line overrides environment variable,
#		environment variable overrides hard-coded default

if (defined($opt_v)) {
	$SERVER_INFO_FILE = $opt_v;
} elsif (exists($ENV{PRUN2_SERVER_INFO})) {
	$SERVER_INFO_FILE = $ENV{PRUN2_SERVER_INFO};
} else {
	$SERVER_INFO_FILE = $DEFAULT_SERVER_INFO_FILE;
}


sub hostname_prefix($) {
  my $hname = $_[0];

	$hname =~ s/[.].*$//g;
	return $hname;
}

sub hostname_suffix($) {
  my $hname = $_[0];

	$hname =~ s/^[^.]+[.]//g;
	return $hname;
}


our $LOCAL_HOSTNAME = hostname;

if (! defined($LOCAL_HOSTNAME)) {
	$LOCAL_HOSTNAME = `hostname`;
	chomp($LOCAL_HOSTNAME);
}

our $LOCAL_SUFFIX = hostname_suffix($LOCAL_HOSTNAME);
our $USERNAME = getlogin() || getpwuid($<);

if (defined($opt_p)) {
	if ($opt_p !~ /^\d+$/) {
		&print_mesg("ERROR: Must specify integer priority value of at least 0 for -p option. Value passed was '$opt_p'\n");
		my_exit(1);
	}

	$workunit_priority = $opt_p;
	@PRUN_ARGV = ('nice', '-n', $workunit_priority, @ARGV);

	if (defined($opt_l)) {
		&print_mesg("Warning: '-p $opt_p' option overrides -l option. Ignoring -l option\n");
	}

} else {
	if (defined($opt_l)) {

		$workunit_priority = $DEFAULT_CPU_PRIORITY;
		@PRUN_ARGV = ('nice', '-n', $workunit_priority, @ARGV);

	} else {
		@PRUN_ARGV = @ARGV;
	}
}

if (defined($opt_q)) {
	$QUIET_MODE = 1;
}

if (defined($opt_f)) {
	@argv = @PRUN_ARGV;
	$MASTER_TODO_FILE = $opt_f;

	if ($MASTER_TODO_FILE =~ /[.]done$/) {
		die "ERROR: work unit file name '$MASTER_TODO_FILE' specified by -f option cannot end with '.done'\n";
	}

	$master_done_file = $MASTER_TODO_FILE . ".done";
	$CONTROL_FILE = $MASTER_TODO_FILE . ".control";
	$WU_SOURCE = $MASTER_TODO_FILE;

	$workunit_source_message = "Got work units from $MASTER_TODO_FILE\n";

	open(MASTER, "< $MASTER_TODO_FILE") || die "can't open $MASTER_TODO_FILE: $!";
	$master_index = -1;

	while (<MASTER>) {
		chomp;
		next if (/^[    ]*[#]/);
		next if (/^[    ]*$/);

		@M = split(',', $_);

		$master_index++;
		$master_list[$master_index] = $M[0];
	}

	close (MASTER);
	$TODO_FILE_INDICATOR = 1;

} else {
	# no -f specified, so try getting source from standard input
	if (! -t STDIN) {
		@master_list = <STDIN>;
	}


	$MASTER_TODO_FILE = "$TEMP_DIR/prun_temp.$$";
	$master_done_file = "$TEMP_DIR/prun_temp.$$.done";
	$CONTROL_FILE = "$TEMP_DIR/prun_temp.$$.control";
	$TODO_FILE_INDICATOR = 0;
	$WU_SOURCE = '{standard input}';

	if ($#master_list >= 0) {
		@argv = @PRUN_ARGV;
		chomp(@master_list);

		if (($#master_list >= 0) and (! (-f $MASTER_TODO_FILE))) {

			$workunit_source_message = "Got work units from standard input\n";

			if (open(MASTER, "> $MASTER_TODO_FILE")) {
				for($i = 0; $i <= $#master_list; $i++) {
					print MASTER $master_list[$i] . "\n";
				}
				close(MASTER);
			} else {
				&print_mesg("Warning: Unable to save recoverable copy of work units to $MASTER_TODO_FILE, continuing without recovery capability : $!\n");
			}
		} else {
			die "Error: Recoverable copy of work units already exists in temp file $MASTER_TODO_FILE\n";
		}

	} else {
		# no -f specified and no records in standard input, so try getting source from command line arguments

		$found_source_arg = 0;
		$last_command_arg_index = 0;

		for($i = $#PRUN_ARGV; $i >= 1; $i--) {
			if ($PRUN_ARGV[$i] =~ /%p/) {
				$last_command_arg_index = $i - 1;
				last;
			} elsif ($PRUN_ARGV[$i] =~ /^--$/) {
				$last_command_arg_index = $i - 1;
				last;
			} elsif ($PRUN_ARGV[$i] =~ /^-/) {
				$last_command_arg_index = $i;
				last;
			} else {
				$found_source_arg = 1;
				$first_source_arg_index = $i;
			}
		}

		if ($found_source_arg) {

			# grab work units from commmand line arguments and save in @master_list
			for($i = $first_source_arg_index; $i <= $#PRUN_ARGV; $i++) {
				push(@master_list, $PRUN_ARGV[$i]);
			}

			@argv = ();
			# create arg list WITHOUT work units arguments (since those will be replaced by %p)
			for($i = 0; $i <= $last_command_arg_index; $i++) {
				push(@argv, $PRUN_ARGV[$i]);
			}

			$WU_SOURCE = '{command line arguments}';
		} else {
			&print_mesg("Error: Cannot find parm list from -f, standard input, or command line arguments.\n");
			&print_mesg("Command line = " . join(' ', @PRUN_ARGV) . "\n");
			my_exit(1);
		}

		$workunit_source_message = "Got work units from command line arguments\n";

		if (open(MASTER, "> $MASTER_TODO_FILE")) {
			for($i = 0; $i <= $#master_list; $i++) {
				print MASTER $master_list[$i] . "\n";
			}
			close(MASTER);
		} else {
			&print_mesg("Warning: Unable to save recoverable copy of work units to $MASTER_TODO_FILE, continuing without recovery capability : $!\n");
		}
	}

}

($vol, $dir, $base_fname) = splitpath($MASTER_TODO_FILE);
@dirs = splitdir(rel2abs $dir);

if ($#dirs >= 1) {
	$WU_LOG_TAG = $dirs[$#dirs - 1] . '/' . $dirs[$#dirs] . '/' . $base_fname;
} elsif ($#dirs == 0) {
	$WU_LOG_TAG = $dirs[0] . '/' . $base_fname;
} else {
	$WU_LOG_TAG = $base_fname;
}

&print_mesg($workunit_source_message);

if (defined($opt_b)) {
	$SORT_WU_OK = 0;
} else {
	$SORT_WU_OK = 1;
}

if (defined($opt_w)) {
	$MAIL_ON_SUCCESS = 1;
	@success_email_addresses = split(',', $opt_w);
	$MAIL_ON_FAILURE = 1;
	@failure_email_addresses = @success_email_addresses;
}

if (defined($opt_k)) {
	$MAIL_ON_SUCCESS = 1;
	@success_email_addresses = split(',', $opt_k);
}

if (defined($opt_u)) {
	$MAIL_ON_FAILURE = 1;
	@failure_email_addresses = split(',', $opt_u);
}

if (defined($opt_j)) {
	$JOB_NAME = $opt_j;
}

if (defined($opt_t)) {
	$remove_temp_wu_on_failures = 0;
} else {
	$remove_temp_wu_on_failures = 1;
}


if (defined($opt_m)) {
	if ($opt_m > 0) {
		$MAX_ATTEMPTS = $opt_m;
	} else {
		&print_mesg("ERROR: -m option value of $opt_m is invalid. Must be an integer of at least 1\n");
		my_exit(1);
	}
} else {
	$MAX_ATTEMPTS = 1;
}


sub server_max_threads($;$) {
  my ($server_name, $max_threads_spec) = @_;
  my $max_threads;

	if (defined($server_name)) {
		if (defined($max_threads_spec)) {
			if ($max_threads_spec =~ /^\s*(\d+)(%)?\s*$/) {

				if (defined($2)) {
					my $max_threads_pct = $1;

					if (exists($server_info{$server_name})) {
						if (exists($server_info{$server_name}{processors})) {
							$max_threads = int($server_info{$server_name}{processors} * $max_threads_pct / 100);

							if (($server_info{$server_name}{processors} >= 1) and ($max_threads <= 0)) {
								$max_threads = 1;
							}
						} else {
							$max_threads = 1;
							&print_mesg("Warnning: server_max_threads(): max threads spec of '$max_threads_spec' requested for $server_name, but processors is not defined for this server. Defaulting to $max_threads.\n");
						}
					} else {
						&print_mesg("Warnning: server_max_threads(): max threads spec of '$max_threads_spec' requested for $server_name, but this server is not recognized.\n");
					}

				} else {
					$max_threads = $1;
				}

			} else {
				$max_threads = 1;
				&print_mesg("Warnning: server_max_threads(): max threads spec of '$max_threads_spec' for $server_name is invalid. Defaulting to $max_threads.\n");
			}
		} else {
			if (exists($server_info{$server_name})) {
				if (exists($server_info{$server_name}{processors})) {
					$max_threads = $server_info{$server_name}{processors};
				} else {
					$max_threads = 1;
					&print_mesg("Warnning: server_max_threads(): cannot determine max threads for server $server_name . Defaulting to $max_threads.\n");
				}
			} else {
				&print_mesg("Warnning: server_max_threads(): max threads for server $server_name cannot be determined because this server is not recognized.\n");
			}
		}
	} else {
		&print_mesg("Warning: server_max_threads(): No server name provided\n");
	}

	return $max_threads;
}


sub set_run_server_info() {
	my ($server_parm_list) = shift;
# Hess changed 5/18/2007
#	my ($initial_state) = shift;
	my (%servers_requested);

	# set run request info based on command line parameters

	%MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO = ();

	foreach $server_parm (split('[ ,]+', $server_parm_list)) {
		($l_server_name, $max_threads, $rsh_cmd) = split(':', $server_parm);

		$l_server_name =~ s/^ +//;
		$l_server_name =~ s/ +$//;
		$rsh_cmd =~ s/^ +//;
		$rsh_cmd =~ s/ +$//;
		$max_threads =~ s/^ +//;
		$max_threads =~ s/ +$//;

		if (! (length($l_server_name) > 0)) {
			&print_mesg("ERROR: Server name missing in server info file $SERVER_INFO_FILE\n");
			my_exit(1);
		}

		if (exists($SERVER_GROUPS{$l_server_name})) {	# this is a group, not a server
			foreach $server_name_temp (keys %server_info) {	# adjust request for each server in group
				if ($server_info{$server_name_temp}{'server_group'} eq $l_server_name) {
					$MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$server_name_temp}{'rsh_cmd'} = $rsh_cmd;

					if (! exists($MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$server_name_temp}{'max_threads'})) {	# don't overwrite server-specific request w/group request
						$MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$server_name_temp}{'max_threads'} = server_max_threads($server_name_temp, $max_threads);
						$MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$server_name_temp}{'info_source'} = 'command line';
					}
				}
			}
		} else {	# adjust request for the server

      $l_server_name = server_name($l_server_name);

			$MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$l_server_name}{'rsh_cmd'} = $rsh_cmd;
			$MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$l_server_name}{'max_threads'} = server_max_threads($l_server_name, $max_threads);
			$MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$l_server_name}{'info_source'} = 'command line';
		}
	}

	# override the command line parameter server request info with the control file request info where appropriate

	&read_control_info();

	foreach $server_name (keys %CONTROL_INFO) {
		if (exists($SERVER_GROUPS{$server_name})) {	# this is a group, not a server
			foreach $server_name_temp (keys %server_info) {	# adjust request for each server in group
				if ($server_info{$server_name_temp}{'server_group'} eq $server_name) {
					$MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$server_name_temp}{'rsh_cmd'} = $server_info{$server_name_temp}{'rsh_cmd'};

					if ($MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$server_name_temp}{'info_source'} ne 'control file') {	# don't overwrite server-specific request w/group request
						$MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$server_name_temp}{'max_threads'} = $CONTROL_INFO{$server_name};
						$MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$server_name_temp}{'info_source'} = 'control file';
					}
				}
			}
		} else {	# adjust request for the server
			my $l_server_name = server_name($server_name);
			$MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$server_name}{'max_threads'} = $CONTROL_INFO{$server_name};
			$MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$server_name}{'info_source'} = 'control file';
		}
	}

	foreach $l_server_name (keys %MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO) {

		if (defined($MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$l_server_name}{'rsh_cmd'})) {
			$rsh_cmd = $MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$l_server_name}{'rsh_cmd'};
		} else {
			$rsh_cmd = '';
		}

		if (defined($MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$l_server_name}{'max_threads'})) {
			$max_threads = $MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$l_server_name}{'max_threads'};
		} else {
			$max_threads = '';
		}

		if (defined($MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$l_server_name}{'info_source'})) {
			$info_source = $MERGED_RUN_REQUEST_INFO{$l_server_name}{'info_source'};
		} else {
			$info_source= 'unknown source';	# should not happen
		}

		if (! (length($l_server_name) > 0)) {
			&print_mesg("ERROR: Server name missing in $SERVER_INFO_FILE. Syntax is server[:threads][:rsh_cmd][,...]\n");
			my_exit(1);
		}


	  foreach $server_name (keys %server_info) {

	    if (($l_server_name eq $server_name) or ($l_server_name eq $server_info{$server_name}{'server_group'})) {
				if ($max_threads eq '') {

					if (defined($server_info{$server_name}{'processors'})) { # get threads_max from server info file
						if ($server_info{$server_name}{'processors'} != $server_info{$server_name}{'threads_max'}) {
							if ($server_info{$server_name}{'threads_max'} == 0) {
								&print_mesg("Note: Adding server " . hostname_display($server_name) . " to current server list, utilizing " . $server_info{$server_name}{'processors'} . " processors, based on server info file.\n");
							} elsif ($server_info{$server_name}{'processors'} == 0) {
								&print_mesg("Note: " . hostname_display($server_name) . " has been removed from the server pool, based on server info file.\n");
							} else {
								&print_mesg("Note: Max threads for " . hostname_display($server_name) . " changed from " . $server_info{$server_name}{'threads_max'} . " to " . $server_info{$server_name}{'processors'} . " , based on server info file.\n");
							}

							$server_info{$server_name}{'threads_max'} = $server_info{$server_name}{'processors'};
						}
					} else {
						&print_mesg("WARNING: Unable to determine number of threads to run for server " . hostname_display($server_name) . " . Prematurely abandoning set_run_server_info() fuction. Server Info file may be corrupt or invalid\n");
						return 0;
					}
				} else {
					if ($max_threads =~ /^[0-9]+$/) {
						if ($max_threads != $server_info{$server_name}{'threads_max'}) {
							if ($server_info{$server_name}{'threads_max'} == 0) {
								&print_mesg("Note: Adding server " . hostname_display($server_name) . " to the current server list, utilizing $max_threads processors, based on ${info_source}.\n");
							} elsif ($max_threads == 0) {
								&print_mesg("Note: " . hostname_display($server_name) . " has been removed from the server pool, based on ${info_source}.\n");
							} else {
								&print_mesg("Note: Max threads for " . hostname_display($server_name) . " changed from $server_info{$server_name}{'threads_max'} to $max_threads , based on ${info_source}.\n");
							}

							if ($max_threads > $server_info{$server_name}{'processors'}) {
								&print_mesg("Warning: Max threads of $max_threads for server " . hostname_display($server_name) . " exceeds pre-defined number of processors of $server_info{$server_name}{'processors'}\n");
							}

							$server_info{$server_name}{'threads_max'} = $max_threads;
						}
					} else {
						&print_mesg("ERROR: Max threads specified for server " . hostname_display($server_name) . " ($max_threads) is invalid, ignoring.\n");
					}
				}

			$servers_requested{$server_name} = 1;
 	   }

#	if ($initial_state eq 'Y') {
		# Hess changed 5/18/2007

		$server_info{$server_name}{'threads_running'} = 0 if ((! exists($server_info{$server_name}{'threads_running'})) || (! defined($server_info{$server_name}{'threads_running'})));
		$server_info{$server_name}{'threads_completed'} = 0 if ((! exists($server_info{$server_name}{'threads_completed'})) || (! defined($server_info{$server_name}{'threads_completed'})));
		$server_info{$server_name}{'threads_failed'} = 0 if ((! exists($server_info{$server_name}{'threads_failed'})) || (! defined($server_info{$server_name}{'threads_failed'})));
#	}

	if (! (length($rsh_cmd) > 0)) {
  		if (! defined($server_info{$server_name}{'rsh_method'})) {
  			&print_mesg("Warning: Unable to determine rsh method for server $server_name. Assuming rsh\n");
  			$server_info{$server_name}{'rsh_method'} = 'rsh';
  		}
	} else {
	  	if (($rsh_cmd ne 'rsh') and ($rsh_cmd ne 'ssh')) {
  			&print_mesg("ERROR: rsh method for server $server_name is not rsh or ssh ($rsh_cmd)\n");
  			my_exit(1);
	  	}
	}

	  }
	}

	my $old_max_threads = get_max_threads;;

	my $max_threads = 0;

	foreach $server_name (keys %server_info) {
		if (! defined($servers_requested{$server_name})) {
			if (defined($server_info{$server_name}{'threads_max'})) {
				if ($server_info{$server_name}{'threads_max'} > 0) {
					&print_mesg("Note: $server_name has been removed from the server pool, based on group membership in server info file.\n");
					$server_info{$server_name}{'threads_max'} = 0;
				}
			}
		}

		$max_threads += $server_info{$server_name}{'threads_max'};
	}

	set_max_threads($max_threads);

	if (defined($old_max_threads) && (get_max_threads != $old_max_threads)) {
		&print_mesg("Note: Max threads changed from $old_max_threads to " . get_max_threads . ".\n");
	}

}


if (defined($opt_i)) {
	$SERVER_INFO_FILE = $opt_i;
}

&print_mesg("=== initialize prun setup info ===\n");

# initialize generic server info

&init_server_info($SERVER_INFO_FILE);

# initialize run-specific server info

if (! defined($opt_r)) {
	if (exists($ENV{PRUN_PARALLEL_HOST_SPEC}) && defined($ENV{PRUN_PARALLEL_HOST_SPEC}) && ($ENV{PRUN_PARALLEL_HOST_SPEC} !~ /^\s*$/)) {
		$server_parm_list = $ENV{PRUN_PARALLEL_HOST_SPEC};
	} else {
		$server_parm_list = `hostname`;
		chomp($server_parm_list);
	}

	if (length($server_parm_list) == 0) {
		&print_mesg("ERROR: Unable to determine hostname\n");
		my_exit(1);
	}
} else {
	$server_parm_list = $opt_r;
}

# Hess changed 5/18/2007
#&set_run_server_info($server_parm_list, 'Y');

&set_run_server_info($server_parm_list);

if (defined($opt_h)) {
	&usage;
	my_exit(0);
}

if (defined($opt_a)) {
	if ($opt_a ne 'unlimited') {
		$max_child_failures = $opt_a;
	}
}

if (! defined($max_child_failures)) {
	$max_child_failures = 999999999999;
}

if (defined($opt_e)) {
	$normal_child_exit = $opt_e;
} else {
	$normal_child_exit = 0;
}


if (($ARGV[0] =~ /^-/) or ($ARGV[0] =~ /^%p/) or (length($ARGV[0]) == 0)) {
	&print_mesg("Error: specified command of " . $ARGV[0] . " is not valid.\n");
	my_exit(1);
}

if ($ARGV[0] eq 'nice') {
	&print_mesg("ERROR: To launch work units at reduced CPU scheduling priority, you must use the '-l' or '-p priority' command line options INSTEAD OF prefixing your command with 'nice'\n");
	my_exit(1);
}

# @argv = @PRUN_ARGV;

$found_parm = 0;
for($i = $#PRUN_ARGV; $i >= 1; $i--) {
	if ($PRUN_ARGV[$i] =~ /%p/) {
# print "found %p in arg $i : $PRUN_ARGV[$i]\n";
		$found_parm = 1;
		last;
	}
}

sub get_wu_from_file() {
	my($wu_file) = shift;
	my($wu_index, $line, $original_max_wu_index, @M, $num_new_wu);

	if (! $MASTER_LIST_RESORTED) {
		if (-r $wu_file) {
			open(WU, "< $wu_file") || &print_mesg("Warning: Unable to look for work units in file $wu_file : $!\n");

			$wu_index = -1;
			$line_num = 0;
			$original_max_wu_index = $#master_list;

			while (<WU>) {

				$line_num++;

				chomp;
				next if (/^[    ]*[#]/);
				next if (/^[    ]*$/);

				@M = split(',', $_);

				$wu_index++;

				if ($wu_index <= $original_max_wu_index) {
					if ($master_list[$wu_index] ne $M[0]) {
						&print_mesg("Warning: Mismatch between previous work units and current work units in $wu_file file on line $line_num . Work unit file may only be appended to. First mismatched line is: $_\n");
						last;
					}
				} else {
					$master_list[$wu_index] = $M[0];
				}
			}

			close (MASTER);
			$TOTAL_MASTER_ITEMS = scalar(@master_list);

			if ($#master_list > $original_max_wu_index) {
				$num_new_wu = $#master_list - $original_max_wu_index;
				$NUM_ITEMS_REMAINING += $num_new_wu;
				&print_mesg("Note: $num_new_wu work units were appended to the $wu_file file\n");
			}
		}

		&sort_master_list();
	}
}


sub hostname_display($) {
  my $hname = shift;
	my $hostname_display;

		if (hostname_suffix($hname) eq $LOCAL_SUFFIX) {
			$hostname_display = hostname_prefix($hname);
		} else {
			$hostname_display = $hname;
		}

	return $hostname_display;
}


sub get_work_unit_cmd_line($@) {
  my $work_unit = shift;
	my @input_command_line_args = @_;

	return map { $_ =~ s/\%p/${work_unit}/g; $_ } @input_command_line_args;
}


sub get_remote_work_unit_cmd_line($@) {
  my $server = shift;
	my @cmd_line_args = @_;
	my $quiet = '';

	$quiet = '-q -o BatchMode=yes' if ($server_info{$server}{'rsh_method'} eq 'ssh');

	return "$server_info{$avail_server}{'rsh_method'} $quiet -n " . hostname_display($server) . " '[ -f /etc/profile ] && . /etc/profile > /dev/null ; [ -f $USER_PROFILE ] && . $USER_PROFILE > /dev/null; cd $CURR_DIR 2> /dev/null; " . join(' ', @cmd_line_args) . " &\n echo PRUN2_CHILD_PID=\$!; wait \$!; echo PRUN2_RSH_RETURN_STATUS=\$?' |";
}


sub setup_termination_sig_handler($) {
  my $code_ref = shift;

	foreach $sig (@TERMINATION_SIGNALS) {
		if ($SIG{$sig} ne 'IGNORE') {
			$SIG{$sig} = $code_ref;
			print "setup signal $sig for pid $$\n";
		}
	}
}


sub run_child_work_unit($$@) {
  my ($server, $work_unit) = (shift, shift);
	my @command_line_args = @_;

	$CURRENT_WORKUNIT = $work_unit;

	if ($server ne $LOCAL_HOSTNAME) {
		close(STDIN);

		# assign signal handler for killing child process
		setup_termination_sig_handler(\&remote_kill);

		$cmd = get_remote_work_unit_cmd_line($server, @command_line_args);

		if (! open(RSH, $cmd)) {
			&print_mesg("Error: Unable to start 'ssh' for $work_unit : $!\n");
			my_exit(1);
		}

		$CURRENT_REMOTE_SERVER = $server;
		$wu_return_status = 1;

		while (<RSH>) {
			chomp;

			# look for return status or child pid tags *anywhere* in a line, since the child process might
			# be careless and output incomplete STDOUT lines, which can cause them to randomly become
			# mixed in on the same line as our prun2 tags.

			if (/PRUN2_RSH_RETURN_STATUS=([0-9]+)/) {
				$wu_return_status = $1;

				# stop reading input *now* instead of waiting for RSH handle to close, because *sometimes* sshd on the remote host
				# will keep waiting (and therefore leave the handle open) indefinitely, even though the child command  has completed.
				# When that happens, the result may be an orphaned sshd process hanging around indefinitely, but that's better than
				# also having a prun2 process that hangs around indefinitely despite child work units that actually did exit.

				last;
			} elsif (/PRUN2_CHILD_PID=([0-9]+)/) {
				$REMOTE_CHILD_PID = $1;
			} else {
				print $_ . "\n";
			}
		}

		close(RSH);

		$CURRENT_REMOTE_SERVER = '';

	} else {
		# run command via exec() instead of rsh/ssh since we are on local host
		exec(@command_line_args);
		$wu_return_status = 1;  # just in case
	}

	return $wu_return_status; 
}


sub get_remaining_time($$) {
  my $wu_start_times = shift;
	my $running_wu = shift;

	my $num_completion_times = scalar(@{$wu_start_times});
	my $num_to_analyze = max(3 * get_max_threads, $NUM_ITEMS_REMAINING / 10);

	$num_to_analyze = 4 if ($num_to_analyze < 4);
	$num_to_analyze = 200 if ($num_to_analyze > 200);
	$num_to_analyze = $num_completion_times if ($num_completion_times < $num_to_analyze);

#print Dumper $wu_start_times;

	my $num_seconds = time() - $wu_start_times->[$num_completion_times - $num_to_analyze];
	my $avg_secs_per_wu = $num_seconds / $num_to_analyze;

	my $secs_for_newest_wu;
	my $threads_running = 0;

#print Dumper $running_wu;

	my $curr_time = time();

	foreach my $child_pid_running (keys %{$running_wu}) {
		$threads_running++;
		$secs_for_newest_wu = $curr_time - $running_wu->{$child_pid_running} if ((! defined($secs_for_newest_wu)) || ($secs_for_newest_wu > ($curr_time - $running_wu->{$child_pid_running})));
	}

print "remaining = $NUM_ITEMS_REMAINING, num_to_analyze = $num_to_analyze, num completion times = $num_completion_times, num secs = $num_seconds, avg = $avg_secs_per_wu, running = $threads_running, newest secs = $secs_for_newest_wu, time = $curr_time\n";

	my $remaining_secs;

	$remaining_secs = $avg_secs_per_wu * ($NUM_ITEMS_REMAINING - $threads_running);
	$remaining_secs += max(0, $avg_secs_per_wu * get_max_threads - $secs_for_newest_wu) if ($threads_running);
# foo
	$remaining_secs = 0 if ($remaining_secs < 0);

	my $remaining_days = int($remaining_secs / 86400);
	my $remaining_hours = int(($remaining_secs - ($remaining_days * 86400)) / 3600);
	my $remaining_minutes = int(($remaining_secs - ($remaining_days * 86400 + $remaining_hours * 3600)) / 60);
	my $remaining_seconds = $remaining_secs - ($remaining_days * 86400 + $remaining_hours * 3600 + $remaining_minutes * 60);

	return sprintf("%02u:%02u:%02u:%02u", $remaining_days, $remaining_hours, $remaining_minutes, $remaining_seconds);
}


if (! $found_parm) {
	push(@argv, '%p');
}

&print_mesg("Command line: " . join(' ', @argv) . "\n");

if (! ($#master_list >= 0)) {
	die "Error: Nothing to do!\n";
}

$WU_RANGE = $master_list[0];

if ($#master_list > 0) {
	$WU_RANGE = "${WU_RANGE}.." . $master_list[$#master_list] . "\n";
}

&sort_master_list();	# sorts master work unit list by file size (descending) if work units are files
&check_master_list_sanity();

$TOTAL_MASTER_ITEMS = scalar(@master_list);
&print_mesg("Total items in master list = $TOTAL_MASTER_ITEMS\n");

$items_previously_completed = 0;

if (($TODO_FILE_INDICATOR) and (-f $master_done_file)) {
	if (-r $master_done_file) {
		open(DONE, "< $master_done_file") || die "can't open $master_done_file";

		while (<DONE>) {
			chomp;
			@data = split(',', $_);
			$done{$data[0]} = 0;
			$items_previously_completed++;
		}

		close (DONE);
	} else {
		die "unable to access $master_done_file";
	}
}

for($i = 0; $i <= $#master_list; $i++) {
	if (! defined($done{$master_list[$i]})) {
		$NUM_ITEMS_REMAINING++;
	}
}

if ($TODO_FILE_INDICATOR) {
	&print_mesg("Work units previously completed = $items_previously_completed\n");
	&print_mesg("Work units remaining = $NUM_ITEMS_REMAINING\n");
}

open(DONE, ">>$master_done_file") || die "can't create $master_done_file";

select(DONE);
$|++;	# turns on autoflush for DONE
select(STDOUT); # change default filehandle back to stdout

$item_index = 0;


&print_mesg("Local host = $LOCAL_HOSTNAME\n");
&print_mesg("Main (parent) prun process ID = $$\n");

&print_mesg("Job owner: $USERNAME\n");

&print_mesg("Max threads possible = " . get_max_threads . "\n");
&print_mesg("Max attempts per work unit = $MAX_ATTEMPTS\n");
&print_mesg("Work unit CPU scheduling priority (nice value) = $workunit_priority\n") if (defined($workunit_priority));
&print_mesg("=== begin prun execution of work units ===\n\n");

$Last_Time = time();
$START_TIME = $Last_Time;

$num_attempts = 1;
$success_retry_exec = 0;
$failed_retry_exec = 0;
my $shutdown = 0;
our $FAILED_DONE_WORK_UNITS = 0;

if (exists($ENV{PWD})) {
	$CURR_DIR = $ENV{PWD};
} else {
	$CURR_DIR = cwd();
}

my ($quiet, $done_record);

$last_log_status_time = time;

my $sleep_seconds = 1;
my $last_threads_running = 0;


until (	(
	($threads == 0)
	 and (
		   ( ($item_index == $TOTAL_MASTER_ITEMS) and ($num_attempts == $MAX_ATTEMPTS) )
		or ( $num_fail > $max_child_failures )
		or (get_max_threads == 0)
		or $shutdown
	     )
	 )
	)
	{

	if ($threads != $last_threads_running) {
		$Debug && &print_mesg("threads running = $threads\n");
		$last_threads_running = $threads;
	}

	# if end of work unit list has been reached, the restart from beginning of work unit list and
	# increment attempts counter

	if (($item_index == $TOTAL_MASTER_ITEMS) and ($threads == 0) and ($num_attempts < $MAX_ATTEMPTS)) {
		$item_index = 0;
		$num_attempts++;
	}

	$avail_server = undef;

	if ($threads < get_max_threads) {

		# run next job if there are any left to run and # of threads running is less than max # threads allowed
		if (($item_index < $TOTAL_MASTER_ITEMS) && ($num_fail <= $max_child_failures)) {

			# skip if it already completed
			if (defined($done{$master_list[$item_index]})) {
				$item_index++;
				next;
			}

			# attempt to find best available server to run work unit on
			$avail_server = get_available_server($threads);

			if (defined($avail_server)) {
				@curr_args = get_work_unit_cmd_line($master_list[$item_index], @argv);

				&print_mesg(&get_time() . ", Running on " . hostname_display($avail_server) . " : " . join(' ', @curr_args) . "\n", 'WU');

				# split me into seperate parent/child process pair

				$PID = fork;

				if (! defined($PID)) {
					&print_mesg("Error: Unable to fork process for $master_list[$item_index]\n");
					$item_index++;
					next;
				}

				if ($PID == 0) {
					# child work unit process executes in here

					close(DONE);  # no need for child to hold open since it doesn't write to DONE file

					my_exit(run_child_work_unit($avail_server, $master_list[$item_index], @curr_args));

				} else {
					# parent process code

					my $curr_time = time();

					$child_server{$PID} = $avail_server;
					$child{$PID} = $master_list[$item_index];
					$child_start{$PID} = $curr_time;
					$item_index++;
					$threads++;
					$server_info{$avail_server}{'threads_running'}++;
					$server_info{$avail_server}{'last_launch_time'} = $curr_time;
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# this is also parent process code
  # wait for any child process to complete

	do {
	# Do a non-blocking wait, to see if any child process has
	# completed.

	$waited_pid = waitpid(-1, WNOHANG);

	if ($waited_pid > 0) {

			$threads--;
			$waited_server = $child_server{$waited_pid};
			$server_info{$waited_server}{'threads_running'}--;

			$child_returncode = ($? >> 8); # return code must be decoded from $?
			$child_start_time = $child_start{$waited_pid};
			$child_elapsed = time() - $child_start_time;
			delete $child_start{$waited_pid};
			delete $child_server{$waited_pid};

			if ($child_returncode != $normal_child_exit) {
				&print_mesg("\n" . &get_time() . ", Work unit $child{$waited_pid} returned error status $child_returncode on $waited_server in $child_elapsed seconds.\n", 'WU');

				$num_fail++;

				if ($num_attempts > 1) {
					$failed_retry_exec++;
				}

				$server_info{$waited_server}{failures}++;

				if (defined($MAX_SERVER_FAILURES) && ($server_info{$waited_server}{failures} >= $MAX_SERVER_FAILURES) && ($server_info{$waited_server}{'threads_max'} >= 1)) {
					&print_mesg("Note: Max threads for $waited_server changed from " . $server_info{$waited_server}{'threads_max'} . " to 0, due to $server_info{$waited_server}{failures} successive failed work units. Max threads changed from " . get_max_threads . " to " . (get_max_threads - $server_info{$waited_server}{'threads_max'}) . ".\n");
					set_max_threads(get_max_threads - $server_info{$waited_server}{'threads_max'});
					$server_info{$waited_server}{'threads_max'} = 0;
					delete $server_info{$waited_server}{failures};	# reset in case user adds server back while still running
				}

			} else {
				$NUM_ITEMS_REMAINING--;

				if ($num_attempts > 1) {
					$success_retry_exec++;
				}

				$done{$child{$waited_pid}} = 0;

				push(@wu_start_times, $child_start_time);

				$remaining_time = get_remaining_time(\@wu_start_times, \%child_start);

				$done_record = join(",", $child{$waited_pid}, $child_elapsed, $threads + 1, $NUM_ITEMS_REMAINING) . "\n";

				if (! print DONE $done_record) {
					&print_mesg("prun2 ERROR: Unable to record completed work unit in done file '$master_done_file' due to '$!' . No new work units will be launched. The following record could not be appended to the done file: $done_record\n");
					$shutdown = 1;
					$FAILED_DONE_WORK_UNITS++;
				}

				&print_mesg("\n" . &get_time() . ", Work unit $child{$waited_pid} completed on " . hostname_display($waited_server) . " in $child_elapsed seconds. Remaining time = $remaining_time . Remaining work units = $NUM_ITEMS_REMAINING .\n", 'WU');

				delete $server_info{$waited_server}->{last_launch_time};

				if (($COMMON_LOGGING) && ((time - $last_log_status_time) >= 1800)) {
					&print_mesg("Remaining time = $remaining_time . Remaining work units = $NUM_ITEMS_REMAINING\n");
					$last_log_status_time = time;
				}

				$num_success++;
				delete $server_info{$waited_server}{failures};	# reset failure count, since we are only tracking *successive* failures
			}

			delete $child{$waited_pid};

		}

	} until (! ($waited_pid > 0));

	if (! defined($avail_server)) {
		# Most of the time there will be no children that have completed so briefly go to sleep to prevent prun3 from spinning it's
		# wheels on waitpid() calls, eating up precious CPU time.

		if (get_max_threads > 0) {
			# this reduces starvation by waiting less time if we are running less than max_threads.
			# the fewer we are running, the less time we wait before checking again for an available server.

			$sleep_seconds = $MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS + rand() * ($MAX_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS - $MIN_SERVER_LAUNCH_DELAY_SECS) * $threads / get_max_threads;
		} else {
			$sleep_seconds = 1;
		}

		$Debug && &print_mesg("debug: sleeping for $sleep_seconds seconds. threads = $threads\n");
		usleep($sleep_seconds * 1000000);
	}

	$curr_time = time();
	$Elapsed = $curr_time - $Last_Time;

	if ($TODO_FILE_INDICATOR) {
		if (&file_updated($MASTER_TODO_FILE)) {
			&get_wu_from_file($MASTER_TODO_FILE);
		}
	}

	if ( (&file_updated($SERVER_INFO_FILE)) or (&file_updated($CONTROL_FILE)) ) {
		&init_server_info($SERVER_INFO_FILE);
		&set_run_server_info($server_parm_list);
	}

}

close(DONE);

if ( ($return_code == 0) && ($NUM_ITEMS_REMAINING >= 1) ) {
		$return_code = 1;
}

&execution_report;
&remove_temp_files();

my_exit($return_code);


#prun_done

if [ "$*" = "" ]
  then
	echo "Usage:
prun_done <done_file1> [done_file2] ...

{usually just run 'prun_done *.done'}"
	exit
fi

for f in $* ALL
  do
	if [ $f = ALL ]
	  then
		echo
		echo "$lines" | sort -nr -k 2

		all_pct_done=`echo "scale=1
		$total_done_count * 100 / $total_master_count" | bc`

		echo "ALL	$all_pct_done"
	else
		bdir=`dirname $f`
		bfname=`basename $f`
		master_fname=`echo $bfname | sed 's/^\(.*\).done$/\1/'`

		if [ "$bdir" = '.' ]
		  then
			bname=$master_fname
		  else
			bname="$bdir/$master_fname"
		fi

		if [ ! -f "$bname" ]
		  then
			echo Cannot find master file $bname for $f
			exit 1
		fi

		master_count=`cat $bname | wc -l`
		done_count=`cat $f | wc -l`

		pct_done=`echo "scale=1
$done_count * 100 / $master_count" | bc`

		total_master_count=`expr ${total_master_count:-0} + $master_count`
		total_done_count=`expr ${total_done_count:-0} + $done_count`

		logfile="${bname}.log"
		if [ -r "${logfile}" ]
		  then
			grep -i 'remaining time' ${logfile} /dev/null | tail -1

			if tail -1 ${logfile} | grep 'Number of failed executions' > /dev/null
				then
					if [ "$pct_done" != 100.0 ]
						then
							run_stat='NOT running'
						else
							run_stat='Completed'
					fi
				else
					run_stat=''
			fi

			num_errors=`grep -i ' returned error status ' ${logfile} | wc -l`
			error_stat=`echo errors=$num_errors`

		fi

		if [ "$lines" = "" ]
		  then
				lines="$f	${pct_done} %	$run_stat	$error_stat"
		  else
				lines="${lines}
$f	$pct_done %	$run_stat	$error_stat"
		fi

	fi
  done

#qa_store_query
#!/usr/bin/perl

use strict;
use warnings;

my $pgm = $0;
$pgm =~ s|.*/||g;

if ((scalar(@ARGV) == 0) && (-t 0)) {
	print "Usage:\n$pgm store_id_file1 store_id_file2 ...\n";
	exit(1);
}


print "SELECT group_id, count(*)
FROM dim_pharmacy_group
where post_date = (SELECT max(post_date) FROM dim_pharmacy_group)
and (\n";

my $total = 0;

while (<>) {
	chomp;

	my $id = $_;

	next if ($id =~ /^\s*$/);

	$id =~ s/^\s+//;
	$id =~ s/\s+$//;

	my $output;

	if ($id =~ /^\d{7}$/) {
		$output = "nabp = '$id'\n";
	} elsif ($id =~ /^\d{10}$/) {
		$output = "npi = '$id'\n";
	} else {
		print STDERR "Warning: value '$id' is not a NPI or NABP! Ignoring...\n";
		next;
	}

	$total++;

	if ($total > 1) {
		$output = "or $output";
	}

	print $output || die "Could not write to output file : $!\n";
}

print ")
group by group_id
order by 1\n";


#qrun
#!/usr/bin/perl

# qrun: Run a sequence of commands until all succeed or one fails. Resume with last failed command from prior run.
# Author: J Hess, RelayHealth
#
# Version 1.0: 2/19/2015
#

use strict;
use warnings;

use Getopt::Long;
use IO::Handle;
use BLUELITE::Common qw(email);

autoflush STDOUT 1;
autoflush STDERR 1;

our $PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s/^.*\///;

our ($FAILURE_EMAIL, $CURRENT_CMD, $COMMAND_FILE);
our $STEP_HISTORY = '';
our $QUIET = 0;
our $SILENT = 0;

sub Usage() {
	print "\n$PGM: Run a sequence of commands until all succeed or one fails. Resume with last failed command from prior run.\n";
	print "\nUsage: $PGM [-options] command_file\n";
	print "Options:\n";
	print "   -reset                Start w/1st command. Do NOT resume from prior run.\n";
	print "   -success-email list   Send email to list when last command succeeds.\n";
	print "   -failure-email list   Send email to list when command fails.\n";
	print "   -step-email    list   Send email to list between each command.\n";
	print "   -cd dir               cd to dir prior to running commands.\n";
	print "   -set var=value        Variable substitutions (use %varname% in command_file). May repeat.\n";
	print "   -novar                Don't check command_file for unused -set variables\n";
	print "   -quiet                Only write error messages to STDERR\n";
	print "   -silent               Never write anything to STDERR\n";
}

sub mylog($) {
  my $msg = shift;

	if ($SILENT || $QUIET) {
		return;
	}

	print STDERR $msg;
}


sub mydie(;$) {
	my $msg = shift;
	no warnings 'uninitialized';
	chomp($msg);

	if (defined($FAILURE_EMAIL)) {
		my $subject = "$PGM error";

		if (defined($CURRENT_CMD)) {
			$subject .= " running $CURRENT_CMD";
		}

		email(to => $FAILURE_EMAIL, subject => $subject, msg => "Command file: $COMMAND_FILE\n\n${STEP_HISTORY}\n\n${msg}");
	}

	print STDERR "$PGM ERROR: $msg\n" if (! $SILENT);
	exit(1);
}

sub trim_line($) {
	no warnings 'uninitialized';
  my $line = shift;

	chomp($line);

	# remove leading/trailing whitespace
	$line =~ s/^\s+//;
	$line =~ s/\s+$//;

	if (($line =~ /^#/) || ($line eq '')) {
		return undef;
	}

	return $line;
}


####### MAIN ######

if (! @ARGV) {
	Usage();
	exit(1);
}

my $reset = 0;
my ($success_email, $step_email, $cd);
my @set = ();
my $novars = 0;

my $ret = GetOptions(
	'reset' => \$reset,
	'success-email=s' => \$success_email,
	'failure-email=s' => \$FAILURE_EMAIL,
	'step-email=s' => \$step_email,
	'cd=s' => \$cd,
	'set=s@' => \@set,
	'novars' => \$novars,
	'QUIET' => \$QUIET,
	'SILENT' => \$SILENT,
);

if (! $ret) {
	Usage();
	exit(1);
}

# default $FAILURE_EMAIL to $success_email or $step_email

if (! defined($FAILURE_EMAIL)) {
	if (defined($success_email)) {
		$FAILURE_EMAIL = $success_email;
	} elsif (defined($step_email)) {
		$FAILURE_EMAIL = $step_email;
	}
}

if (@ARGV == 0) {
	mydie("ERROR: Must specify command_file");
}

if (@ARGV != 1) {
	mydie("ERROR: Only one command_file allowed");
}

if ($QUIET && $SILENT) {
	mydie("-quiet and -silent cannot be used together");
}

my %vars = ();

# organize and sanity-check -set variables

foreach my $assignment (@set) {
	if ($assignment =~ /^([A-Z][A-Z0-9_]*)=(.*)$/i) {
		$vars{$1} = "$2";
	} else {
		mydie("invalid -set option of '$assignment' . Correct syntax is 'varname=value'");
	}
}

# open command file for reading
$COMMAND_FILE = shift(@ARGV);
open(CF, $COMMAND_FILE) || mydie("Could not open $COMMAND_FILE for reading: $!");

# remove ".done" file if -reset requested
my @done = ();
my $done_file = "${COMMAND_FILE}.done";

if ($reset && (-e $done_file) && ! unlink($done_file)) {
	mydie("Reset requested, but cannot remove file $done_file : $!");
}

# read previously completed commands from ".done" file
if (-e $done_file) {
	open(DF, $done_file) || mydie("Could not open $done_file for reading: $!");

	while (<DF>) {
		chomp;
		push(@done, $_);
	}

	close(DF) || mydie("Could not close $done_file: $!");
}


my $command_num = 0;
my $line_num = 0;
my @commands = ();
my $last_successful_cmd;
my %found_vars = ();

# Load and sanity-check the command-file to @commands array

while (<CF>) {
	$line_num++;
	my $cmd = trim_line($_);

	# ignore blank/comment lines
	next if (! defined($cmd));

	# do variable substitution, if -set used on command-line
	foreach my $var_key (keys %vars) {
		if ($cmd =~ s/%$var_key%/$vars{$var_key}/g) {
			$found_vars{$var_key} = undef;
		}
	}

	# make sure all variables, if any, were substituted
	if ($cmd =~ /%([A-Z][A-Z0-9_]*)%/i) {
		mydie("Line $line_num in command file $COMMAND_FILE contains variable '$1' that was not specified via -set option");
	}

	$command_num++;

	# skip if this command was successful in prior run

	if (exists($done[$command_num - 1])) {
		my $done_cmd = $done[$command_num - 1];

		if ($done_cmd eq $cmd) {
			$last_successful_cmd = $cmd;
			next;
		} else {
			mydie("Resume command mismatch: Line $line_num in $COMMAND_FILE: [$cmd] Line $command_num in $done_file: [$done_cmd]");
		}
	}

	# add command to list to execute
	push(@commands, $cmd);
}

close(CF) || mydie("Could not close $COMMAND_FILE: $!");

if (! $novars) {
	# make sure all -set variables were found in command file

	foreach my $var (keys %vars) {
		if (! exists($found_vars{$var})) {
			mydie("No reference to variable %$var% found in command file $COMMAND_FILE . Specify -novar to ignore.");
		}
	}
}

# do nothing and exit successfully if no commands to run
my $num_commands_to_run = scalar(@commands);

if ($num_commands_to_run == 0) {
	exit(0);
}

# display init stats
my $num_previous_commands = scalar(@done);

if ($num_previous_commands >= 1) {
	my $total_commands = $num_previous_commands + $num_commands_to_run;
	mylog("$PGM: Total commands: $total_commands\n");
	mylog("$PGM: Previous commands completed: $num_previous_commands\n");
}

mylog("$PGM: Commands to run: $num_commands_to_run\n");

if ($num_previous_commands >= 1) {
	mylog("$PGM: Last successful command: [$last_successful_cmd]\n");
	mylog("$PGM: Resuming...\n");
}

# open ".done" file in append mode
open(DF, ">> $done_file") || mydie("Could not open $done_file for appending: $!");

select(DF);
$|++; # turns on autoflush for DF
select(STDOUT); # change default filehandle back to stdout

# cd to requested dir if -cd used
if ($cd && ! chdir($cd)) {
	mydie("Cannot cd to $cd : $!\n");
}

my $start_time = time;
my $email_step_txt = '';


# Main command execution loop

foreach my $cmd (@commands) {
	mylog("$PGM: Running: [$cmd]\n");

	$email_step_txt .= "\nRunning:\n$cmd";
	$CURRENT_CMD = $cmd;
	$CURRENT_CMD =~ s/\s.*$//;

	if (defined($step_email)) {
		email(to => $step_email, subject => "$PGM step: $CURRENT_CMD", msg => "Command file: ${COMMAND_FILE}\n\n${email_step_txt}");
	}

	my $time0 = time;
	my $ret = system($cmd);
	my $elapsed_seconds = time - $time0;

	if ($ret == 0) {
		mylog("$PGM: Completed in $elapsed_seconds seconds: [$cmd]\n");
		print DF "$cmd\n" || mydie("Could not append successful command to $done_file due to $! . Command: [$cmd]");

		$email_step_txt = "Completed in $elapsed_seconds seconds: [$cmd]\n";
		$STEP_HISTORY .= $email_step_txt;
	} else {
		my $eight_bit_status = $ret >> 8;
		mydie("Failed with exit status $eight_bit_status ($ret) in $elapsed_seconds seconds: [$cmd]");
	}

	$CURRENT_CMD = undef;
}

# get elapsed time, close ".done" file, and send email (if requested)

my $total_elapsed_seconds = time - $start_time;

close(DF) || mydie("Could not close $done_file");

mylog("$PGM: Time to successfully complete these commands: $total_elapsed_seconds seconds\n");

if (defined($success_email)) {
	email(to => $success_email, subject => "$PGM complete: $COMMAND_FILE", msg => "Command file: ${COMMAND_FILE}\n\n${STEP_HISTORY}\n\nTime to successfully complete all commands in this run: $total_elapsed_seconds seconds\n");
}


#quicksar
#!/bin/bash

sar | tail -n2 | head -n1 | cut -c58-61

#quick_medrecon
#!/bin/bash

/ds/common/bin/medrecon -v $1 20080801 20081231 OTC PRODUCTS 19010101 M 30519

#recdiff
#!/usr/bin/perl

# recdiff: analyze, summarize, and detail differences between two similarly-formatted delimited flat files
#
# Author: J. Hess, RelayHealth
# Initial release: 1/30/2009
#
# Version 1.0 - 1/30/2009
# - Initial release
#
# Version 1.1 - 5/22/2009
# - Fixed bug with recdif .... file1.dat file2.dat usage
# - Added single-quotes around delimiter character on sort command-line
# - Added check for sort failure on file handle close calls
#
# Version 1.2 - 1/26/2010
# - Fixed bug where "division by zero" would appear if no comparisons could be made
# - Fixed bug where pipe and other special characters could not be used as a delimiter
#
# Version 1.3 - 3/16/2010
# - Fixed bug where "sort command failed" would sometimes be encountered due to closing
# the sort pipe before all of it had been read.
#
# Version 1.4 - 3/25/2010
# - Added -show-exclusive-keys command line option
#
# Version 1.5 - 5/19/2010
# - Added -decrypt-field command line option (to avoid requirement to create config file for field decryption)
#
# Version 1.6 - 7/22/2010
# - Fixed bug that inflated key counts when dupes are encountered
# - Added -show-duplicate-keys command line option
# - Duplicate keys are no longer displayed by default
#
# Version 1.61 7/23/2010
# - Fixed bug that inflated some percentages in the report
#
# Version 1.62 8/16/2010
# - Fixed bug that sometimes inflated the percentages in the "Field-count stats" section.
# It was using the # of compared keys as the denominator instead of the number of compared records.
#
# Version 2.0 8/10/2012
# - Added xml-formatted config file option with layout and AutoQA sections.
# - Some command-line opts can now be specified in xml config (e.g. header/trailer regex, key fields, num-fields, ignore)
# - Field names can now be defined in xml config instead of previous non-xml config
# - AutoQA section in xml config can be used to specify difference constraints. Exceeding the constraints
#   will cause recdiff to exit with error status, for automated QA.
# - Added -input2-dir command-line option, which will find previous file so that -input2 option can be omitted
#
# Version 2.1 9/7/2012
# - Fixed dupe counting bug where key was not counted as dupe when it was dupe in one file but exists as non-dupe in other file
# - Added # of records compared to report
# - Renamed variable for # of records compared
#
# Version 2.2 10/2/2012
# - Tweaked various code/functions to improve overall performance
# - Prefixed sort command with LANG=POSIX to preserve collating sequence locale of traditional sort (i.e. uppercase comes before lowercase).
# Prior to this, incorrect key stats could be reported on a RHEL6 system.
#

use Getopt::Long;
eval "use BLUELITE::Deid::Std_Encryption";
use Data::Dumper;
use XML::Simple;
use XML::LibXML;
use List::Util qw(min max);
use Params::Validate qw(:all);
use File::Basename;
use File::stat;

no strict;
no warnings;

#use strict;
#use warnings;

my $TOP_DIFF_COMBINATIONS_TO_SHOW = 3;
our $MAX_ID_LENGTH = 30;
our $DISABLE_DECRYPTION = 0;
our $DEFAULT_XSD = 'recdiff.xsd';
our $REQUESTED_XSD;
our $PGM = $0;
$PGM =~ s/.*\///g;

our $VERSION = '2.2';
our $VERSION_DATE = '10/2/2012';
our $VERSION_COPYRIGHT = 'RelayHealth';

my $start_time = time;

sub Usage() {
	my $common_args = "-delimiter D -num-fields # -key # [-key # ..] [-options]";

	print "Usage 1: $PGM $common_args file1 file2\n";
	print "Usage 2: $PGM $common_args -input1 file [-input1 file ..] -input2 file [-input2 file ..]\n";
	print "\n";
	print "a) D may be any single character or a 2 character hex code (e.g. 'EC')\n";
	print "b) -key numbers must be positive integers. 1st key index is 1.\n";
	print "c) ONLY records with matching key fields are compared.\n";
	print "\nOptions:
	[-config fname.xml]      {If used, these are optional: -delimiter, -num-fields, -key}
	[-num-sample-records #]
	[-decrypt-type DT]       {DT supported: WK}
	[-min-num-fields n]
	[-header-regex RE]
	[-trailer-regex RE]
	[-ignore-regex RE]
	[-disable-decryption]
	[-top-diffs #]           {defaults to $TOP_DIFF_COMBINATIONS_TO_SHOW}
	[-ignore-field #]        [-ignore-field #] [...]
	[-decrypt-field #]       [-decrypt-field #] [...]
	[-show-exclusive-keys]   {Lists all keys exclusive to each file}
	[-show-duplicate-keys]   {Lists all duplicate keys in each file}
	[-xsd fname.xsd]         Verify fname.xml structure against fname.xsd {default \$RECDIFF_XSD}\n";

}

sub pct2dec($) {
  my $pct = shift;

	no warnings 'uninitialized';

	if (defined($pct) && ($pct =~ /^\s*(\d+)([.]\d+)?\s*%\s*$/)) {
		my $val = "${1}${2}";
		return $val / 100 if ($val >= 0 && $val <= 100);
	}

	return undef;
}

sub get_field_index($$) {
	my ($name, $fields) = @_;

	foreach my $index (keys %{$fields}) {
		return $index if ($fields->{$index}->{name} eq $name);
	}

	return undef;
}


sub get_xsd_filename() {

	no warnings 'uninitialized';

	if (defined($REQUESTED_XSD) && (! -r $REQUESTED_XSD)) {
		die "$PGM: ERROR: Requested XSD file $REQUESTED_XSD cannot be accessed!\n";
	}

	foreach my $xsd_file ($REQUESTED_XSD, $ENV{RECDIFF_XSD}, $DEFAULT_XSD, 'recdiff.xsd') {
		return $xsd_file if (defined($xsd_file) && (-f $xsd_file));
	}

	return undef;
}


sub get_config(%) {
  my %option = validate_with
    ( params  => \@_,
      spec    => {
									CONFIG_FILE => { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 },
									DELIMITER => { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 },
									NUM_FIELDS => { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 },
									MIN_NUM_FIELDS => { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 }, 
									HEADER_REGEX =>  { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 },
									TRAILER_REGEX =>  { type => SCALAR, optional => 1 },
									IGNORE_REGEX => { type => ARRAYREF, optional => 1 },
									IGNORE_FIELDS => { type => ARRAYREF, optional => 1},
									DECRYPT_FIELDS => { type => ARRAYREF, optional => 1},
									KEYS => { type => ARRAYREF, optional => 1}
                },
      called  => 'read_config',
      normalize_keys => sub { my $k = shift; $k =~ s/^-//; return uc $k }
  );

	my $config_info;

	if (exists($option{CONFIG_FILE})) {
		$config_info = read_config_file($option{CONFIG_FILE});
		die "ERROR: Could not parse config file " . $option{CONFIG_FILE} . "\n" if (! defined($config_info));
	} else {
		$config_info = { layout => {} };
	}

	my $layout = $config_info->{layout};
	foreach my $layout_parameter ('DELIMITER', 'NUM_FIELDS', 'MIN_NUM_FIELDS', 'HEADER_REGEX', 'TRAILER_REGEX') {
		if (exists($option{$layout_parameter})) {
#print "debug: $layout_parameter = $option{$layout_parameter}\n";
			$layout->{lc($layout_parameter)} = $option{$layout_parameter};
		}
	}

	if (exists($option{IGNORE_REGEX})) {
		for(my $i = 0; $i < @{$option{IGNORE_REGEX}}; $i++) {
			$layout->{ignore}->{cmdline_$i} = $option{IGNORE_REGEX}->[$i];
		}
	}

	my $fields = $layout->{fields};


	foreach my $field_num (@{$option{IGNORE_FIELDS}}) {
		$fields->{$field_num}->{ignore} = 1;
	}

	$layout->{IGNORE} = [grep { $fields->{$_}->{ignore} == 1 } (keys %{$fields})];

	print "ignored fields: " . join(', ', @{$layout->{IGNORE}}) . "\n" if (@{$layout->{IGNORE}});

	foreach my $field_num (@{$option{DECRYPT_FIELDS}}) {
		$fields->{$field_num - 1}->{encrypted} = 1;
	}

	$layout->{ENCRYPTED} = [grep { $fields->{$_}->{encrypted} == 1 } (keys %{$fields})];

	print "encrypted fields: " . join(', ', @{$layout->{ENCRYPTED}}) . "\n" if (@{$layout->{ENCRYPTED}});

	if (exists($option{KEYS})) {
		foreach my $field_index (keys %{$fields}) {
			$fields->{$field_index}->{key} = 0;
		}

		foreach my $field_index (@{$option{KEYS}}) {
			$fields->{$field_index - 1}->{key} = 1;
		}
	}

	# find fields that are keys and add one to each position (for sort command)
	foreach my $field_id (sort { $a <=> $b } keys %{$fields}) {
		push(@{$layout->{KEYS}}, $field_id + 1) if ($fields->{$field_id}->{key});
	}

	$layout->{min_num_fields} = $layout->{num_fields} if (! exists($layout->{min_num_fields}));

	foreach my $required_layout_parameter ('delimiter', 'num_fields', 'min_num_fields', 'KEYS') {
		if (! exists($layout->{$required_layout_parameter})) {
			die "$PGM: ERROR: '$required_layout_parameter' parameter was not provided!\n";
		}
	}

	print "key fields: " . join(', ', @{$layout->{KEYS}}) . "\n";

	if ($layout->{delimiter} =~ /^[0-9A-F][0-9A-F]$/i) {
		$layout->{delimiter} = chr(hex($layout->{delimiter}));
	}

	my $num_fields = $layout->{'num_fields'};

	if ($num_fields < 1) {
		die "$PGM: ERROR: num_fields is $num_fields, which is invalid. Must be at least 1\n";
	}

	my $min_num_fields = $layout->{'min_num_fields'};

	if (($min_num_fields < 1) || ($min_num_fields > $num_fields)) {
		die "$PGM: ERROR: min_num_fields is $min_num_fields, which is invalid. Must be between 1 and ${num_fields}.\n";
	}

#print Dumper $layout;

	#push(@{$layout->{IGNORE_REGEX}}, );

	my ($autoqa, $attributes, $qa_field);
	$autoqa = $config_info->{autoqa} if (exists($config_info->{autoqa}));

	if (defined($autoqa)) {
		$attributes = $autoqa->{attributes} if (exists($autoqa->{attributes}));

		if (defined($attributes)) {
			if (exists($attributes->{default_max_diff})) {
				foreach my $field_index (keys %{$fields}) {
					$fields->{$field_index}->{qa_max_diff_pct} = pct2dec($attributes->{default_max_diff});
				}
			}

			$qa_field = $attributes->{qa_field} if (exists($attributes->{qa_field}));

#print Dumper $qa_field;
#print Dumper $fields;

			if (defined($qa_field)) {
				foreach my $field_name (keys %{$qa_field}) {
					my $field_index = get_field_index($field_name, $fields);

					if (defined($field_index)) {
						$fields->{$field_index}->{qa_max_diff_pct} = pct2dec($qa_field->{$field_name}->{max_diff}) if (exists($qa_field->{$field_name}->{max_diff}));
					} else {
						die "ERROR: qa_field '$field_name' does not exist as a field in the layout section\n";
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	return $config_info;
}


sub read_config_file($) {
  my $fname = shift;

	die "Config file '$fname' does not exist!\n" if (! -f $fname);

	# see if this is a parseable xml file

	my $xml_doc;
	eval { $xml_doc = XML::LibXML->new->parse_file($fname) };

	if (! defined($xml_doc)) {
		print STDERR "ERROR: Could not parse xml config file $fname: $@\n";
		return undef;
	}

	print "Using xml config file $fname\n";

	my $xsd_file = get_xsd_filename();

	if (defined($xsd_file)) {

		print "Validating xml config file against XSD file $xsd_file\n";

		# guarantee that the xml config file adheres to the structure defined in xsd file
		my $xml_schema;
		eval { $xml_schema = XML::LibXML::Schema->new(location => $xsd_file) };

		if (! defined($xml_schema)) {
			print STDERR "ERROR: Could not interpret or open XSD file $xsd_file : $! $@\n";
			return undef;
		}

		my $validation_status = 1;

		eval { $validation_status = $xml_schema->validate($xml_doc); };

		if (($validation_status != 0) || ($@)) {
			print STDERR "ERROR: Validation of config file $fname failed schema defined in $xsd_file \n$@\n";
			return undef;
		}
	} else {
		print STDERR "WARNING: Unable to attempt validation of config file $fname because XSD file could not be located.\n";
	}

	# read validated xml file into $ref data structure
	my $ref;
	eval { $ref = XMLin($fname, KeyAttr => { field => 'id', ignore => 'id', 'qa_field' => 'id' }, ForceArray => ['field', 'qa_field', 'ignore']) };

	if (! defined($ref)) {
		print STDERR "Could not open config file '$fname' : $@\n";
		return undef;
	}

#	print Dumper $ref;

	my $field_config;
	my @keys = ();

	if (exists($ref->{layout})) {
		my $layout = $ref->{layout};

		my $num_expected_fields;
		$num_expected_fields = $layout->{num_fields} if (exists($layout->{num_fields}));

		if (exists($layout->{field})) {
			my $fields = $layout->{field};

			foreach my $field_id (keys %{$fields}) {
				my $field_info = $fields->{$field_id};
				my $index = $field_info->{num};

				if ($index < 1) {
					print STDERR "Field $field_id has position 'num' of $index, which is invalid. Lowest 'num' should be 1!\n";
					return undef;
				}

				$index--;

				if (exists($field_config->{$index})) {
					print STDERR "Fields '$field_id' and '" . $field_config->{$index}->{id} . "' both have field num of '$index'\n";
					return undef;
				}

				my $key = 0;

				if (exists($field_info->{key})) {
					my $key_val = $field_info->{key};

					if ($key_val =~ /^\s*(y|yes|true|1)\s*$/i) {
						$key = 1;
						push(@keys, $index);
					} elsif ($key_val =~ /^\s*(n|no|false|0)\s*$/i) {
						$key = 0;
					} else {
						print STDERR "Key attribute of layout field '$field_id' has invalid value of '$key_val'. Must be 1 or 0.\n";
						return undef;
					}
				}

				my $ignore = 0;

				if (exists($field_info->{ignore})) {
					my $ignore_val = $field_info->{ignore};

					if ($ignore_val =~ /^\s*(y|yes|true|1)\s*$/i) {
						$ignore = 1;
					} elsif ($ignore_val =~ /^\s*(n|no|false|0)\s*$/i) {
						$ignore = 0;
					} else {
						print STDERR "Ignore attribute of layout field '$field_id' has invalid value of '$ignore_val'. Must be 1 or 0.\n";
						return undef;
					}
				}

				$field_config->{$index} = {
					id => $field_id,
					ignore => $ignore,
					encrypted => 0,
					name => $field_id,
					key => $key
				};
			}

			my $min_field_num = min(keys %{$field_config});

			if ($min_field_num != 0) {
				print STDERR "Field num 1 is missing in layout!\n";
				return undef;
			}

			my $max_field_num = max(keys %{$field_config});

			if (defined($num_expected_fields) && $max_field_num > $num_expected_fields) {
				print STDERR "Max field # defined in layout is $max_field_num, but declared num_fields is $num_expected_fields !\n";
				return undef;
			}

			if (! defined($num_expected_fields)) {
				$num_expected_fields = $max_field_num;
				$layout->{num_fields} = $max_field_num;
			}

			my $width = length($num_expected_fields);

			for(my $i = 1; $i <= $num_expected_fields; $i++) {

				if (! exists($field_config->{$i})) {

					my $id = sprintf("field_%0${width}d", $i + 1);

					$field_config->{$i} = {
						id => $id,
						ignore => 0,
						encrypted => 0,
						name => $id,
						key => 0
					};
				};
			}

			delete $layout->{field};
			$layout->{fields} = $field_config;
		}
	}

	$ref->{keys} = \@keys;

#	print "config is good\n";
#print Dumper $ref;
	return $ref;
}

sub _normalize_fname($) {
