  my $fname = shift;
	my $re = basename($fname, '.gz');
	$re =~ s/\d/D/g;

	return $re;
}

# find similarly-named file on $search_dir that was created prior to $current_file
sub get_previous_file($$) {
  my ($search_dir, $current_file) = @_;

	my $file_re = _normalize_fname($current_file);
	my $curr_file_stat = stat($current_file);
	my $curr_file_mtime = $curr_file_stat->mtime;

	my @candidate_files = ();
	opendir(DIR, $search_dir) || die "$PGM: ERROR: Cannot open directory $search_dir to search for previous file : $!\n";

	while ($_ = readdir DIR) {
		my $full_fname = "${search_dir}/$_";
		my $stat = stat($full_fname);
		my $orig_fname = $full_fname;

		my $fname = _normalize_fname($_);
		next if ($fname !~ /^$file_re$/);

		next if ($stat->mtime >= $curr_file_mtime);

		push(@candidate_files, { fname => $orig_fname, mtime => $stat->mtime });
	}

	return undef if (! @candidate_files);

	foreach my $file (sort { $b->{mtime} <=> $a->{mtime} } @candidate_files) {
		return $file->{fname};
	}
}


my (@cmd_keys, $cmd_delimiter, @input1, @input2, $cmd_num_fields, $config_file, $num_sample_records, $decrypt_type, $cmd_min_num_fields, $cmd_header_regex, $cmd_trailer_regex, $input2_dir);

						'num-sample-records=i' => \$num_sample_records,
						'ignore-field=i@' => \@cmd_ignore_fields,
						'decrypt-field=i@' => \@cmd_decrypt_fields,
						'decrypt-type=s' => \$decrypt_type,
						'min-num-fields=i' => \$cmd_min_num_fields,
						'header-regex=s' => \$cmd_header_regex,
						'trailer-regex=s' => \$cmd_trailer_regex,
						'ignore-regex=s@' => \@cmd_ignore_regex,
						'disable-decryption' => \$DISABLE_DECRYPTION,
						'top-diffs=i' => \$TOP_DIFF_COMBINATIONS_TO_SHOW,
						'-show-exclusive-keys' => \$show_exclusive_keys,
						'-show-duplicate-keys' => \$show_duplicate_keys,
						'-xsd=s' => \$REQUESTED_XSD
) || exit(1);

push(@config_opts, config_file => $config_file) if (defined($config_file));

push(@config_opts, num_fields => $cmd_num_fields) if (defined($cmd_num_fields));
push(@config_opts, min_num_fields => $cmd_min_num_fields) if (defined($cmd_min_num_fields));
push(@config_opts, header_regex => $cmd_header_regex) if (defined($cmd_header_regex));
push(@config_opts, trailer_regex => $cmd_trailer_regex) if (defined($cmd_trailer_regex));
push(@config_opts, ignore_regex => \@cmd_ignore_regex) if (@cmd_ignore_regex);
push(@config_opts, ignore_fields => \@cmd_ignore_fields) if (@cmd_ignore_fields);
push(@config_opts, decrypt_fields => \@cmd_decrypt_fields) if (@cmd_decrypt_fields);
push(@config_opts, keys => \@cmd_keys) if (@cmd_keys);

my $all_config_info = &get_config(@config_opts);

die "Could not get config info!\n" if (! defined($all_config_info));

my $layout = $all_config_info->{'layout'};
my $autoqa;
$autoqa = $all_config_info->{'autoqa'} if (exists($all_config_info->{'autoqa'}));

my $supp_config_info = {};

$supp_config_info->{min_num_fields} = $layout->{min_num_fields};
$supp_config_info->{num_fields} = $layout->{num_fields};

if (defined($layout->{header_regex})) {
	$supp_config_info->{ignore_regex}->{$layout->{header_regex}} = 'header';
}

if (defined($layout->{trailer_regex})) {
	$supp_config_info->{ignore_regex}->{$layout->{trailer_regex}} = 'trailer';
}

if (defined($layout->{ignore})) {
	foreach my $ignore_regex_id (keys %{$layout->{ignore}}) {
		$supp_config_info->{ignore_regex}->{$layout->{ignore}->{$ignore_regex_id}->{regex}} = "$ignore_regex_id";
	}
}

#if (scalar(@{$layout->{ignore}}) >= 1) {
#	foreach my $regex (@ignore_regex) {
#		$supp_config_info->{ignore_regex}->{$regex} = "ignored via regex $regex";
#	}
#}

my $delimiter = $layout->{delimiter};

print "Field delimiter = $delimiter\n\n";

if ((scalar(@input1) == 0) && (scalar(@input2) == 0)) {
	if (scalar(@ARGV) == 0) {
		&Usage;
		exit(1);
	}

	if (scalar(@ARGV) == 2) {
		@input1 = (shift @ARGV);
		@input2 = (shift @ARGV);
	} elsif (scalar(@ARGV) == 1) {
		@input1 = (shift @ARGV);
	} else {
		die "$PGM: ERROR: Must specify 1 or 2 file names when not using -input1 or -input2 parameters\n";
	}
} else {
	if (scalar(@input1) == 0) {
		if (scalar(@ARGV) == 0) {
			die "$PGM: ERROR: Missing -input1 parameter\n";
		}

		@input1 = @ARGV;
		@ARGV = ();

		if (! defined($input2_dir)) {

			@input2 = @ARGV;

			}
		}
	}
}

if (scalar(@input2) == 0) {

		if (scalar(@input1) == 1) {
			my $input2_file = get_previous_file($input2_dir, $input1[0]);

			if (defined($input2_file)) {
				print "Found previous (input2) file $input2_file\n";
				@input2 = ($input2_file);
			} else {
				die "$PGM: ERROR: Could not determine or find input2 (previous) file in directory $input2_dir\n";
			}

			die "$PGM: ERROR: Cannot specify more than one -input1 file when using the -input2-dir option\n";
		}
	} else {
		die "$PGM: ERROR: No -input2 file was specified and -input2-dir option was not used\n";
	}
}

my $config_info = $all_config_info->{layout}->{fields};

	$IGNORE_INDEX->{$i} = 1 if (exists($config_info->{$i}->{ignore}) && $config_info->{$i}->{ignore});

print "Input 1 files: " . join(' ', @input1) . "\n";

my @keys = @{$layout->{KEYS}};

	$read_cmd1 = "$sort_command $input1_file_list |";

	die "$PGM: ERROR: Some files for -input1 are gzip compressed and others are uncompressed, which is unsupported. All -input1 files must be gzipped or uncompressed.\n";
}

my $num_input2_gz_files = grep(/[.]gz$/, @input2);

if ($num_input2_gz_files == scalar(@input2)) {
	$read_cmd2 = "gunzip -c $input2_file_list | $sort_command |";
} elsif ($num_input2_gz_files == 0) {
	$read_cmd2 = "$sort_command $input2_file_list |";
} else {
	die "$PGM: ERROR: Some files for -input2 are gzip compressed and others are uncompressed, which is unsupported. All -input2 files must be gzipped or uncompressed.\n";
}

#print Dumper $supp_config_info->{ignore_regex};

	my $ignore_re = join('|', (keys %{$supp_config_info->{ignore_regex}}));
	$read_cmd1 .= " egrep -v '$ignore_re' |";
	$read_cmd2 .= " egrep -v '$ignore_re' |";
}

print "read command 1 = $read_cmd1\n";
print "read command 2 = $read_cmd2\n\n";

our $INPUT1 = 'input1';
our $INPUT2 = 'input2';

$INPUT1 = basename($input1[0]) if (@input1 == 1);
$INPUT2 = basename($input2[0]) if (@input2 == 1);

if ($INPUT1 eq $INPUT2) {
	$INPUT1 = $input1[0];
	$INPUT2 = $input2[0];
}

if (@input1 > 1 || @input2 > 1) {
	print "input1 files: $input1_file_list\n";
	print "input2 files: $input2_file_list\n";
	print "\n";
}

our $INPUT1_LENGTH = length($INPUT1);
our $INPUT2_LENGTH = length($INPUT2);

my ($F1, $F2);

$F1->{read_cmd} = "$read_cmd1";
open($F1->{fh}, $F1->{read_cmd}) || die "$PGM: ERROR: could not sort input1 files '$input1_file_list' : $!\n";

$F1->{id} = 'input1';
$F1->{alt_id} = $INPUT1;

$F2->{read_cmd} = "$read_cmd2";

$F2->{id} = 'input2';
$F2->{alt_id} = $INPUT2;
$F2->{file_list} = $input2_file_list;
$F2->{diff_max_rec_num} = 0;

sub get_rec($$$) {
  my ($f_object, $delim, $supp_config_info) = @_;
	my $fh = $f_object->{fh};

#	if (eof($fh)) {
#		return undef;
#	}

	my (@data, $min_num_fields);

	if (exists($supp_config_info->{min_num_fields})) {
		$min_num_fields = $supp_config_info->{min_num_fields};
	}

#	my ($regexes, $line_type, $regex);
	my $line_type;

#	if (exists($supp_config_info->{ignore_regex})) {
#		$regexes = $supp_config_info->{ignore_regex};
#	}

	while (<$fh>) {
		$_ =~ s/\r?\n$//o;

		$f_object->{debug_recnum}++;
#print $f_object->{file_list} . " debug_recnum = " . $f_object->{debug_recnum} . "\n";
		@data = split(/[$delim]/o, $_, -1);
#print "debug: got " . scalar(@data) . " fields\n";
		$line_type = undef;

#		if (defined($regexes)) {
#			foreach $regex (keys %{$regexes}) {
#				if ($_ =~ /$regex/) {
#					$line_type = $regexes->{$regex};
#					last;
#				}
#			}
#		}

		if (! defined($line_type)) {
			$f_object->{counted_lines}++;

			if (defined($min_num_fields) && (scalar(@data) < $min_num_fields)) {
				$line_type = 'short';
			}
		}

		$line_type = 'record' if (! defined($line_type));


		if ($line_type ne 'record') {
			$f_object->{skipped}->{$line_type}++;
			print "...Skipping the following '$line_type' record in " . $f_object->{alt_id} . " :\n";
			print $_;
			print "\n\n";
			next;
		}

		$f_object->{recnum}++;
#print $f_object->{file_list} . " recnum = " . $f_object->{recnum} . "\n";

		return { data => \@data, recnum => $f_object->{recnum}, debug_recnum => $f_object->{debug_recnum}};
	}

	return undef;
}


sub compare_keys($$$) {
	my ($rec1_object, $rec2_object, $keys) = @_;

	if (! defined($rec1_object)) {
		if (! defined($rec2_object)) {
			die "$PGM: ERROR: compare_keys() was given two undefined records!\n";
		}
		return 1;
	} elsif (! defined($rec2_object)) {

		return -1;
	}

	my $rec1 = $rec1_object->{data};
	my $rec2 = $rec2_object->{data};

	foreach my $key_index (@{$keys}) {
		$cmp_result = $rec1->[$key_index - 1] cmp $rec2->[$key_index - 1];
		return $cmp_result if ($cmp_result != 0);
	}

	return 0; # keys were equal
}


sub is_populated($) {
	return 1 if (defined($_[0]) && ($_[0] ne ''));
	return 0;
}

sub values_equal($$) {

	#no warnings 'uninitialized';

	if ($_[0] eq $_[1]) {
		return 1;
	} else {
		return 0;
	}
}


sub compare_recs($$$$$) {
  my ($rec1_object, $rec2_object, $proper_last_index, $comp_info, $config_info) = @_;
	my $rec1 = $rec1_object->{data};
	my $rec2 = $rec2_object->{data};

	my $last_rec1_index = $#{$rec1};
	my $last_rec2_index = $#{$rec2};

	#my @indexes = sort { $b <=> $a } ($proper_last_index, $last_rec1_index, $last_rec2_index);
	my $last_index = max($proper_last_index, $last_rec1_index, $last_rec2_index);
	#my $last_index = $indexes[0];

	if ($last_rec1_index < $proper_last_index) {
		$comp_info->{input1}->{shortrec}++;
	} elsif ($last_rec1_index > $proper_last_index) {
		$comp_info->{input1}->{longrec}++;
	}

	if ($last_rec2_index < $proper_last_index) {
		$comp_info->{input2}->{shortrec}++;
	} elsif ($last_rec2_index > $proper_last_index) {
		$comp_info->{input2}->{longrec}++;
	}

	my $num_fields_to_compare;
  my $found_difference = 0;
	my ($rec1_value, $rec2_value);

	for (my $i = 0; $i <= $last_index; $i++) {

		#next if (defined($config_info) && exists($config_info->{$i}) && ($config_info->{$i}->{ignore}));
